# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Answer-Conditioned Chain-of-Thought Distillation for Few-Shot Industrial Vision with Small VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10666)
*Shubham Rao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种基于答案条件链式思维（answer-conditioned chain-of-thought）蒸馏的方法，利用前沿视觉语言模型（VLM）生成带推理过程的视觉解释，对小模型（3B参数）进行LoRA微调，在仅使用18-30张标注图片的情况下，在四项工业视觉检测任务上全面超越直接微调，平均提升1.7至4.4个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业场景中基于人工智能（AI）的视觉检测面临需求频繁变更、新型缺陷不断出现、大规模标注数据集难以获取等挑战，亟需一种能够快速适应新任务且仅需少量标注数据的模型适配方法。

Method: 采用答案条件链式思维（answer-conditioned CoT）蒸馏策略：前沿视觉语言模型（frontier VLM）在已知正确答案的条件下，为每张训练图像生成带有推理过程的视觉解释；随后，一个3B参数的小型视觉语言模型（VLM）通过低秩适配（LoRA）在这些推理增强的样本上进行微调。通过将推理条件化于正确答案，确保训练推理始终指向正确结论。

Result: 在四项工业分类任务（涵盖三种图像模态）上，每任务仅使用18至30张标注图片，每任务4个随机种子共32次训练运行中，该方法在所有16个种子-任务组合上均优于直接微调，平均提升1.7至4.4个百分点。消融实验表明，无答案条件化的基线因错误推理导致性能下降17.8个百分点。在焊缝射线照片分类任务上，微调后的3B模型仅用24张训练图片即超过GPT-4.1达10.0个百分点。

Conclusion: 答案条件化链式思维蒸馏能够在极少量标注数据下，快速将小型视觉语言模型适配至新的工业视觉检测任务，且性能提升来源于推理质量而非额外训练步数，为工业场景中的小样本（few-shot）模型部署提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Deploying AI-based visual inspection in manufacturing is hard because requirements change often, new defect types appear, and large labeled datasets are rarely available. We propose answer-conditioned chain-of-thought (CoT) distillation for rapidly adapting small vision-language models (VLMs) to new industrial tasks using minimal labeled data. A frontier VLM receives each training image along with its correct label and generates a justified visual explanation. A 3B-parameter model is then fine-tuned on these reasoning-augmented examples via LoRA. By conditioning on correct answers, we ensure all training reasoning is directed toward the correct conclusion, which is critical because frontier models score as low as 24.1% on our hardest task. We validate on four industrial classification tasks spanning three image modalities using only 18 to 30 labeled images per task. Across 4 seeds per task (32 training runs), our method outperforms direct fine-tuning on all 16 seed-task combinations, with mean improvements of +1.7 to +4.4 percentage points. A controlled equal-budget experiment confirms the improvement comes from reasoning quality, not additional training steps. An unconditioned baseline demonstrates that with out answer-conditioning, wrong reasoning degrades performance by 17.8 percentage points. On weld radiograph classification, the fine-tuned 3B model outperforms GPT-4.1 by 10.0pp using just 24 training images.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.stat-mech'></div>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Geometric Universality and Thermodynamic Microstructure of Real Fluids in a Unified Entropic Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10076)
*Carlos E. Romero-Figueroa,Jose Miguel Ladino,Sasha A. Zaldivar,Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的熵框架，将范德瓦耳斯、Berthelot、Redlich–Kwong和Peng–Robinson四种真实流体状态方程纳入共同的热力学描述中；通过几何热力学（GTD）的标量曲率分析微观相互作用，发现曲率奇点与宏观临界现象精确对应，曲率为零时对应分子间吸引力与排斥力平衡的状态；引入的无量纲临界振幅比揭示了临界区域的普适几何特征，并可作为不同分子物种的分类参数；采用贝叶斯推断与马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法统计重构零曲率曲线，验证了GTD几何标度行为的自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有真实流体的状态方程（如van der Waals、Berthelot、Redlich–Kwong、Peng–Robinson）在形式上各自独立，缺乏统一的热力学描述框架；此外，这些方程的微观相互作用机制与宏观临界现象之间的几何对应关系尚未被系统探索。

Method: 采用几何热力学（Geometrothermodynamics, GTD）方法，计算平衡流形的标量曲率$\mathcal{R}$以表征微观相互作用；引入一组无量纲临界振幅比$Q^i_{j}$揭示临界区域的几何特征；利用贝叶斯推断与马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法统计重构零曲率曲线。

Result: 曲率奇点精确再现宏观临界现象；曲率$\mathcal{R}=0$对应分子间吸引力与排斥力平衡的特定热力学状态；临界振幅比$Q^i_{j}$为尺寸无关的无量纲不变量，能依据临界强度的强弱组织不同分子物种，并编码普适标度特征；后验分布支持GTD几何标度行为的自洽性。

Conclusion: 临界振幅比$Q^i_{j}$具有作为稳健分类参数的潜力；GTD流形编码了底层的热力学模型信息，几何热力学框架能有效统一描述不同真实流体状态方程的微观与宏观行为。

Abstract: We introduce a unified entropic framework for real fluids that encompasses the van der Waals, Berthelot, Redlich Kwong, and Peng Robinson equations of state within a common thermodynamic description. The corresponding microscopic interactions are then explored using Geometrothermodynamics, GTD, through the scalar curvature $mathcal{R}$ of the equilibrium manifold. We show that curvature singularities accurately reproduce macroscopic critical phenomena, while vanishing curvature $\mathcal{R}=0$ identifies specific thermodynamic states where attractive and repulsive intermolecular forces effectively balance. Furthermore, we introduce a set of dimensionless critical-amplitude ratios $Q^i_{j}$, which reveal universal geometric features of the critical regime. Although individual critical amplitudes exhibit a logarithmic dependence on the system size, these invariant ratios organize different molecular species according to the strength of criticality and encode universal scaling features, suggesting their potential as robust classification parameters. Finally, employing Bayesian inference and Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC methods, we statistically reconstruct the zero-curvature curves. The posterior distributions support the consistency of the geometric scaling behavior, demonstrating that the GTD manifold encodes non-trivial information about the underlying thermodynamical models.

</details>


### [3] [Dimensional and Spin Interpolation for the O$(n)$ Model: From Exact Anchors to RG-Improved Critical Exponents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10865)
*Kumar Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了O$(n)$普适类家族的双轴插值框架，将空间维度$D$和自旋分量数$n$作为独立连续参数，连接精确极限解，在无需可调参数的情况下准确预测了三维伊辛模型的临界耦合与临界指数，并建立了插值成功的兼容性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对临界现象（critical phenomena）的研究通常局限于整数维度或整数自旋分量数，缺乏一个统一的连续参数框架来连接不同极限下的精确解。本文旨在建立一种双轴插值方法，同时沿空间维度$D$和自旋分量数$n$两个方向进行连续插值，从而在统一框架下预测O$(n)$普适类（universality class）的临界行为。

Method: 沿空间轴，以$D=2$时的Onsager解和$D\to\infty$时的平均场理论（mean-field theory）为锚点进行插值；沿自旋轴，建立单调性兼容性判据（compatibility criterion），并结合微扰$1/n^2$展开（perturbative expansion）与Wilson-Fisher约束多项式插值（polynomial interpolation）。

Result: 空间轴：预测三维伊辛临界耦合$K_c=0.2204$（基准值$0.22165$），指数$ν=2/3$、$β=31/96$、$η=35/864$（基准值分别为$0.6299$、$0.3265$、$0.0362$），并复现共形自举（conformal bootstrap）在$3\le D<4$的结果。自旋轴：$ν(3)=0.7493$（基准$0.7112$），$β(3)=0.3797$（基准$0.3689$），$γ(3)=1.489$（基准$1.396$），并预测O$(2.5)$普适类的$ν(2.5)=0.7143$。

Conclusion: 维度插值与自旋插值构成了一种统一且具有预测能力的临界现象研究方法；插值成功的结构条件是可观测量在锚点之间单调变化，文章建立的兼容性判据为后续应用提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We develop a two-axis interpolation framework for the O$(n)$ universality family, treating the spatial dimension $D$ and the spin-component number $n$ as independent continuous parameters connecting exact limiting solutions. On the spatial axis, anchoring between the Onsager solution at $D=2$ and mean-field theory at $D\to\infty$ yields a closed-form prediction for the 3D Ising critical coupling that agrees well with Monte Carlo benchmarks $K_c = 0.2204$ (benchmark: $0.22165$) with no adjustable parameters. Wilson--Fisher-constrained polynomial interpolation gives $ν=2/3$, $β=31/96$, and $η=35/864$ at $D=3$ (benchmarks: $0.6299$, $0.3265$, $0.0362$), and reproduces conformal-bootstrap results across $3 \le D < 4$. On the spin axis, we establish a necessary compatibility criterion: two-anchor interpolation succeeds only for observables that vary monotonically between the anchor values. The critical coupling $K_c(n)$ violates this criterion because the Heisenberg value falls below the spherical limit, whereas the correlation-length exponent $ν(n)$ satisfies it. A perturbative $1/n^2$ expansion yields $ν(3) = 0.7493$ (benchmark: $0.7112$), and propagation through exact scaling relations gives $β(3) = 0.3797$ (benchmark: $0.3689$) and $γ(3) = 1.489$ (benchmark: $1.396$), without introducing additional parameters. The framework naturally extends to non-integer spin, producing the prediction $ν(2.5) = 0.7143$ for the O$(2.5)$ universality class. These results establish dimensional and spin interpolation as a unified and predictive approach to critical phenomena, while clarifying the structural conditions under which interpolation succeeds.

</details>


### [4] [Revisiting the non-equilibrium phase transitions of the continuous-trait Axelrod model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10381)
*Sandro M. Reia,Paulo R. A. Campos,José F. Fontanari*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过重新分析连续特质Axelrod模型（continuous-trait Axelrod model）中的非平衡相变（non-equilibrium phase transition），发现以往研究中看似连续的相变实则受有限尺寸效应（finite-size masking effects）严重干扰。通过转向中位数尺度（median scaling）和完整概率分布分析，研究揭示：当特质维度F=2时，系统呈现真正的混合相变（hybrid transition），包含一个微小但有限的潜跃变（latent jump）和非解析幂律标度；当F=3时，由于特质空间维度升高抑制了局域涨落，系统转变为传统的一阶相变（first-order transition）。该框架还成功统一描述了离散Poisson变体模型中的相变类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究认为连续特质Axelrod模型的非平衡相变是混合型（hybrid），基于域密度μ的连续行为和最大域分数ρ的不连续跳变。但这一结论可能受到有限尺寸效应的严重干扰，因而需要更精确的统计方法来重新审视相变的真实本质。

Method: 研究将方法论焦点从域密度μ的均值转向中位数$\tildeμ$的尺度行为（scaling），并分析完整概率分布$P(μ)$，以检测双峰结构（bimodal structure）和不相交的极大值。对于F=2和F=3两种情况，分别进行临界阈值附近的有限尺寸标度分析，并提取临界指数β。

Result: 对于F=2，系统在临界阈值$d_c \approx 0.0784$处发生混合相变：存在一个微小但有限的潜跃变$μ_c \approx 0.089$，且从下方趋近时遵循非解析幂律标度，平均场临界指数$β\approx 1/2$。对于F=3，更高的特质空间维度抑制局域涨落，导致传统的非混合一阶相变。该框架成功应用于离散Poisson变体模型，确认了其已知的F=2连续相变和F=3不连续非混合相变。

Conclusion: 研究建立了一个统一的相变分类框架，系统刻画了Axelrod类系统中非平衡相变的混合与非混合、连续与不连续特征，揭示了有限尺寸效应对相变类型判断的关键影响。

Abstract: We investigate the non-equilibrium phase transitions of the continuous-trait Axelrod model, an agent-based framework where individual culture is represented by a vector of $F$ continuous features confined to the interval $(0,1)$. Local interactions are governed by a metric similarity threshold $d$, which acts as a continuous control parameter of social tolerance. The dynamics inevitably freeze into one of two absorbing configuration classes: an ordered, homogeneous monocultural state at high tolerance, or a highly fragmented, disordered state at low tolerance. While previous studies characterized the transition as hybrid based on the continuous behavior of the domain density $μ$ alongside a discontinuous jump in the largest domain fraction $ρ$, we show that this apparent continuity is an artifact of severe finite-size masking effects. By shifting the methodological focus to the scaling of the median $\tildeμ$ and analyzing the full probability distributions $P(μ)$, we unveil a clear bimodal structure with disjoint maxima across independent simulation runs. Our results reveal that for $F=2$, the system undergoes a genuinely hybrid transition in the contemporary sense, featuring a tiny but finite latent jump ($μ_c \approx 0.089$) at the critical threshold $d_c \approx 0.0784$ while scaling toward it from below via a non-analytical power law with a mean-field exponent $β\approx 1/2$. Conversely, for $F=3$, the higher trait-space dimensionality suppresses local fluctuations, yielding a traditional, non-hybrid first-order transition. We apply this framework to the alternative discrete Poisson variant of the model, successfully confirming its known continuous transition for $F=2$ and discontinuous, non-hybrid transition for $F=3$, thereby establishing a unified characterization of phase transitions in Axelrod-like systems.

</details>


### [5] [A Cascade of Volterra-Operator BBP Transitions in a Correlated Wigner Matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10503)
*Masato Hisakado*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类Wigner型随机矩阵，其非对角相关性由行与列共享的随机因子产生。尽管体谱矩遵循纯半圆律，但相关性矩阵分解为零化体谱和可数族离群特征值，这些特征值收敛于紧Volterra积分算子的奇异值（通过布朗运动的Karhunen–Loève展开获得闭式解）。每个奇异值随耦合强度增加驱动独立的Baik–Ben Arous–Péché (BBP)转变，产生均匀间隔的离散临界层级，而非单一转变。该机制可推广至更广泛的相关结构族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有行-列共享随机因子相关结构的Wigner型随机矩阵，揭示其谱分解与离群特征值的渐近行为，以及耦合强度驱动的临界转变层级结构。

Method: 采用紧Volterra（累积和）积分算子与布朗运动的Karhunen–Loève展开相结合的方法，推导离群特征值的闭式解；通过数值对角化验证前二十个奇异值（误差优于1%）；分析耦合强度增加时每个奇异值驱动的独立Baik–Ben Arous–Péché (BBP)转变。

Result: 体谱矩保持纯半圆律；相关性矩阵分解为零化体谱和可数族离群特征值；固定秩k下离群特征值收敛于紧Volterra积分算子的奇异值；每个奇异值驱动独立的BBP转变，产生均匀间隔的离散临界点层级，每个临界点处一个特征值从半圆边缘脱离。

Conclusion: 该特征值脱层机制可推广至更广泛的相关结构族，临界层级由关联紧积分算子的谱决定。

Abstract: We study a Wigner-type random matrix in which the off-diagonal correlation between entries is generated by a random factor shared among all entries in a given row and column, with the coupling strength held fixed as the matrix size grows. Although the bulk spectral moments remain those of the pure semicircle law, we show that the underlying correlation matrix decomposes into a vanishing bulk together with a countable family of outlier eigenvalues that, at fixed rank $k$, converge to the singular values of a compact Volterra (cumulative-sum) integral operator -- obtained in closed form via the classical Karhunen--Loève expansion of Brownian motion and confirmed numerically to better than one percent across the top twenty such values. Each singular value drives an independent Baik--Ben Arous--Péché (BBP) transition as the coupling strength increases, producing an evenly spaced, discrete hierarchy of critical points -- rather than a single transition -- at each of which one further eigenvalue detaches from the semicircle edge, in close agreement with direct diagonalization. We show that this mechanism generalizes to a broader family of correlation structures, with the critical hierarchy in every case set by the spectrum of an associated compact integral operator.

</details>


### [6] [Finite-time Scaling of the surface special transition in a 3D classical Heisenberg model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11066)
*Dongxu Liu,Zhe Wang,Shuai Yin,Zheng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用蒙特卡洛模拟，研究三维经典海森堡模型（经典海森堡模型，classical Heisenberg model）中跨越特殊表面相变（special surface phase transition）的非平衡驱动动力学，发现当从反常对数（extraordinary-log）边界临界态驱动时，大速率标度关系出现对数修正，并给出了推广的有限时间标度（finite-time scaling, FTS）形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有对数（logarithmic）而非幂律（power-law）衰减相关的反常对数边界临界态在非平衡驱动下的标度行为，并检验有限时间标度（FTS）和Kibble-Zurek机制（Kibble-Zurek mechanism）在此类边界临界态中的适用性。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation），针对三维经典海森堡模型实现四种驱动协议：温度加热与冷却穿越特殊转变点，以及从普通（ordinary）和反常对数（extraordinary-log）边界临界态向特殊点（special point）的表面耦合斜坡（surface-coupling ramp）。

Result: 从反常对数临界态驱动时，大速率标度关系呈现出对数修正形式：$M^{2}_{s}\propto R^{(1+η_{s})/r_{s}}[\log(LR^{1/η_{s}})]^{-q}$，其中$R$为驱动速率，$L$为系统尺寸，$η_{s}$为表面反常维数（surface anomalous dimension），$r_{s}$为$R$的标度维数，$q$为对数边界临界性指数。在广泛系统尺寸和驱动速率下实现了优异的数据坍塌（data collapse）。

Conclusion: 反常对数初始态会改变非平衡临界标度行为，将边界有限时间标度（boundary FTS）从传统的幂律初始条件推广至对数型初始条件，从而扩展了FTS框架的适用范围。

Abstract: We investigate nonequilibrium driven dynamics across the special surface phase transition in the three-dimensional classical Heisenberg model with open boundaries, where tuning the surface coupling gives access to an extraordinary-log boundary critical state characterized by logarithmic, rather than power-law, decay of correlations. Using Monte Carlo simulations, we realize four driving protocols: temperature heating and cooling across the special transition, and surface-coupling ramps from the ordinary and extraordinary-log critical states into the special point. For temperature-driven protocols, the surface order parameter obeys a generalization of the finite-time scaling (FTS) and the Kibble-Zurek mechanism. The central finding emerges when the system is driven from the extraordinary-log critical state: the large-rate scaling relation acquires a logarithmic correction and takes the novel form $M^{2}_{s}\propto R^{(1+η_{s})/r_{s}}[\log(LR^{1/η_{s}})]^{-q}$ , where $R$ is the driving rate, $L$ the system size, $η_{s}$ the surface anomalous dimension, $r_{s}$ the scaling dimension of $R$, and $q$ the exponent governing the logarithmic boundary criticality. We demonstrate that this form follows from the general FTS framework by incorporating the logarithmic initial-state memory, and we achieve excellent data collapse over a wide range of system sizes and driving rates. Our results establish that extraordinary-log initial states alter nonequilibrium critical scaling, extending boundary FTS beyond conventional power-law initial conditions.

</details>


### [7] [Harnessing finite-size effects to gauge aging in the $2D$ Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11524)
*Dustin Warkotsch,Malte Henkel,Wolfhard Janke*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有最近邻相互作用的二维伊辛模型（2D Ising model）趋向平衡的弛豫行为，重点分析了双时间自关联函数（two-time autocorrelator）C(t,s)的有限尺寸效应，并利用这些标度关系在小格点上精确估计了自关联指数λ和动力学指数z。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解二维伊辛模型在趋向平衡过程中的弛豫行为，特别是双时间自关联函数C(t,s)中由有限尺寸效应引起的饱和与平台现象，并利用这些效应在小格点上精确估算关键动力学指数。

Method: 通过分析有限尺寸效应对生长磁畴的影响，发现C(t,s)呈现饱和现象并出现一个高度为C_{\infty}^{(2)}(s,L)的独特平台，该平台高度随等待时间（waiting time）s和格点尺寸L呈代数标度关系。研究者利用这些标度关系，在刻意选取的小格点上估计自关联指数λ和动力学指数z。此外，将光滑畴壁（smooth domain walls）的处理方式类比于晶格边界，将其对C(t,s)的影响理解为一种过早出现的有限尺寸现象。

Result: 发现了C(t,s)中由有限尺寸效应导致的饱和平台，其高度C_{\infty}^{(2)}(s,L)与s和L满足代数标度关系；利用这些标度关系在小格点上获得了自关联指数λ和动力学指数z的精确估计。

Conclusion: 光滑畴壁对C(t,s)的影响可以被视为一种过早的有限尺寸现象（premature finite-size phenomenon），从而将所提出的标度关系（ansatz）推广到尚未达到平衡的系统中。

Abstract: The relaxation behavior towards equilibrium of the $2D$ Ising model with nearest-neighbor interactions has been studied with focus on the two-time autocorrelator $C(t,s)$. Finite-size effects affecting the growing magnetic domains lead to the saturation of $C(t,s)$ with a distinct plateau of height $C_{\infty}^{(2)}(s,L)$ scaling algebraically with waiting time $s$ and lattice size $L$. These scaling relations are used to produce precise estimates for the autocorrelation exponent $λ$ and dynamical exponent $z$ with deliberately small lattices. Treating smooth domain walls in a similar manner to the lattice boundaries, their effect on $C(t,s)$ can be understood as premature finite-size phenomenon, extending our ansatz to systems not yet in equilibrium.

</details>


### [8] [Thermal phase transitions in a mixed-spin Ising model on the Lieb lattice: Exact results beyond zero magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11661)
*Jozef Strecka,Katarina Karlova*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了掺杂单轴单离子各向异性和磁场的混合自旋-1/2与自旋-1 Ising模型在装饰方格(Lieb)晶格上的基态与有限温度性质。通过广义装饰-迭代变换，模型被精确映射为有效自旋-1/2 Ising模型，从而在有效场为零时成为精确可解模型。基态分析揭示三个不同相：亚铁磁相(FRI)、无序相(DP)和铁磁相(FM)。FRI与DP之间的基态边界形成穹顶状不连续热相变表面，终止于伊辛型临界点连续相变线。在窄参数区域中识别出两次连续不连续热诱导重入相变DP-FRI-DP。所有精确解析结果均经经典蒙特卡洛模拟独立验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究混合自旋系统在格子上的精确可解性，以及外加磁场和单轴各向异性对基态和有限温度相行为的影响，尤其是重入相变(Reentrant phase transition)和热驱动相变等非平凡现象。

Method: 采用广义装饰-迭代变换(generalized decoration-iteration transformation)，将混合自旋模型精确映射为简单方格上的有效自旋-1/2 Ising模型；结合基态分析和经典蒙特卡洛模拟(Monte Carlo simulation)进行独立验证。

Result: 基态存在亚铁磁相(FRI)、无序相(DP)和铁磁相(FM)三种相；FRI-DP边界形成穹顶状不连续热相变表面，终止于伊辛型临界点(Ising-type critical point)连续相变线；窄参数区域内识别出两次连续不连续热诱导重入相变DP-FRI-DP。

Conclusion: 混合自旋-1/2与自旋-1 Ising模型在有效场为零条件下可精确求解；精确预测的重入现象、场驱动和热驱动相变均可由蒙特卡洛模拟验证，表明解析方法可靠。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state and finite-temperature properties of a mixed spin-1/2 and spin-1 Ising model on a decorated square (Lieb) lattice incorporating a uniaxial single-ion anisotropy and magnetic field. By employing the generalized decoration-iteration transformation, the model is mapped exactly onto an effective spin-1/2 Ising model on the square lattice characterized by an effective nearest-neighbor interaction and an effective field. The studied model consequently becomes exactly solvable even for finite values of the applied magnetic field whenever the effective field vanishes. The ground-state analysis reveals three distinct phases: ferrimagnetic phase (FRI), disordered phase (DP), and ferromagnetic (FM) phase. The ground-state boundary between FRI and DP phases gives rise to a dome-shaped surface of discontinuous thermal phase transitions, which is terminated by a line of Ising-type critical points associated with continuous thermal phase transitions. Both continuous and discontinuous thermal phase transitions belong to the exactly solvable parameter regime defined by a vanishing effective field in spite of the fact that the applied magnetic field is finite. Two consecutive discontinuous thermally-induced reentrant phase transitions DP-FRI-DP are identified in a narrow parameter region. The exact analytical predictions including reentrance, field- and thermally-driven phase transitions are independently verified by classical Monte Carlo simulations.

### [9] [Still life in a classic Blume-Capel model: pseudo-transitions in a spin-1 diamond chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11669)
*Elham Shahhosseini Shahrabadi,Majid Moradi,Jozef Strecka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix method）精确研究了磁场中自旋-1 Blume-Capel 菱形链的基态、磁性与热力学性质，发现非简并基态与竞争性宏观简并低能激发态之间的极小能隙会导致熵驱动的赝转变（pseudo-transitions），表现为磁化与熵的陡峭连续变化以及磁化率和比热的尖锐有限峰。该结果将赝转变的存在范围扩展至经典自旋-1 Blume-Capel 模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究自旋-1 Blume-Capel 菱形链在磁场中的精确基态相图与有限温度行为，特别是验证赝转变现象是否也存在于经典自旋-1 模型中，从而扩展已知可展现赝转变的一维自旋系统类别。

Method: 采用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix method）对磁场中自旋-1 Blume-Capel 菱形链的基态、磁性与热力学性质进行精确解析研究，建立完整的基态相图并表征各基态自旋构型。

Result: 非简并基态与竞争性宏观简并低能激发态之间存在极小的能隙，由此产生熵驱动的赝转变。这些赝转变表现为磁化（magnetization）和熵（entropy）类似不连续跳变的陡峭但连续的变化，而磁化率（magnetic susceptibility）和比热（specific heat）则呈现类似发散但实为有限尖锐峰的结构。

Conclusion: 赝转变也可在经典自旋-1 Blume-Capel 模型中产生，从而将该类现象的已知模型范围扩展至更广泛的一维自旋系统。

Abstract: We exactly investigate the ground-state, magnetic, and thermodynamic properties of a spin-1 Blume-Capel diamond chain in a magnetic field by means of the transfer-matrix method. After establishing the complete ground-state phase diagram and characterizing each ground-state spin configuration, we examine the finite-temperature behavior in the vicinity of selected phase boundaries and triple points. It is demonstrated that an extremely small energy gap between a nondegenerate ground state and competing macroscopically degenerate low-lying excited states gives rise to entropically-driven pseudo-transitions. These pseudo-transitions manifest themselves through abrupt but continuous changes in the magnetization and entropy resembling discontinuous jumps, while the magnetic susceptibility and specific heat exhibit exceptionally sharp yet finite peaks resembling divergences. Our results provide the exact evidence that pseudo-transitions can also emerge in the classical spin-1 Blume-Capel model and thereby extend the class of one-dimensional spin systems known to display pseudo-transitions.

### [10] [A Fokker-Planck approach to a stochastic multiplicative wealth model with taxation and redistribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11755)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展由P.M.C. de Oliveira提出的原始随机乘性经济增长模型，引入一般化的再分配协议，以理解税收、再分配与乘性噪声之间的相互作用如何影响财富不平等的形成机制。

Method: 采用福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）描述财富分布的动力学；引入一般化的再分配协议，涵盖一类广泛的状态依赖转移机制；特别考察了一种模拟有条件现金转移（conditional cash transfer）项目的两态协议；利用基尼指数（Gini index）量化不平等程度，并通过基于智能体的模拟（agent-based simulations）对理论结果进行验证。

Result: 推导出了稳态财富分布（stationary wealth distributions）的解析表达式；揭示了乘性噪声（multiplicative noise）、税收与再分配之间的相互作用如何塑造不平等的出现；理论结果与基于智能体的模拟结果一致；分析表明，特定的非均匀再分配方案可以显著缓解财富差距。

Conclusion: 再分配协议的设计对财富不平等有重要影响，非均匀的再分配机制比均匀机制更能有效降低贫富差距；所提出的理论框架为评估不同再分配政策的效果提供了分析工具。

Abstract: We develop a Fokker-Planck description of the dynamics of wealth distribution in a stochastic multiplicative economic growth model with taxation and redistribution, as introduced by P.M.C. de Oliveira. Extending the original formulation, our theoretical framework includes general redistribution protocols, encompassing a broad class of state-dependent transfer mechanisms. As a particular case, we investigate a two-state protocol designed to emulate conditional cash transfer programs. Analytical expressions for the stationary wealth distributions are derived, revealing how the interplay between multiplicative noise, taxation, and redistribution shapes the emergence of inequality. The theoretical results are corroborated by agent-based simulations. To quantify and compare the impact of the different protocols, we employ the Gini index as a measure of inequality. Our analysis highlights how specific nonuniform redistribution schemes can significantly mitigate wealth disparities.

### [11] [Extending the Mpemba effect to the underdamped realm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11797)
*Shahaf Aharony Shapira,Gene Chen,Marija Vucelja,Oren Raz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在欠阻尼（underdamped）体系中研究姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect），证明该效应在过阻尼极限（overdamped limit）存在的前提下，可在有限阻尼下延续；在超弱阻尼极限（ultra-weak-damping limit）下，对于光滑单阱势（single-well potentials）和正则初始态（canonical initial states）该效应无法出现，但可在更复杂的势（如双阱势，double-well potentials）中发生。数值模拟验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 姆潘巴效应已在多种经典过阻尼体系（overdamped systems）中被实验证实，但在惯性不可忽略的欠阻尼体系（underdamped regime）中是否存在尚未明确。本文旨在探索该效应在欠阻尼条件下的存在性及其条件。

Method: 采用布朗粒子（Brownian particle）在势场中的欠阻尼动力学作为模型，通过微扰论（perturbation theory）分析有限阻尼情形，并在超弱阻尼极限下对光滑单阱势与更复杂势进行理论推导与数值模拟验证。

Result: 若效应在过阻尼极限存在，则在足够大但有限的阻尼条件下效应仍然持续。在超弱阻尼极限下，光滑单阱势与正则初始态组合时效应不存在，但在更复杂的势（如双阱势）中效应可以出现。

Conclusion: 姆潘巴效应在欠阻尼体系中的存在性高度依赖阻尼强度与势能形状。该结果扩展了对这一反直觉现象在惯性主导区域中的理解。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect is the counterintuitive phenomenon in which an initially hotter system cools faster than a colder, otherwise identical system. It has been experimentally demonstrated in various classical overdamped systems. Here, we explore the existence of the same effect in a regime where inertia cannot be neglected, namely, the underdamped regime. We consider the underdamped dynamics of a Brownian particle in a potential. We show perturbatively that, if the effect exists in the overdamped limit, it persists for sufficiently large but finite damping. In the ultra-weak-damping limit, we show that the effect cannot occur for smooth confining single-well potentials with canonical initial states, but can arise in more complex potentials. We demonstrate our results numerically using double-well potentials, the canonical setting for the Mpemba effect in the overdamped limit.

</details>


### [12] [Slow is fast: raising barriers to accelerate thermal relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11877)
*Yubo Wang,Zhiyue Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，在可逆系统弛豫到平衡的过程中，直观上“打开所有能垒（gate）”的策略在三个层级上最优（局部电导、瞬时速度、弛豫本征值），但第四层级——本征向量旋转（eigenvector rotation）——存在反直觉的有限时间最优解。非对易性（noncommutativity）允许时间调度重投影残余振幅，从而加速弛豫；最优调度为bang-bang型，且存在反栅控（counter-gating）策略。论文证明了非对易性的必要性，并揭示了对偶调度在保持非平衡自由能方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索可逆系统弛豫到平衡过程中，是否存在超越直观“全开栅极”策略的有限时间最优控制方案，并揭示其背后的理论机制。

Method: 通过四个层级的理论分析（局部电导、f-散度的瞬时速度、弛豫本征值、本征向量旋转），引入非对易性框架和bang-bang最优调度，并结合反栅控策略进行数值验证。

Result: 直观的全开栅格策略在前三个层级最优，但第四层级（本征向量旋转）揭示了有限时间最优调度；最优调度为bang-bang型，反栅控策略可将末端残余降低至全开策略的1/130、最佳静态景观的1/7。非对易性被证明是必要条件。

Conclusion: 加速或延缓弛豫的栅格控制在约化马尔可夫系统上不做功，仅重新分配固定的总耗散预算；对偶调度在维持非平衡自由能方面显著优于直觉策略。

Abstract: For a reversible system relaxing to equilibrium, the obvious fastest strategy is to lower all kinetic barriers (open all gates). We find that such intuition holds at three levels: the all-open-gate strategy achieves the highest local conductance, it maximizes the instantaneous speed of approach in every $f$-divergence, and it simultaneously maximizes all relaxation eigenvalues. Nevertheless, we show that a counter-intuitive finite-time optimum lies beyond this intuition and operates at a fourth level, invisible to all three: eigenvector rotation. Noncommutativity enables timed schedules to reproject residual amplitudes across relaxation modes, thereby achieving faster relaxation. Optimal schedules are bang--bang. In our illustrative example, the best-found schedule also employs counter-gating, transiently raising selected barriers, and reduces the terminal residual by a factor of $130$ relative to all-open, and by $7$ relative to the best static landscape. A no-go theorem shows that noncommutativity is necessary: commuting generators collapse every schedule to a static time-averaged landscape, worse than the intuitive static control. In the reverse problem, the dual schedule preserves nonequilibrium free energy far more effectively than intuitively keeping all barriers at maximum heights. Whether accelerating or delaying relaxation, barrier control performs no work on the reduced Markov system; it only re-times a fixed total dissipation budget.

</details>

### [13] [Odd Polycatenanes Tank-Tread in Strong Shear Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09928)
*Ali Seyedi,Charles W. Manke,Alex Albaugh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粗粒化布朗动力学模拟，结合流体动力学相互作用，研究了线性聚链烷烃（polycatenanes）在强稳态剪切流中的单分子动力学，发现了一种稳定的“坦克践踏”（tank-treading）状态，且该状态几乎仅出现在奇数环数的聚链烷烃中，并提出其潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚链烷烃是一类通过机械键（mechanical bond）连接环状分子形成的互锁聚合物，但其在剪切流中的单分子动力学行为尚不清楚，尤其是否存在类似拉伸流中的特殊构象和奇偶效应（odd-even effect）有待探究。

Method: 采用粗粒化布朗动力学（coarse-grained Brownian dynamics）模拟，并考虑流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions），对线性聚链烷烃在强稳态剪切流中的行为进行数值研究。

Result: 发现一种稳定的坦克践踏状态，其中单个环连续旋转，而整体聚合物保持高度伸展并与流方向对齐；该状态几乎仅出现在奇数环数的聚链烷烃中；马尔可夫状态模型（Markov state model）证明该动态行为在长时间尺度上稳定；此外，坦克践踏聚链烷烃可用于在强剪切流中完全伸展其他分子。

Conclusion: 奇数环聚链烷烃的末端环在流-梯度平面内的取向是产生奇偶效应的关键机制，末端环起到“锚点”作用稳定聚合物的伸展；坦克践踏行为在旋转流中操纵分子方面具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Polycatenanes are mechanically interlocked polymers composed of ring molecules linked through mechanical bonds. Here, we investigate the single-molecule dynamics of linear polycatenanes under strong steady shear flow using coarse-grained Brownian dynamics simulations with hydrodynamic interactions. We identify a stable tank-treading state in which individual rings rotate continuously while the overall polymer remains highly extended and aligned with the flow direction, adopting conformations typically associated with extensional flow. Remarkably, tank-treading is observed almost exclusively in odd polycatenanes, polycatenanes with an odd number of rings. We attribute this odd-even effect to the orientation of the terminal rings within the flow-gradient plane, where they act as anchors that stabilize polymer extension, a configuration accessible only to odd polycatenanes. Furthermore, our simulations and a Markov state model demonstrate that this dynamic behavior remains stable over long timescales. Finally, we show that tank treading polycatenanes can be used to fully extend other molecules in strong shear flow, hinting at applications of this behavior to manipulate molecules in rotational flows.

</details>


### [14] [Nonreciprocal multi-body interactions activate liquid state of acoustically levitated particle ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09960)
*Nina M. Brown,Heinrich M. Jaeger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过声悬浮被动微球实验发现，即使物体间成对相互作用完全互易，非成对多体相互作用（non-pairwise multi-body interactions）也能在构型对称性破缺时涌现出非互易性力（nonreciprocal forces），使粒子集体行为类似液滴，展现出超扩散运动、非高斯速度分布及极低界面张力下的自相似收缩特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在物体本身相同且各向同性、两两之间相互作用完全互易的条件下，非互易力是否可能通过非成对多体相互作用涌现，并考察这种涌现非互易性（emergent nonreciprocity）如何影响粒子集合体的集体动力学行为。

Method: 在空气中利用声悬浮（acoustic levitation）技术捕获被动微球（passive microspheres），形成包含数百个粒子的自由浮动单层（monolayer），使其表现为二维液滴（two-dimensional liquid droplet）。粒子间的非互易多体力源于声散射（acoustic scattering）与声诱导粘性微流（sound-induced viscous microstreaming）的耦合。实验中还引入横向探针进行悬挂液滴（pendant drop）和缩颈断裂（pinch-off）实验。

Result: 非互易多体力驱动粒子表现出超扩散运动（superdiffusive motion）以及速度分布中的非高斯拖尾（non-Gaussian tails）。液滴的运动粘度（kinematic viscosity）与水相当，但界面张力（interfacial tension）极低。缩颈断裂由非互易性诱导的主动涨落驱动，断裂区域呈现双锥颈部轮廓（double-cone neck profile），其标度指数异常小。

Conclusion: 涌现非互易性可以驱动被动粒子集合体表现出类似液体的行为，且具有区别于普通液体的独特特征，如超扩散、非高斯统计与异常标度行为，为非平衡主动物质（active matter）系统提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal forces are often a consequence of asymmetry in the properties of the interacting objects. However. even if all objects are identical and isotropic, and the pairwise interactions between two objects are completely reciprocal, nonreciprocal forces can still appear when an arrangement of many objects breaks configurational symmetry in the presence of non-pairwise, multi-body interactions. Here we demonstrate that such emergent nonreciprocity can activate a particle ensemble to behave like a liquid, albeit with unique traits. In our experiments, passive microspheres are acoustically levitated in air, where they form a freely floating monolayer containing up to a couple hundred particles and collectively behave like a two-dimensional liquid droplet. The particles interact via nonreciprocal multi-body forces that arise from the combination of acoustic scattering and sound-induced viscous microstreaming. We find that these forces drive superdiffusive particle motion with non-Gaussian tails in the particles' speed distribution. Using probes that reach laterally into the levitation plane, we perform liquid pendant drop and pinch-off experiments. Compared to ordinary liquids, the droplets are found to have a kinematic viscosity similar to that of water, but in combination with an extremely low interfacial tension. The pinching-off is driven by nonreciprocity-induced active fluctuations and exhibits the self-similar double-cone neck profile seen also in liquid nanojets close to rupture, however here characterized by power law behavior with a scaling exponent that is anomalously small.

</details>


### [15] [Spatiotemporal Disk Packing for Directed Growth of Complex Geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09991)
*Yigit Hergul,Yun Seong Kim,Rohan Shah,Sameh Tawfick,Varda F. Hagh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于圆盘填充算法（disk packing algorithm）的几何框架，用于生长预设的二维形状。通过将目标几何区域填充为由物理约束（生长速度、启动时间、并行启动数）限定的圆盘，并引入最大间隙算法（Largest Gap Algorithm, LGA）生成物理可行的填充方案，最终将填充指令直接用于实验（如CO₂激光引发的前沿聚合），实现了复杂形状的生长控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂形状的生长需要同时控制生长的起始位置和时间演化过程。现有的方法难以在物理约束下简单、有效地将几何目标转化为生长指令，因此有必要建立一个连接几何与动力学的通用框架。

Method: 采用圆盘填充算法，其中圆盘中心定义生长起始点，半径定义每个区域的生长时长。圆盘尺寸受生长速度、启动时间及并行启动数等物理因素约束。提出最大间隙算法（Largest Gap Algorithm, LGA），依次用满足几何与动力学约束的最大圆盘填充剩余最大间隙。填充结果可直接转化为时空生长指令，并通过多起点引发的CO₂激光前沿聚合在黏性双环戊二烯（DCPD）树脂中实验实现。

Result: 该方法在多种几何形状下均实现了高覆盖率的圆盘填充，且生成的填充指令可直接用于实验。实验表明，通过编程少量局部启动事件即可生长出复杂形状。

Conclusion: 该几何框架建立了形状几何与生长动力学之间的简单联系，证明只需控制少量局部启动事件就能实现复杂形状的生长，为可控生长过程提供了实用的设计策略。

Abstract: Growing complex shapes requires control over both where growth begins and how it evolves in time. Here, we introduce a geometric framework for growing prescribed 2D shapes using a disk packing algorithm. In this approach, a target geometry is filled by disks whose centers define where growth is initiated and whose radii define how long each region is allowed to grow. The allowed disk sizes are constrained by the physics of the process, including the growth velocity, the time required to initiate each growth event, and the number of initiations that can occur in parallel. To generate physically realizable packings, we introduce the Largest Gap Algorithm (LGA), which sequentially fills the largest remaining gaps in a target shape with the largest disk that satisfies both geometric and kinetic constraints. We show that this method produces high coverage packings for a variety of geometries and that the resulting packings can be directly converted into spatiotemporal packing instructions. We then demonstrate that these instructions can be realized experimentally using multi-point initiation of frontal polymerization in viscosified dicyclopentadiene (DCPD) resin using CO$_2$ laser. Our results show that complex shapes can be grown by programming a small number of local initiation events, providing a simple connection between geometry and dynamics of growth.

### [16] [Arrhenius-Type Description and Noise-Composition Dependence of Single-Vacancy Hopping in Active Brownian Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10192)
*Hiroto Tomida,Yoshihiro Yamazaki*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过对二维活性布朗粒子晶体（active Brownian-particle crystal）中单个空位（vacancy）介导的跳跃动力学（hopping dynamics）进行模拟，发现活性驱动下跳跃速率不能用自由粒子的有效噪声振幅（effective noise amplitude）统一描述，并且在被动极限下跳跃速率符合阿伦尼乌斯型（Arrhenius-like）激活趋势，但有效噪声比较显示活性成分比例会系统性地影响跳跃动力学，从而表明有效温度描述（effective-temperature description）在活性晶体中的微观缺陷介导输运中失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性物质（active matter）中晶体缺陷（crystal defect）介导的微观输运机制，特别是检验是否可以用有效温度（effective temperature）这一概念统一描述活性晶体中的空位跳跃动力学。

Method: 构建二维活性布朗粒子晶体模型，引入单个空位缺陷，通过数值模拟研究空位跳跃速率（hopping rate）与主动驱动强度、有效噪声及活性分数（active fraction）之间的关系，并与被动极限（passive limit）下的阿伦尼乌斯行为进行对比。

Result: 活性驱动下跳跃速率并不由自由粒子的有效噪声振幅单独决定；被动极限下跳跃速率随平移扩散系数（translational diffusion coefficient）呈阿伦尼乌斯型激活趋势；有效噪声比较表明动力学对活性分数存在系统性依赖；热涨落与持续活性涨落的组成影响跳跃动力学。

Conclusion: 活性晶体中微观缺陷介导的输运无法用有效温度描述来描述，即有效温度框架在此类体系中失效。

Abstract: We study vacancy-mediated hopping in a two-dimensional active Brownian-particle crystal with a single vacancy. Under active driving, the hopping rates are not organized by the free-particle effective noise amplitude alone. In contrast, in the passive limit, the hopping rate follows an Arrhenius-like activated trend with respect to the translational diffusion coefficient. Effective-noise comparisons show systematic dependence on the active fraction, indicating that the composition of thermal and persistent active fluctuations affects the hopping kinetics. These results demonstrate a breakdown of an effective-temperature description for microscopic defect-mediated transport in an active crystal.

### [17] [Topological delocalisation of confined 3D active nematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10234)
*Louise C. Head,Pasquale Digregorio,Davide Marenduzzo,Ignacio Pagonabarraga,Daniel A. Beller,Giuseppe Negro*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过数值模拟揭示了三维活性向列相（active nematic）在封闭圆柱体中的缺陷线动力学，发现被动弹性与活性之间的竞争导致缺陷在边缘局域化或去局域化，并识别出多种静态与动态局域化态。研究发现，随着活性增强，系统呈现相变信号，且限域效应引入了一个活性无关的特征长度，其标度行为类似自避聚合物，表明不均等曲率的限域是调控活性拓扑动力学的一种通用机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维活性向列相中的缺陷线（defect lines）是引人关注的拓扑奇点（topological singularities），其非平衡动力学在限域环境（confined settings）中尚不明朗。本文旨在阐明几何曲率与活性（activity）在限域条件下如何协同调控缺陷线的行为。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，研究封闭圆柱体（closed cylinders）内三维活性向列相的动力学。通过改变边界曲率（boundary curvature）、活性强度和圆柱半径（cylinder radius），系统扫描了缺陷线的局域化状态空间。

Result: 发现了被动弹性（passive elasticity）与活性之间的竞争：前者使缺陷在边缘局域化，后者赋予缺陷运动性并导致无序去局域化。识别出包括手柄状构型（handle-like configurations）和端盖内混沌运动在内的多种态。活性增强时出现相变信号，包括剧烈涨落、缺陷数量的幂律标度（power law scaling），以及平均缺陷长度。限域强烈改变这些标度性质，引入一个活性无关的特征长度，其指数与自避限域聚合物（self-avoiding confined polymers）类似。

Conclusion: 不均等曲率的限域为控制活性拓扑动力学提供了一种通用机制，相比体系统（bulk systems）中活性主导长度分布，限域条件能引入独立于活性的特征长度，从而调控缺陷行为。

Abstract: Defect lines in 3D active nematic systems are intriguing topological singularities whose out-of-equilibrium dynamics remain elusive in confined settings. Here, we numerically study 3D active nematics confined within closed cylinders to elucidate the roles of geometry and activity. We reveal a competition between passive elasticity, which causes localisation of defects near edges, and activity, which endows defects with motility and gives rise to disorderly, delocalised dynamics. Varying boundary curvature, activity strength, and cylinder radius reveals a state space of static and dynamic localisation states, including handle-like configurations and chaotic motion bounded within the cylinder endcap. As activity is tuned to induce delocalisation, we identify phase transition signatures, including pronounced fluctuations and an emergent power law scaling of defect number and average defect length. We find that these scaling properties are strongly altered by confinement: unlike in bulk systems where activity governs length distributions, confinement tunes an activity-independent characteristic length, with an exponent reminiscent of self-avoiding confined polymers. These results establish confinement of inhomogeneous curvature as a versatile mechanism for controlling active topological dynamics.

### [18] [Numerical analysis of capillarity-driven thinning rheometry for polydisperse polymer solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10376)
*Isaac Pincus,Vincenzo Calabrese,Simon J. Haward,Gareth H. McKinley*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 对于真实的多分散聚合物溶液，其毛细自缩颈液桥在弹-毛细（elastocapillary）过程中测得的特征松弛时间τ_{EC}仅反映被流动拉伸的那部分分子量（molecular weight）分布子集，而非聚合物的完整松弛时间。该实验测量值取决于分子量分布、总浓度及实验参数，是一个实验特定量而非本征流体性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，基于Oldroyd-B模型，弹-毛细（elastocapillary）衰减速率提取的特征时间τ_{EC}被直接视为聚合物松弛时间（relaxation time）τ的度量。作者旨在揭示真实多分散聚合物溶液中这一解释的局限性，澄清τ_{EC}的物理含义。

Method: 采用多模FENE-PM模型（multi-mode FENE-PM model），显式纳入分子量分布（molecular weight distribution）。模型通过与Calabrese等人[Phys. Rev. X 15, 021025 (2025)]在双分散（bidisperse）窄分布低/高分子量聚苯乙烯溶液中的细丝拉伸（filament thinning）实验进行对照验证。

Result: 模型预测只有有效韦森堡数Wi = \dot{\varepsilon} τ > 1/2的链段会被流动拉伸并贡献弹性应力；这种阈值天然偏向高分子量物种。实测τ_{EC}由该应力贡献子集（stress-contributing sub-ensemble）决定，而非完整分布。τ_{EC}同时依赖于分子量分布、总聚合物浓度、预拉伸及初始细丝直径等实验参数。

Conclusion: τ_{EC}应被理解为一个实验特定量（experiment-specific quantity），而非聚合物的本征流体性质（intrinsic fluid property），这对利用液桥拉伸实验测量聚合物松弛时间的传统解释提出了重要修正。

Abstract: Liquid bridges of polymer solutions that are self-thinning due to the action of capillarity undergo a transition from Newtonian-like linear thinning to exponential elastocapillary (EC) thinning when the polymer chains are stretched by the elongational flow and the resulting elastic contribution to the stress exceeds the viscous stress. As the Oldroyd-B model predicts that the EC thinning rate is set by the relaxation time ($τ$) of the polymer, the characteristic thinning timescale extracted from the exponential decay ($τ_{EC}$) is commonly interpreted as a direct measure of $τ$. Here we show that for real polydisperse polymer solutions, $τ_{EC}$ reflects only a subset of the molecular weight (MW) distribution -- those chains actively stretched by the flow. We demonstrate this using a multi-mode FENE-PM model that explicitly incorporates the molecular weight distribution, validated against the filament thinning experiments of Calabrese et al. [Phys. Rev. X 15, 021025 (2025)] on bidisperse blends of narrowly-distributed low-MW and high-MW polystyrene solutions. The model predicts that only chains with effective Weissenberg number $Wi = \dot{\varepsilon} τ> 1/2 $ are extended by the flow and contribute elastic stress; this threshold naturally favors high molecular weight species, whose longer relaxation times allow them to remain stretched throughout the elastocapillary regime. The measured $τ_{EC}$ is therefore set by this stress-contributing sub-ensemble rather than the full distribution. Further, our model predicts that $τ_{EC}$ depends on both the molecular weight distribution and total polymer concentration, as well as experimental parameters including pre-stretch and initial filament diameter, confirming that it is best understood as an experiment-specific quantity rather than an intrinsic fluid property.

</details>


### [19] [Growing, Buckling, and Swirling: motility from polymerization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10446)
*Naveen Kumar D,Michael J. Shelley,Brato Chakrabarti*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个连续介质力学框架，揭示由聚合物丝状体聚合驱动的自推进（self-propulsion）机制，并证明了长波长屈曲不稳定性（long-wavelength buckling instability）导致自发对称性破缺，从而产生多种运动模式，包括自发旋转、定向运动和手性游动（chiral swimming）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面锚定的丝状体通过聚合和集体重新定向来实现推进——这一现象在细菌（如Acetobacter xylinum）和合成胶体实验中均有观察到，表明聚合作用本身可作为一种通用的自推进（self-propulsion）路径。然而，同时解析丝状体动力学（filament kinetics）、取向动力学（orientational dynamics）和流固相互作用（fluid-structure interactions）并自洽耦合至运动的理论框架尚缺失。

Method: 构建一个连续介质框架（continuum framework），其中主动力（active forces）从丝状体的成核（nucleation）、生长（growth）、灾难性解聚（catastrophe）以及水动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）中自洽地涌现。该框架被耦合至一个无力和无力矩的游动球体（motile spheroidal particle）上。

Result: 解析证明聚合诱导的压缩力（polymerization-induced compressive forces）驱动长波长屈曲不稳定性（long-wavelength buckling instability），导致丝状体“地毯”的自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）并产生大尺度流动。耦合至游动球体后，出现自发旋转（spontaneous spinning）、定向运动（directed motility）和手性游动（chiral swimming）等多种行为，其模式由聚合丝状体的空间图案（spatial patterning）决定。

Conclusion: 该结果为聚合丝状体集体动力学驱动的运动建立了普遍的理论基础，并为设计合成微米级游动器（micron-scale swimmers）提供了新的设计原理。

Abstract: Locomotion in low-Reynolds-number environments is achieved through a remarkable diversity of strategies, from flagellar rotation and ciliary beating to large-scale body deformations. A distinct and biologically important class of propulsion arises when surface-anchored filaments grow and collectively reorient - as seen in the cellulose-extruding bacterium Acetobacter xylinum and in recent experiments on actin-propelled synthetic colloids inspired by the motility of Listeria monocytogenes - suggesting that polymerization itself is a generic route to self-propulsion. Developing a theoretical framework for this class of problems requires simultaneously resolving filament kinetics, their orientational dynamics, and fluid-structure interactions - all self-consistently coupled to the resulting locomotion. To address this, we formulate a continuum framework in which the active forces driving locomotion emerge self-consistently from filament nucleation, growth, catastrophe, and hydrodynamic interactions. We show analytically that polymerization-induced compressive forces drive a long-wavelength buckling instability, leading to spontaneous symmetry breaking of the filament carpet and large-scale flows. In coupling this framework to a force- and torque-free motile spheroidal particle, a wide variety of behaviors emerge - this includes spontaneous spinning, directed motility, and chiral swimming - whose selection is governed by the spatial patterning of polymerizing filaments. These results establish a general theoretical foundation for motility, driven by collective dynamics of polymerizing filaments and point towards new design principles for synthetic micron-scale swimmers.

### [20] [Enhanced diffusion of colloidal tracers due to enzymatic activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10646)
*Mauricio Gomez,Erick Leyva,Justine Miqueu-Petit,Dakota Feldcamp,Anthony Estrada,W. Benjamin Rogers,Jennifer L. Ross,Wylie W. Ahmed*

TL;DR: 本文通过差分动态显微镜（DDM）和光镊（OT）两种实验方法，研究了酶催化反应在两种构型（被动粒子分散于酶活性溶液、以及酶修饰粒子表面直接催化）下对胶体示踪粒子运动与力波动的影响，发现活性增强效应依赖于示踪粒子尺寸、活性定位、观测时标及增强度量指标。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验采用两种构型：（1）被动胶体粒子分散在酶活性溶液中；（2）酶直接修饰在粒子表面进行催化。同时结合差分动态显微镜（differential dynamic microscopy, DDM）测量系综平均的长时扩散，以及光镊（optical tweezer, OT）测量短时力波动，并使用多种互补指标量化活性增强效应。

Result: 对于1 μm示踪粒子，两种构型均观测到活性诱导的增强，其中酶修饰粒子的增强扩散和非热力波动最为显著。对于200 nm粒子，增强效应更微弱且依赖于方法：DDM检测到裸粒子扩散的适度增加，但OT未解析出相应特征。

Abstract: Enzymatic catalysis can generate nonequilibrium fluctuations, but how these couple to tracer motion at larger length scales depends on physical context. Here, we investigate colloidal tracers in two configurations: passive particles dispersed in an enzymatically active solution, and enzyme-decorated particles where catalysis occurs directly at the tracer surface. We combine differential dynamic microscopy (DDM), which probes ensemble-averaged long-time diffusion, with optical tweezer (OT) measurements of short-time force fluctuations, and compare several complementary metrics for quantifying activity-induced enhancement. For 1 $μ$m tracers, we observe activity-induced enhancements in both configurations, with the strongest effects for enzyme-decorated particles, which exhibit enhanced diffusion and increased non-thermal force fluctuations. For 200 nm tracers, enhancements are more subtle and method-dependent: DDM detects modest increases in diffusion for bare particles, while corresponding signatures are not resolved by the OT. These results demonstrate that enzymatic activity can be transduced from molecular to microscale motion and forces, but that the apparent magnitude and detectability of enhancement depend strongly on tracer size, localization of activity, the timescales probed by the measurement, and the metric used to quantify enhancement. More broadly, understanding how enzyme activity modifies transport and fluctuations across scales is important for interpreting nonequilibrium dynamics in active soft matter, intracellular transport, and chemically crowded biological environments.

### [21] [Assembly pathways of anisotropic lipid membrane-deforming colloids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10917)
*Ali Azadbakht,Thomas Weikl,Daniela J. Kraft*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和数值计算，系统研究了各向异性物体（如椭球体、哑铃体、立方体等）在脂质膜（lipid membrane）下方受限时，通过膜形变介导的相互作用如何驱动组装。研究发现，膜变形物体首先在曲率最高区域相互吸引，随后重新定向为近似球形的紧密堆积构型，其中高曲率区域会形成能量势垒，影响组装路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管各向同性膜形变（isotropic membrane deformations）介导的相互作用已被广泛研究，但各向异性形变（anisotropic deformations）在生物系统中普遍存在，其作用仍缺乏系统探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，揭示各向异性膜形变如何影响蛋白质及其他内含物的空间组织和组装行为。

Method: 实验上，研究将各向异性胶体物体（包括椭球体、哑铃体、立方体、不等边三角形、四面体和弯曲棒）限制在脂质膜下方，使其在不直接附着于膜的情况下诱导膜形变。同时结合数值计算（numerical calculations），分析多种形状物体之间通过膜形变介导的相互作用。

Result: 膜变形物体首先通过曲率最高的区域相互吸引，随后重新定向并排列成近似球形的紧密堆积构型。这一过程中，平面对齐（若可能则配准对齐）和局部优化的几何堆积（geometric packing）起关键作用；高曲率区域会引入能量势垒（energy barriers），从而影响组装路径。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了各向异性膜形变如何普遍地调控组装路径和最终粒子排列方式，为理解膜变形蛋白质及其他内含物的行为提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Membrane-deformation mediated interactions play an important role in the spatial organization of proteins on the cell membrane. Although interactions between isotropic membrane deformations have been extensively investigated, the role of anisotropic deformations remains largely unexplored despite their prevalence in biological systems. Here, we experimentally investigate the assembly of anisotropic colloidal objects that deform a lipid membrane while being confined underneath it, without direct attachment. Combining experiments and numerical calculations, we analyze how a wide range of shapes, including ellipsoids, dumbbells, cubes, scalene triangles, tetrahedra, and bent rods, interact with each other through the membrane deformations they induce. We find that membrane-deforming objects initially attract through regions of highest curvature and subsequently reorient into close packed arrangements with an approximately spherical circumference. This is achieved through the alignment of flat faces - if possible in register - and locally optimized geometric packing, with regions of high curvature imposing energy barriers that influence the assembly pathway. Our work reveals general principles how anisotropic membrane deformations govern the assembly pathways and final particle arrangements, providing new insights into the behavior of membrane-deforming proteins and other inclusions.

</details>


### [22] [Molecular Dynamics-Derived Coloured Noise Mediates Anderson Localisation and Environment-Assisted Transport of Tryptophan Excitons in Tubulin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11135)
*Chen Xin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过全原子分子动力学模拟，该研究揭示了微管蛋白αβ-二聚体中色氨酸残基的位点能量涨落具有三指数衰减的非马尔可夫特征：亚100飞秒和皮秒模式源于水分子动力学，纳秒模式源于蛋白质构象重排。慢速蛋白质模式引起准静态无序并导致安德森局域化，而快速水模式则通过共振调谐实现环境辅助量子输运（ENAQT），这与标准白噪声Haken-Strobl模型预测的均匀退局域化形成鲜明对比。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对310 K温度下溶剂化的微管蛋白二聚体进行全原子分子动力学（all-atom molecular dynamics）模拟，结合10飞秒和10皮秒采样间隔的高频与长时间轨迹，分析位点能量涨落的时序自相关函数。

Result: 位点能量涨落的自相关函数呈三指数（tri-exponential）衰减，包含三个分离良好的衰减模式：亚100飞秒和皮秒模式（由水动力学驱动），以及纳秒模式（源于蛋白质构象重排）；所有三种模式均处于非马尔可夫（non-Markovian） regime；慢速蛋白质模式引入强准静态无序导致安德森局域化（Anderson localisation），快速水模式通过共振调谐实现环境辅助量子输运（environment-assisted quantum transport, ENAQT）；在完整八位点网络上，有色噪声浴将激子限制在强耦合的近端色氨酸对中，与标准白噪声Haken-Strobl模型预测的均匀退局域化截然不同。

Conclusion: 该工作流程可推广至其他具有溶剂暴露发色团（solvent-exposed chromophores）的色素-蛋白质系统。

Abstract: The tryptophan residues in tubulin $αβ$-dimers form an ordered aromatic network that has been proposed to support quantum exciton transport even under physiological environmental noise. Existing studies of this system mostly assume white-noise dephasing, but the statistical properties of the protein-solvent bath coupled to tryptophan sites remain uncharacterised under physiological conditions. Here we characterise this fluctuation bath via all-atom molecular dynamics simulations of a solvated tubulin dimer at 310~K, combining high-frequency and long-time trajectories with 10~fs and 10~ps sampling intervals. The resulting autocorrelation of the site-energy fluctuations is tri-exponential, with three well-separated decay modes: sub-100-fs and picosecond fluctuations driven by water dynamics, and a nanosecond mode originating from protein conformational rearrangements. All three modes fall deep within the non-Markovian regime. We further demonstrate that the slow protein mode introduces strong quasi-static disorder, which results in Anderson localisation, while the two fast water modes frequently tune chromophore pairs through resonance, enabling environment-assisted quantum transport (ENAQT). On the full eight-site network, the coloured-noise bath confines excitons predominantly to strongly coupled proximal tryptophan pairs, in marked contrast to the more uniform delocalisation predicted by the standard white-noise Haken--Strobl model. Our workflow generalises to other pigment--protein systems with solvent-exposed chromophores.

### [23] [Vectorial driving of multistable materials: singularities, pt-graphs, and non-generic paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11179)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的转移图（t-graphs）仅能描述标量驱动下的多稳态材料响应，而矢量驱动会产生路径依赖响应，需要新框架来描述。高阶奇点在此过程中的作用尚未被充分理解。

Method: 结合链状超材料的实验与最小弹簧模型，分析高阶奇点如何塑造路径转移图（pt-graphs）和路径依赖响应，并考察通过高阶奇点的非泛函驱动路径中自发对称性破缺的作用。

Result: 发现高阶奇点对pt-graphs的结构和路径依赖响应起决定性作用；非泛函驱动路径通过高阶奇点时，响应由自发对称性破缺控制；t-graphs可作为pt-graphs的一维极限情形而自然涌现。

Conclusion: 建立了基于奇点的路径依赖响应理论框架，将标量与矢量驱动统一于图方法，为设计可编程顺序功能的多稳态材料（用于智能传感、软体机器人和材料内计算）提供了基础。

Abstract: Describing and predicting the response of multistable materials to external driving is central to memory formation, programmable metamaterials, soft robotics, and in-materia computing. While scalar driving is captured by transition graphs (t-graphs), vectorial driving produces path-dependent responses that require the recently introduced path-transition graphs (pt-graphs). In both cases, transitions are governed by singularities in the energy landscape: for scalar driving these correspond to saddle-node bifurcations, but for vectorial driving, higher-order singularities become important. Combining experiments on chain-like metamaterials with a minimal spring model, we investigate how higher-order singularities shape pt-graphs and the resulting path-dependent responses. We moreover discuss the role of non-generic driving paths through higher-order singularities, where the response is governed by spontaneous symmetry breaking. Finally, we demonstrate how t-graphs emerge as the one-dimensional limit of pt-graphs, unifying scalar and vectorial driving within a common graph-based framework. These results establish a singularity-based approach to path-dependent responses and provide a foundation for designing multistable materials with programmable sequential functionality for smart sensing, soft robotics, and in-materia computation.

Result: 通过与黑塞矩阵直接对角化获得的基准结果进行直接基准测试，发现IWM结果与真值吻合良好；同时展示了该方法在有限尺寸标度下的应用，可提取决定波衰减率和谱宽度的力学无序基本度量。

Conclusion: IWM是一种有效且简单的提取固体中弹性波色散的方法，并可通过有限尺寸效应分析为表征力学无序提供新的途径。

Abstract: The dispersion of elastic waves in disordered solids plays a key role in determining the vibrational density of states and harmonic wave attenuation rates. As such, the availability of robust computational approaches to the precise extraction of the dispersion is of key importance. Here we present a simple method -- the imposed wave method (IWM) -- , which provides direct access to the dispersion of elastic waves in computer models of solids, without any fitting involved. We directly benchmark the method against the `ground-truth' obtained from direct diagonalization of solids' hessian matrices, to find good agreement. We discuss limitations of and finite-size effects in the method, and show that exploiting the method's finite-size scaling provides access to a fundamental quantifier of mechanical disorder that determines wave attenuation rates and spectral widths.

### [25] [Colloid recovery from porous structures under ambient flow: enhanced extraction via phoretic and osmotic mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11474)
*Jitendra Dhakar,Kapil Upadhyaya,Akash Choudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过有限元模拟，揭示了多孔介质中溶质梯度取向（溶质释放 vs. 溶质吸收）对胶体趋流-渗透提取（phoretic-osmotic extraction）的定性影响差异，并发现扩散渗透滑移（diffusioosmotic slip）在溶质吸收模式下对提取的增强效果更为显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作已证明，在死端微孔中通过控制盐梯度取向可调控泳动（phoretic）与渗透（osmotic）输运，但该取向对大规模时空模式及胶体提取程度的影响尚未被充分探索。本研究旨在系统表征溶质梯度取向（溶质释放 vs. 溶质吸收）对多孔结构中胶体提取行为的影响。

Method: 采用二维多孔结构模型，该结构由按等间距六方有序排列（hexagonal packing）的柱体/纤维阵列构成。通过有限元模拟（finite-element simulations），对比了两种溶质梯度取向模式：溶质释放模式（solute-out，即多孔介质释放溶质）与溶质吸收模式（solute-in，即多孔介质消耗溶质）。

Result: 两种模式下胶体提取行为呈现定性差异：溶质释放模式中，胶体从多孔结构的外围区域被提取；溶质吸收模式中，提取主要发生在停滞核心区（stagnant core）。柱体/纤维内表面的扩散渗透滑移（diffusioosmotic slip）在两种模式下均增强了提取效果，且由于内部时空流动模式的差异，该增强效应在溶质吸收模式下更为显著。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了多孔介质中渗透输运对溶质梯度取向的高度敏感性。这些发现可为增强膜过滤（membrane filtration）、衣物去污（laundry detergency）及强化采油（enhanced oil recovery）等应用提供指导。

Abstract: Chemical gradients are widely employed to enhance particle transport in porous media, such as laundry detergency and enhanced oil recovery. Diffusiophoresis and diffusioosmosis refer to the movement of colloid and movement of near-surface fluid in response to electrolyte gradients, respectively. These mechanisms play a crucial role in colloid and drug transport in constricted regions where bulk transport is infeasible. Our earlier work [Tiwari et al., Langmuir 41, 18583 (2025)] has shown that phoretic and osmotic transport in dead-end micro-pores can be controlled by orienting salt gradients into or out of the pores; however, the extent to which this orientation influences large-scale spatiotemporal patterns and colloid extraction is not thoroughly explored. In this work, we study the phoretic and osmotic colloidal extraction from porous structure exposed to an ambient flow. We characterize the impact of solute gradient orientation, such as solute-out (i.e., solute-emitting porous media) and solute-in (i.e., solute-consuming media) modes. The two-dimensional porous structure is made of a number of pillars/fibers arranged in a lattice ordered hexagonal packing with equal spacing. The results from finite-element simulations show that phoretic colloidal extraction exhibits a qualitatively distinct behavior in the two modes: in the solute-out mode, colloids are extracted from the peripheral region of the porous structure, whereas in the solute-in mode, extraction predominantly occurs from the stagnant core. Diffusioosmotic slip on the internal surface of pillars/fibres further amplifies extraction in both modes, with a relatively larger enhancement in the solute-in mode due to internal spatiotemporal flow patterns. Beyond demonstrating the sensitivity of osmotic transport in porous media, these insights can guide enhanced membrane filtration, laundry detergency, and enhanced oil recovery.

### [26] [Hygroscopic hysteresis drives intermittent salt creeping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11587)
*Javier Rodríguez-Rodríguez,Manikuntala Mukhopadhyay,Lijun Thayyil Raju,Detlef Lohse,Jasper van der Gucht,Uddalok Sen*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过毛细管单向蒸发实验，揭示了盐爬（salt creeping）本质上是一种间歇性、非平衡过程，并证明潮解-风化滞后（hygroscopic hysteresis）是驱动其间歇性动力学的核心机制，将盐爬重新定义为一种弛豫振荡器（relaxation oscillator）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盐爬现象在地质学、文化遗产风化、喷墨打印和碳封存等领域广泛存在，但其动力学有时平滑、有时剧烈间歇的原因长期未得到解释。

Method: 在毛细管中限制盐溶液蒸发（仅单向失水），系统改变初始盐浓度和环境相对湿度，结合时间分辨测量和最小理论模型，研究晶体在外毛细管壁沉积的动力学行为。

Result: 识别出晶体沉积伴随非单调、间歇性动力学的参数区间；间歇性由水周期性地吸入毛细管外壁生长的盐结构所维持，形成蒸发-结晶的自放大反馈；潮解-风化浓度之间的滞后（hygroscopic hysteresis）足以产生振荡性盐积累和间歇动力学。

Conclusion: 盐爬应被重新理解为一种弛豫振荡器（relaxation oscillator），潮解-风化滞后是稳态蒸发转变为间歇盐爬的“开关”，为蒸发多组分流体中的间歇性现象提供了一条通用机制路径。

Abstract: Salt creeping -- the precipitation of salt crystals away from an evaporating liquid interface along surrounding surfaces -- occurs across settings from geology and cultural-heritage weathering to inkjet printing and carbon sequestration. Yet why its dynamics are sometimes smooth and sometimes violently intermittent has remained unexplained. Here we investigate the confined evaporation of salt solutions from a capillary with unidirectional water loss and show that salt creeping is an intrinsically intermittent, out-of-equilibrium process. By systematically varying the initial salt concentration and the ambient relative humidity, we identify regimes in which crystal deposition on the outer capillary surface goes hand in hand with non-monotonic, intermittent dynamics. Time-resolved measurements reveal that these intermittent dynamics are sustained by episodic water imbibition into the growing salt structures on the outer surface of the capillary, which sets up a self-amplifying feedback between evaporation and crystallization. Combining experiments with a minimal theoretical model, we demonstrate that hysteresis between deliquescence and efflorescence concentrations is sufficient to generate oscillatory salt accumulation and intermittent dynamics. Hygroscopic hysteresis, in other words, is the switch that turns steady evaporation into intermittent creeping. Our results recast salt creeping as a relaxation oscillator, and point to the hysteretic phase change as a generic route to intermittency in evaporating multicomponent fluids.

In particular, we examine azobenzene solutions in toluene, whose conductivity can be adjusted by two colors of light: UV induces trans to cis isomerization, leading to an increase in conductivity, while blue light triggers cis to trans back-isomerization, decreasing conductivity. ### [28] [How do 3M Command strips work? A fracture mechanics approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11650)
*Xue-Ling Luo,Nikolaos Bouklas,Chung-Yuen Hui*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究针对3M Command条这类可移除胶粘系统，推导了超弹性拉伸释放胶粘剂在承载与释放条件下的界面裂纹能量释放率解析表达式，并通过有限元模拟验证。结果表明最大承载与释放力之比与粘接长度/胶厚比呈线性关系，此外还通过解析与模拟探讨了几何驱动的交替裂纹扩展机制，建立了预测释放力与失稳裂纹扩展的失效包络图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有限变形力学（finite-deformation mechanics）分析超弹性（hyperelastic）拉伸释放胶粘系统，推导承载与释放条件下界面裂纹的能量释放率（energy release rate）解析表达式，并通过有限元模拟中的$J$积分（$J$-integral）进行验证。同时结合解析解与仿真研究背衬与基底界面间的交替裂纹扩展（alternating crack propagation），并基于界面断裂韧性（interfacial fracture toughness）参数化绘制失效包络图（failure envelopes）。

Result: 最大承载与释放力之比与粘接长度（bonded length）与胶粘剂厚度（adhesive thickness）之比呈线性关系；该比值通常很大。交替裂纹扩展行为可通过解析与模拟的方法加以描述，参数化研究得到的失效包络图为预测释放力及失稳裂纹扩展提供了定量框架。

Conclusion: 研究建立了多层拉伸释放胶粘系统中承载与释放力关系的解析理论，揭示了关键几何参数的缩放规律，为优化该类可移除胶粘系统的力学设计提供了预测性工具。

Abstract: Removable adhesive systems such as 3M Command strips are designed to support substantial loads while allowing clean, damage-free removal from the substrate. These systems rely on a highly extensible adhesive strip that bonds strongly during use but releases when stretched, causing the adhesive layer to elongate and progressively debond from the surfaces. A central challenge in the design of stretch-release adhesives is therefore to maximize load-bearing capacity while minimizing the force required for removal. This study investigates the finite-deformation mechanics governing both load support and tape release in a hyperelastic stretch-release adhesive system, with particular focus on the 3M Command tape geometry. Explicit analytical expressions are derived for the energy release rate of interfacial cracks under both load-bearing and release conditions and are validated against $J$-integral evaluations from finite element simulations. The results show that the ratio of maximum supported load to release force scales linearly with the ratio of bonded length to adhesive thickness, which is typically very large. We also investigate geometry-driven alternating crack propagation between the backing and substrate interfaces, governing tape removal, by analytical solutions and simulations. Parametric studies of competing interfacial fracture toughnesses produce failure envelopes that provide a predictive framework for estimating release forces and unstable crack propagation in multilayer stretch-release adhesive systems.

### [29] [Universal scalings and switching entropy in yield-stress fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11799)
*Rajam Elancheliyan,Jean Marc Fromental,Edouard Chauveau,Domenico Truzzolillo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发现屈服应力流体（yield-stress fluids）在大振幅振荡测试中，其非线性响应在低频率下表现出隐藏的普适性：一阶粘弹性模量（first-harmonic viscoelastic moduli）随应变幅值坍缩至主曲线。这一现象源于恒定的应力平台与弛豫时间（relaxation time）的唯一时间轨迹。作者基于对称性破缺的李雅普诺夫函数（Lyapunov function）提出新流变模型，揭示了可恢复弹性能、脆性（fragility）与应力反转熵产之间的内在关联，定义了一个统御屈服陡峭程度的单一粘塑性参数，为动态屈服应力（dynamic yield stress）提供了新的热力学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在揭示屈服应力流体在循环（oscillatory）加载条件下隐藏的非线性响应普适性，并为其背后的热力学机制提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 采用大振幅振荡试验，并结合基于对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）的李雅普诺夫函数推导出新的流体模型（fluidity model），用以捕捉模量坍缩与应力平台行为。

Result: 在低频率下，一阶粘弹性模量随应变幅值（strain amplitude）坍缩至主曲线（master curves），揭示了恒定的应力平台（stress plateau）和弛豫时间的唯一时间轨迹。

Conclusion: 可恢复弹性能、脆性及应力反转熵产（entropy produced during stress inversion）三者相互关联，定义了一个统一的粘塑性参数（viscoplastic parameter），为动态屈服应力提供了新的热力学基础。

Abstract: Yield-stress fluids undergo a singular solid-to-liquid transition at a critical stress threshold. While conventionally investigated under steady shear, large-amplitude oscillatory tests force these materials to cyclically navigate between arrested and fluidized states. Here, we uncover a hidden universality in their non-linear oscillatory response: at sufficiently low frequencies their first-harmonic viscoelastic moduli collapse onto master curves against strain amplitude. This collapse reflects an invariant intra-cycle stress plateau, showing that the material rearranges almost instantaneously to maintain a constant stress state governed by a unique temporal trajectory of its relaxation time. We capture this phenomenology using a new fluidity model derived from a Lyapunov function exhibiting symmetry breaking. Our framework reveals that recoverable elastic energy, fragility, and the entropy produced during stress inversion are fundamentally intertwined, defining a single viscoplastic parameter that governs yielding abruptness and provides a novel thermomechanical foundation for the dynamic yield stress.

</details>

### [30] [The Dirac equation in (split-)octonions: origins, variants, and modern context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09703)
*J. Köplinger*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本篇综述将八元数（octonions）与分裂八元数（split-octonions）在狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）中的表示方法划分为四类，并重点验证了近期一篇论文声称的“分裂八元数狄拉克方程”实为已有直接积表示（direct-product representation）的重标号版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管八元数和分裂八元数已被以多种概念上不同的方式用于表达物理中的狄拉克方程，但这些表示方法尚缺乏系统分类与比较。此外，近期出现的所谓“新形式”分裂八元数狄拉克方程需要独立验证其新颖性。

Method: 作者将已有文献中的八元数/分裂八元数表示狄拉克方程的方法归纳为四类：2-因子（直接积）表示、3-因子表示、投影表示以及传统上使用八元数承载作用于旋量（spinors）的狄拉克代数。针对Gogberashvili和Gurchumelia提出的“分裂八元数狄拉克方程”，采用显式保结构旋转（structure-preserving rotation）进行等价性检验。

Result: 分类结果表明存在四种主要表示方法。对2024年论文的验证显示，其“分裂八元数狄拉克方程”与J. Köplinger于2006年基于C. Musès猜想提出的2-因子（直接积）表示在重标号后完全等价，并非真正的新形式。

Conclusion: 该综述为八元数在狄拉克方程中的应用提供了系统分类框架，并通过对近期工作的独立验证澄清了文献中的误解；同时指出被检验论文中仍存在其他实质性贡献。

Abstract: Octonions and split-octonions have been used to express the Dirac equation in physics in several conceptually distinct ways. This review sorts them into four groups: the 2-factor (direct-product), 3-factor, and projection representations, which use (split-)octonion basis elements natively to model a spacetime basis; and the conventional use of octonions to carry Dirac algebra acting on spinors. Pointers to their modern use, and to recent methods for native split-octonionic analysis, are given throughout. Within the 2-factor approach, we document its origin (J. Köplinger, Appl. Math. Computation 182 (2006) 443, following a conjecture of C. Musès). As a side aspect, we examine the "split octonionic Dirac equation" of M. Gogberashvili and A. Gurchumelia (Int. J. Geom. Meth. Mod. Phys. 21 (2024) 2450214). An explicit structure-preserving rotation shows it to be this same direct-product representation, up to relabeling: an independent verification rather than "the novel forms" [the opening words of the authors' abstract]. Its genuine contributions are credited.

</details>


### [31] [PBW bases and centralisers for the $q$-Onsager algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10097)
*Haoran Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文解决了关于q-Onsager代数的PBW基（Poincaré–Birkhoff–Witt basis）与中心化子（centraliser）的五个猜想。作者去除了先前所需的超越性假设（transcendence hypothesis），证明了Baseilhac–Kolb根向量（root vectors）在q不是单位根时构成任意线性序下的PBW基；建立了交替生成元（alternating generators）中的十二个PBW基，并证明它们在交替中心扩张（alternating central extension）的任意标量中心特化（scalar central specialisation）下保持不变；最终确定了负交替子代数与虚交替子代数的中心化子，并证明所有四个单族交替多项式子代数（single-family alternating polynomial subalgebras）都是极大交换的（maximal commutative）。证明方法结合了Damiani根向量（Damiani root vectors）的显式规整化（explicit straightening）、退化（degeneration）gr O_q ≃ U_q^+(𝔰𝔩̂₂)以及大指标三角交叉论证（large-index triangular crossing arguments）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: q-Onsager代数在量子可积系统（quantum integrable systems）和表示论（representation theory）中具有核心地位，但其PBW基的普适存在性与中心化子的结构长期存在未解决的猜想。本文旨在不使用超越性假设，直接证明五个关于PBW基和中心化子的核心猜想，从而完善该代数的结构理论。

Method: 证明方法包含三个关键技术：一是对Damiani根向量进行显式规整化（explicit straightening），以处理基的线性序问题；二是利用退化同构（degeneration isomorphism）gr O_q ≃ U_q^+(𝔰𝔩̂₂)，将问题转化为已知结构；三是采用大指标三角交叉论证（large-index triangular crossing arguments），处理子代数之间的交换性与中心化子计算。

Result: 去除了超越性假设，证明Baseilhac–Kolb根向量在q非单位根时在任意线性序下均构成PBW基。建立了交替生成元中的十二个PBW基，并证明它们在交替中心扩张的任意标量中心特化下保持成立。确定了负交替子代数与虚交替子代数的中心化子，并证明所有四个单族交替多项式子代数均为极大交换的。

Conclusion: 该工作完全解决了q-Onsager代数领域关于PBW基和中心化子的五个公开猜想（包括Terwilliger以及Baseilhac和Belliard提出的猜想），为该代数的进一步结构研究和应用提供了坚实的基础。

Abstract: We settle five conjectures concerning PBW bases and centralisers for the $q$-Onsager algebra. We first prove that the Baseilhac--Kolb root vectors give a PBW basis in every linear order whenever $q$ is not a root of unity, removing the previous transcendence hypothesis. We next establish twelve PBW bases in the alternating generators and show that they persist under arbitrary scalar central specialisation of the alternating central extension. This proves conjectures of Terwilliger and of Baseilhac and Belliard. Finally, we determine the centralisers of the negative and imaginary alternating subalgebras and show that all four single-family alternating polynomial subalgebras are maximal commutative. The proofs combine explicit straightening for Damiani root vectors, the degeneration $\mathrm{gr} O_q \simeq U_q^+(\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}_2)$, and large-index triangular crossing arguments.

</details>


### [32] [The existence of full dimensional KAM tori for infinite dimensional Hamiltonian systems with long range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10259)
*Hongzi Cong,Wanran Ding,Zhihan Zhang,Juan Zhao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Bourgain型丢番图条件（Diophantine condition）下，证明了具有长程相互作用（long range interactions）的无穷维力学系统中全维KAM环面（full dimensional KAM tori）的存在性，且不变环面的半径满足更慢的衰减速率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将KAM理论（Kolmogorov-Arnold-Moser theory）从有限维系统推广到无穷维系统，特别是处理具有长程相互作用的力学系统，以克服传统KAM条件在无穷维情形下的严格限制。

Method: 采用Bourgain型丢番图条件（Bourgain-type Diophantine condition）对频率进行约束，并在此条件下构造不变环面（invariant tori），同时放宽对环面半径衰减速率的要求。

Result: 成功证明了在Bourgain型丢番图条件下，具有长程相互作用的无穷维力学系统中全维KAM环面的存在性，且不变环面半径的衰减速率比以往结果更慢。

Conclusion: 该结果扩展了KAM理论在无穷维系统中的应用范围，为长程相互作用系统的拟周期运动（quasi-periodic motion）存在性提供了更宽松的条件。

Abstract: We prove the existence of full dimensional KAM tori for infinite dimensional mechanical systems exhibiting long range interactions, under a Diophantine condition of Bourgain type [Bourgain2005JFA], in which the radius of the invariant tori satisfies a slower decay.

### [33] [Path-Dependent Entropic Lagrangian for Probability Flows: Balance--Entropy Routing and Composable Information Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10493)
*Huilong Ren*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种路径依赖的熵拉格朗日（entropic Lagrangian）计算框架，将最大熵（maximum entropy）原理从静态状态选择扩展为概率路径演化，通过受限生成元（restricted generators）、历史上限项和显式平衡-熵端口路由（balance–entropy port routing）来描述概率运输、耗散和信息交换过程，并在数值实验中验证了质量守恒、能量分解和总自由能记账的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最大熵原理（maximum entropy principle）能选择约束下的概率状态，但无法说明该状态如何达到、概率如何运输（transport），以及路径上的耗散（dissipation）和外部信息交换如何被计入，因此需要建立路径依赖的框架来描述概率演化过程。

Method: 构建了路径依赖的熵拉格朗日（entropic Lagrangian）计算框架，引入受限生成元（restricted generators）、上限历史项（upper-limit history terms）和显式平衡-熵端口路由（balance–entropy port routing），在标准迁移率闭包（mobility closure）下导出热态关系、保守概率平衡和非负产率。

Result: 框架的KL/Shannon扇区（KL/Shannon sector）将最大熵和贝叶斯定律（Bayesian laws）恢复为稳态无通量状态；时间依赖的信息势（information potentials）将内部耗散与外部供给信息功率分离；可组合的信息势和结构势（structural potentials）在不改变记账架构的前提下控制尾部、稀疏性、鲁棒性、正则化和非局部多模态特性。数值实验验证了质量守恒、能量分解和总自由能记账的有效性。

Conclusion: 该路径依赖的熵拉格朗日框架成功将最大熵原理从静态选择扩展为包含耗散、信息交换和概率运输的动态演化过程，为概率学习提供了一种结构化的信息记账体系。

Abstract: Probability distributions are central to information theory, statistical inference, and modern probabilistic learning. Maximum entropy selects a probability state under prescribed constraints, but it does not specify how that state is reached, how probability is transported, or how dissipation and external information exchange are accounted for along the path. We develop a path-dependent entropic Lagrangian calculus that extends static state selection to probability-path evolution through restricted generators, upper-limit history terms, and explicit balance--entropy port routing. The construction yields the thermal state relation, conservative probability balance, and nonnegative production under standard mobility closure. Its KL/Shannon sector recovers maximum-entropy and Bayesian laws as stationary no-flux states, while time-dependent information potentials separate internal dissipation from supplied information power. Composable information and structural potentials control tails, sparsity, robustness, regularization, and nonlocal multimodality without changing the accounting architecture. Two numerical examples verify mass conservation, energy decomposition, and the total free-energy ledger.

</details>


### [34] [Rigorous bound on the aspect ratio for the formation of a nematic phase in hard rod and hard rectangle systems on $\mathbb{Z}^2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10510)
*Qidong He*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了在方格（square lattice）上具有两种允许取向的大长宽比硬矩形（hard rectangle）模型中存在向列相（nematic phase），基于双尺度簇展开（two-scale cluster expansion）方法，并首次给出了形成向列相所需长宽比的严格估计（k ≥ 10^72）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究硬矩形系统中向列相的存在性问题，提供其形成所需长宽比的严格数学估计，填补此前定性论证中常量和参数未明确追踪的空白。

Method: 采用Disertori–Giuliani等人先前为二维硬棒和三维硬板发展的双尺度簇展开方法，并明确追踪其中的常量和参数，完成先前工作中遗留的论证环节，从而导出定量条件并从中提取长宽比估计。

Result: 在非优化条件下得到所需长宽比的下界为 k ≥ 10^72，远大于数值预测的 k_min=7，但这是首次对硬矩形系统中向列相形成所需长宽比给出的严格估计。

Conclusion: 本研究为硬矩形系统向列相的存在性提供了第一个严格的解析证明，其定量条件可为进一步优化长宽比估计奠定数学基础。

Abstract: We prove the existence of a nematic phase in a model of $l\times w$ hard rectangles on the square lattice with two allowed orientations and a large aspect ratio $k:=l/w$. The proof is based on a two-scale cluster expansion method developed previously by Disertori--Giuliani for hard rods in 2D and Disertori--Giuliani--Jauslin for hard plates in 3D. Our main contributions lie in explicitly tracking the constants and parameters and completing the arguments left implicit in these works. Hence, the proof produces a sufficient set of quantitative conditions from which estimates for the required aspect ratio can be extracted. A non-optimized evaluation of these conditions yields the bound $k\ge 10^{72}$. Although it vastly overshoots the numerical prediction, $k_{\min}=7$, our result appears to be the first rigorous estimate of the aspect ratio required for the formation of a nematic phase in hard rectangle systems.

</details>


### [35] [Jordan Pair Quantum Theory and the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10833)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用理论对应分析方法，将双例外埃尔米特若尔当三元组（bi-Cayley三元组）的数学结构与标准模型的基本组成进行对照，并基于埃尔米特若尔当三元组对量子力学的标准形式进行重新表述与推广。

Result: 发现了双例外埃尔米特若尔当三元组与粒子物理标准模型结构之间存在惊人的对应关系；同时证明了普通量子力学可以借助埃尔米特若尔当三元组进行重构和推广。

Abstract: Jordan pairs and hermitian Jordan triples were discovered by mathematicians studying Jordan algebras, which describe the possible algebras of observables in quantum mechanics. We point out a striking correspondence between the doubly exceptional hermitian Jordan triple (the so-called ``bi-Cayley'' triple) and the structure of the Standard Model of particle physics. We also point out how ordinary quantum mechanics may be reformulated, and generalized, using hermitian Jordan triples.
