### [36] [Beyond Critical Slowing Down: Slow Modes, Extreme Tails, and Field Decoherence in Tipping Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11350)
*Mickaël D. Chekroun,Valerio Lucarini*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在亚稳态随机Ghil–Sellers能量平衡模型中，从简化Ruelle–Pollicott共振、极值统计和全场数据自适应谐波模式三个互补视角分析气候临界转型（climate tipping）的早期预警信号，发现转型并非由单个谱隙标志，而是表现为慢模式束的集体衰减、冷尾极值的不对称组织以及全场相位退相干（phase decoherence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统气候临界预警通常依赖单一标量指标，但可能忽略临界转型的多方面交互特征。本文旨在通过多种互补视角揭示亚稳态临界转型的不同方面，从而提供更丰富的预警信号。

Method: 使用简化转移算子（reduced transfer operator）构造全球平均温度与经向热对比的简化RP共振与Kolmogorov模式；基于极值理论（Extreme Value Theory）分析冷尾的双峰与非对称组织；采用数据自适应谐波模式（Data-Adaptive Harmonic Mode, DAHM）分析全场温度场的空间相位组织变化。

Result: 临近转型时，多个主导衰减率下降，模式沿共同慢方向协调一致，格林函数（Green's function）产生延迟恢复尾部与增强的低频敏感性；冷尾极值的形状与极端指数显示冷异常更易出现且更具聚集性；全场DAHM的主导模式仍捕捉大尺度趋势，但固定秩重建退化、DAHM相位分布展宽，表明全场相位退相干。

Conclusion: 亚稳态临界转型（metastable tipping）由简化谱响应、极端事件统计与全场相位相干性三者联合重组所标志，预警信号并非单一指标，而是一束慢模式（bundle of slow modes）的集体行为。

Abstract: We study early-warning signals of climate tipping in the metastable stochastic Ghil--Sellers energy balance model. Rather than relying on a single scalar indicator, we analyze the transition through three complementary lenses: reduced Ruelle--Pollicott (RP) resonances, extreme value statistics, and full-field data-adaptive harmonic modes. This distinguishes bulk relaxation, tail excursions, and spatial phase organization as interacting aspects of tipping. First, using a reduced transfer-operator construction for global mean temperature and meridional thermal contrast, we estimate reduced RP resonances and Kolmogorov modes. Near tipping, several dominant decay rates drop and their modes harmonize along a common slow direction. Consequently, Green's functions aligned with this direction acquire coherent delayed-recovery tails and enhanced low-frequency susceptibility. The warning is thus carried by a bundle of slow modes rather than a single spectral gap. Second, Extreme Value Theory reveals that the cold tail of the global mean temperature anomaly becomes less sharply bounded and more persistent near the transition. The shape and extremal indices show an asymmetric organization: cold excursions probing the escape direction become more accessible and clustered. Third, Data-Adaptive Harmonic Mode (DAHM) analysis of the full temperature field shows that near tipping, leading modes still capture the large-scale trend, but fixed-rank reconstruction degrades and the DAHM phase distribution broadens. We interpret this as multivariate phase decoherence: the field retains a coherent transition component while losing sharp latitudinal phase organization. Ultimately, metastable tipping is marked by a joint reorganization of reduced spectral response, extreme-event statistics, and full-field phase coherence.

</details>


### [37] [Correlated and uncorrelated long--time asymptotics of type D ASEP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11376)
*Jeffrey Kuan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究类型D ASEP（type D ASEP）的长时渐近行为，证明了在固定q机制下流体动力学极限与Tracy-Widom涨落解耦，在弱不对称（Edwards–Wilkinson）机制下两个密度涨落场解耦但极限正态随机变量存在新的相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 类型D ASEP是由$U_q(\mathfrak{so}_{2n})$表示论构造的双物种相互作用粒子系统，已获得其可逆测度与正交多项式对偶，但长时渐近行为尚未被研究，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在固定q机制下，利用精确流解耦恒等式（exact current–decoupling identity）进行分析；在弱不对称机制（$q=1-c/N^2$）下，研究密度涨落场的渐近行为，并计算极限正态随机变量的相关性。

Result: 固定q机制下流体动力学极限与Tracy–Widom涨落完全解耦；弱不对称机制下两个密度涨落场解耦，各自收敛到线性随机热方程，漂移项与噪声项均无交叉耦合，但两个极限正态随机变量之间存在相关性，相关函数为$(1-e^{-4c})/(4c)$，其正部相关性由Bessel–Struve函数表达。

Conclusion: 类型D ASEP的长时动力学表现出非平凡的涨落结构：涨落场解耦但极限随机变量存在新颖的相关性，揭示了双物种排斥粒子系统中宏观行为与微观对称性之间的深层联系。

Abstract: The type D ASEP is an asymmetric two--species interacting particle system on $\Z$, in which two separately conserved species hop, bind into a composite ``bound pair'', and split. The model, along with its reversible measures and orthogonal polynomial duality, was constructed using the representation theory of $U_q(\so_{2n})$. The reversible measures and orthogonal polynomial duality are each a product of two copies of the single-species ASEP reversible measures and orthogonal polynomial duality. In this paper, we study the long-time asymptotics of the type D ASEP.
  In the fixed--$q$ regime, using an exact current--decoupling identity, we prove that the asymptotic hydrodynamic limit and Tracy--Widom fluctuations decouple, as predicted from the duality. In the weak--asymmetry (Edwards--Wilkinson) regime, when $q=1-c/N^2$, we prove that the two density fluctuation fields \underline{decouple}: each converges to a linear stochastic heat equation, with no cross--coupling in either the drift or the noise, the limiting noises having vanishing cross--correlation. More surprisingly, we then prove that the two limiting normal random variables are \underline{correlated} with a seemingly new correlation function. The correlation is exactly equal to $(1-e^{-4c})/(4c)$, with the positive parts of the normal random variables having correlations expressed by the Bessel--Struve function.
  This paper, with the exception of the abstract and introduction, was written entirely by Claude Opus 4.8 and Fable 5. The proofs were then formalized in Lean, using Aristotle by Harmonic AI. The human author of this paper verified the proofs manually.

</details>


### [38] [On The Eigenvalue Rigidity of the Laguerre Unitary Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11547)
*Chenhao Lu,Xiaolu Yue*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了拉盖尔酉系综（Laguerre unitary ensemble）特征值的最优全局刚性（optimal global rigidity）估计，通过构造基于特征值计数函数的随机测度，证明其收敛到高斯乘性混沌测度（Gaussian multiplicative chaos measure），从而得到刚性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立拉盖尔酉系综特征值的最优全局刚性估计，这是随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）中关于特征值分布精细结构的重要问题。

Method: 首先利用中心极限定理（central limit theorem），通过特征值计数函数（eigenvalue counting function）构造一个随机测度；然后应用Claeys等人[7]给出的充分条件，对相应的指数矩（exponential moments）进行渐近分析（asymptotic analysis），从而证明该随机测度收敛到高斯乘性混沌测度。

Result: 证明了所构造的随机测度收敛到高斯乘性混沌测度，由此得到了拉盖尔酉系综特征值的最优全局刚性估计。

Conclusion: 通过随机测度收敛到高斯乘性混沌测度这一途径，成功建立了拉盖尔酉系综特征值的最优全局刚性结果。

Abstract: In this paper, we establish an optimal global rigidity estimate for the eigenvalues of the Laguerre unitary ensemble. Using the central limit theorem, we first construct a random measure via the eigenvalue counting function and then prove its convergence to a Gaussian multiplicative chaos measure, which yields the desired rigidity result. To prove this convergence, we apply a sufficient condition due to Claeys et al. [7] and carry out an asymptotic analysis of the corresponding exponential moments.

</details>

### [39] [Staggered Potential and Elliptical Light Driven Topological Phase Transitions in $α$-$\mathcal{T}_{3}$ Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10153)
*Muhammad Faisal,Muhammad Irfan Sarwar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文理论研究了非共振椭圆偏振光场下六方氮化硼（h-BN）衬底对α-𝒯₃晶格电子性质的影响，发现了一个与交错势M无关的几何奇点α=1/√2，在该奇点以下光场无法闭合下带隙，从而形成稳定的拓扑窗口并实现C=1的陈绝缘体（Chern insulator），而在该奇点以上可进一步实现从C=1到C=2的拓扑相变，并给出了量子化反常霍尔电导率和热电Seebeck响应的实验可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, h-BN）衬底引入的交错势（staggered potential）和椭圆偏振光场对α-𝒯₃晶格电子性质的联合调控机制，寻找稳定高陈数（Chern number）拓扑相的实现条件。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，通过非共振椭圆偏振光场驱动α-𝒯₃晶格，并引入h-BN衬底导致的交错势M来破缺子晶格反演对称性（sublattice inversion symmetry），系统研究不同α参数下的能隙闭合与拓扑相变行为。

Result: 发现了一个与M无关的几何奇点α=1/√2：当α<1/√2时光场无法闭合下带隙，形成稳定的拓扑窗口，导带-平带反转产生C=1的陈绝缘体；当α>1/√2时下带隙可在有限光强下闭合，接近骰子极限（dice limit, α=1）时实现从C=1到C=2的转变。C=1和C=2相分别对应量子化反常霍尔电导率σ_xy=e²/h和σ_xy=2e²/h，每个谷贡献½e²/h。C=1态在0-300 K保持鲁棒，C=2态因能隙较窄需T<100 K。高度不对称的热电Seebeck响应可作为各拓扑相的实验指纹。

Conclusion: 研究为在衬底支撑的α-𝒯₃材料中实现稳定的高陈数拓扑相提供了可行理论框架，揭示了几何奇点对拓扑相变的调控作用，并给出了反常霍尔电导率和热电响应等可实验验证的特征信号。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate the influence of hexagonal boron nitride (h-BN) on the electronic properties of an $α$-$\mathcal{T}_{3}$ lattice driven by an off-resonant elliptically polarized light field. The staggered potential $M$ breaks the sublattice inversion symmetry, transforming the initial semimetal into a trivial insulator with Chern number $C=0$. We identify a fundamental geometric singularity at $α=1/\sqrt{2}$, independent of $M$, below which no finite drive can close the lower band gap, creating a stable topological window where conduction--flat band inversion yields a Chern insulator with $C=1$. Above this critical value the lower gap closes with finite intensity, allowing a transition from $C=1$ to $C=2$ as the dice limit ($α=1$) is approached. The topological phases are characterized by quantized anomalous Hall plateaus at $σ_{xy}=e^2/h$ ($C=1$) and $σ_{xy}=2e^2/h$ ($C=2$), with each valley contributing exactly $\frac{1}{2}e^2/h$. The $C=1$ plateau remains robust from $0$ K to $300$ K, while $C=2$ requires $T<100$ K due to its narrower gap. A highly asymmetric thermoelectric Seebeck response further serves as an experimental fingerprint of each phase, providing a realistic framework for realizing stable high-Chern-number phases in substrate-supported $α$-$\mathcal{T}_{3}$ materials.

### [40] [Evidence for spin swapping from modulation of transverse resistance in magnetic heterostructures with Rashba interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10189)
*Heeman Kim,Shutaro Karube,Juan Borge,Junyeon Kim,Kouta Kondou,YoshiChika Otani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过对比Cu/Bi2O3与Ag/Bi2O3 Rashba界面磁异质结在面外磁场下的横向响应，发现两种界面对横向电阻的相反贡献恰好与它们自旋/电荷相互转换（spin/charge interconversion）的符号相反一致，推测这一现象源于转换自旋电流发生的自旋交换（spin swapping），两种金属层中自旋流方向取决于转换自旋电流的自旋方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有Rashba界面的磁异质结在面外磁场下的横向响应（transverse response），并厘清自旋/电荷相互转换与横向电阻变化之间的物理关联。

Method: 以Cu/Bi2O3和Ag/Bi2O3两种Rashba界面磁异质结为研究对象，测量其在面外磁场（out-of-plane magnetic field）作用下的横向电阻（transverse resistance）变化，并对比两种界面自旋/电荷相互转换符号的差异。

Result: Cu/Bi2O3与Ag/Bi2O3界面对横向电阻呈现相反的贡献，这一差异与两种界面的自旋/电荷相互转换符号完全一致；此外，Cu和Ag层内部均因自旋交换产生横向自旋流（transverse spin flow），但自旋流的方向取决于转换自旋电流的自旋方向（spin direction）。

Conclusion: 推测两种界面对横向电阻的相反影响源于转换自旋电流中发生了自旋交换（spin swapping）过程，横向自旋流的产生及其方向由自旋电流的自旋取向决定。

Abstract: We investigate the transverse response under the out-of-plane magnetic field for magnetic heterostructures with Cu/Bi2O3 or Ag/Bi2O3 Rashba interfaces. We detect opposite contributions on the transverse resistance by the Cu/Bi2O3 and the Ag/Bi2O3 interfaces, which interestingly coincide well with the opposite signs of the spin/charge interconversion from the two interfaces. We suppose the opposite influences on the transverse resistance feature spin swapping occurrence of the converted spin current. The transverse spin flow emerges due to the spin swapping in both Cu and Ag layer, but the direction of the spin flow is opposed dependent on the spin direction of the converted spin current.

</details>


### [41] [Retarded interaction between opposite chiral edges in anomalous Hall crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10320)
*Wangqian Miao,Mu-Yang Chen,Binghai Yan,Chunli Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出反常霍尔晶体（anomalous Hall crystal）中横向体声子（transverse bulk phonons）可在样品两侧反向传播的手征边缘模（chiral edge modes）之间产生延迟耦合，形成具有延迟边缘间耦合（delayed inter-edge coupling）的Luttinger液体变体；在菱方五层石墨烯中，载流子密度降低会软化长波横向声子模式，导致边界投影声子连续谱与边缘色散重叠，其探测信号为非局域测量中的边缘响应延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索反常霍尔晶体中自发电子结晶化与陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）能隙共存所产生的新颖动力学效应，特别是横向体声子介导的手征边缘模之间的延迟相互作用机制。

Method: 采用微观含时Hartree-Fock（time-dependent Hartree-Fock）计算，研究对象为菱方五层石墨烯（rhombohedral pentalayer graphene）体系。

Result: 降低载流子密度可软化长波横向声子模式；在该不稳定性边界附近，边界投影的声子连续谱与边缘色散产生重叠，从而允许二者耦合。

Conclusion: 反常霍尔晶体中存在通过横向体声子实现的对向手征边缘模之间的延迟耦合，可通过非局域测量（nonlocal measurement）——即对一个边缘施加驱动而在另一边缘观测到延迟响应——作为直接实验探针。

Abstract: An anomalous Hall crystal combines spontaneous electronic crystallization with a Chern insulating gap, supporting both chiral edge modes and low-energy electronic phonons. We show that this coexistence produces a distinct dynamical effect from ordinary Chern insulators: transverse bulk phonons can mediate a retarded interaction between counterpropagating chiral edge modes on opposite sides of the sample, realizing a Luttinger-liquid variant with delayed inter-edge coupling. Using microscopic time-dependent Hartree--Fock calculations for rhombohedral pentalayer graphene, we find that lowering the carrier density softens the long-wavelength transverse phonon mode. Near this instability regime, the resulting boundary-projected phonon continuum inevitably overlaps with the edge dispersion, thereby enabling their coupling. A smoking-gun probe is a nonlocal measurement: a drive applied to one edge can induce a response on the other edge, delayed by the transverse phonon time of flight across the sample.

### [42] [Lifshitz-Kosevich Theory of Anomalous Landau Levels in Topological Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10328)
*Chao-Xing Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文推导了拓扑平带中反常量子振荡的Lifshitz-Kosevich理论，发现其有效质量远大于正常带且具有磁场依赖性，热阻尼可直接测量量子度量，从而将量子振荡建立为探测平带量子几何的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 常规金属中的量子振荡由费米面回旋轨道的朗道量子化（Landau quantization）主导，其动力学由Lifshitz-Kosevich（LK）理论描述。完美平带具有零群速度，理论上应导致无限回旋质量并完全热抑制量子振荡，但拓扑平带可支持由量子几何（quantum geometry）而非能带曲率产生的反常朗道能级（Landau levels, LLs），使得量子振荡得以持续存在。本文旨在解决此类反常平带LL在LK框架下的行为及其热阻尼是否能够揭示量子几何信息。

Method: 使用具有完全平坦拓扑能带的最小模型，推导了这些反常LL的LK理论，并分析了固定密度下的磁化振荡。

Result: 得到的振荡表现出有限的LK有效质量，该质量显著大于正常带的值，并具有很强的磁场依赖性。在弱场极限下，该反常质量反映了LL间距的量子几何起源，且与磁场和量子度量（quantum metric）的迹成反比。

Conclusion: 平带量子振荡的热阻尼可直接测量量子度量，从而将量子振荡确立为探测平带量子几何的有效手段。

Abstract: In conventional metals, quantum oscillations arise from Landau quantization of Fermi-surface cyclotron orbits, whose dynamics are governed by the Fermi velocity and cyclotron effective mass within Lifshitz-Kosevich (LK) theory. A perfectly flat band, by contrast, has vanishing group velocity, which would naively imply an infinite cyclotron mass and complete thermal suppression of quantum oscillations. Yet topological flat bands can support anomalous Landau levels (LLs) whose finite-field spacing is generated by quantum geometry rather than band curvature, allowing quantum oscillations to persist. This work addresses how such anomalous flat-band LLs behave within the LK framework and whether their thermal damping can reveal quantum geometric information. Using a minimal model with exactly flat topological bands, we derive an LK theory for these anomalous LLs and analyze fixed-density magnetization oscillations. The resulting oscillations exhibit a finite LK effective mass that is substantially larger than the normal-band value and possesses a strong magnetic-field dependence. In the weak-field limit, this anomalous mass reflects the quantum geometric origin of the LL spacing and scales inversely with both the magnetic field and the trace of the quantum metric. Thus, thermal damping of flat-band quantum oscillations directly measures the quantum metric, establishing quantum oscillations as a probe to flat-band quantum geometry.

</details>


### [43] [Layer-Resolved Topological Metals in the Bilayer Lieb Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11009)
*Mengjie Yang,S Rahul,Giandomenico Palumbo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在双层Lieb晶格中识别出一种二维时间反演不变拓扑金属相，该相由量子化的层分辨赝自旋陈数（layer-resolved pseudo-spin Chern number）刻画；通过调控层内轨道角动量依赖耦合（intralayer OAM-dependent coupling），体系可在拓扑半金属与拓扑金属之间转换，并展现出非对称边界态（asymmetric boundary states），包括完美平带（perfectly flat bands）与一维狄拉克锥（one-dimensional Dirac cone）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间反演对称系统中拓扑金属相的存在条件，并研究层分辨拓扑不变量（layer-resolved topological invariants）在无带隙（gapless）体系中的定义与稳定性，为在合成材料和量子材料中实现层分辨拓扑无带隙相（layer-resolved topological gapless phases）提供理论路径。

Method: 基于双层Lieb晶格（bilayer Lieb lattice）模型，引入层内轨道角动量依赖耦合（intralayer OAM-dependent coupling）以及边缘局域层间耦合（edge-localized interlayer coupling），通过分析全局能谱、直接带隙（direct gap）、赝自旋带隙（pseudo-spin gap）及层分辨赝自旋陈数（layer-resolved pseudo-spin Chern number）来刻画体系的拓扑性质与边界态结构。

Result: 无OAM依赖耦合时，体系表现为时间反演不变拓扑半金属（topological semimetal），具有零间接带隙（zero indirect gap）和量子化的赝自旋陈数；加入相反符号的层内OAM依赖耦合后，体系转变为拓扑金属（topological metal），全局谱呈金属性，但层分辨赝自旋陈数在直接带隙和赝自旋带隙保持开放时仍良好定义。边界态呈现非对称性：半金属区一侧为完美平带，对侧为无带隙反向传播模（counter-propagating modes）构成的一维狄拉克锥；边缘局域层间耦合仅使反向传播模打开带隙，而平带边界几乎不受影响；层内OAM依赖耦合则将平带弯曲为色散边界模（dispersive boundary mode），但不影响已开带隙的狄拉克边缘。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了层内OAM依赖耦合在调控层分辨拓扑无带隙相中的关键作用，为在合成材料和量子材料中定向设计层分辨拓扑金属相提供了理论依据与调控策略。

Abstract: We identify a two-dimensional time-reversal-invariant topological metallic phase on a bilayer Lieb lattice, characterized by a quantized layer--resolved pseudo-spin Chern number. Without the orbital-angular-momentum-dependent (OAM-dependent) coupling, the system gives rise to a time-reversal-invariant topological semimetal with a zero indirect gap and quantized pseudo-spin Chern number. Opposite-sign intralayer OAM-dependent coupling immediately converts the zero-indirect-gap semimetal into a metal, in which the global spectrum is metallic while the layer--resolved pseudo-spin Chern number remains well defined as long as the direct gap at each crystal momentum and the pseudo-spin gap remain open. The model also exhibits asymmetric boundary states: in the semimetallic regime, one edge hosts perfectly flat bands, whereas the opposite edge supports gapless counter-propagating modes forming a one-dimensional Dirac cone. An edge-localized interlayer coupling gaps only the counter-propagating edge states, leaving the flat-band edge essentially intact, while intralayer OAM-dependent coupling bends the exact flat band into a dispersive boundary mode without affecting the gapped Dirac edge. These results open a route toward the controlled engineering of layer--resolved topological gapless phases in synthetic and quantum materials.

</details>


### [44] [Staggered orbital magnetization from itinerant electrons: orbital antiferro- and ferrimagnetic phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10355)
*Lucas L. Lage,Kevin J. U. Vidarte,Tarik P. Cysne,Tatiana G. Rappoport,A. Latgé,R. B. Muniz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实空间方法分解晶格中巡游电子的轨道磁化强度为子晶格贡献，发现标准与修正Haldane模型中存在轨道铁磁、反铁磁及亚铁磁序，并由两种不同的谷机制解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中电子轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）本质上是非局域的，其对磁性的贡献通常被表述为净轨道磁化强度（net orbital magnetization），但轨道序（如铁磁/反铁磁）的存在性尚不清楚，因此需要研究巡游电子能否生成轨道磁相。

Method: 采用实空间形式（real-space formulation），将巡游轨道磁化强度分解为子晶格（sublattice）贡献 $M_A$ 和 $M_B$，并构造净组合 $M_z=M_A+M_B$ 和交错组合 $M_z^s=M_A-M_B$ 来识别轨道序。在蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice）上分别使用标准Haldane模型和修正Haldane模型进行演示。

Result: 发现了不同的轨道磁相：修正Haldane模型中的(PT)对称轨道反铁磁（orbital antiferromagnet），标准Haldane模型中的轨道铁磁（orbital ferromagnet），以及净与交错轨道磁化共存的亚铁磁金属态（ferrimagnetic metallic states）；在绝缘区中，铁磁与反铁磁轨道特征可以互换。

Conclusion: 该现象可通过低能理论（low-energy theory）中的两种不同谷机制（valley mechanisms）解释：标准Haldane模型中的谷依赖狄拉克质量（valley-dependent Dirac masses）和修正Haldane模型中的谷依赖能量移动（valley-dependent energy shifts）。

Abstract: Because electronic orbital angular momentum in solids is inherently non-local, its contribution to magnetism is usually cast in terms of a net orbital magnetization. Here, we show that itinerant electrons can generate orbital magnetic phases with ferromagnetic, antiferromagnetic, or ferrimagnetic orders. We demonstrate this possibility in a honeycomb lattice, using both the standard and a modified Haldane model. Employing real-space formulations, we decompose the itinerant orbital magnetization into sublattice contributions, $M_A$ and $M_B$. Their net ($M_z=M_A+M_B$) and staggered ($M_z^s=M_A-M_B$) combinations are then used to identify the orbital order. By varying the sublattice potential and the Fermi energy, we find distinct regimes: a (PT)-symmetric orbital antiferromagnet in the modified Haldane model, an orbital ferromagnet in the standard Haldane model, ferrimagnetic metallic states where net and staggered orbital magnetizations coexist, and insulating regimes in which the ferro- and antiferromagnetic orbital characters can be interchanged.These findings are explained by a low-energy theory in terms of two distinct valley mechanisms: valley-dependent Dirac masses in the standard Haldane model and valley-dependent energy shifts in its modified version.

</details>


### [45] [Nonperturbative magnetotransport from band geometry in Weyl semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10468)
*L. Medel Onofre,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）中磁输运（magnetotransport）的非微扰半经典理论，揭示了贝里曲率（Berry curvature）和轨道磁矩（orbital magnetic moment）效应下，磁场展开与动量积分不可交换，导致标量输运系数中出现非解析贡献，从而识别出一个低载流子密度或中等磁场下的非微扰输运区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有外尔半金属磁输运理论多局限于弱场微扰展开，无法处理贝里曲率和轨道磁矩在有限磁场下的完整效应。本文旨在建立保留磁场全阶依赖的非微扰半经典框架，并揭示传统弱场展开失效的条件与机制。

Method: 采用非微扰半经典理论（nonperturbative semiclassical theory），保留费米面电导率（Fermi-surface conductivity）对磁场的完整依赖性，推导出在半经典区域内对磁场所有阶次均有效的闭式表达式。针对轨道磁矩奇异行为导致的红外敏感性（infrared sensitivity），引入物理启发的正则化（regularization）方案。

Result: 完整电导率张量（conductivity tensor）虽可约化为标准二次磁电导率（quadratic magnetoconductivity），但磁场展开与动量积分并不交换顺序，导致标量输运系数（scalar transport coefficients）中出现非解析贡献（nonanalytic contributions）。识别出一个低载流子密度或中等磁场下的非微扰输运（nonperturbative transport）区域。

Conclusion: 外尔半金属中磁输运在特定条件下本质上是非微扰的，无法被传统弱场展开方法捕捉。该发现对于理解低载流子密度或中等磁场下的输运行为具有重要意义，为相关实验和理论建模提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a nonperturbative semiclassical theory of magnetotransport in Weyl semimetals, retaining the full magnetic-field dependence of the Fermi-surface conductivity in the presence of Berry curvature and orbital magnetic moment effects. We obtain closed-form expressions valid to all orders in the magnetic field within the semiclassical regime. We show that the exact continuum formulation exhibits an intrinsic infrared sensitivity associated with the singular behavior of the orbital magnetic moment, requiring a physically motivated regularization. While the full conductivity tensor reduces to the standard quadratic magnetoconductivity, we demonstrate that magnetic-field expansion and momentum integration do not commute, leading to nonanalytic contributions at the level of scalar transport coefficients. Our results identify a regime, relevant for low carrier densities or moderate magnetic fields, where magnetotransport becomes intrinsically nonperturbative and cannot be captured by conventional weak-field expansions.

</details>


### [46] [Spectral-Domain Deep Learning of Intrinsic Scattering Operators for Arbitrarily Shaped Compact 3D Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10570)
*Daize Li,Jiafu Shen,Yifei Liu,Bonan Zhang,Heping Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双谱域神经散射模型（dual spectral-domain neural scattering model），通过将粒子几何形状压缩为256个球谐系数（spherical-harmonic coefficients）、光学响应编码为T矩阵（complex T-matrix），并采用谱标记Transformer（spectral-token Transformer）学习从形态谱到T矩阵的直接映射，实现了对任意形状三维粒子光学散射的快速预测，并在分布外形状和天然沙粒形态上展现出良好的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任意形状三维粒子的光学散射快速预测在粒子光学与光子学表征中具有重要意义，但由于复杂形态的多样性和散射响应的强角度依赖性，这一任务仍然具有挑战性。现有方法受限于高维欧几里得几何表示（如体素网格、点云或网格）的高计算代价和可重用性差的问题。

Method: 该方法的核心是双谱域表示：粒子几何形状被压缩为256个球谐系数（morphology spectrum），构成紧致有序的描述子；光学响应则由球面矢量波基（spherical-vector-wave basis）下的复T矩阵（T-matrix）编码。基于50,000个不规则粒子在1064 nm波长下的数据，训练一个谱标记Transformer（spectral-token Transformer），将形态谱直接映射到T矩阵。

Result: 预测得到的T矩阵能够恢复模态结构（modal structure），重现全角微分散射图（full-angle differential scattering maps）和入射角扫描（incidence-angle scans）。该方法对分布外合成形状与天然沙粒形态均展现出良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 双谱域架构从几何谱到多极散射（multipolar scattering）学到了内在关系，确立了谱域算子学习作为对复杂三维粒子进行可重用、角度和偏振分辨的光学散射预测的紧致路径。

Abstract: Rapid prediction of optical scattering from arbitrarily shaped three-dimensional particles is important for particle optics and photonic characterization, but remains challenging because of the large variability of complex morphologies and the strong angular dependence of their scattering responses. To address both issues, a dual spectral-domain neural scattering model is introduced in which morphology and scattering are represented in physically ordered bases: particle geometry is compressed into only 256 spherical-harmonic coefficients, and the optical response is encoded by the complex T-matrix in a spherical-vector-wave basis. The morphology spectrum replaces high-dimensional Euclidean geometry representations, such as voxel grids, point clouds, or meshes, with a compact ordered descriptor, while the T-matrix represents a geometry-determined scattering operator that can be queried for different incidence directions, polarizations, and observation angles. A spectral-token Transformer trained on 50{,}000 irregular particles at 1064~nm maps the morphology spectrum directly to the T-matrix. The predicted operators recover modal structure and reproduce full-angle differential scattering maps and incidence-angle scans. Generalization to out-of-distribution synthetic shapes and natural sand-particle morphologies shows that the dual spectral architecture learns an intrinsic relation from the geometry spectrum to multipolar scattering. This establishes spectral-domain operator learning as a compact route for reusable, angle- and polarization-resolved optical scattering prediction of complex 3D particles.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文研究了多端邻近效应（proximitized）器件中手性马约拉纳费米子（chiral Majorana fermions）的输运性质，发现配对能隙（pairing gap）的复相位（complex phase）可控制电导和热导干涉效应，并预测了由电压偏置驱动的交流马约拉纳效应（AC Majorana effect）及基于超导岛的三端马约拉纳路由器（Majorana router）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究了两端和三端构型下的磁性拓扑绝缘体纳米带（magnetic topological insulator nanoribbons），其中包含邻近效应区域和渐近正常电极（asymptotic normal leads），并聚焦于单手性马约拉纳（single chiral Majoranas）输运区域。

Result: 手性马约拉纳的特征电学和热学干涉（interferometry）可通过配对能隙的复相位进行调控；预测了交流马约拉纳效应，即电压偏置引起的相位动力学（phase dynamics）会产生可测量的时变电导振荡；三端结在合适配置复相位时可作为马约拉纳路由器使用。

Conclusion: 配对能隙的复相位是实现多端邻近效应器件中手性马约拉纳输运主动控制的关键参数，可产生交流振荡效应和定向路由功能。

Abstract: Transport in devices with multiple proximitized sectors depends heavily on the complex phases of the pairing gaps of those sectors. We investigate magnetic topological insulator nanoribbons in two- and three-terminal setups with proximitized sectors and asymptotic normal leads. Our focus is on the regime of single chiral Majoranas. The characteristic electric and thermal interferometries of chiral Majoranas can be controlled by the complex phases of the pairing. We predict an AC Majorana effect, in which phase dynamics induced by a voltage bias generate measurable time-dependent conductance oscillations. A three-terminal junction with superconducting islands can be used as a Majorana router when the relative complex phases are configured.

### [48] [Parity-driven RKKY decoupling and anomalous $1/R$ Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction in $p$-wave magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10757)
*Morteza Salehi,Tohid Farajollahpour*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用实空间格林函数形式论，理论上研究了施加Rashba自旋轨道耦合的二维p波磁体中的RKKY间接交换作用，揭示了宇称驱动的空间退耦、可调谐的DM相互作用以及反常的降维交叉行为，表明p波磁体是构建稳健非共线自旋织构的有前景平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非传统p波磁体（p-wave magnet）具有奇宇称动量依赖的自旋劈裂，为非共线自旋电子学（non-collinear spintronics）提供了全新的范式，然而其间接交换机制尚未被充分理解。本文旨在揭示p波磁体中RKKY相互作用的独特行为及其可调控性。

Method: 采用解析实空间格林函数形式论（analytical real-space Green's function formalism），对二维p波磁体在Rashba自旋轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）下的Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida（RKKY）间接交换进行理论分析。

Result: 发现以下结果：(1) 面外Ising相互作用因奇宇称交换场与宏观p波调制结构上退耦，在偏移费米波矢下各向同性振荡；(2) 面内Heisenberg分量呈现显著的方向可调谐空间拍频；(3) 杂化能带产生高度可调的三分量Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用及对称离轴各向异性；(4) 面外手性扭转由非相对论性p波动量位移驱动，面内手性分量则严格为相对论性起源；(5) p波节线几何与Rashba能隙的竞争引发反常降维交叉，面内手性分量在节线方向沿中间距离窗口呈现一维1/R空间衰减，最终恢复二维1/R²渐近行为。

Conclusion: 上述发现确立了p波磁体作为工程化稳健、方向可调谐的非共线自旋织构的有前景平台。

Abstract: Unconventional $p$-wave magnets, characterized by an odd-parity momentum-dependent spin splitting, offer a fundamentally distinct paradigm for non-collinear spintronics. Here, we theoretically investigate the Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida indirect exchange in a two-dimensional $p$-wave magnet subjected to Rashba spin-orbit coupling. Using an analytical real-space Green's function formalism, we uncover a parity-driven spatial decoupling in the magnetic response. Because of the odd-parity exchange field, the out-of-plane Ising interaction is structurally insulated from the macroscopic $p$-wave modulation, oscillating isotropically at the shifted Fermi wavevector. Conversely, the in-plane Heisenberg components exhibit pronounced, directionally tunable spatial beating. Beyond collinear exchange, the hybridized bands generate a highly tunable, three-component Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction alongside symmetric off-diagonal anisotropies. We reveal that the out-of-plane chiral twisting is driven by the massive, nonrelativistic $p$-wave momentum shift, while the in-plane chiral components are strictly relativistic. Furthermore, the competition between the $p$-wave nodal geometry and the Rashba gap drives an anomalous, dimension-reducing crossover, in which the in-plane chiral components follow a 1D-like $1/R$ spatial decay along the nodal lines over an extended intermediate-distance window before ultimately recovering the conventional 2D $1/R^2$ asymptote. These findings establish $p$-wave magnets as promising platforms for engineering robust, directionally tunable non-collinear spin textures.

### [49] [Single-Contact Problem in Atomically Flat Interfaces: a Simulation Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10979)
*Rui Dong,Ahmed Uluca,Graham Cross,Stefano Sanvito*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究结合原子模拟与修正连续介质模型，探讨了晶态SiO₂/SiO₂界面的滑动起始机制。通过计算界面滑动势能面(ISPES)，发现剪切强度与最小尺度滑动(MSS)摩擦力在3GPa以下随正压力线性变化，且在零压下非零。将这些参数纳入扩展的Mindlin模型（包含黏附与纳米尺度载荷效应），可描述真实赫兹应力分布下的粘滑转变。模型表明，非均匀压力分布会显著降低有效静摩擦力，振荡剪切实验验证了模型对实际微凸起摩擦学的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用原子模拟（atomistic simulations）计算晶态SiO₂/SiO₂界面的界面滑动势能面(ISPES)，提取随载荷变化的剪切强度与最小尺度滑动(MSS)摩擦力；在此基础上，通过引入黏附（adhesion）与纳米尺度载荷效应，扩展了经典的Mindlin模型，使其能够描述赫兹应力分布下的粘滑转变。

Result: 剪切强度与MSS摩擦力在3GPa以下正压力范围内呈线性依赖关系，且在零压力下为非零值；非均匀压力分布显著降低了有效静摩擦力；振荡剪切实验再现了预测的刚度塌陷特征（stiffness-collapse signature），并在钝化极限下观察到了与模拟一致的黏附限制剪切强度。

Conclusion: 所构建的修正Mindlin模型能够将原子尺度的摩擦参数与微观赫兹接触几何下的摩擦行为联系起来，实验验证支持该模型对真实微凸起摩擦学（micro-asperity tribology）的适用性。

Abstract: Understanding friction at single-asperity contacts is essential for bridging the gap between nanoscale structural superlubricity and realistic tribological systems dominated by Hertzian contact geometry. In this work, we combine atomistic simulations and a modified continuum model to investigate the onset of sliding at crystalline SiO$_2$/SiO$_2$ interfaces. Interfacial sliding potential energy surfaces (ISPES) are computed to determine the load-dependent shear strength and minimal-scale sliding (MSS) friction. Both quantities exhibit linear dependence on normal pressure below 3 GPa, and have non-zero values at zero pressure. Incorporating these parameters, we extend the classical Mindlin model by including adhesion and nanoscale load effects, allowing us to describe the stick to slip transition under realistic Hertzian stress distributions. The model shows that nonuniform pressure distributions substantially lower the effective static friction, and oscillatory-shear experiments on graphene-passivated contacts reproduce both the predicted stiffness-collapse signature and, in the passivated limit, the adhesion-limited shear strength obtained from simulation, supporting the model's relevance to real micro-asperity tribology.

### [50] [Spectroscopy of low-lying valley states in hot Si/SiGe quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11048)

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文比较了脉冲栅极光谱法（PGS）和失谐轴光谱法（DAPS）在硅（Si）基量子点中提取谷分裂（valley splitting）的性能，发现DAPS在高达700 mK的温度下能够分辨低至约86 μeV的谷分裂，分辨率优于PGS（约210 μeV），表明DAPS可在高通量低温恒温器中高效提取谷分裂。

Method: 在高达700 mK的温度下，分别采用脉冲栅极光谱法（pulsed-gate spectroscopy, PGS）和失谐轴光谱法（detuning axis spectroscopy, DAPS）测量Si/SiGe量子点中的谷分裂，并比较两种方法的能量分辨率。

Conclusion: DAPS可在高温（高达700 mK）和高通量低温恒温器（high throughput cryostats）中高效提取谷分裂，为快速优化Si/SiGe异质结构提供一种有效的表征手段。

Abstract: The presence of low-lying valley states in Si may hinder the development of large-scale spin-based quantum processors. Rapid prototyping of novel Si/SiGe heterostructures and gate stacks will be central to identifying pathways that increase the valley splitting. We compare the performance of pulsed-gate spectroscopy (PGS) and detuning axis spectroscopy (DAPS) at temperatures up to 700 mK. We find that DAPS outperforms PGS, with DAPS resolving valley splittings as small as ~86 $μ$eV, while the energy resolution of PGS is only ~210~$μ$eV. Our work demonstrates that DAPS can be used to efficiently extract valley splittings at elevated temperatures in high throughput cryostats.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为表面各向异性纳米磁体的宏观磁化动力学建立微观理论基础，定量描述表面效应引起的自旋错位（spin misalignment）对磁化进动、阻尼和章动的修正。

Method: 采用自旋相干态路径积分形式，从原子自旋哈密顿量出发，先获得包含Wess–Zumino–Witten（Berry phase）项、交换、塞曼（Zeeman）及核/表面各向异性贡献的连续欧几里得作用量（Euclidean action）；再将局域磁化密度分解为缓慢变化的宏观自旋分量和表面效应驱动的横向自旋错位涨落，在绝热近似（adiabatic approximation）下将横向涨落展开至二阶并利用静态格林函数（Green's function）消除，得到封闭的扩展Landau–Lifshitz方程。

Result: 得到的扩展Landau–Lifshitz方程中有效场包含自旋错位的非平凡修正，这些修正重整化（renormalize）了塞曼场和各向异性场，并引入类似章动（nutation）和阻尼的附加项。对应的铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）频率偏移和线宽展宽可用标准GHz谱仪测量。

Conclusion: 研究为表面诱导的纳米磁体磁化章动提供了微观基础，建立了估算进动频率和有效阻尼修正的理论框架，且所采用的绝热消去机制可推广至任何与快涨落模式耦合的慢磁变量系统。

Abstract: An effective dynamical equation for the magnetization of a nanomagnet with surface anisotropy is derived from an atomistic spin Hamiltonian using the spin coherent-state path integral formalism. The derivation proceeds in two steps. First, the continuum Euclidean action for the many-spin nanomagnet is obtained, including the Wess--Zumino--Witten (Berry phase) term, as well as exchange, Zeeman, and core/surface anisotropy contributions. Second, the local magnetization density is decomposed into a slowly varying macrospin component and transverse spin-misalignment fluctuations driven by surface effects.
  A systematic expansion of the action is then performed up to quadratic order in the transverse-fluctuation variables. Under the adiabatic approximation, in which transverse modes relax much faster than the macrospin, these modes are eliminated by using their static Green's function solution. This results in a closed, extended Landau--Lifshitz equation for the macrospin, featuring an effective field with nontrivial corrections from spin misalignment. These corrections renormalize both the Zeeman and anisotropy fields and introduce additional terms that act as nutation- and damping-like contributions. ...
  Together, these results establish a microscopic foundation for surface-induced magnetization nutation in nanomagnets and provide a framework to estimate corrections to the precession frequency and effective damping. The corresponding shift in the ferromagnetic-resonance frequency and linewidth is measurable with standard GHz spectrometers, and the underlying adiabatic-elimination mechanism is expected to generalize to any slow magnetic variable coupled to a bath of fast-fluctuating modes.

</details>


### [54] [Theory of phonon-induced spin relaxation in a structured phononic reservoir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11479)
*Raseeb F. Haroon,Paweł Machnikowski*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过结合马尔可夫（Markovian）与非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）开放量子系统理论和有限元模拟，发展了一套关于结构化声子库中电子自旋弛豫的理论。以量子点（QD）嵌入声子波导为例，发现自旋弛豫率在大部分区域比体材料高一个数量级，但在模式色散带隙和对称性选择定则作用下，弛豫可在特定参数窗口被压制多个数量级；边界处则由范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）引发弛豫率奇点，对此提出了幂律标度律和非马尔可夫动力学描述，揭示了自旋被慢声学模式极化子修饰（polaronic dressing）的物理图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解混合系统中涉及机械模式的自旋动力学，并为结合自旋自由度与光子、声子架构的器件设计提供理论依据，这类器件在中磁场对应的声子态密度调制区间工作。

Method: 将马尔可夫和非马尔可夫开放量子系统理论与有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）相结合，以声子波导中的量子点（Quantum Dot, QD）作为代表性模型系统进行分析。

Result: 与体材料相比，结构化声子库中的自旋弛豫率通常高出一个数量级；但在模式色散带隙和对称性选择定则（selection rules）的作用下，弛豫可在特定参数窗口被压制多个数量级；在两类区域边界处，范霍夫奇点导致弛豫率出现奇点。

Conclusion: 提出了用于描述弛豫率奇点附近的幂律标度律（power-law scaling）及非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian dynamics）理论框架，揭示了自旋被慢声学模式极化子修饰的物理机制。

Abstract: By combining Markovian and non-Markovian open quantum system theory with finite-element simulations, we develop a theory of electron spin relaxation in a structured phononic reservoir. This problem is crucial for understanding spin dynamics in hybrid systems involving mechanical modes, as well as for the design of devices combining spin degrees of freedom with photonic and phononic architectures, where the phonon density of states is modulated in the relevant spectral range corresponding to moderate magnetic fields. Taking a QD in a phononic waveguide as a representative and technologically relevant example, we show that spin relaxation in such environments is much more complex than in bulk. While the relaxation rates are typically an order of magnitude higher than in bulk, there are parameter windows where the relaxation is suppressed by many orders of magnitude due to gaps in mode dispersion and selection rules imposed by mode symmetry. At the border between these two sectors, van Hove singularities in phonon dispersion lead to singularities in relaxation rates, for which we develop power-law scaling and propose a non-Markovian description of the dynamics, revealing polaronic dressing of the spin into slow acoustic modes.

*Peter Gschwandtner,Quirin Buchinger,Krishna Chand Maurya,Mohamed Helal,Barbara Souza Damasceno,Ravindra Kumar,Hyemin Kim,Ievgen Brytavskyi,Silke Kuhn,Arne Ludwig,Dirk Reuter,Yong-Hoon Cho,Tobias Huber-Loyola,Sven Höfling*

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种同时具备高效率、高重复率和确定性电荷控制的稳健器件架构，满足了下一代量子网络硬件（quantum network hardware）的关键要求。

Abstract: The development of efficient, deterministic, and tunable single-photon sources is a cornerstone for the realization of long-distance quantum communication, quantum repeaters, and photonic quantum computing technologies. In this study, we demonstrate a bright, charge-tunable single-photon source in the 900 nm wavelength range based on InAs quantum dots (QDs) embedded in a p-i-n doped GaAs membrane, which shows blinking free emission.
  We use a modified circular Bragg grating (CBG) as a micro-resonator. By adding fourfold symmetric bridges in a labyrinth-like geometry, we provide a conductive pathway to the central disk, thereby enabling electrical contact to the QD while maintaining high Purcell enhancement and photon extraction efficiency (PEE). For the negative trion (X-), we demonstrate a lifetime of $44.3 \pm 0.2$ ps - corresponding to a Purcell factor of $18.0 \pm 0.7$ and a PEE of $68.1% \pm 3.1$ %. Furthermore, the device is blinking-free with very low multi-photon contribution, evidenced by a second-order autocorrelation value $g(2)(0) < 0.017 \pm 0.015$. By applying a vertical diode bias, we demonstrate precise charge-state control, resolving distinct emission plateaus ranging from the single negatively charged trion ($X^-$) to triply negatively charged excitons ($X^{3-}$).
  These results showcase a robust architecture that simultaneously provides high efficiency, high repetition rates, and deterministic charge control, fulfilling key requirements for the next generation of quantum network hardware.

Abstract: While a minimal Kitaev chain is promised to host unprotected Majorana zero modes, its role for spin qubits is relatively underappreciated. Long-distance, anisotropic exchange coupling can be mediated by the Andreev bound states (ABSs) in the hybrid segment. ### [57] [Discovery of a symmetry-driven electronic cascade in a $d$-wave altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11567)
*Zhouyi Yin,Zheng Shi,Shuxuan Zhang,Changchao Liu,Xingkai Cheng,Fayuan Zhang,Han-Bin Deng,Jia-Xin Yin,Chaoyu Chen,Guang-Han Cao,Junwei Liu,Yue Zhao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Altermagnets host magnetic compensation together with non-relativistic spin-split bands, a coexistence enabled by crystal symmetry. Yet whether and how crystal symmetry organizes collective electronic order remains largely unexplored. Here we uncover a symmetry-driven cascade of finite-$q$ charge order in a $d$-wave altermagnet Rb$_{1-δ}$V$_2$Te$_2$O, using phase-resolved scanning tunneling microscopy. A primary density-wave instability drives an initial electronic reconstruction, followed by the emergence of a nematic component and an off-axis modulation with wave vectors geometrically tied to the preceding orders. Phase-resolved spectroscopy distinguishes these components through separate contrast-inversion energies and maps out branch-selective spectral-weight redistribution within the off-axis mode. Together with doping and temperature evolution, these observations establish a highly coordinated hierarchy of coupled density-wave instabilities, consistent with successive symmetry lowering. This multi-component hierarchy can be well described in the Landau framework through sequential softening of the charge orders, where bilinear coupling to their compatible octupolar partners at the lower-symmetry stages enables mutual stabilization within an intertwined charge-multipole state. Such a transparent realization of a charge-order cascade shows how altermagnetic symmetry can extend beyond band formation to organize collective electronic order, offering a new perspective on emergent many-body states in correlated quantum materials.

### [58] [Anomalous Dissipation in Current Biased Josephson Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11647)
*Johannes Hauff,Niklas Gaiser,Joachim Ankerhold,Dominik Maile*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上探讨了电流偏置约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）中出现的一种新相位扩散（phase diffusive）机制，该机制源于将结嵌入具有反常耗散（anomalous dissipation）的电路环境中。通过在结旁并联一个电阻与电容的串联支路，电磁涨落有效耦合至结的电荷，从而产生丰富的约瑟夫森动力学，特别是在零电压态退出的开关过程中。将这一过程建模为假想相位粒子从亚稳态势阱的逃逸，研究发现反常耗散在量子隧穿主导低温区间具有显著影响。使用实际电路参数时，量子逃逸过程显著增强，随后出现短时电压脉冲并以高概率再次捕获。这类电路可用于微波光子探测或耗散量子退火过程，同时为利用反常环境在非线性系统中工程化耗散动力学提供了通用框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将约瑟夫森结嵌入一个并联电阻-电容串联支路的电路环境中，使得电磁涨落（electromagnetic fluctuations）耦合至结的电荷。利用相位粒子（phase-particle）从亚稳态势阱（metastable well）逃逸的经典模型，结合量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）与热激活（thermal activation）理论，进行理论分析与计算。

Result: 反常耗散在量子隧穿主导的低温区间对逃逸过程影响显著；使用实际电路参数时，量子逃逸过程被大幅增强，逃逸后出现短电压脉冲并以高概率重新捕获（re-trapping）。

Conclusion: 该研究为利用反常环境在非线性系统中工程化耗散动力学提供了通用框架，且这类电路可用于微波光子检测或耗散量子退火（dissipative quantum annealing）等应用。

Abstract: A new phase diffusive regime in a current biased Josephson junction is theoretically explored which originates from embedding the junction in a circuit environment with anomalous dissipation. This is realized by placing parallel to the junction a resistor in series with a capacitor such that electromagnetic fluctuations effectively couple also to the charge of the junction. This leads to rich Josephson dynamics, in particular for the switching of the junction out of a zero voltage state. Modelled as the escape process of a fictitious phase-particle out of a metastable well, a detailed study reveals that anomalous dissipation has a strong impact at low temperatures when quantum tunneling dominates against thermal activation. As a manifestation, a regime is found, where for realistic circuit parameters the quantum escape process is substantially enhanced, followed by a short voltage pulse and re-trapping with high probability. This class of circuits may be leveraged for detecting microwave photons or dissipative quantum annealing processes. In addition, the analysis provides a general framework for engineering dissipative dynamics in nonlinear systems using anomalous environments.

### [59] [Thermodynamic bound on the Fano factor of a coherent thermoelectric heat engine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11704)
*Nahual Sobrino,Rosario Fazio,Matteo Acciai*

TL;DR: 本文针对费米子相干热电输运中的热机操作，推导了一种热力学不确定关系，该关系对电荷电流的Fano因子施加了F > 1/2的普适下限。研究表明，经典马尔可夫过程热力学不确定关系的违反（通常与量子优势相关）在热机中比一般热力学过程更受限制。对于玻色子和经典载流子，最小Fano因子增至F > 1，且经典马尔可夫过程的热力学不确定关系从未被违反。数值证据表明所有界限都是紧的，并可通过适当设计的透射达到饱和。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于费米子相干热电输运的理论分析，推导热机操作下电荷电流的Fano因子（Fano factor）下限；同时针对玻色子和经典载流子进行对比分析。

Conclusion: 经典马尔可夫过程热力学不确定关系的违反在热机场景下受到比一般热力学过程更严格的限制；对于玻色子和经典载流子，该关系从未被违反。

Abstract: We show that for fermionic coherent thermoelectric transport, selecting heat-engine operation yields a thermodynamic uncertainty relation for the charge current that imposes a universal lower limit of $F > 1/2$ on the corresponding Fano factor. We find that violations of the thermodynamic uncertainty relation for classical Markov processes, typically associated with a quantum advantage, are far more restricted for heat engines than what is allowed by a generic thermodynamic process. For bosonic and classical carriers, the minimum Fano factor increases to $F > 1$, and the thermodynamic uncertainty relation for classical Markov processes is never violated. We provide numerical evidence that all the obtained bounds are tight and can be saturated by properly designed transmissions.

### [60] [High-field Josephson effect enabled by a moiré Hofstadter spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11721)
*A. Díez-Carlón,M. Cárdenes Wuttig,N. Wei,D. Ivanov,P. Altpeter,P. Hakonen,K. Watanabe,T. Taniguchi,L. I. Glazman,D. K. Efetov*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁场通常会抑制相位相干的约瑟夫森输运（Josephson transport），从而限制了超导干涉仪在相对较低磁场下的应用。本文旨在克服这一制约，探索在更高磁场下实现相位相干超导干涉的可能性。

Method: 采用弹道石墨烯/六方氮化硼（graphene/hBN）结，通过法布里-珀罗振荡（Fabry-Pérot oscillations）和夫琅禾费干涉（Fraunhofer interference）建立相位相干的安德烈夫输运（Andreev transport）；结合霍夫施塔特谱（Hofstadter-spectrum）计算进行对比分析。

Result: 在分形霍夫施塔特蝴蝶（fractal Hofstadter-butterfly）区域中，相位相干的约瑟夫森干涉（coherent Josephson interference）可维持至高达6特斯拉的磁场，远超传统弹道石墨烯结的预期范围。超导性在摩尔势将具有猝灭群速度的朗道能级转变为具有有限准粒子群速度的色散磁布洛赫带时得以保持。

Conclusion: 霍夫施塔特微带（Hofstadter minibands）能够在传统上与量子霍尔区域（quantum Hall regime）相关的参数域深处稳定相位相干超导性，为高磁场超导干涉测量建立了一个新平台。

Abstract: Magnetic fields generally suppress phase-coherent Josephson transport, limiting superconducting interferometry to relatively low fields. Here we show that moiré-engineered graphene Josephson junctions can overcome this constraint. Using ballistic graphene/hBN junctions, we establish phase-coherent Andreev transport through Fabry-Pérot oscillations and Fraunhofer interference that persist across both the primary Dirac cone and reconstructed moiré minibands. We then demonstrate phase-coherent Josephson interference up to 6 T in the fractal Hofstadter-butterfly regime, well beyond the range expected for conventional ballistic graphene junctions. Comparison with Hofstadter-spectrum calculations reveals that superconductivity survives where the moiré potential transforms Landau levels with quenched group velocity into dispersive magnetic Bloch bands with finite quasiparticle group velocity, enabling extended electron-hole Andreev trajectories across the junction. Our results show that Hofstadter minibands can stabilize phase-coherent superconductivity deep into the parameter domain conventionally associated with the quantum Hall regime, establishing a new platform for high-field superconducting interferometry.

</details>

### [61] [Electrical networks, Grassmannians, and cluster algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09975)
*B. Bychkov,L. Guterman,A. Kazakov*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究具有零行和对称矩阵的循环全正性（circular total positivity），这类矩阵恰好对应电网的响应矩阵。主要结果包括：在Grassmannian $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ 的坐标环上构造了一个由循环子式（circular minors）组成的种子，并将其簇结构（cluster structure）与代数 $\mathcal{CM}_n$ 进行比较；证明了 $\mathcal{LM}_n$ 同构于电网非紧化空间的坐标环，即Grove代数的某个局部化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 循环全正性问题是分析具有零行和对称矩阵结构性质的核心，这类矩阵与电网响应矩阵直接对应。Alman、Lian 和 Tran 已在两种相关代数框架（cluster algebra $\mathcal{CM}_n$ 与 Laurent Phenomenon algebra $\mathcal{LM}_n$）中描述了循环全正性的检验方法，本文旨在进一步揭示这些框架之间的深层代数结构与几何对应关系。

Method: 本文通过构造一个完全由循环子式组成的种子，在 $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ 的坐标环上的Scott簇代数（cluster algebra）结构中建立了新种子表示。通过比较该种子诱导的簇结构与 $\mathcal{CM}_n$ 的关系，特别针对奇数 $n$ 的情况，证明了 $\mathcal{CM}_n$ 同构于 $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ 上经过自然冻结和某些簇变量平凡化后的簇代数结构。此外，通过代数同构证明 $\mathcal{LM}_n$ 与电网非紧化空间的坐标环（即Grove代数的局部化）等价。

Result: 第一，构造了Grassmannian $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ 坐标环中完全由循环子式构成的种子，并揭示了该簇结构与 $\mathcal{CM}_n$ 之间的同构关系（对于奇数 $n$）。第二，证明了 $\mathcal{LM}_n$ 同构于电网非紧化空间的坐标环，等价于Grove代数的某个局部化。这些结果将循环全正性与Grassmannian中的正性（positivity）联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文通过代数同构建立了循环全正性、簇代数结构与Grassmannian正性之间的桥梁，深化了对具有零行和对称矩阵的循环全正性的理解，并揭示了电网络响应矩阵背后的代数几何结构。

Abstract: The paper studies the problem of circular total positivity of the symmetric matrices with zero row sums. These matrices are exactly response matrices of the electrical networks. Alman, Lian and Tran described tests for circular total positivity in two related frameworks: the cluster algebra $\mathcal{CM}_n$ and the Laurent Phenomenon algebra $\mathcal{LM}_n$. Our first result is the construction of a seed in Scott's cluster algebra structure on the coordinate ring of the Grassmannian $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ that consists entirely of circular minors. We compare the cluster structure induced by this seed with $\mathcal{CM}_n$. In particular, for odd $n$ the cluster algebra structure $\mathcal{CM}_n$ is isomorphic to the cluster algebra structure on $\mathrm{Gr}(n-1,2n)$ subject to natural freezing and trivialization of certain cluster variables in their initial seeds. We use this isomorphism to relate circular total positivity to positivity in the Grassmannian. Our second result is that the Laurent Phenomenon algebra $\mathcal{LM}_n$ is isomorphic to the coordinate ring of the noncompactified space of electrical network, or equivalently, to a certain localization of the grove algebra.

### [62] [SlaKoNet-VQD: A universal Slater-Koster tight-binding Hamiltonian for variational quantum band-structure calculations on near-term hardware](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09761)
*Akshaya Ajith,Jaehyung Lee,Charles Rhys Campbell,Kamal Choudhary*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出SlaKoNet-VQD工作流，将基于深度学习和Slater-Koster紧束缚框架训练的通用神经网络哈密顿量生成器（SlaKoNet）与变分量子本征值求解器（VQD）相结合，实现了从晶体结构到能带计算的端到端量子计算流程，在硅和五种常规超导体上表现出与精确对角化接近的精度，并在IBM量子硬件上完成了铝的基态计算，进一步拓展至关联Hubbard模型和动力学平均场理论（DMFT）求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分量子算法（如VQE、VQD）在近期待计算的电子结构研究中具有潜力，但对于周期性固体，其应用受限于构建精确二次量子化哈密顿量的高成本（通常依赖DFT加Wannier化或手动拟合紧束缚参数）。现有方法无法实现高通量、结构无关的哈密顿量生成，制约了量子算法在凝聚态材料中的规模化应用。

Method: 该方法将基于深度学习的Slater-Koster紧束缚参数化模型（SlaKoNet，覆盖65种元素）与基于Qiskit的VQD算法耦合。SlaKoNet模型在JARVIS-TBmBJ数据集上训练，作为通用神经哈密顿量生成器替代传统昂贵的哈密顿量构建过程。该工作流（SlaKoNet-VQD）具有结构无关性和可微性，并进一步将哈密顿量提升至关联Hubbard模型，通过动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）求解。

Result: 在硅的基准测试中，沿标准k路径恢复全部八条能带，与3量子比特模拟器上的精确对角化相比，平均绝对偏差（mean absolute deviation, MAD）为1.78 meV。在五种常规超导体（Al, Ta, Nb, V, ZrN）上获得类似精度。在IBM量子硬件上完成铝的k点基态计算，平均绝对误差（MAE）约为0.37 eV。DMFT扩展分析显示第5族金属中关联效应减弱，以及La2CuO4中的强准粒子重整化。

Conclusion: 该工作流实现了跨元素周期表的高通量变分量子算法（VQA）基准测试，并为基于梯度的哈密顿量-拟设协同优化（ansatz-Hamiltonian co-optimization）开辟了途径，可用于材料发现。该研究还将关联材料的杂质问题（impurity problem）识别为自然的量子求解器目标，为量子计算在凝聚态物理中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Variational quantum algorithms such as VQE and VQD are promising for near-term electronic structure calculations, but for periodic solids their reach is limited by the cost of building a faithful second-quantized Hamiltonian, typically via DFT plus Wannierization or hand-fit tight-binding parameters. SlaKoNet addresses this by combining deep learning with the Slater-Koster tight-binding formalism to fit hopping and overlap parameters across 65 elements, enabling deterministic Hamiltonian construction for any crystal built from these elements. Here we couple a SlaKoNet model trained on JARVIS-TBmBJ with a Qiskit-based VQD algorithm, replacing costly Hamiltonian construction with a universal neural Hamiltonian generator. The resulting SlaKoNet-VQD workflow is structure-agnostic, differentiable, and suited to high-throughput bandstructure screening. We benchmark on silicon, recovering the full eight-band structure along the standard k-path with mean absolute deviation of 1.78 meV from exact diagonalization on a 3-qubit simulator, and extend to five conventional superconductors (Al, Ta, Nb, V, ZrN) with similar accuracy. We demonstrate execution on IBM Quantum hardware for a k-point ground-state calculation on aluminum (MAE ~0.37 eV). We further promote the Hamiltonian to a correlated Hubbard model solved via dynamical mean-field theory, recovering weakening correlations across group-5 metals and strong quasiparticle renormalization in La2CuO4, identifying the impurity problem as a natural quantum solver target. This pipeline enables high-throughput VQA benchmarking across the periodic table and gradient-based ansatz-Hamiltonian co-optimization for materials discovery. Web app: https://atomgpt.org/quantum.

</details>


### [63] [Approximate explicit formulas for Stoner-Wohlfarth hysteresis loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09881)
*Savin Vladimir P.,Koksharov Yury A*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文推导了Stoner-Wohlfarth模型中磁滞回线的近似显式公式，涵盖单颗粒与随机取向颗粒系综两种情况，并通过分段函数匹配实现了高精度近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stoner-Wohlfarth模型是描述单畴颗粒磁滞行为的经典模型，但缺乏简洁的解析表达式。本文旨在推导实用的近似显式公式，以便更便捷地预测磁滞回线形状。

Method: 基于物理假设：低场时磁矩靠近易轴（easy axis）方向，高场时靠近外场方向。通过对不同磁场区间定义的分段函数进行适当匹配（matching），构造出通用分段公式以最大化精度。

Result: 低场近似公式在约化磁场h0不很小时（甚至接近Stoner-Wohlfarth小行星体区域）仍近似有效。对系综平均磁滞回线，公式与数值计算结果的最大偏差出现在h0 = 0.5处，对应磁化斜率急剧变化的区域，且偏差合理可控。

Conclusion: 所提出的分段近似公式能够在关键参数区间以有限的精度损失替代数值计算，为Stoner-Wohlfarth模型磁滞回线的解析分析提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Approximate explicit formulas for the hysteresis loops in the Stoner-Wohlfarth model are derived. We consider the hysteresis loops both for a single particle with a fixed easy-axis direction and for an ensemble of particles with randomly oriented anisotropy axes. The physical assumption used to derive the formulas is that the particle magnetic moment lies in the vicinity of the easy axis or the external field direction, at low and high fields, respectively. Surprisingly, the low-field formula is approximately valid even near the Stoner-Wohlfarth astroid, where the reduced magnetic field h0 is not very small. The general piecewise formula is obtained by an appropriate matching of the functions defined on different intervals of the magnetic field, which are chosen to maximize the formula accuracy. For the averaged hysteresis loop, the maximal, but reasonably small, deviation of our formula from numerically calculated magnetization occurs at h0 = 0.5, which corresponds to the sharp change in magnetization slope.

</details>


### [64] [Bragg Interferometry of Moiré Superlattices: From Geometric Phase Principles to Atomic Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09901)
*Isaac M. Craig,D. Kwabena Bediako*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了用于表征莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中亚埃级原子重构的多种电子显微镜和X射线光谱技术，重点讨论了暗场中布拉格反射干涉的几何相位提取方法，并通过扭曲双层和三层石墨烯以及过渡金属二硫属化物（transition metal dichalcogenide）等案例展示了布拉格干涉测量法（Bragg interferometry）在测量层间位移场和应变方面的优势与挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭曲和堆叠二维材料形成的莫尔超晶格产生了亚埃级原子重构的成像需求，但现有的表征技术难以在微米级视场范围内实现高精度结构映射，因此需要系统性地梳理和发展能够提取几何相位（geometric phase）的测量方法。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，系统调研了电子显微镜和X射线光谱中提取几何相位的多种技术路线，包括几何相位分析（geometric phase analysis）、会聚束电子衍射全息术（converged beam electron diffraction holography）以及多种叠层衍射成像范式（ptychographic paradigms），并重点比较了暗场布拉格干涉测量法的原理与应用。

Result: 通过扭曲双层和三层石墨烯以及过渡金属二硫属化物莫尔系统的案例研究，展示了布拉格干涉测量法在测量层间位移场（interlayer displacement fields）和应变（strain）方面的实用性，尤其适用于探测埋藏界面和封装异质结构（encapsulated heterostructures）。同时指出了在动力学散射（dynamical scattering）存在时解释不完整相位信息的固有困难。

Conclusion: 本文通过审视各方法的物理原理，揭示了高分辨率结构映射技术中的概念相似性和实际权衡；强调结构弛豫与电子行为之间的相互作用构成了现代凝聚态物理、纳米材料工程和界面化学交叉领域的前沿科学问题。

Abstract: The emergence of moiré superlattices formed by twisting and stacking two-dimensional materials has created a need for characterization techniques capable of mapping sub-angstrom atomic reconstruction across micron-scale fields of view. This review surveys a suite of methodologies developed to extract geometric phases in electron microscopy and X-ray spectroscopy, with a primary focus on the interference of overlapping Bragg reflections in the dark field. We provide a comparative analysis of some established techniques, including geometric phase analysis, converged beam electron diffraction holography, and various ptychographic paradigms, culminating in a discussion of Bragg interferometry for measuring interlayer displacement fields and strain in moiré materials. We demonstrate the utility of Bragg interferometry through case studies of twisted bilayer and trilayer graphene as well as transition metal dichalcogenide moiré systems. Special attention is given to the unique advantages of this dark-field interferometric method for probing buried interfaces and encapsulated heterostructures, as well as the inherent challenges of interpreting incomplete phase information in the presence of dynamical scattering. By examining the physical principles underlying these approaches, this review highlights the conceptual similarities and practical trade-offs involved in high-resolution structural mapping of materials in which the interplay between structural relaxation and electronic behavior defines a scientific frontier at the nexus of modern condensed matter physics, nanomaterials engineering, and interfacial chemistry.

### [65] [The Precursor Genome: A Pairwise Reaction Dataset for Solid-State Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09903)
*Lauren N. Walters,Matthew J. McDermott,Bernardus Rendy,Yuxing Fei,Kristin A. Persson,Gerbrand Ceder*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Precursor Genome数据集，这是一个由A-Lab自主实验室自动生成的包含1,035个二元固态反应实验记录的数据集，涵盖了完整的实验元数据、X射线衍射（XRD）分析结果以及人工验证的物相鉴定，为固态反应性的预测模型训练与评估提供了符合FAIR原则的可复用基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态反应（solid-state reactions）仍是合成无机材料的主要途径，但当前缺乏大规模、机器可读且具有一致来源溯源的实验数据集，这阻碍了第一性原理（first-principles）、数据驱动（data-driven）和机器学习（machine-learning）方法在合成科学中的应用。

Method: 利用A-Lab自驱动实验室（self-driving laboratory）自主生成1,035个二元固态反应数据；所有产物混合物均通过Dara框架进行自动化Rietveld精修（Rietveld refinement），从原始X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction, 1,351次扫描）中鉴定物相；精修结果（共1,950个案例）由人类专家按三级质量标尺独立验证；数据通过Pydantic验证的JSON账本（Pydantic-validated JSON ledger）分发，保留从前驱体对到最终物相分配的完整可追溯性（traceability）。

Result: 构建了Precursor Genome数据集，涵盖46种前驱体（precursors）和39种元素，记录了所有反应的完整实验元数据，包括热分布曲线（thermal profiles）、前驱体与回收质量及仪器配置；产物鉴定经过自动化精修与人工验证双重质量控制。

Conclusion: Precursor Genome建立了一个符合FAIR原则的可复用基准（benchmark），用于训练和评估固态反应性（solid-state reactivity）的预测模型。

Abstract: Solid-state reactions remain the dominant route to inorganic materials, yet no large, machine-readable dataset reports their experimental protocols and outcomes with consistent provenance; this gap obstructs first-principles, data-driven, and machine-learning approaches to synthesis science. Here, we present the Precursor Genome, a dataset of 1,035 pairwise solid-state reactions generated autonomously by the A-Lab self-driving laboratory, spanning 46 precursors and 39 elements. Every reaction is reported together with its full experimental metadata, including measured thermal profiles, precursor and recovered masses, and instrument configuration. Every product mixture is identified from raw X-ray diffraction (1,351 scans) through automated Rietveld refinement with the Dara framework, yielding 1,950 refinement cases that are independently validated by human experts on a three-tier quality scale. Raw pattern files, serialized refinement objects, and reviewer annotations are distributed through a Pydantic-validated JSON ledger, preserving full traceability from each precursor pair to its final phase assignment. The Precursor Genome establishes a FAIR, reusable benchmark for training and evaluating predictive models of solid-state reactivity.

</details>


### [66] [Auditing Machine-Learning Models and Their Training Data with Explainability and First-Principles Verification: Application to Spin Hall Conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09910)
*Mohammed Mahshook,Rudra Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种模型无关的审计协议，结合SHAP归因、反事实偏依赖分析和Rashomon式跨模型验证，并辅以目标密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，用于检验材料属性机器学习模型的两大隐含假设：特征是否反映真实物理机制，以及训练标签是否正确。在自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity）任务上的实验表明，该协议能以少量DFT计算为代价，揭示模型特征中的虚假相关性（如平均p价电子描述符与Pt含量的统计纠缠）和训练标签中的显著错误（如HfC标签的30倍误差）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料属性的机器学习模型依赖两个标准验证从未检验的隐含假设：一是模型的特征（features）反映的是属性的物理机制而非训练分布中的偶然因素，二是训练标签（training labels）本身是正确的。然而现有验证方法无法系统检测这两类问题，因此需要一种通用的审计协议来识别模型中的虚假相关性和数据中的标签错误。

Method: 该方法是一个模型无关的审计协议，结合了SHAP归因（SHAP attribution）、反事实偏依赖分析（counterfactual partial dependence analysis）和Rashomon式跨模型验证（Rashomon-style cross-model verification），所有发现均经由目标密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算裁决。在自旋霍尔电导率（intrinsic spin Hall conductivity）任务上，使用仅基于成分（composition-only）的随机森林（Random Forest）模型，无需弛豫晶体结构。

Result: 审计发现：平均p价电子描述符（average p-valence descriptor）与Pt含量产生统计纠缠，这是学习表征（learned representation）的属性而非物理机制；DFT验证表明，无Pt化合物HgOsPb₂的真实自旋霍尔电导率（SHC）几乎是模型预测值的四倍。数据审计发现HfC训练标签存在30倍误差，该误差不可检测地继承到所有基于相同数据训练的黑箱模型（black-box model）中。

Conclusion: 所提出的审计协议能够以少量DFT计算的成本，对一个材料属性机器学习模型及其训练数据进行系统检验。该协议适用于任何由一个元素主导高属性值区间（high-property regime）的场景，有效识别特征表征中的统计伪影和训练数据中的标签错误。

Abstract: Machine-learning models for materials properties rest on two assumptions that standard validation never tests: that a model's features reflect the physics of the property rather than accidents of the training distribution, and that the training labels are themselves correct. We introduce a model-agnostic audit protocol for both, combining SHAP attribution, counterfactual partial dependence analysis, and Rashomon-style cross-model verification, with every finding adjudicated by targeted density functional theory (DFT). Demonstrated on intrinsic spin Hall conductivity using a composition-only Random Forest, the model needs no relaxed crystal structure, reaching accuracy competitive with structure-aware graph networks while remaining applicable to the far larger space of compositions for which no structure has been computed. The model audit reveals that the average p-valence descriptor becomes statistically entangled with Pt content - a property of the learned representation rather than the physics; DFT confirms the consequence, a Pt-free compound (HgOsPb$_2$) whose true SHC is nearly four times the prediction. The data audit exposes a thirtyfold error in the HfC training label, inherited undetectably by every black-box model trained on the same data. The protocol audits a model and its training data for the cost of a few DFT calculations, wherever one element dominates the high-property regime.

</details>

### [69] [Anisotropic representations for E(3)-equivariant machine learning coarse-grained potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10002)

Method: 将原子核的点粒子表示扩展为质量椭球珠子（massive ellipsoidal beads），引入取向依赖特征；采用等变消息传递神经网络（equivariant message-passing neural network）学习各向异性CG势，直接从原子级数据拟合能量、力和力矩。

Abstract: Coarse-graining (CG) lowers the computational cost of atomistic simulations by representing groups of atoms as effective interaction sites, reducing the degrees of freedom of the system but often compromising structural fidelity or requiring system-specific parameterization. Here, we introduce a novel anisotropic machine learning CG potential that extends the point particle representation of atomic nuclei to massive ellipsoidal beads with orientation-dependent features, enabling the learning of energies, forces, and torques directly from atomistic data. The anisotropic representation is physically motivated for polar and asymmetric molecules, where directional interactions and shape anisotropy play important roles in determining structure and dynamics. Using an equivariant message-passing neural network, the model accurately reproduces radial and angular distribution functions as well as relative orientation correlations in liquid water, demonstrating that both translational and rotational dynamics are well captured. Comparison with an isotropic baseline reveals that the lack of orientation information leads to systematic errors in short and long range order and degradation of angular correlations, proving orientation features are essential for accurate coarse-graining. The anisotropic model also exposes rotational structural observables fundamentally inaccessible to isotropic representations, with minimal computational overhead. Even for coarse-graining just three degrees of freedom, CG simulations achieve 7-27$\times$ speedups while preserving structural fidelity, highlighting the efficiency gains of this systemic reduction. This framework establishes the feasibility and necessity of learned equivariant representations for anisotropic CG modeling and provides a path towards accurate and efficient mesoscopic simulations of complex molecular liquids, polymers, and biomolecular systems.

Furthermore, the energy dispersion of the electride bands remains insensitive to the choice of exchange-correlation functional (LDA vs.~PBEsol), indicating that local exchange and correlation effects have minimal influence on the IAEs.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Two-dimensional magnetic materials offer unique opportunities for exploring low-dimensional spin phenomena and next-generation spintronic devices. In this work, we present a density functional theory study of CrX3 compounds and their ternary alloys. Our results show that for the pure compounds, the ground state is ferromagnetic (FM), with the antiferromagnetic-zigzag (AFM-Z) and paramagnetic (PM) phases being close in energy. For these pure systems, the band gap variation among different magnetic phases does not exceed 0.16 eV, and the average magnetic moments on Cr atoms increase from Cl to Br to I. For the alloys, the FM state remains the lowest-energy configuration, but the energy difference towards the AFM-Z phase decreases for compounds with lower iodine concentration. *Paula Mellado,Hanu Arava*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从底层图的邻接谱构建一系列非齐次转移矩阵，利用Husimi树（Husimi tree）表示有限系统，并使用由局域玻尔兹曼因子（local Boltzmann factors）构建的转移概率来建模。

Result: 该框架预测了双峰动力学行为（bimodal kinetic behavior），即长时俘获（trapping）与突然雪崩式弛豫交替出现；低至四十代Husimi树的低温数据坍塌为一条符合幂律标度形式的曲线，表明边界截断即可产生标度不变的磁通阻塞。

Conclusion: 该框架将平衡态能量景观概念与非平衡现象（如动力学阻塞（kinetic arrest）和电报噪声（telegraph noise））联系起来，为实现有限阻挫网络中输运的间歇性预测与设计提供了工具。

Abstract: We present a quantitative framework for predicting how kinetic barriers governing temperature dependent relaxation arise in finite square magnetic networks. By formulating a series of non homogeneous transfer matrices from the adjacency spectrum of the underlying graph, we show how local coordination shapes the energy landscape and identifies geometric regions that act as bottlenecks for flux transport. Our approach predicts bimodal kinetic behavior, in which long intervals of trapping within charge compensated manifolds are interrupted by sudden, avalanche like relaxation episodes. Representing finite systems with a Husimi tree, we find that low temperature data from forty generations collapse onto a single curve consistent with a power law scaling form, implying that boundary truncation alone can give rise to scale invariant flux arrest, analogous to athermal granular jamming. By employing transition probabilities constructed from local Boltzmann factors, this framework connects equilibrium energy landscape concepts to non equilibrium phenomena, including kinetic arrest and telegraph noise, thereby enabling the prediction and design of intermittent transport in finite, frustrated networks.

### [73] [Engineering Topology by Design in Two-dimensional Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10049)
*Arjyama Bordoloi,Sobhit Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过范德华（van der Waals, vdW）异质结构工程，利用界面耦合（interfacial coupling）而非仅仅依赖本征材料属性来产生非平庸能带拓扑（nontrivial band topology）。该方法引入多种可调自由度，包括堆叠构型（stacking configuration）、扭转角（twist angle）和化学功能化（chemical functionalization），并辅以电场、应变和光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）等外部刺激实现动态且可逆的拓扑特性调控。

Result: 该方法结合范德华界面工程与外部调制，使得即使在原本拓扑平庸的系统中也能实现二维拓扑绝缘体（2D TI）相，从而大幅扩展了可用的材料体系。

Abstract: Two-dimensional topological insulators (2D TIs) have emerged as a cornerstone of next-generation spintronic technologies due to their robust, dissipationless edge states protected by time-reversal symmetry. Initial realizations of 2D TIs have primarily focused on materials with strong intrinsic spin-orbit coupling capable of driving band inversion, an approach that significantly constrains the accessible materials landscape. More recently, a paradigm shift has occurred toward engineering topological phases in van der Waals (vdW) heterostructures, where nontrivial band topology can arise from interfacial coupling rather than relying solely on intrinsic material properties. This framework provides an exceptionally versatile platform with multiple tunable degrees of freedom, including stacking configuration, twist angle, and chemical functionalization, allowing systematic manipulation of the band topology. Furthermore, external stimuli, such as electric fields, strain, and light-matter coupling, enable dynamic and reversible control of the topological character. The combined use of vdW interface engineering and external modulation allows the realization of 2D TI phases even in otherwise topologically trivial systems, substantially expanding the accessible materials landscape. This Research Update reviews key milestones in the development of vdW-engineered 2D topological quantum materials, critically assesses outstanding theoretical and experimental challenges, and outlines promising directions for future breakthroughs.

### [74] [Polarization Rotation Drives a Spin-Topological Transition in Ferroelectric Bismuth Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10063)
*Jinming Zhai,Lingzhi Cao,Yateng Wang,Huicong Li,Zhilong Yang,Yali Yang,Jiangang He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过第一性原理晶格动力学和对称性适配模式分析，发现铋单层（bismuth monolayer）中存在一种被忽视的面内极化旋转（rotational pathway）开关机制，其能垒比直接反转低四倍以上，且该旋转可驱动自旋拓扑转变（spin-topological transition），使自旋陈数（spin Chern number）从-2变为0。单轴应变可进一步调控极化取向与拓扑转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现面内极化旋转路径的能垒比直接反转低四倍以上，可自然解释分子动力学模拟中观察到的涡旋状畴结构（vortexlike domain textures）。极化旋转还会驱动自旋拓扑转变，自旋陈数从-2变为0。定向单轴应变可进一步调控极化取向并调节拓扑转变。

Conclusion: 极化旋转（polarization rotation）被确立为铁电铋单层的开关机制，并可作为二维铁电体中电学与力学可编程拓扑（electrically and mechanically programmable topology）的高效路径。

Abstract: Bismuth monolayer is the first two-dimensional elemental ferroelectric and an appealing platform for coupling polar order to spin-orbit-driven topology. However, its microscopic switching mechanism remains elusive. Here, using first-principles lattice dynamics and symmetry-adapted mode analysis, we identify a previously overlooked rotational pathway for in-plane polarization switching. Its energy barrier is more than four times lower than that of direct reversal, naturally explaining the vortexlike domain textures observed in molecular dynamics simulations. Remarkably, this polarization rotation also drives a spin-topological transition, changing the spin Chern number from $C_s=-2$ to $0$. Directional uniaxial strain further steers the polarization orientation and tunes the associated topological transition. These results establish polarization rotation as the switching mechanism of ferroelectric Bi monolayer and as an efficient route to electrically and mechanically programmable topology in two-dimensional ferroelectrics.

### [75] [Dynamical Nonrelativistic Spin Splitting via THz Nonlinear Phononics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10091)
*Linding Yuan,ChanJu You,Ankit Disa,James M. Rondinelli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文结合第一性原理计算（DFT）与非线性声子学（nonlinear phononics），证明太赫兹（THz）激光脉冲可在共线反铁磁体（collinear antiferromagnets）中实现非相对论自旋劈裂（NRSS）的超快、可逆控制，并提出了识别可激活或放大NRSS的拉曼活性声子模式的两个对称性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（DFT）与非线性声子学方法；推导出两个对称性判据，分别考虑声子与磁波矢的兼容性以及序参量宇称（order-parameter parity），用于筛选能够激活或放大NRSS的拉曼活性（Raman-active）声子模式。

Result: 在NiO中，共振驱动11.08 THz红外活性模式可通过双二次非谐耦合（biquadratic anharmonic coupling）将自旋简并的NiO瞬态转变为NRSS态，产生约40 meV的时间平均自旋劈裂；在LaFeO₃中，选择性激发可使已有的NRSS放大约100%。两种材料中诱导的自旋劈裂均伴随瞬态的自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）诱导净磁矩，可通过磁光克尔效应（magneto-optical Kerr effect）探测。

Conclusion: 该框架确立了非线性声子学作为超快调控自旋劈裂反铁磁相的一般性路径，其效果远超静态应变所能达到的范围。

Abstract: Nonrelativistic spin splitting (NRSS) in collinear antiferromagnets offers a route to high-frequency spintronics immune to stray fields, but its dynamic control has remained elusive. We demonstrate, using density functional theory (DFT) and nonlinear phononics, that THz laser pulses can achieve ultrafast, reversible control of NRSS on picosecond timescales in antiferromagnets. We derive two symmetry criteria, accounting for phonon and magnetic wavevector compatibility and order-parameter parity, to identify which Raman-active phonon modes can activate or amplify NRSS. In LaFeO$_3$, selective excitation amplifies the existing NRSS by about 100%. In both cases, the induced spin splitting is accompanied by a transient SOC-induced net moment detectable via the magneto-optical Kerr effect. This framework establishes nonlinear phononics as a general route for ultrafast manipulation of spin-split antiferromagnetic phases well beyond the reach of static strain.

### [76] [Correlated Plasmonic Excitation in Twisted Nematic Plasmonic Superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10122)
*Rui Huang,Jordan Austin-Frank Wilson,Anders Dollard,Nicholas C Fisher,Zixian Fang,John T. Fourkas,Zhiwei Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种可重构扭曲等离激元超晶格（twisted plasmonic superlattice）中，向列型等离激元超结构的集体偏振效应与单个纳米棒等离激元激发之间的关联光-物质相互作用。通过垂直堆叠组装混合Fe3O4和Au纳米棒构建的等离激元向列型液晶，实现了依赖扭转角度的等离激元激发增强，并利用磁取向控制实现了可编码的向列畴和等离激元图案，从而构建出具有可定义域颜色、特征尺寸、周期性和对称性的可重构光子摩尔超晶格（photonic moire superlattice）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有扭曲构型的超晶格（如摩尔晶格（moire lattice））因其独特的电子、磁性和光学性质而受到广泛关注。纳米尺度扭曲超晶格的一个显著特征是其独特的晶格对称性以及周期相与非周期相之间的连续相变，这为研究许多新兴物理现象提供了独特机遇。本研究旨在探索可重构扭曲等离激元超晶格中，集体偏振效应与单个纳米棒等离激元激发之间的关联光-物质相互作用。

Method: 以混合Fe3O4和Au纳米棒为构建单元，组装了具有单向排列纳米棒的等离激元向列型液晶（plasmonic nematic liquid crystal），随后通过垂直堆叠组装方法进一步组装成摩尔等离激元晶格（moire plasmonic lattice）。利用磁取向控制（magnetic orientation control）实现混合Fe3O4和Au纳米棒在聚合物基底中的精确排列，并在每个子晶格中编码向列畴（nematic domain）和等离激元图案（plasmonic pattern）。

Result: 在双层等离激元超晶格的扭曲结构中识别出依赖扭转角度的等离激元激发（twist angle dependent plasmonic excitation），具体表现为：在0°扭转角处横向等离激元激发增强，在90°扭转角处纵向等离激元激发增强。这种关联等离激元激发由液晶相的集体偏振效应与单个纳米棒各向异性等离激元激发之间的相关性诱导产生。

Conclusion: 关联等离激元激发和光偏振效应能够构建可重构的光子摩尔超晶格，其特征包括定义明确的域颜色、特征尺寸、周期性、对称性和维度，这些特征由扭曲等离激元晶格中的扭转角度和位移决定。该工作为利用扭曲等离激元超结构实现可调控光-物质相互作用提供了新途径。

Abstract: Superlattices with twisted configurations, such as moire lattices, have recently been extensively exploited for their unique electronic, magnetic, and optical properties. One remarkable feature of nanoscale twisted superlattices is the distinct lattice symmetries and the continuous phase transitions between periodic or aperiodic phases, representing a unique opportunity to study many emerging physical phenomena. Here, we report a correlated light and matter interaction between the collective polarization effect of nematic plasmonic superstructures and the plasmonic excitation of individual constituent nanorods in reconfigurable twisted plasmonic superlattices. Using hybrid Fe3O4 and Au nanorods as building blocks, we assembled plasmonic nematic liquid crystals with unidirectionally aligned nanorods, which could be further assembled into moire plasmonic lattices through a vertical stacking assembly method. A twist angle dependent plasmonic excitation is recognized in the twisted bilayer of two plasmonic superlattices, featuring enhanced transverse and longitudinal plasmonic excitation at a twisting angle of 0 degree and 90 degree, respectively. Such correlated plasmonic excitation in twisted plasmonic superstructures is induced by the correlation between the collective polarization effect of the liquid crystal phases and the anisotropic plasmonic excitation of individual nanorods. The magnetic orientation control allows for precise alignment of hybrid Fe3O4 and Au nanorods in polymer substrates and enables the coding of nematic domains and plasmonic patterns in each sublattice. The correlated plasmonic excitation and light polarization create reconfigurable photonic moire superlattices with well-defined domain colors, feature sizes, periodicities, symmetries, and dimensions determined by twist angles and displacements in the twisted plasmonic lattices.

### [77] [Chiral charge density waves in transition metal dichalcogenide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10182)
*Ettore Carpene*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算（density functional theory, DFT）和对称性分析，论证了1T-TiSe₂电荷密度波（CDW）中手性的起源并非源于电荷密度分量间的相对相位移动，而是源于一种近简并的亚稳态CDW相堆叠序（monoclinic stacking order），并揭示了CDW的双重物理本质及圆偏振光（circularly polarized light）诱导手性畴（chiral domain）简并破缺的耦合机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1T-TiSe₂的CDW相中涌现的手性（chirality）实验上已被广泛观测，但其微观起源存在争议。主流解释将其归因于电荷密度分量间的相对相位移动（phase shift），但这一假说缺乏严格的能量评估与对称性验证。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）进行第一性原理总能计算，并结合晶体对称性分析（symmetry analysis），评估不同CDW堆叠构型的能量稳定性与对称性破缺特征。

Result: 发现相移态（phase-shifted states）具有过高的形成能（prohibitive energy costs），无法成为基态。取而代之，识别出一种近简并的亚稳态CDW相堆叠序，其具有单斜（monoclinic）对称性，能够天然破缺镜面（mirror）和反演（inversion）对称性。CDW展现出双重物理本质：电子电荷重分布为键调制（bond-modulated）型，而周期性晶格畸变为原子中心横波（atom-centered transverse）型。基于这一空间分离，圆偏振光可以打破手性畴之间的能量简并。

Conclusion: 实验结果中局域探针观测到的“自发”手性，实际上是CDW相堆叠畴（phase stacking domains）的统计分布；而宏观尺度的光致旋光（gyrotropic）有序则源于圆偏振光驱动的简并破缺机制。该结论调和了此前相互矛盾的实验观测。

Abstract: The emergence of chirality in the charge density wave (CDW) phase of 1$T$-TiSe$_2$ has recently attracted significant attention, yet its microscopic origin remains debated. The prevailing interpretation attributes chirality to a relative phase shift between the charge density components. Here, using density functional theory and symmetry analysis, it is demonstrated that such phase-shifted states entail prohibitive energy costs, rendering them unlikely candidates for the ground state. Instead, a nearly degenerate metastable CDW phase stacking order with monoclinic symmetry is identified, that naturally breaks mirror and inversion symmetries. The CDW in 1$T$-TiSe$_2$ possesses a dual physical nature: the electronic charge redistribution is intrinsically bond-modulated, while the periodic lattice distortion is atom-centered transverse. This spatial separation allows a specific optical coupling mechanism where circularly polarized light breaks the energetic degeneracy between chiral domains. These results reconcile conflicting experimental observations, identifying the "spontaneous" chirality observed in local probes as a statistical distribution of CDW phase stacking domains, while establishing the mechanism for macroscopic, light-induced gyrotropic order.
