### [78] [Self-Consistent Phonon Spectral Functions and Thermal Transport Beyond the Quasiparticle Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10211)
*Yi Xia*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自洽谱函数（self-consistent spectral function）框架，通过将每个声子（phonon）表示为完整的频率分布而非锐利定义的频率，并以此修饰三声子气泡自能（three-phonon bubble self-energy）的内线，从而在无需人工展宽参数且超越准粒子近似（quasiparticle approximation）的情况下，自洽地确定自能的实部与虚部。应用于闪锌矿 HgTe 时，该框架显著拓宽声子谱、激活单次准粒子计算无法访问的散射通道，并将晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity）降低约五倍至实验量级，同时再现其温度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于第一性原理的声子线宽计算通常假设声子准粒子具有锐利定义的频率，这忽略了声子频散的非洛伦兹展宽效应，并依赖外部引入的展宽参数来强制能量守恒，限制了晶格动力学与热输运计算在准粒子近似失效情形下的适用性。

Method: 提出自洽谱函数框架，将每个声子由其完整的频率分布（谱函数）表示，并利用所得谱函数修饰三声子气泡自能的内线；在迭代过程中自洽地求解自能的实部与虚部，无需外部选择的展宽参数，从而将晶格动力学与热输运计算拓展至准粒子近似（quasiparticle approximation）之外。

Result: 应用于闪锌矿 HgTe 时，自洽性显著展宽了声学与光学声子谱，激活了单次准粒子计算中无法访问的散射通道；晶格热导率降低约五倍，达到实验量级且再现其温度依赖性；模式分辨的谱函数（mode-resolved spectral function）与直接分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟的功率谱一致。

Conclusion: 自洽谱函数框架在准粒子微扰论（quasiparticle perturbation theory）与全动力学模拟之间建立了实用的桥梁，并且该框架可推广至更高阶的非简谐过程。

Abstract: Anharmonic lattice dynamics shapes phonon spectra and thermal transport, yet first-principles linewidth calculations typically assume phonon quasiparticles with sharply defined frequencies. Here, we introduce a self-consistent spectral function framework that represents each phonon by its full frequency distribution and uses the resulting spectra to dress the internal lines of the three-phonon bubble self-energy. The method self-consistently determines the real and imaginary parts of the self-energy on equal footing, eliminates externally chosen smearing parameter for enforcing energy conservation, and extends lattice dynamics and thermal transport calculations beyond the quasiparticle approximation. Applied to zincblende HgTe, self-consistency substantially broadens acoustic and optical phonon spectra, activates scattering channels inaccessible in the one-shot quasiparticle calculation, and reduces the lattice thermal conductivity by approximately a factor of five to the experimental scale while reproducing its temperature dependence, without explicitly invoking higher-order interactions. Mode-resolved spectral functions are further validated against the power spectra from direct molecular dynamics simulations. These results establish self-consistent spectral functions as a practical bridge between quasiparticle perturbation theory and fully dynamical simulations, and provide a framework readily generalizable to higher-order anharmonic processes.

</details>

Conclusion: 层状“314”结构的稳定化由氧空位的存在和有序化驱动，而非A位阳离子有序化；缺氧氧化后的化合物代表完全化学计量比相之前的一个中间正交态。磁性与输运性质的演化可用Co的自旋态（spin state）变化、氧摄取导致的Co $3d$–O $2p$ 轨道重叠增强，以及由残余氧空位和混合 $\mathrm{Co}^{3+}/\mathrm{Co}^{4+}$ 价态引起的磁不均匀铁磁态来解释。

High-resolution neutron powder diffraction combined with synchrotron x-ray powder diffraction reveals that increasing the oxygen content induces a structural transition from a layered $I4/mmm$ ($2a_p \times 2a_p \times 4a_p$) to an oxygen-deficient orthorhombic $Pmmm$ ($a_p \times a_p \times 2a_p$) phases with preferential oxygen-vacancy occupation. This transition is accompanied by a crossover from G-type antiferromagnetic with a weak ferromagnetic component to a ferromagnetic state, and a drastic decay in resistivity. The evolution of the magnetic and transport properties is discussed in terms of changes in the Co spin state, enhanced Co $3d$ - O $2p$ orbital overlap upon oxygen uptake, and a magnetically inhomogeneous ferromagnetic state associated with residual oxygen vacancies and mixed $\mathrm{Co}^{3+}/\mathrm{Co}^{4+}$ valence. Our findings experimentally confirm that the stabilization of the layered "314" structure is driven by the presence and ordering of oxygen vacancies rather than A-site cation ordering, whereas the oxygen-deficient oxidized compounds represent an intermediate orthorhombic state preceding fully stoichiometric phases.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PdCoO₂作为一种具有超高电导率的层状氧化物金属，其优异导电性源于Pd衍生的近自由电子带（nearly-free-electron band）。理解其在高压下的结构、成键与电子性质演化，有助于揭示该材料异常压缩行为的根源及其高导电性的稳健性。

Method: 采用高压单晶X射线衍射（high-pressure single-crystal X-ray diffraction）结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），在0–10 GPa压力范围内研究了PdCoO₂的结构、成键与电子演化。利用晶体轨道哈密顿布居分析（Crystal Orbital Hamilton Population, COHP）评估键合强度变化，并通过玻尔兹曼输运计算（Boltzmann transport calculations）分析电导率行为。

Result: PdCoO₂在整个压力范围内保持菱方R-3m结构，无结构相变。晶格表现出异常的各向异性压缩：面内a轴收缩幅度大于面外c轴，与多数层状材料相反。尽管压缩行为反常，Pd-O和Co-O局域配位环境变化很小，表明成键框架高度刚性。COHP分析显示仅存在轻微的键合增强，未出现不利的Pd相关反键态（antibonding states）。Pd衍生的金属性带和准二维费米面（quasi-two-dimensional Fermi surface）基本不变。面内电导率几乎与压力无关，面外电导率略有下降，导致输运各向异性（transport anisotropy）轻微增大。

Conclusion: PdCoO₂的异常压缩性源于其稳健的化学键网络（robust chemical bonding network），该网络在压力下同时保持了晶体结构和高度导电的Pd衍生物态，从而解释了该材料在高压下导电性的稳定性。

Abstract: The layered delafossite PdCoO$_2$ is an exceptional oxide metal whose ultrahigh conductivity arises from a Pd-derived nearly-free-electron band. Here, high-pressure single-crystal X-ray diffraction combined with first-principles calculations is used to investigate its structural, bonding, and electronic evolution up to 10 GPa. PdCoO$_2$ retains the rhombohedral R-3m structure throughout the investigated pressure range, with no structural phase transition. The lattice exhibits an unusual anisotropic compression, with the in-plane a-axis contracting more strongly than the stacking c-axis, opposite to the behavior of most layered materials. Despite this anomalous compressibility, only minor changes are observed in the local Pd-O and Co-O coordination environments, indicating a remarkably rigid bonding framework. Crystal orbital Hamilton population analysis reveals only subtle strengthening of the existing bonding interactions, without the emergence of destabilizing Pd-related antibonding states. Consistent with these findings, the Pd-derived metallic band and quasi-two-dimensional Fermi surface remain essentially unchanged under compression. Boltzmann transport calculations further show that the in-plane conductivity is nearly pressure-independent, whereas the out-of-plane conductivity decreases modestly, resulting in a slight increase in transport anisotropy. These results demonstrate that the anomalous compressibility of PdCoO$_2$ originates from its robust chemical bonding network, which preserves both the crystal structure and the highly conductive Pd-derived metallic state under pressure.

</details>


### [82] [Why Do Thick MOCVD-Grown beta-Ga2O3 Epilayers on (001) Substrates Crack: Crystallographic Origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10378)
*Martin Frentrup,Indraneel Sanyal,Dan Lamb,Ciaran P. Llewelyn,Jonathan Evans,Owen J. Guy,Mike Jennings,Saptarsi Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了MOCVD在（001）取向β-Ga2O3衬底上生长同质外延层的表面形貌、结构取向及裂纹形成机制，发现外延层呈现（-401）择优取向，由晶格失配引起的面内拉伸应变（理论最大值约+4.1%）驱动了裂纹沿垂直方向生成，并指出该外延关系与富氧条件下衬底表面因能量最小化驱动的重构有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在约3.5 μm/h的生长速率下，系统制备了厚度从0.3 μm到3.5 μm的β-Ga2O3外延层，采用高分辨X射线衍射（high resolution X-ray diffraction）、摇摆曲线（rocking curve）分析等手段对表面形貌、晶体取向和应变状态进行表征。

Conclusion: 该外延关系可能与退火过程中（001）衬底表面在富氧MOCVD生长条件下因表面能最小化驱动的面重构（faceted reconstruction）有关。

Abstract: Thick, defect free epitaxial layers grown using industry standard techniques are a fundamental requirement for the widespread adoption of fully vertical power devices based on ultra wide bandgap gallium oxide (Ga2O3). However, metal-organic chemical vapour deposition (MOCVD) of such layers on native beta-Ga2O3 substrates with the largest diameter (001) orientation remains relatively unexplored, and the origins of the reported surface roughening and cracking with increasing thickness are not yet fully understood. To address this, we report a systematic study of MOCVD grown beta-Ga2O3 epilayers deposited at growth rates of ~3.5 um/h, with thicknesses from 0.3 to 3.5 um. The epilayers exhibit a relatively smooth but striated surface morphology, with progressively increasing nanometre-scale roughness beyond coalescence and crack formation observed from ~1.8 um thickness. High resolution X ray diffraction reveals that, despite growth on (001) substrates, the epilayers adopt a predominantly (-401)-oriented structure from the earliest stages of growth. Rocking curve analysis further indicates a higher degree of in-plane twist than tilt, both decreasing with increasing epilayer thickness. While the epilayer and substrate are lattice-matched along the [010] in plane direction, the epitaxial alignment in the orthogonal epilayer [104] in plane direction imposes, in theory, a maximum tensile in-plane strain of approximately +4.1% arising from the underlying lattice mismatch, thereby driving crack formation perpendicular to this direction. Our results suggest that this epitaxial relationship is likely associated with faceted reconstruction of the (001) substrate surface during annealing, driven by the minimisation of surface energy under oxygen-rich MOCVD growth conditions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MOSAIC框架的核心步骤是：在倒易空间（reciprocal-space）中选择覆盖感兴趣散射特征的区域，对带有相位（phase-bearing）的散射振幅施加傅里叶滤波（Fourier filter），从而反演出实空间中负责这些特征的原子位移（atomic displacements）与位点占据（site occupancies）分布图。

Result: 该方法能够有效探查大尺度结构模型中原子间关联的性质与空间分布，适用于反向蒙特卡洛（Reverse Monte Carlo）精修、分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟、蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟所得构型，以及原子分辨率电子显微镜（atomic-resolution electron microscopy）图像导出的二维结构投影。

Conclusion: MOSAIC为从已获得的原子构型中解析局域结构关联的实空间起源提供了一种有效的计算工具，弥合了倒易空间散射特征与实空间原子排列之间的解释鸿沟。

Abstract: Local structural correlations are encoded in diffuse scattering, but identifying atomic motifs that produce specific diffuse features can be challenging. We introduce MOSAIC, a computational framework for this task when an atomistic configuration is available and a phase-bearing scattering amplitude can be calculated. Our approach relies on applying the Fourier filter to this amplitude over the reciprocal-space regions encompassing the scattering features of interest to obtain maps of atomic displacements and site occupancies responsible for those features. The method is effective in interrogating the nature and spatial distributions of interatomic correlations in large-scale structural models, such as obtained using Reverse Monte Carlo refinements from experimental data, molecular dynamics, or Monte Carlo simulations, or 2D structural projections derived from atomic-resolution electron microscopy images.

Abstract: Monolayer 1T'-WS2 is predicted to be a two-dimensional topological insulator, but its intrinsic electronic properties are masked by strong interlayer coupling in its metallic and superconducting bulk parent phase, 2M-WS2. Here we show that 2M-WS2 undergoes amine intercalation through a simple wet-chemical reaction, yielding superlattices in which the 1T' layers are structurally preserved but electronically decoupled by neutral molecular spacers. Chiral amine intercalation further induces chiroptical activity in WS2 electronic transitions. Overall, the successful intercalation challenges the long-held view that group VIB dichalcogenides are inert toward neutral-molecule intercalation and demonstrates molecular intercalation as a general chemical route for realizing monolayer-like topological-insulator physics and enabling chiral van der Waals superlattices in bulk single crystals.

Abstract: We study the response of axion topological materials under the presence of external static electric and magnetic fields. We focus on the macroscopic quasi-static magnetoelectric response of topological insulators. We use techniques based on surface variables that have been previously employed in soft condensed matter problems for the description of heterogeneous systems composed of multiple homogeneous materials. A complete description of the whole system is written in terms of surface degrees of freedom, which in this case correspond to effective surface charge and surface current densities. ### [87] [Nonlinear Tellegen limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10584)
*Abhinava Chatterjee,Nikhil Kalyanapuram*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了非线性磁电耦合会导致一种新型的Tellegen极限（非线性Tellegen极限），该极限可通过外加静电场或静磁场进行调控，并受磁点群对称性约束；逼近该极限时伴随场可调的Faraday旋转，其最大值由该极限设定。作者在d波交变磁体和M型六角铁氧体两种体系中演示了该极限与场空间稳定性相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性Tellegen极限（linear Tellegen limit）仅由材料参数固定，难以调控；本文旨在探索非线性磁电耦合（nonlinear magnetoelectric coupling）是否会产生新的、场可调的电磁稳定性边界，并揭示其与磁点群对称性（magnetic point group symmetry）的关联。

Method: 通过理论分析推导非线性磁电耦合下的Tellegen极限，结合磁点群对称性确定非线性磁电张量（nonlinear magnetoelectric tensor）的结构；在d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet）和M型六角铁氧体（M-type hexagonal ferrite）两种材料体系中构建场空间稳定性相图（field-space stability phase diagram）进行验证。

Result: 发现了非线性Tellegen极限（nonlinear Tellegen limit），该极限随外加静电场或静磁场变化，在材料特定的临界场下导致电磁不稳定性（electromagnetic instability）；逼近该极限时Faraday旋转（Faraday rotation）随外加场线性增长，其上限由非线性Tellegen极限决定；在两种磁有序材料体系中，磁点群对称性决定了非线性磁电张量的结构及电磁不稳定性的行为。

Conclusion: 非线性磁电耦合引入了一种场可调的新Tellegen极限，突破了线性Tellegen极限的固定性；该极限为磁电介质的电磁稳定性（electromagnetic stability bound）提供了新的普适边界，且磁点群对称性在其中起核心作用。

Abstract: The Tellegen limit is the fundamental electromagnetic stability bound on magnetoelectric media. We show that nonlinear magnetoelectric coupling gives rise to a new Tellegen limit, which we term the nonlinear Tellegen limit. Unlike the linear Tellegen limit, which is fixed by material parameters, the nonlinear Tellegen limit is field-tunable -- a static electric or magnetic field drives the system toward electromagnetic instability at a material-specific critical field determined by the magnetic point group symmetry. The approach to this limit is accompanied by a field-tunable Faraday rotation that grows linearly with the applied field and is bounded from above by a universal maximum set by the nonlinear Tellegen limit -- beyond which the medium becomes electromagnetically unstable. We demonstrate the nonlinear Tellegen limit and the field-space stability phase diagram in two magnetically ordered material systems -- a d-wave altermagnet and an M-type hexagonal ferrite -- showing that the symmetry of the magnetic point group governs both the structure of the nonlinear magnetoelectric tensor and the resulting electromagnetic instability.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尖晶石铁氧体在多个领域（如超级电容器、锂离子电池、水分解、化学传感器、生物医学等）具有广泛应用前景，但其在电化学应用中的设计原则和性能增强机制尚需系统梳理，以满足可持续世界中新兴功能应用的需求。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，梳理了通过形貌控制（morphology control）、引入碳基材料（carbon-based materials）、组成替代（compositional substitution）、掺杂（doping）以及形成组成体系（composition systems）等手段调控尖晶石铁氧体基电极材料的电化学性能，尤其关注纳米结构形式下的优化策略。

Result: 尖晶石铁氧体因其良好的化学稳定性、高比表面积以及多重氧化态（multiple oxidation states）带来的优异电化学行为，适合检测多种气态分析物（如挥发性有机化合物、重金属离子、生物分子和环境污染物），并在超级电容器中展现出高效储能能力。

Conclusion: 该综述为从事电化学器件（尤其是气体传感器和超级电容器）电极材料合成与性能增强技术的研究人员提供了综合性参考资源，有助于推动这些先进材料在新可持续发展方向下的应用。

Abstract: Spinel ferrites have shown wide range of applications in various fields, including supercapacitors, Li-ion batteries, water splitting, chemical sensors, catalytic activity, high-frequency magnetic devices, and biomedical, hyperthermia, drug delivery applications., etc. This review focuses on the latest progress and trends on design of spinel ferrites (MFe2O4; M = Divalent transition metal ion) based materials for electrochemical applications. Spinel ferrites exhibit good chemical stability, high surface area and excellent electrochemical behaviour with their multiple oxidation states, making them suitable for the detection of a wide range of gaseous analytes including volatile organic compounds, heavy metal ions, biomolecules, and environmental pollutants. It also makes spinel ferrites a great choice for efficient energy storage and utility in supercapacitors. The electrochemical performance of spinel ferrite-based electrode materials can be effectively tuned via morphology control, incorporation of carbon-based materials, compositional substitution, doping and forming composition systems, especially in nanostructured form. This review will serve as a comprehensive resource for researchers interested in the synthesis and various enhancement techniques for electrode material composition of electrochemical device applications specifically, gas sensors and supercapacitors, which are two of the highest emerging functional applications for the new sustainability directed world, utilizing these advanced materials.

### [89] [Catalog of Altermagnetism in Magnetic Wallpaper/Space Groups and Nonsymmorphic Altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10857)
*Congcong Le,Fan Cui,Iao-Fai Io,Moritz Hirschmann,Xianxin Wu,Ching-Kai Chiu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该工作利用无自旋时间反演对称性（spinless time-reversal symmetry）系统拓展了交变磁性（altermagnetism）在所有非中心对称晶体（non-centrosymmetric crystals）中的对称性分类，给出了二维磁性墙纸群和三维磁性空间群的完整目录，并揭示了非对称性对称性（nonsymmorphic symmetries）可导致超越已有六种波类型的新交变磁性能带结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交变磁性局限于中心对称晶体，其分类尚不完整，且对非中心对称情形及非对称性对称性带来的新能带结构的认识不足。

Method: 以无自旋时间反演对称性替代反演对称性来维护自旋态等价性，分析必要对称性条件，系统分类了所有二维磁墙纸群和三维磁空间群中的交变磁有序，并将其归入已有文献中六种交变磁波类型。

Result: 识别出17个交变磁墙纸群（12个中心对称、5个非中心对称）和422个交变磁空间群（160个中心对称、262个非中心对称）；发现低能波类型描述不一定扩展到整个布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ），自旋简并节线和节面可脱离高对称面；非对称性对称性通过沙漏型色散（hourglass dispersions）产生新的交变磁BZ模式。

Conclusion: 该工作扩展了交变磁性的对称性目录，揭示了无自旋时间反演对称性的核心作用，以及非对称性对称性对于实现超越六种波类型的交变磁能带结构（如四方BZ中的i波状自旋缠绕）的重要性。

Abstract: Conventional altermagnetism, characterized by compensated collinear spin alignment and spin splitting, exhibits identical spin states at opposite momenta. In this work, we employ a non-spatial global symmetry $S$, the spinless time-reversal symmetry, which effectively replaces inversion symmetry in preserving the spin-state equivalence; hence, we systematically extend the classification of altermagnetism to all possible non-centrosymmetric crystals. By analyzing the necessary symmetry conditions, we provide a complete catalog of altermagnetic orders for all 2D magnetic wallpaper groups and all 3D magnetic space groups, identifying 17 altermagnetic wallpaper groups (12 centrosymmetric and 5 non-centrosymmetric) and 422 altermagnetic space groups (160 centrosymmetric and 262 non-centrosymmetric). This catalog assigns each altermagnetic wallpaper and space group to one of the six altermagnetic wave types established in the literature and presents its distinct spin distribution in the Brillouin zone (BZ); notably, the low-energy wave-type description does not necessarily extend throughout the full BZ, since the spin-degenerate nodal lines and planes can be unpinned from the high-symmetry planes. Beyond the catalog, nonsymmorphic symmetries further bring new patterns of the altermagnetic BZs through the emergence of hourglass dispersions, which arise from the compatibility relations between two symmetry-protected degenerate manifolds: same-spin and opposite-spin degeneracies. In both the non-centrosymmetric altermagnetism and the emergence of the hourglass dispersion, the spinless time-reversal symmetry plays the key role. Our work extends the symmetry catalog of altermagnetism and reveals that nonsymmorphic symmetries are essential for realizing altermagnetic band structures beyond the six established wave types, such as an $i$-wave-like spin winding in a tetragonal BZ.

### [90] [High-Quality Ge-Doped (010) $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ Homoepitaxial Films Grown by Low-pressure CVD: Structural, Electrical, and Schottky Diode Characteristics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10907)
*Ahmed Ibreljic,Saleh Ahmed Khan,Sourav Sarker,Stephen Margiotta,Stephen Lam,Anhar Bhuiyan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过低压化学气相沉积（LPCVD）在 (010) β-Ga₂O₃ 衬底上生长了 Ge 掺杂 β-Ga₂O₃ 同质外延薄膜，实现了可控 n 型掺杂（载流子浓度 7.4×10¹⁷–2.57×10¹⁸ cm⁻³，电子迁移率 105–62 cm²/V·s），并制备了性能良好的垂直 Ni/β-Ga₂O₃ 肖特基势垒二极管，表明 LPCVD 生长的 Ge 掺杂 β-Ga₂O₃ 在高电压功率电子器件领域具有应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: β-Ga₂O₃ 因其超宽带隙（~4.8 eV）在高电压功率电子器件中备受关注，但实现可控 n 型掺杂并保持高晶体质量和电子迁移率仍是关键挑战。本研究旨在利用低压化学气相沉积（LPCVD）技术生长 Ge 掺杂 β-Ga₂O₃ 同质外延薄膜，系统表征其结构、电学性能及器件特性，以验证该技术路线在功率电子领域的可行性。

Method: 采用低压化学气相沉积（LPCVD）在原生 (010) β-Ga₂O₃ 衬底上生长 Ge 掺杂 β-Ga₂O₃ 同质外延薄膜；通过 X 射线衍射、拉曼光谱和 X 射线光电子能谱表征晶体结构与化学组分；利用温度依赖霍尔测量和电中性及输运建模分析掺杂与迁移行为；制备垂直 Ni/β-Ga₂O₃ 肖特基势垒二极管（SBD），结合电流-电压（I-V）和电容-电压（C-V）测量评估器件性能。

Result: 室温下载流子浓度范围为 7.4×10¹⁷–2.57×10¹⁸ cm⁻³，电子迁移率 105–62 cm²/V·s；薄膜 RMS 粗糙度 2.94–3.97 nm；在 116 K 时获得峰值电子迁移率 234 cm²/V·s；浅施主能级的激活能为 14 meV；垂直 Ni/β-Ga₂O₃ SBD 的开态电压为 0.74 V，理想因子 1.32，肖特基势垒高度 1.02 eV（I-V）和 1.13 eV（C-V），比导通电阻 2.49 mΩ·cm²。

Conclusion: LPCVD 技术能够在对 β-Ga₂O₃ 薄膜保持高结构质量和近化学计量比组成的前提下，实现可控的 Ge 掺杂及优异的电学性能。制备的肖特基势垒二极管显示出良好的整流行为，证实 LPCVD 生长的 Ge 掺杂 β-Ga₂O₃ 是未来高电压功率电子器件的有前途的平台。

Abstract: In this work, Ge-doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ homoepitaxial films were grown on native (010) $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ substrates using low-pressure chemical vapor deposition (LPCVD). Controlled $n$-type doping was achieved with room-temperature carrier concentrations ranging from $7.4\times10^{17}$ to $2.57\times10^{18}\ \mathrm{cm}^{-3}$ and corresponding electron mobilities of 105-62 cm$^2$/V$\cdot$s. The films exhibited smooth surface morphology with RMS roughness values of 2.94-3.97 nm, while X-ray diffraction, Raman spectroscopy, and X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy confirmed phase-pure $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ with excellent crystalline quality and near-stoichiometric composition. Temperature-dependent Hall measurements on the film with a room-temperature carrier concentration of $7.4\times10^{17}\ \mathrm{cm}^{-3}$ and mobility of 105 cm$^2$/V$\cdot$s yielded a peak electron mobility of 234 cm$^2$/V$\cdot$s at 116 K, while charge-neutrality and transport modeling revealed a dominant shallow donor level with an activation energy of 14 meV, confirming efficient electrical activation of Ge donors. Vertical Ni/$β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ Schottky barrier diodes fabricated using the Ge-doped drift layer exhibited good rectifying behavior with a turn-on voltage of 0.74 V, an ideality factor of 1.32, a Schottky barrier height of 1.02 eV, and a specific on-resistance of 2.49 m$Ω\cdot$cm$^2$. Capacitance-voltage measurements yielded a net donor concentration of $7.7\times10^{17}\ \mathrm{cm}^{-3}$ and a Schottky barrier height of 1.13 eV, in good agreement with Hall and current-voltage measurements. These results demonstrate that LPCVD enables controllable Ge doping while maintaining high structural and electronic quality, establishing LPCVD-grown Ge-doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ as a promising platform for future high-voltage power electronic devices.

### [91] [High-Mobility Ge-Doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ Growth on Sapphire by Low-Pressure Chemical Vapor Deposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10908)
*Ahmed Ibreljic,Saleh Ahmed Khan,Sourav Sarker,Ibrahim Isah,Stephen Margiotta,Michael Davenport,Stephen Lam,Anhar Bhuiyan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了通过低压化学气相沉积（LPCVD）在具有不同偏切角（0°、2°、6°、8°）的c面蓝宝石衬底上异质外延生长高质量Ge掺杂β-Ga₂O₃薄膜。研究发现，增大蓝宝石偏切角促进了台阶流生长模式，改善了薄膜表面形貌与结晶质量；电学输运性质对偏切角依赖显著，6°偏切角样品实现了创纪录的室温迁移率117 cm²/V s（载流子浓度1.43×10¹⁷ cm⁻³）与低温迁移率337 cm²/V s（128 K）。通过电荷中性方程与玻尔兹曼输运模型拟合，提取了浅施主激活能（12.5–19 meV）、深施主能级（80 meV）、低受主补偿浓度（< 5×10¹⁵ cm⁻³）及约10⁹ cm⁻²的穿透位错密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: β-Ga₂O₃作为超宽禁带半导体在功率电子器件中具有重要潜力，但异质外延生长时衬底偏切角对薄膜质量与电学性能的系统影响尚不明确。本研究旨在通过调控蓝宝石衬底的偏切角，优化Ge掺杂β-Ga₂O₃薄膜的晶体质量与输运性能，并深入理解其散射机制与掺杂行为。

Method: 采用低压化学气相沉积（LPCVD）在偏切角分别为0°、2°、6°和8°的c面蓝宝石衬底上异质外延生长Ge掺杂β-Ga₂O₃薄膜。利用X射线衍射（XRD）与拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）表征晶体结构与取向，X射线光电子能谱（XPS）分析化学计量比与成分。电学输运性质通过变温霍尔效应测量获得，并结合电荷中性方程（charge-neutrality equation）与玻尔兹曼输运模型（Boltzmann transport model）进行拟合，纳入极化光学声子、电离杂质、中性杂质、声学形变势与位错散射机制。

Result: 增大c面蓝宝石偏切角促进了台阶流生长模式，使薄膜表面台阶排列更规整、粗糙度降低、结晶质量提升。XRD与Raman确认了纯单斜β相与强（-201）择优取向，XPS显示O/Ga比为1.48的近化学计量比成分。室温霍尔迁移率从0°偏切角的15 cm²/V s提升至6°时的117 cm²/V s（载流子浓度1.43×10¹⁷ cm⁻³），6°样品在128 K获得峰值低温迁移率337 cm²/V s（载流子浓度8.96×10¹⁶ cm⁻³），为同类Ge掺杂β-Ga₂O₃蓝宝石衬底薄膜迄今最高值。模型拟合给出浅施主激活能12.5–19 meV、深施主能级80 meV、受主补偿浓度低于5×10¹⁵ cm⁻³以及约10⁹ cm⁻²的穿透位错密度。

Conclusion: 蓝宝石衬底偏切角是调控β-Ga₂O₃异质外延薄膜晶体质量与电学性能的有效手段。通过优化偏切角至6°，可显著提高Ge掺杂β-Ga₂O₃薄膜的霍尔迁移率，并实现目前蓝宝石衬底上的最高记录。输运模型分析揭示了低受主补偿与适中的位错密度是获得高迁移率的关键，浅施主与深施主共存有助于理解Ge掺杂行为。

Abstract: In this work, high-quality Ge-doped (-201) $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ thin films were heteroepitaxially grown on c-plane sapphire substrates with offcut angles of 0 deg, 2 deg, 6 deg, and 8 deg using low-pressure chemical vapor deposition (LPCVD). Increasing sapphire offcut promoted step-flow growth, resulting in improved terrace alignment, reduced surface roughness, and enhanced crystalline quality. Phase-pure monoclinic $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ with strong (-201) preferential orientation was confirmed by X-ray diffraction and Raman spectroscopy, while X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy revealed near-stoichiometric composition with an O/Ga ratio of 1.48. Electrical transport properties exhibited a strong dependence on substrate offcut angle, with room-temperature Hall mobility increasing from 15 to 117 cm$^2$/V s as the offcut angle increased from 0 deg to 6 deg, across carrier concentrations spanning $1.43 \times 10^{17}$ to $2.75 \times 10^{18}$ cm$^{-3}$. The 6 deg offcut sample achieved a room-temperature mobility of 117 cm$^2$/V s at a carrier concentration of $1.43 \times 10^{17}$ cm$^{-3}$ and a peak low-temperature mobility of 337 cm$^2$/V s at 128 K with a carrier concentration of $8.96 \times 10^{16}$ cm$^{-3}$, representing the highest reported room-temperature and low-temperature mobilities for Ge-doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ films grown on sapphire substrates. Carrier concentration and mobility data were analyzed using charge-neutrality and Boltzmann transport models incorporating donor activation together with polar optical phonon, ionized impurity, neutral impurity, acoustic deformation potential, and dislocation scattering mechanisms. The fitting revealed shallow donor activation energies of 12.5-19 meV, a deeper donor level at 80 meV, low acceptor compensation ($< 5 \times 10^{15}$ cm$^{-3}$), and threading dislocation densities on the order of $10^9$ cm$^{-2}$.

### [92] [A Cluster-Based Model of the Spectrum of Erbium-Doped GdVO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10924)
*Zachary H. Roberts,Masaya Hiraishi,Luke S. Trainor,Jevon J. Longdell*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于团簇（cluster-based）的模型，用于描述掺杂在钒酸钆（GdVO₄）反铁磁晶体中的铒离子（Er³⁺），该模型仅需较少且物理意义明确的参数即可拟合实验光谱，有望用于预测微波-光学转换（microwave-to-optical transduction）。

Method: 提出一个团簇模型，将铒离子与其四个最近邻钆离子直接耦合，而这些钆离子再耦合到晶体其余部分构成的平均场（mean field）中。

Conclusion: 该团簇模型准确地描述了 Er:GdVO₄ 的光学光谱，表明它可能对预测未来实验中的微波-光学转换（microwave-to-optical transduction）具有实用价值。

Abstract: Experimental observations of rare-earth ions doped into an antiferromagnetic crystal show an enriched optical spectrum. In this paper we present a cluster-based model to describe erbium ions doped into a gadolinium vanadate (Er:GdVO$_4$) host crystal, wherein the erbium ion couples directly to its four nearest neighbour gadolinium ions, which in turn couple to the mean field of the rest of the crystal. Compared to previous models in the literature, the parameters used to fit this model are fewer in number, with clearer physical origins. Agreement with the experimentally observed optical spectrum of Er:GdVO$_4$ suggests that our model succeeds in capturing the most important interactions of the system, suggesting that it may be useful for predicting microwave-to-optical transduction in future experiments.

### [93] [Measurement of Kerr rotation using a variable-angle polarizer method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11002)
*Shusmita Podder Pooza,Hailey Cossey,Dipanjan Mazumdar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于Wollaston棱镜测量正交光分量并拟合解析表达式的方法，用于精确提取纵向磁光Kerr效应中的Kerr旋转角，消除单点测量中的固有不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁光Kerr效应（magneto-optical Kerr effect, MOKE）的精确测量一直具有挑战性，因为该效应依赖于多个光学参数，而传统单点测量方法存在固有的不确定性。

Method: 在钴（Cobalt）薄膜上开展纵向MOKE测量，使用p偏振和s偏振激光，在不同偏振器角度下测量反射偏振光的正交分量，并利用Wollaston棱镜进行分离。随后将正交光分量的解析表达式（analytical expressions）拟合至平均强度和MOKE信号，以提取Kerr旋转角。

Result: 对于633 nm激光在45°入射角下，p-Kerr旋转为0.46毫弧度（milliradians），s-Kerr旋转为0.65毫弧度，与基于文献数据估算的钴材料结果高度吻合。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅精度高，而且能够消除单点测量Kerr旋转角时固有的不确定性，为精确MOKE测量提供了一种可靠途径。

Abstract: The magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) occurs when polarized light reflects from a magnetized surface, causing a small change in the polarization angle and state. Measurement of the rotation in the angle (Kerr rotation) is well established and typically performed close to the null configuration in a polarizer-analyzer geometry. However, accurate measurement always remains a challenge and as the effect depends intricately on several optical parameters. Here we performed a series of longitudinal magneto-optical Kerr effect (MOKE) measurements on $p$ and $s$ polarized laser light at various polarizer angles on a Cobalt thin film and measured the orthogonal components of the reflected polarized light using a Wollaston prism. Analytical expressions for the orthogonal light components were fitted to the average intensity and the MOKE signal measured at different polarizer angles to obtain the Kerr roations. Our analysis yielded a $p (s)$-Kerr rotation of 0.46 (0.65) milliradians for a 633~nm laser at 45$^\circ$ angle of incidence, which agrees very well with our estimated value for Co using available literature data. Apart from being very accurate, the advantage of the process is that it eliminates the inherent uncertainties in single-point measurements of the Kerr rotation.

</details>


### [94] [Telecom-band Chiral Light Detection through Hidden Giant Third-Order Nonlinear Circular Dichroism in Two-dimensional Halide Perovskite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11037)
*Yuki Takahashi,Daichi Okada,Koshi Oi,Kazuki Mitamura,Takahiko Endo,Yasumitsu Miyata,Taishi Takenobu,Kenichi Yamashita*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过极化分辨的三次谐波产生圆二色性（THG-CD）测量，在手性二维钙钛矿(R/S-MBACl)2PbI4中发现了隐藏的巨量THG-CD各向异性，揭示了传统基于总强度评估会严重低估手性非线性光学响应不对称性，并实现了超过1.9的不对称因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性材料的非线性光学（NLO）响应研究主要集中在二阶NLO过程，而手性在三阶NLO过程中的作用仍知之甚少。本研究旨在探索手性三维NLO响应及其在通信波段圆偏振光（CPL）检测中的应用潜力。

Method: 采用极化分辨的三次谐波产生圆二色性（THG-CD）测量，在手性二维钙钛矿(R/S-MBACl)2PbI4中进行偏振分辨的THG信号检测，分离正交THG极化通道中的手性NLO贡献。

Result: 正交THG极化通道中出现相反的手性NLO响应，总THG信号中这些手性各向异性贡献相互抵消，导致基于总THG强度的传统评估严重低估THG-CD不对称性。通过分离这些隐藏的手性贡献，观察到超过1.9的极大不对称因子，并在无结构手性反转条件下实现了相反手性NLO响应的选择性提取。

Conclusion: 极化分辨分析对于评估材料固有的更准确手性NLO响应至关重要。该工作为通信波段的光学信息处理、加密和防伪技术提供了有前景的材料平台。

Abstract: Chiral nonlinear optical (NLO) responses enable efficient discrimination of circularly polarized light (CPL) and are attracting increasing interest for optical and optoelectronic technologies. However, studies on NLO properties in chiral materials have largely focused on second-order NLO processes, while the role of chirality in third-order NLO processes remains poorly explored. Here, we demonstrate telecom-band CPL detection by third harmonic generation circular dichroism (THG-CD) in the chiral two-dimensional perovskite (R/S-MBACl)2PbI4 and uncover a giant hidden THG-CD anisotropy that is accessible via polarization-resolved detection. Polarization-resolved THG measurements reveal that opposite chiral NLO responses emerge in orthogonal THG polarization channels. Therefore, these chiral anisotropic contributions largely cancel each other in the total-THG signal detection, leading to underestimation of the THG-CD dissymmetry in conventional evaluations based on total-THG intensity. By separating these hidden chiral contributions, we observe exceptionally large dissymmetry factors exceeding 1.9 and achieve selective extraction of chiral NLO responses with opposite handedness, without any structural chiral inversion. These findings highlight the importance of polarization-resolved analysis for evaluating more accurate chiral NLO responses inherent to the material and provide a promising platform for optical information processing, encryption, and anti-counterfeiting technologies at technologically relevant telecommunication wavelengths.

</details>


### [95] [Neural-network-based reconstruction of spin and orbital angular momentum from X-ray magnetic circular dichroism spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11058)
*Tetsuro Ueno*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出基于神经网络（neural network）的反问题求解方法，直接从X射线磁圆二色性（XMCD）与X射线吸收谱（XAS）的全谱线形中重建自旋角动量⟨S_z⟩和轨道角动量⟨L_z⟩，克服了传统求和规则（sum rules）在多参数耦合下信息提取不足的局限，并通过Fe、Co、Ni的多体多重态计算数据验证了该方法的准确性与无偏性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将XMCD分析形式化为反问题（inverse problem），构建一个神经网络（neural network, NN），以Fe、Co、Ni的L_{2,3}边XAS与XMCD全谱线形为输入，系统变化晶场分裂、自旋-轨道耦合和交换场等关键参数，通过多体多重态计算（many-body multiplet calculations）生成物理定义明确的训练数据集，训练网络直接映射谱线形到⟨S_z⟩和⟨L_z⟩的期望值。

Result: 神经网络在严格的仅测试数据上实现了对自旋角动量⟨S_z⟩和轨道角动量⟨L_z⟩的精确且无偏的重建，证明了基于数据驱动的反问题重构从XAS与XMCD光谱提取信息的可行性。

Conclusion: 利用完整的XAS和XMCD线形能够获取超越传统求和规则分析的信息，同时与既有理论框架保持一致，为光谱分析提供了新的数据驱动范式。

Abstract: X-ray magnetic circular dichroism (XMCD) is a powerful probe of element-specific spin and orbital angular momentum. Conventional analyses based on sum rules, however, rely on integrated spectral intensities and can become insufficient when multiple parameters influence the spectral line shape. Here, we formulate XMCD analysis as an inverse problem and develop a neural-network (NN) based approach to reconstruct spin and orbital angular momentum directly from full spectral line shapes. Using many-body multiplet calculations of Fe, Co, and Ni $L_{2,3}$-edge X-ray absorption spectra (XAS) and XMCD spectra as a physically well-defined training dataset, we systematically vary key parameters including crystal-field splitting, spin--orbit coupling, and exchange field. The NN is trained to map spectral line shapes onto the expectation values of spin and orbital angular momentm $\langle S_z \rangle$ and $\langle L_z \rangle$, and validated using strictly test-only data. The results demonstrate accurate and unbiased reconstruction, establishing a proof of concept for data-driven inverse reconstruction from XAS and XMCD spectra. These findings show that exploiting the full XAS and XMCD line shapes provide access to information beyond conventional sum-rule analyses while remaining consistent with established theoretical frameworks.

### [96] [Effect of annealing temperature on the structure and properties of co-sputtered Fe-Mn-Sn films near 2:1:1 ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11077)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本研究表明，制备相纯（phase-pure）的三元合金如Fe₂MnSn高度依赖于精确的温度控制；同时，Fe₂MnSn在纳米尺度（<100 nm）存在严重的无序生长问题，限制了其在实际器件中的厚度缩放应用。

Abstract: Research in recent years has focused on the thin-film synthesis of high-quality ternary alloys, identified for their tunable properties and potential in spintronics (e.g., Heusler alloys, Kagome magnets). In a previous study, we identified the conditions for stabilizing Fe$_2$MnSn, a Kagome magnet with a high Curie temperature and magnetic anisotropy. However, ternary phases such as Fe$_2$MnSn are challenging to synthesize and stabilize within a narrow temperature window, as binary and elemental phases can also form during the growth process. To highlight these observations, we investigated the thin film phases in the Fe-Mn-Sn system near the 2:1:1 ratio as a function of annealing temperature, ranging from 400 to 700\degree C. The elemental Fe, Mn, and Sn targets were pre-calibrated to a close to 2:1:1 ratio and co-sputtered at room temperature, followed by annealing. Two binary hexagonal structures, Fe$_3$Sn$_2$ and Fe$_5$Sn$_3$, along with the elemental Fe phase, are stabilized between 400-550\degree C, but disappear at 580\degree C, where Fe$_2$MnSn is the only stable phase. Elemental Mn phase starts to appear starting from 600\degree C, and becomes dominant by 750\degree C. Electrical, magnetic and magneto-optical properties are observed to correlate with the structural findings and the best properties are observed in the temperature range where Fe$_2$MnSn is the dominant phase. In general, our study highlights the difficulty in growing phase-pure ternary alloys such as Fe$_2$MnSn, which is very strongly based on precise temperature conditions. We also observed significant disordered growth below 100 nm for Fe$_2$MnSn, implying poor thickness scaling behavior.

### [97] [Tiling decomposition multiplicity predicts stability of GaN(0001) surface reconstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11105)
*Tetsuji Kuboyama,Akira Kusaba,Karol Kawka,Pawel Kempisty*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出将GaN(0001)-$(6\times6)$表面的稳定吸附原子构型搜索问题转化为离散铺砌问题（discrete tiling problem）进行穷举求解，通过枚举所有菱形铺砌（rhombus tiling）及符合电子计数规则（electron counting rule）的吸附原子排列，获得416,683种构型的完整目录。研究发现铺砌分解重数（tiling decomposition multiplicity）$n_\mathrm{til}$可预测稳定性，该规则将候选集从416,683缩减至24个，最终由第一性原理计算（DFT）完成排序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法依赖采样（sampling）通过DFT能量引导启发式或贝叶斯搜索寻找半导体表面稳定吸附原子构型，但构型空间过大无法穷举覆盖，缺乏完备性保证。

Method: 将搜索转化为离散铺砌问题：穷举表面晶格的所有菱形铺砌，并在其上构建所有符合电子计数规则的吸附原子排列；使用基于机器学习的原子间势能（machine-learning interatomic potential）进行稳定性筛选，并利用DFT对710个结构进行验证。

Result: 获得固定化学计量比（3个Ga吸附原子和18个H原子）下416,683种构型的完整目录，按对称性分为14个Ga放置类别；铺砌分解重数$n_\mathrm{til}$最大的构型在13个类别中严格最稳定，剩余一个类别中偏差仅为8.5 meV，在生长温度下可忽略；规则将候选集缩减至24个DFT评估构型。

Conclusion: 铺砌枚举（enumeration）提供了采样无法实现的覆盖保证（coverage guarantee），并建立了稳定结构预测的路径：第一性原理输入仅用于最终排序步骤。局部机制被识别为避免相邻裸露表面位点（adjacent bare surface sites）。

Abstract: The stable adatom configurations of a semiconductor surface have traditionally been sought by sampling: density functional theory (DFT) energies steer a heuristic or Bayesian search through a configuration space far too large to cover. Here we show that, for the GaN(0001)-$(6\times6)$ surface under the electron counting (EC) rule, the search can instead be posed as a discrete tiling problem and solved exhaustively. Enumerating all rhombus tilings of the surface lattice, together with all EC-compatible adatom arrangements built on them, yields the complete catalog of 416,683 configurations at fixed stoichiometry (3 Ga adatoms and 18 H atoms), organized by symmetry into 14 Ga placement classes. The number of tilings compatible with a given configuration, its tiling decomposition multiplicity $n_\mathrm{til}$, predicts stability. Within each class, the configuration maximizing $n_\mathrm{til}$ is the most stable. The rule holds strictly in 13 of the 14 classes; in the remaining class the minimum is itself among the highest-multiplicity configurations, with the $n_\mathrm{til}$-max configuration only 8.5 meV above it; this ordering is reproduced by independent DFT calculations, and the difference is negligible at growth temperature. Stability screening uses a machine-learning interatomic potential validated against 710 DFT-computed structures. The rule reduces the candidate set for first-principles evaluation from 416,683 to 24 configurations, all of which have been evaluated with DFT. Analysis of the rule identifies the local mechanism, the avoidance of adjacent bare surface sites, while the existence of a compatible tiling remains a separate requirement with an energy cost of its own. Enumeration thus provides what sampling cannot: a coverage guarantee, and a route to stable-structure prediction in which first-principles input enters only at the final ranking step.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推导了一个广义Frank-Bilby方程（GFBE），将界面缺陷的位错分量与台阶分量（step component）显式纳入同一数学框架，从而统一描述界面位错的两种特征。

Conclusion: 广义Frank-Bilby方程（GFBE）弥补了经典FBE的理论局限，为更完整地描述实际晶体材料中的界面结构提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: The classical Frank-Bilby equation (FBE) is commonly used to predict the structure of interfaces in crystalline materials in terms of interfacial dislocation networks. However, in general, the line defects in interfaces are disconnections, possessing both dislocation and step character, which are not captured by the classical FBE. As a result, the FBE cannot fully describe the structure of most interfaces of practical interest. To address this issue, we derive a generalized Frank-Bilby equation (GFBE) that explicitly incorporates both dislocation and step components of interfacial defects. We demonstrate its application to several representative interface systems.

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect in time-reversal symmetric materials offers a powerful probe into quantum geometry. While the monolayer features a highly rigid band structure and modest BCD tunability, the bilayer architecture exhibits substantial field-induced band modifications, including a progressive Rashba splitting and eventual gap closure in the $β$ phase. ### [100] [Temperature dependence of charge-to-spin conversion in rhombohedral (110) bismuth thin film](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11189)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: (110)取向铋中的电荷-自旋转换主要归因于偏斜散射（skew scattering），而非先前文献中认为的与有效g因子（effective g-factor）直接相关的机制。该结论为理解室温下(110)铋中巨大自旋霍尔效应的物理起源提供了关键实验依据。

The conversion efficiency at room temperature in rhombohedral (110) bismuth is notably large as expected from its large spin-orbit interaction, and such a large SHE is ascribed to the large effective g-factor in bismuth [N. Fukumoto et al., Proc. Nat. Acad. Sci. 120, e2215030120 (2023)]. Despite the successful observation of the large conversion efficiency, a more detailed physical mechanism of the SHE in (110) bismuth is still elusive and under debate. In this work, we investigate the temperature dependence of charge-to-spin conversion in an epitaxial Bi(110)/Ni bilayer system using the second harmonic Hall method, revealing that both spin Hall conductivity and spin diffusion length augment with decreasing temperature. This finding suggests that spin scattering in (110) bismuth is dominated by the Elliott-Yafet mechanism, and the charge-to-spin conversion is mainly attributed to skew scattering.

### [101] [Anomalous Transverse Response and Multi-Field Ferrialtermagnetic-Ferroelectric Valve with CrSb Flakes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11222)
*Long Zhang,Xinfeng Chen,Hongfei Liang,Jianting Dong,Fei Zou,Yi Yan,Guangqian Ding,Guoying Gao*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体兼具反铁磁体的零杂散场和铁磁体的自旋极化特性，在自旋电子学中具有巨大潜力。然而，传统交变磁体的自旋劈裂在对称性等效的亚晶格间相互抵消，缺乏对扰动的内在鲁棒性；因此，需要探索一种新的交变磁子类，其自旋劈裂不能被完全抵消，并能提供更强的稳定性和多场调控能力。

Method: 本文首先从理论上定义铁交变磁性——交变磁亚晶格因对称性不等价而具有非相同的奈尔矢量，从而阻止交替自旋劈裂的相互抵消。在实验上，通过生长三层CrSb(110)薄片实现该概念，并测量其磁光克尔效应和反常霍尔效应。在应用层面，将铁交变磁体CrSb与铁电体Sc2CO2及铜间隔层集成，设计出铁交变磁-铁电阀器件，并分别计算其在平衡态和非平衡态（偏压、热场或光场驱动）下的隧穿磁电阻与电电阻。

Result: 三层CrSb(110)薄片展现出344 meV的自旋劈裂、适中的单轴磁各向异性和高达657 K的奈尔温度；同时观察到磁光克尔效应和反常霍尔效应。所设计的铁交变磁-铁电阀在平衡态下实现约10^3%的隧穿磁电阻与电电阻，在偏压、热或光场驱动下达到约10^4%，自旋过滤效率高达90%；此外还实现了负微分电阻效应、光生伏打效应以及283.8的光电流消光比。

Conclusion: 铁交变磁体作为交变磁体家族的新子类，为多场控制、超紧凑和自供电的自旋电子学与电子学提供了富有前景的材料平台。该工作不仅扩展了交变磁体家族的理论框架，还通过具体材料实现了优异性能，展示了在低功耗、多物理场调控器件中的巨大应用潜力。

Abstract: Altermagnets combine the zero-stray-field of antiferromagnets with the spin polarization of ferromagnets, showing great potential for spintronic applications. Here, we propose ferrialtermagnetism as a distinct subclass of altermagnetic family, where symmetry-inequivalent altermagnetic sublattices possess nonidentical Neel vectors, preventing mutual cancellation of alternating spin splitting and conferring intrinsic robustness against perturbations. This concept is realized in the three-atomic-layer CrSb (110) flakes, which exhibits spin splitting of 344 meV, moderate uniaxial magnetic anisotropy, and high Neel temperature of 657 K. The magneto-optical Kerr and the anomalous Hall effects are observed. Integrating this ferrialtermagnetic CrSb with ferroelectric Sc2CO2 and Cu spacer, we design an ferrialtermagnetic-ferroelectric valve. This device displays equilibrium tunneling magnetoresistance and electroresistance of ~10^3%, and non-equilibrium magnitudes under bias, thermal, or light field reaches ~10^4% with high spin filtering of 90%. The negative differential resistance and photogalvanic effects, and photocurrent extinction ratio of 283.8 are achieved. These findings establish ferrialtermagnetism as a fertile platform for multi-field-controlled, ultracompact, and self-powered spintronics and electronics.

</details>


### [102] [Anisotropic hot carrier relaxation mediated by electron phonon scattering in TiN thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11237)
*Hemant Verma,Tzu-Yu Peng,Shyr-Shyan Yeh,Sheng-Chieh Huang,Pritam Sardar,Yang-Hao Chan,Yu-Jung Lu,Chao-Cheng Kaun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与超快泵浦-探测瞬态吸收光谱相结合，发现氮化钛（TiN）薄膜的电子-声子（e-ph）介导弛豫具有显著的面内取向依赖性：[111]取向的散射寿命（15.96 fs）和冷却时间（110 fs）均长于[100]和[110]取向，表明晶向可有效调控TiN薄膜中e-ph控制的能量弛豫过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究过渡金属氮化物薄膜中晶体取向如何影响超快能量弛豫过程，特别是电子-声子（electron-phonon, e-ph）介导的弛豫机制，为可调控的难熔等离激元和能量转换平台提供设计指导。

Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）计算结合最大局域化Wannier函数（maximally localized Wannier functions）评估费米能级附近的e-ph准粒子散射寿命；同时在MgO衬底上生长准外延、取向可控的TiN薄膜，利用超快泵浦-探测瞬态吸收光谱（ultrafast pump-probe transient absorption spectroscopy）测量热电子冷却时间。

Result: 计算表明TiN [111]取向的e-ph散射寿命（15.96 fs）长于[100]（13.69 fs）和[110]（11.12 fs），呈现各向异性；泵浦-探测测量显示[111]薄膜的热电子冷却时间（110 fs）显著慢于[100]（90 fs）和[110]（80 fs），两者趋势一致。

Conclusion: 晶体取向（crystallographic orientation）提供了一种实用而强大的途径来调控TiN薄膜中e-ph主导的弛豫过程，为难熔等离激元和能量转换平台提供了关键的设计准则。

Abstract: Crystal orientations can shape the ultrafast energy relaxations of transition-metal nitride thin films. Here, we investigate the orientation-dependent electron-phonon (e-ph) mediated relaxation in titanium nitride (TiN) thin films along the [100], [110], and [111] directions by combining first-principles calculations with ultrafast pump-probe transient absorption spectroscopy. Using maximally localized Wannier functions, we evaluate e-ph quasiparticle scattering lifetimes near the Fermi level and identify a clear anisotropy: The TiN [111] orientation exhibits a longer e-ph scattering lifetime (15.96 fs) than [100] (13.69 fs) and [110] (11.12 fs), indicating reduced intrinsic e-ph scattering strength. Furthermore, we grew quasi-epitaxial, orientation-controlled TiN thin films on MgO substrates. Pump-probe measurements reveals that the population-level relaxation (hot-electron cooling) time also depends on orientations, with [111] films showing a significantly slower decay (110 fs) than [100] (90 fs) and [110] (80 fs). We emphasize that the calculated few-femtosecond scattering lifetimes and the measured few-hundred-femtosecond cooling time respectively represent single-event scattering and collective cooling, yet they exhibit consistent trends. These results demonstrate that crystallographic orientation provides a practical and powerful route to tune e-ph-governed relaxation in TiN thin films, offering essential design guidelines for refractory plasmonic and energy-conversion platforms.

Method: 采用双温模型下的分子动力学模拟；利用基于局域电子密度（local electron density）的无阈值耦合方法同时描述电子阻止（electronic stopping）和电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）；在多种初始撞击原子（primary knock-on atom）能量下，使用两种不同的耦合函数和两种原子间势进行比较。

Result: 离子-电子耦合的函数形式对缺陷产生效率、缺陷聚集和缺陷复合行为有决定性影响；耦合对级联冷却阶段中缺陷复合的影响取决于所选原子间势。

Conclusion: 为了可靠预测辐射损伤，必须对离子-电子耦合的函数形式进行谨慎选择，同时需要基于物理原理的描述来刻画电子效应和原子-原子相互作用。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the role of ion-electron coupling in simulations of radiation damage formation in silicon using molecular dynamics simulations within a two-temperature model. We explore predictions of a threshold-free approach to the coupling that accounts for both the electronic stopping and electron-phonon coupling using a local electron density-based formalism. We compare two different coupling functions across a range of primary knock-on atom energies using two interatomic potentials. Our results demonstrate that the functional form of the ion-electron coupling plays a critical role in determining defect production efficiency, clustering, and recombination, and must therefore be carefully considered for accurate modeling of radiation damage formation. Furthermore, we find that the impact of the coupling in particular on the recombination of defects during the cooling phase of the cascade depends on the choice of interatomic potential, emphasizing the importance of physically grounded descriptions for both electronic effects and atom-atom interactions for reliable radiation damage predictions.

### [104] [PAC Studio Machine Learning: Human-in-the-Loop Analysis of TDPAC Spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11298)
*Thien Thanh Dang,Doru Constantin Lupascu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍PAC Studio ML——一个人机协同（human-in-the-loop）的Python桌面环境，用于物理信息驱动的时间微分扰动角关联（TDPAC/PAC）谱逆分析，通过集成机器学习（ML）预测器、哈密顿量正向模型、自动位点筛选和ML种子非线性最小二乘精修等模块，加速参数搜索、提升可复现性，但最终模型选择与物理解释仍由研究人员负责。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间微分扰动角关联（TDPAC/PAC）分析是一个病态逆问题（ill-conditioned inverse problem），位点计数、相互作用类型、相关超精细参数（hyperfine parameters）、阻尼及初始化选择等因素会导致多种竞争性的数值解，亟需一种能兼顾物理约束与计算效率的分析工具。

Method: PAC Studio ML集成了基于哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的正向PAC模型、用户定义的合成训练库、特征提取（feature extraction）、一到三位点机器学习预测器、直接参数预测、自动位点模型族筛选（Auto sites model-family screening）、ML种子非线性最小二乘精修（ML-seeded nonlinear least-squares refinement）、可视化、基准测试、诊断和模型卡报告等功能。ML组件旨在加速参数探索、建议合理的初始化区域、比较位点计数假设及提升可复现性，而非替代传统拟合与专家解读。

Result: 留出法合成测试（held-out synthetic tests）验证了该软件的可运作性，并展示了PAC参数在困难逆问题中可恢复性（recoverability）的不均衡性。BiFeO3实例展示了常规、直接ML、ML种子和自动位点四种工作流程，但定位为软件案例研究，而非完整的实验验证语料库。

Conclusion: PAC Studio ML被定位为专家PAC分析的辅助工具：它能够提升工作流程速度和诊断透明度，但最终模型选择、物理约束及材料学解释仍由研究者负责。

Abstract: Time-differential perturbed angular correlation (TDPAC or PAC) analysis is an ill-conditioned inverse problem in which site count, interaction type, correlated hyperfine parameters, damping, and initialization choices can produce competing numerical solutions. This software paper presents PAC Studio ML, a human-in-the-loop Python desktop environment for physics-informed inverse analysis of PAC spectra. The software integrates a Hamiltonian-based forward PAC model, user-defined synthetic training libraries, feature extraction, one-, two-, and three-site machine-learning predictors, direct parameter prediction, Auto sites model-family screening, ML-seeded nonlinear least-squares refinement, visualization, benchmarking, diagnostics, model-card reporting, and export tools. The ML component is designed to support, not replace, conventional fitting and expert interpretation by accelerating parameter exploration, suggesting plausible initialization regions, comparing site-count hypotheses, and improving reproducibility. Held-out synthetic tests demonstrate proof of operation and illustrate the unequal recoverability of PAC parameters in difficult inverse problems. Selected BiFeO3 examples demonstrate conventional, direct-ML, ML-seeded, and Auto sites workflows as software case studies, not as a complete experimental validation corpus. PAC Studio ML is therefore positioned as a supporting tool for expert PAC analysis: it improves workflow speed and diagnostic transparency while final model choice, physical constraints, and materials interpretation remain the responsibility of the researcher.

Method: 构建了一个基准测试框架（benchmarking framework），包括一个针对典型非晶体系（canonical amorphous systems）的精选参考数据集（curated reference dataset），以及结构和性质的验证（validation for structures and properties）。基于该框架对当前主流预训练模型进行系统评估，并研究面向无序相（disordered phases）的微调策略（fine-tuning strategies）。

Abstract: Pre-trained or 'foundational' machine-learned interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are now widely used in materials modelling. However, early pre-trained models and benchmarks have largely focused on ordered, crystalline structures, and their transferability to non-crystalline solids remains unclear. Here, we show that the amorphous state is indeed a central challenge for future universal MLIPs, based on a systematic evaluation of current mainstream models in this domain. We introduce a benchmarking framework built on a curated reference dataset of canonical amorphous systems, as well as validation for structures and properties. Our study identifies limitations in the transferability of many current pre-trained models and investigates fine-tuning strategies tailored to disordered phases. Together, our results can facilitate future applications of MLIPs in the fast-growing field of amorphous functional materials, and they provide guidance for designing next-generation training datasets and transferable atomistic models.

### [106] [Capturing the calendering U-shape in lithium-ion electrode thermal conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11521)
*Julius Störk*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种考虑压延过程影响的 Zehner–Bauer–Schlünder 模型扩展，用于预测锂电池电极的面内有效热导率，在27个压延状态上将平均绝对百分比误差从31.1%降低至4.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 压延（calendering）是锂电池电极制造中的关键步骤，通过降低孔隙率（porosity）提升体积能量密度，但其对穿面有效热导率（through-plane effective thermal conductivity）的影响呈非单调变化——石墨负极在早期压延时热导率下降，随后在高压实下恢复。传统基于孔隙率的有效介质闭合模型（porosity-based effective-medium closures）无法再现这种U形行为。

Method: 提出一种压延感知的 Zehner–Bauer–Schlünder 模型扩展，将克努森修正多孔介质基线（Knudsen-corrected porous-medium baseline）与压缩索引接触贡献（compression-indexed contact contribution）相结合。对于石墨电极，模型刻画了颗粒接触增加与压延诱导的各向异性石墨颗粒重新取向之间的竞争效应；对于准各向同性 NMC 正极，则通过过程依赖的接触网络演化（process-dependent contact-network evolution）来捕捉观测响应。

Result: 在涵盖薄和厚石墨负极、NMC622 及 NMC811 正极的27个压延状态上，该闭合模型将平均绝对百分比误差（mean absolute percentage error）从无拟合参考模型的31.1%降至4.5%。

Conclusion: 纳入过程依赖的微结构演化（process-dependent microstructural evolution）是捕捉实测热导率极小值的关键；模型在更多电极配方（formulations）、厚度和化学体系（chemistries）上的验证仍有待开展，以评估其可迁移性（transferability）。

Abstract: Calendering is a key manufacturing step in lithium-ion electrode production, increasing volumetric energy density by reducing electrode porosity. Its effect on through-plane effective thermal conductivity, however, can be non-monotonic: measurements of graphite-based anodes show an initial decrease in thermal conductivity during early calendering followed by recovery at higher compaction. Conventional porosity-based effective-medium closures cannot reproduce this U-shaped behaviour. We develop a calendering-aware extension of the Zehner--Bauer--Schlünder model that combines a Knudsen-corrected porous-medium baseline with a compression-indexed contact contribution. For graphite electrodes, the model represents the competing effects of increasing particle contact and calendering-induced reorientation of anisotropic graphite particles, which initially reduces favourable through-plane heat-transport pathways. For quasi-isotropic NMC cathodes, the observed response is instead captured through process-dependent contact-network evolution. Across 27 calendering states spanning thin and thick graphite anodes and NMC622 and NMC811 cathodes, the proposed closure reduces the mean absolute percentage error from 31.1% for the zero-fit reference model to 4.5%. The result shows that incorporating process-dependent microstructural evolution is necessary to capture the measured conductivity minimum. Validation across additional electrode formulations, thicknesses, and chemistries remains necessary to assess transferability.

### [107] [Synthesis of Ti2B2Clx MBenes in molten salts from theoretical and experimental perspectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11550)

Result: In 原子被完全移除并被氯表面端基（chlorine surface terminations）取代，覆盖度 x 在 1.1 至 1.4 之间；原位 XRD 显示 Ti2InB2 直接转变为多层 MBene，无中间相形成；DFT 计算表明多层 MBene 形成反应自由能为负，优于所有竞争过程；A 元素（Zn）取代进入三维 Ti2ZnB2 相被预测为吸能反应（endergonic），与实验未观察到该相的结果一致；锂离子电池初始性能评估显示稳定的放电容量，与 MAX 相及其他硼化物相当或更优。

Conclusion: 所建立的理论框架与材料合成及表征相结合，为二维材料开发提供了一种通用方法，有助于进一步扩展二维材料家族。

Abstract: The unique properties and application possibilities of two-dimensional (2D) materials motivates the exploration of different nanolaminated compounds. Here, by using a molten salt approach, we selectively etch Ti2InB2 with ZnCl2 to produce a multilayer (ml) Ti2B2Clx MBene. Scanning transmission electron microscopy, in combination with energy dispersive X-ray, and electron energy loss spectroscopies show that In atoms are completely removed from the precursor upon etching, being replaced by chlorine surface terminations with a coverage 1.1 < x < 1.4. Further, in situ X-ray diffraction indicates a direct biphasic transformation from Ti2InB2 to ml-MBene, with no signs of intermediate phase formation. A computational framework based on density functional theory further corroborates these experimental observations by showing a negative reaction free energy for the formation of ml-MBene, favourable over all competing processes. In addition, A-element substitution into to the 3D Ti2ZnB2 phase is predicted to be endergonic, consistent with the absence of experimental evidence for its formation. Initial Li-ion battery performance evaluation showed a stable discharge capacity similar or better than MAX phases and other borides. Altogether, the theoretical framework combined with materials synthesis and characterization provides a general approach for 2D materials development, for further expansion of the family of 2D materials.

### [108] [Exchange topology and criticality in ferrite and chromium spinels: a unified Monte Carlo analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11729)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前缺乏对两类不同磁性尖晶石体系（反式铁氧体和铬尖晶石）在交换常数、相变温度、临界指数、磁滞和磁热响应等性质上的统一比较分析，尤其缺少约化量来量化几何阻挫（geometric frustration）和自旋连续对称性对居里温度（Curie temperature, T_C）的抑制效应。

Method: 采用Metropolis蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）方法，对反式铁氧体Fe^{3+}_A[M^{2+}Fe^{3+}]_B O_4（M = Co, Cu, Fe, Ni）和铬尖晶石A Cr_2 X_4（A = Zn, Cd, Hg, X = S, Se）以及呼吸晶格铬酸盐LiM Cr_4 O_8（M = Ga, In）进行统一模拟，并引入两个新的约化量θ_CW/T_C和t* = k_B T_C / [J_1 S(S+1)]进行分析。

Result: 反式铁氧体的θ_CW/T_C比值集中在0.94-1.19，接近平均场（mean-field）预期值1，表明A-B超交换主导且无阻挫；其临界指数β=0.20-0.26、γ=1.23-1.27、δ=4.76-4.78符合三维伊辛类（three-dimensional Ising class）。铬体系根据t*值分为三个区间：t*≈1.4-1.9（伊辛类处理的硫化物）、t*≈0.99（海森堡类处理的硒化物）和t*≈0.24-0.25（反铁磁呼吸铬酸盐），定量反映了连续自旋对称性和几何阻挫对T_C的联合抑制。Fe_3O_4的有限厚度模拟揭示了在2到4个单胞之间的维度交叉（dimensionality crossover）。

Conclusion: 两个新的约化量有效地将不同磁性尖晶石体系纳入统一框架。铬铁矿中阻挫体系所预测的普适类（universality class）是伊辛类还是海森堡类，取决于自旋对称性的处理方式，这被识别为主要未解决的核心问题。

Abstract: We report a unified analysis of Metropolis Monte Carlo results for two families of magnetic spinels: inverse ferrites Fe$^{3+}_{A}$[M$^{2+}$Fe$^{3+}$]$_{B}$O$_4$ (M = Co, Cu, Fe, Ni), where superexchange couples two chemically distinct sublattices, and chromium spinels $A$Cr$_2X_4$ ($A$ = Zn, Cd, Hg, $X$ = S, Se) together with the breathing-lattice chromates Li$M$Cr$_4$O$_8$ ($M$ = Ga, In), where a single Cr$^{3+}$ species occupies a corner-sharing tetrahedral network. Placing the exchange constants, transition temperatures, critical exponents, hysteresis, and magnetocaloric responses of these systems on a common footing, we introduce two reduced quantities not previously reported: the ratio $θ_{\mathrm{CW}}/T_C$ for the ferrites and the normalized ordering scale $t^{*}=k_BT_C/[J_1S(S+1)]$ for the chromium compounds. The ferrites cluster in the range $θ_{\mathrm{CW}}/T_C = 0.94$-$1.19$, close to the mean-field expectation of unity and the signature of dominant, unfrustrated A-B superexchange, and their exponents ($β= 0.20$-$0.26$, $γ= 1.23$-$1.27$, $δ= 4.76$-$4.78$) follow the three-dimensional Ising class. The chromium systems split into three regimes: $t^{*} \approx 1.4$-$1.9$ for Ising-treated sulfides, $t^{*} \approx 0.99$ for Heisenberg-treated selenides, and $t^{*} \approx 0.24$-$0.25$ for the antiferromagnetic breathing chromates, quantifying the combined suppression of $T_C$ by continuous spin symmetry and by geometric frustration. Finite-thickness simulations of Fe$_3$O$_4$ resolve a dimensionality crossover between two and four unit cells. We identify the Ising-versus-Heisenberg dependence of the predicted universality class in frustrated chromites as the principal open problem.

</details>


### [109] [Strain-controlled crystalline--amorphous transition and flat-band tuning in buckled silicon kagome](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11790)
*Chenhaoyue Wang,Amartya S. Banerjee*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由硅原子构成的屈曲型卡戈梅晶格（buckled silicon kagome lattice, SiKL）二维材料，其近费米能级平带可受双轴应变的调控。研究发现，该材料在约10%的应变下带宽显著降低、密度泛函峰接近费米能级，并能稳定至室温以上；经典分子动力学模拟揭示出应变控制的晶态-非晶态转变和局域键合转变。该平台为无功能化、仅靠应变调控的元胞硅平带电子关联物理提供了候选体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中的平带（flat band）有助于增强电子相互作用与抑制动能（kinetic energy）的竞争，从而产生强关联物理现象；目前尚缺乏仅由单质（elemental）材料构成且仅通过应变即可实现稳定平带调制的方案。

Method: 基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的电子结构和晶格动力学计算，结合从头算分子动力学（ab initio MD）和经典分子动力学（classical MD）模拟。通过跟踪三种软区心声子（soft zone-centre phonons）并弛豫位移结构，获得两种近简并的屈曲构型。在Ag(111)衬底上建立探索性模型以评估外延失配应力效应。

Result: 高屈曲构型保留了部分平带；10%双轴应变使带宽显著减小、态密度峰接近费米能级，最软声子硬化；315 K时未应变网络无序化而应变网络保持有序；50 ns经典MD显示约2%应变附近存在晶态-非晶态转变与局域键合转变；低应变呈现渐进两阶段无序化，高应变呈现一阶类突变塌缩，转变温度在10%应变下约600 K。

Conclusion: 屈曲型SiKL是一种无功能化的单质硅候选平台，仅依靠应变就能将热亚稳性（thermal metastability）、键重排和近费米能级平带调控耦合起来，可用于应变控制的平带和电子关联物理研究。

Abstract: Electronic flat bands in an elemental two-dimensional material provide an attractive setting for electron interactions competing with suppressed kinetic energy. Here we propose a buckled silicon kagome lattice (SiKL), an unfunctionalized six-atom monolayer of bond-linked Si$_3$ triangles and dodecagonal pores. Its planar parent hosts a dispersionless Kohn--Sham band near the Fermi level but is unstable to out-of-plane distortions. Following three soft zone-centre phonons and relaxing displaced structures yields two nearly degenerate buckled forms. The high-buckling form retains a partially flat kagome-derived band near the Fermi level. Biaxial tension controls lattice dynamics and electronic dispersion: at 10% strain, the bandwidth decreases significantly, the density-of-states peak approaches the Fermi level, and the softest phonon hardens. At 315 K, $6\times6$ ab initio MD shows the unstrained network disordering while the strained network remains ordered, indicating finite-temperature metastability. Fifty-nanosecond classical MD of $36\times36$ sheets reveals a strain-controlled crystalline--amorphous transition and local-bonding crossover near 2% strain. Low-strain trajectories show gradual, two-stage disordering; higher strains undergo an abrupt, first-order-like collapse, with the transition temperature reaching approximately 600 K at 10% strain. An exploratory Ag(111) substrate model suggests epitaxial mismatch could supply comparable tension, retain a narrow SiKL band, and preserve crystalline order above room temperature. Unlike passivated or hybrid-lattice silicon kagome proposals aimed mainly at conventional semiconductors, SiKL is elemental and uses strain alone to couple thermal metastability, bond rearrangement, and near-Fermi flat-band tuning. Buckled SiKL is a candidate platform for strain-controlled flat-band and electronic correlation physics.

</details>


### [110] [Direct writing of individual quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11864)
*Weikun Zhu,Natalie Ngoh,Shelly Ben-David,Maxwell Conte,Teddy Hsieh,Sarah O. Spector,Tara Sverko,Patricia Jastrzebska-Perfect,Will Jack,Jinwoo Sim,Peter F. Satterthwaite,Farnaz Niroui*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种利用热扫描探针方法直接书写单个钙钛矿量子点（quantum dot, QD）的技术，实现了亚25纳米空间精度的位点选择性合成，并展示了室温下单光子纯度高达98%的CsPbI3单光子发射器阵列及其与光子腔的确定性耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无机卤化物钙钛矿纳米晶是极具前景的单光子源，但其在溶液中的随机分散（stochastic dispersion）阻碍了单个发射体与光子结构的确定性和稳定集成，且传统自上而下（top-down）的制造工艺因分辨率和材料兼容性限制无法满足这种异质集成（heterogeneous integration）需求。

Method: 采用热扫描探针方法（thermal scanning probe method）诱导纳米尺度限域形成体积（nanoscale-confined formation volume），实现位点选择性合成（site-selective synthesis）至单个原子尺度量子点，并具备光谱可调性（spectral tunability）和小于25纳米的空间控制。

Result: 实现了高产量CsPbI3单光子发射器阵列，具有窄线宽（narrow linewidths）和室温下高达98%的单光子纯度（single-photon purity）。还实现了发射体与光子腔（photonic cavities）的精确、按需耦合，观测到自发发射速率（spontaneous emission rate）的增强。

Conclusion: 该工作将化学合成的原子尺度可调性与增材制造（additive manufacturing）的空间控制相结合，为解决胶体材料在下一代量子技术中的集成障碍提供了新的发射体工程策略。

Abstract: Quantum light sources capable of generating single photons are fundamental building blocks for photonic quantum technologies. In the ongoing search for an ideal quantum emitter, inorganic halide perovskite nanocrystals have emerged as a promising source of single photons. Their unique optical response, with an unmatched ease of synthetic tunability, stands out amongst the competing platforms. However, their stochastic dispersion in solution challenges the deterministic and stable integration of individual emitters with photonic structures that is required for practical technologies. Notably, resolution and material compatibility constraints make conventional top-down fabrication processes insufficient for such heterogeneous integration. Here, we report direct writing of perovskite quantum dots (QDs) with individual-emitter resolution. By inducing a nanoscale-confined formation volume using a thermal scanning probe method, we achieve site-selective synthesis down to a single atomic-scale QD with spectral tunability and < 25 nm spatial control. As a result, we demonstrate high-yield arrays of CsPbI3 single-photon emitters with narrow linewidths and high single-photon purity up to 98% at room temperature, performance consistent with that of their state-of-the-art colloidal counterparts. Through such deterministic control, we uniquely realize the precise, on-demand coupling of these emitters to photonic cavities, as evidenced by a measured enhancement in the spontaneous emission rate. This represents a key advancement toward addressing the longstanding integration obstacles of these materials. Overall, by combining the atomic-scale tunability of chemical synthesis with the spatial control of additive manufacturing, our work opens new emitter engineering strategies to realize the untapped potential of colloidal materials for next-generation quantum technologies.

### [111] [Global existence and optimal decay for a three-dimensional penalized Navier--Stokes system with biharmonic damping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10657)
*Kabiru Michael Adeyemo,Mohamed Majdoub,Subha Pal*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个三维抛物型系统，该系统通过超粘性（hyperviscous）和惩罚（penalization）逼近不可压缩Navier–Stokes方程。论文证明了弱解的整体存在性、小初始条件下强解的唯一性，以及最优大时间衰减估计，且所有先验估计关于惩罚参数一致成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为不可压缩Navier–Stokes方程构造一种结合经典粘性扩散、双调和超粘性正则化（biharmonic hyperviscous regularization）和散度惩罚（divergence penalization）的逼近方法，并建立其数学分析的严格基础。

Method: 模型结合三种耗散机制：经典粘性扩散、双调和超粘性正则化以及散度惩罚，并在非线性对流项中引入Temam型修正以补偿弱可压缩性效应。分析基于统一关于惩罚参数ε的先验估计。

Result: 对于L²(R³)中的任意初始数据，证明弱解的整体存在性；对于H²(R³)中足够小的初始数据，建立全局强解的存在唯一性；对于L¹∩H²中的初始数据，推导出与经典热方程相同的最优大时间衰减率。

Conclusion: 所有先验估计关于惩罚参数ε一致成立，为惩罚逼近不可压缩流动问题提供了稳定且严格的解析基础。

Abstract: We investigate a three-dimensional parabolic system that arises as a hyperviscous and penalized approximation of the incompressible Navier--Stokes equations. The model combines three complementary dissipative mechanisms: the classical viscous diffusion, a biharmonic (hyperviscous) regularization, and a divergence penalization. In addition, a Temam-type correction is incorporated into the nonlinear convection term to compensate for the weak compressibility effects generated by the penalization procedure.
  We prove the global existence of weak solutions for arbitrary initial data belonging to $L^2(\mathbb{R}^3)$. For sufficiently small initial data in $H^2(\mathbb{R}^3)$, we establish the existence and uniqueness of global strong solutions. Furthermore, for initial data in $L^1(\mathbb{R}^3)\cap H^2(\mathbb{R}^3)$, we derive optimal large-time decay estimates, showing that the solutions exhibit the same asymptotic decay rates as those of the classical heat equation. A key feature of our analysis is that all the obtained a priori estimates are uniform with respect to the positive penalization parameter $\varepsilon$. These uniform bounds provide a stable and rigorous analytical foundation for the study of the penalized approximation of incompressible flows.

### [112] [Singular mean-field limits via a multiscale mollification metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10686)
*Quoc Hung Nguyen,Sylvia Serfaty*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对一大类平均场（mean-field）框架下N个相互作用粒子的一阶常微分方程（ODE）系统，提出了一种基于热核磨光多尺度度量（mollification by heat kernels）的新方法，用以证明离散系统向平均场方程解的定量收敛，并在不同奇异性和维度下给出了收敛性的最优时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如调制能量法（modulated energy method））通常要求相互作用可从一个势函数导出，限制了其适用范围。本文旨在处理更广泛的一类相互作用——包括具有逆幂型奇异性（inverse power type singularity）的吸引或排斥相互作用，且不必然源自势函数——并建立离散系统到平均场极限的定量收敛性。

Method: 引入一种新的度量方法，通过热核（heat kernel）对经验测度（empirical measure）与其极限之间的差异进行磨光，从而构建一个多尺度控制（multiscale control）的度量，并研究该度量随时间的演化。

Result: (i) 在任意维度下，若奇异性为亚库仑型（sub-coulombic），或在一维和二维中为库仑型（coulombic），收敛性可延续到极限方程光滑解的最大存在时间；(ii) 在三维及以上维度的库仑型奇异性下，短时间收敛成立；(iii) 对于超库仑型（super-coulombic）相互作用，在所有维度下收敛性仅在一个与N相关的短时间尺度内成立。后两种结果被证明是最优的，因为对于一类吸引相互作用，碰撞发生的时间尺度与之相同。

Conclusion: 该新方法有效克服了传统调制能量法的局限性，为不具备势函数结构的高奇异相互作用提供了定量收敛证明，并揭示了奇异性强度与收敛时间尺度之间的最优关系。

Abstract: We consider a general class of first order ODE systems for the evolution of $N$ interacting particles (in Euclidean space $\mathbb{R}^d$) in a mean-field regime. The class of interactions treated includes singular interactions of inverse power type up to power $d+1$, attractive or repulsive, and not necessarily deriving from a potential -- unlike, for instance, the modulated energy method. We introduce a new method to prove quantitative convergence of the discrete system to solutions of the mean-field equation. It relies on studying the evolution of a metric encoding a multiscale control of the difference between the empirical measure and its limit, via mollification by heat kernels.
  We prove that the desired convergence holds (i) up to the maximal time of existence of the smooth solution to the limiting equation if the singularity is sub-coulombic in any dimension, or coulombic in dimensions 1 and 2 (where, to do so, we introduce a notion of weak solution to the ODE system), or (ii) for short time in the case of Coulomb singularity in dimension 3 and above and (iii) up to a short $N$-dependent timescale for super-coulombic interactions in all dimensions. The latter two results are demonstrated to be optimal as we prove that collisions occur within the same timescale for a class of attractive interactions.

</details>


### [113] [Sharp Broken-Power Lorentz Estimates for Fractional Powers of Radial Schrödinger Operators with Inverse-Square Asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11280)
*Haochen Liu,Qinghao Yu,Hongyan Zhou*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了非负径向薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operator）$H=-Δ+V(|x|)$ 的分数幂 $H^{-s/2}$ 的积分核的双边估计及其加权不等式。确定了核估计成立的 $s$ 的最大开区间，并给出了加权 $L^p$-$L^q$ 有界性的充要分类，涵盖符号基态指数、$q<p$ 完全范围、单边权等式、标度等式及同时端点角点情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数幂算子 $H^{-s/2}$ 的积分核估计和加权有界性是调和分析与偏微分方程中的核心问题。已有的径向薛定谔算子的基态热核双边估计为研究其分数幂核提供了基础，但 $H^{-s/2}$ 核的“干净双边估计”（clean two-sided estimate）成立的 $s$ 范围未知，且相应的加权加权不等式分类缺乏完整刻画，特别是符号基态指数、$q<p$ 范围以及同时端点角点情形尚未被覆盖。

Method: 基于 Ishige, Kabeya 和 Ouhabaz 的双边基态热核估计，利用干净核分析（clean-kernel analysis）、局部Lorentz-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev估计（local Lorentz-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev estimates）、秩一端点论证（rank-one endpoint arguments）、几何环状序列空间（geometric annular sequence spaces）、三角矩阵定理（triangular matrix theorem）和九块分解（nine-block decomposition）等工具，综合推导核估计成立的范围并分类加权不等式。

Result: 确定了 $H^{-s/2}$ 核具有干净双边估计 $K_s^H(x,y)\simeq |x-y|^{s-d}U(|x|)U(|y|)/[U(|x|+|x-y|)U(|y|+|x-y|)]$ 的最大 $s$ 范围为 $0<s<\min\{d,d-2σ_0,d-2σ_\infty\}$。在此范围内，给出了加权不等式 $\|w_{-β_0,-β_\infty}H^{-s/2}f\|_{L^{q,v}}\lesssim \|w_{α_0,α_\infty}f\|_{L^{p,u}}$ 对 $1<p,q<\infty$、$1\le u,v\le\infty$ 成立的充要分类，覆盖符号基态指数、$q<p$ 全范围、所有单边权等式、两个标度等式及同时端点角点。标度等式由 $u\le v$ 支配（含 $q<p$ 情形）；输入或输出幂端点分别要求 $u=1$ 或 $v=\infty$；同侧幂/标度角点仅允许 $(u,v)=(1,\infty)$。

Conclusion: 该工作完整刻画了非负径向薛定谔算子分数幂 $H^{-s/2}$ 的核估计范围及其加权有界性，特别是首次处理了符号基态指数和 $q<p$ 的非对角情形，并统一了所有端点与角点情形。所用方法具有一般性，可推广到其他满足双边基态热核估计的算子。

Abstract: Let $H=-Δ+V(|x|)$ be a nonnegative radial Schrödinger operator on $\mathbb{R}^d$, $d\ge 2$, whose positive harmonic function satisfies $U(r)\simeq r^{-σ_0}$ for $0<r\le 1$ and $U(r)\simeq r^{-σ_\infty}$ for $r\ge 1$, with $-d/2<σ_0,σ_\infty<d/2$. Assuming the two-sided ground-state heat-kernel estimate of Ishige, Kabeya, and Ouhabaz, we determine the maximal open range in which the kernel of $H^{-s/2}$ admits the clean two-sided estimate $K_s^H(x,y)\simeq |x-y|^{s-d}U(|x|)U(|y|)/[U(|x|+|x-y|)U(|y|+|x-y|)]$, namely $0<s<\min\{d,d-2σ_0,d-2σ_\infty\}$. In this range we give a complete necessary-and-sufficient classification of the broken-power estimate $\|w_{-β_0,-β_\infty}H^{-s/2}f\|_{L^{q,v}}\lesssim \|w_{α_0,α_\infty}f\|_{L^{p,u}}$ for $1<p,q<\infty$ and $1\le u,v\le\infty$. The result covers signed ground-state exponents, the full range $q<p$, all one-sided weight equalities, both scale equalities, and simultaneous endpoint corners. Scale equality is governed by $u\le v$, including when $q<p$; an input or output power endpoint requires respectively $u=1$ or $v=\infty$; and at a same-side power/scale corner the only admissible pair is $(u,v)=(1,\infty)$. The proof combines clean-kernel analysis, local Lorentz-Hardy-Littlewood-Sobolev estimates, rank-one endpoint arguments, geometric annular sequence spaces, a triangular matrix theorem, and a nine-block decomposition.

</details>


### [114] [Absence of non-compactly supported minimisers for the Lieb-Oxford bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11440)
*Simone Di Marino,Rodrigue Lelotte*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了对于固定粒子数 N≥1，Lieb-Oxford 泛函下界（Lieb-Oxford bound）的极小化元（minimiser）必然具有紧支撑（compactly supported），将 Lieb 和 Oxford 的单一粒子结果推广到了多粒子情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lieb 和 Oxford 先前已证明单粒子情形下泛函下界极小化元具有紧支撑，但多粒子（N≥1）情形是否成立尚不清楚。本研究旨在填补这一空白，验证该性质对于任意固定粒子数 N 仍成立。

Method: 采用分析极值问题的变分法（variational method）与泛函分析（functional analysis）工具，对 Lieb-Oxford 泛函下界的极小化元进行理论推导，通过反证法或紧性论证证明其支撑集的有界性。

Result: 成功证明对于任意固定粒子数 N≥1，极小化元（若存在）必然具有紧支撑，将原有单粒子结论推广至多粒子系统。

Conclusion: 该结果确认了多粒子情形下 Lieb-Oxford 泛函下界极小化元的紧支撑性质，为电子密度泛函理论（density functional theory）中交换-关联泛函的数学基础提供了更坚实的支撑。

Abstract: We prove the minimisers of the Lieb-Oxford bound (if any) for a fixed (and finite) number of particles $N \geq 1$ are necessarily compactly supported, extending a result proved by E. H. Lieb and S. Oxford in the one-particle case.

</details>


### [115] [From diffusion to transmission via EDP-convergence: a paradigmatic multiscale limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11478)
*Thomas Frenzel,Alexander Mielke*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用EDP-收敛（EDP-convergence）方法，分析由自由能（free energy）和耗散势（dissipation potential）定义的梯度结构，并通过尺度化扩散系数来逼近膜上的透射条件，从而推导出有效的膜动力学关系（kinetic relation）。

Result: EDP-收敛提供了唯一确定的极限梯度结构，将透射条件重新表述为膜的有效动力学关系，该关系联系了化学势（chemical potential）的跳跃与通过膜的通量（flux）。一个令人惊讶的结果是，从Otto梯度结构中的线性昂萨格关系（Onsager relation）出发，导出了指数增长的Marcelin-De Donder动力学关系。

Conclusion: 自由能和微观扩散迁移率（mobility）的属性会迁移并影响有效的膜动力学关系。线性扩散方程对应的线性昂萨格关系在EDP-收敛极限下转变为非线性的指数型Marcelin-De Donder动力学，揭示了微观尺度到宏观动力学的非平凡映射。

Abstract: We consider nonlinear diffusion equations on an interval where the diffusion coefficient in a small region near the center is scaled such that it approximates a transmission condition at a membrane. While the limiting behavior of the solutions is well-understood, we study the convergence in the sense of the energy-dissipation principle (EDP) of associated gradient structures given in terms of a free energy and a dissipation potential.
  EDP-convergence provides a uniquely specified limiting gradient structure that reformulates the transmission condition in terms of an effective kinetic relation for the membrane, which relates the jump of the chemical potential and the flux through the membrane. We show how \AAA properties of the chosen free energy and the mobility of small-scale diffusion migrate to the effective kinetic relation. A surprising result is that starting from the linear Onsager relation of Otto's gradient structure for the linear diffusion equation, one obtains an exponentially growing kinetic relation, the so-called Marcelin-De Donder kinetic.

### [116] [On the global asymptotic stability for the 3D Peskin Problem at critical regularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11731)
*Eduardo García-Juárez,Susanna V. Haziot,Po-Chun Kuo,Yoichiro Mori,Han Zhou*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 证明三维Peskin问题的整体适定性和渐近稳定性：初始数据可在最优正则空间$W^{1,\infty}(\mathbb{S}^2)$中包含无穷多个角点，但被流动的抛物光滑效应瞬间去奇异化，最终指数收敛到经过平移和缩放后的共形球面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维Peskin问题描述浸入不可压缩Stokes流体中的闭合弹性膜，其数学分析因流体非线性产生的高度奇异多线性算子而极具挑战。本文旨在建立该问题在最优正则初始数据下的整体适定性和渐近稳定性理论。

Method: 采用球面$\mathbb{S}^2$上的谱Littlewood-Paley投影（spectral Littlewood-Paley projections）构建泛函框架，以控制来自流体非线性的高度奇异多线性算子。通过非线性估计与共形稳态的10维流形（10-dimensional manifold of conformal steady states）的精确结构解耦相结合，证明无穷维耗散扰动被严格抑制。

Result: 初始数据在$W^{1,\infty}(\mathbb{S}^2)$中可含无穷多个角点，但被流的抛物光滑效应（parabolic smoothing effect）瞬间去奇异化，对所有$t>0$变为光滑。解在$C^1$拓扑（topology）下指数收敛到平移和缩放后的共形球面（conformal sphere）。

Conclusion: 三维Peskin问题在最优正则空间中具有整体适定性和渐近稳定性，建立了从含角点初始构型到光滑共形球面的指数收敛路径，为弹性膜-流体耦合系统提供了严格的数学分析框架。

Abstract: We prove global well-posedness and asymptotic stability for the three-dimensional Peskin problem, which models a closed, elastic membrane immersed in an incompressible Stokes fluid. We work with initial data in the optimal regularity space $W^{1,\infty}(\mathbb{S}^2)$, which may contain infinitely many corners. These initial configurations are instantly desingularized by the flow's parabolic smoothing effect, becoming smooth for all $t > 0$. Then we establish that the solutions converge exponentially in the $C^1$ topology to a translated and dilated conformal sphere.
  The stability is achieved by combining our nonlinear estimates with an exact structural decoupling of the 10-dimensional manifold of conformal steady states, demonstrating that the infinite-dimensional dissipative perturbation is strictly controlled. The core of our analysis is a functional framework on the sphere $\mathbb{S}^2$ that uses spectral Littlewood-Paley projections to control the highly singular multilinear operators arising from the fluid nonlinearity

### [117] [Zeitlin truncation of a Shallow Water Quasi-Geostrophic model for planetary flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2306.15481)
*Arnout Franken,Martino Caliaro,Paolo Cifani,Bernard Geurts*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文针对球面上的浅水准地转方程（Shallow-Water Quasi Geostrophic equation），提出了一种保持 Casimir 不变量（Casimir conserved quantities）的数值方法，用于大气环流的长时程模拟；方法结合了有限维 Lie-Poisson 系统的构造与等谱时间积分器（isospectral time integrator），成功模拟了旋转诱导的急流（jet）形成等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 球面上的浅水准地转方程具有丰富的 Lie-Poisson 几何结构（Lie-Poisson structure）和无穷多个 Casimir 守恒量，但现有数值方法难以在长时程模拟中精确保持这些守恒量，从而影响模拟的长期可靠性与物理一致性。

Method: 方法分两步：首先构造一个 N 维 Lie-Poisson 系统，使其在 N → ∞ 极限下收敛到连续系统；然后利用由 Modin 和 Viviani（2020）提出的等谱时间积分器（isospectral time integrator）对有限维系统进行时间积分，从而保持 Casimir 不变量。

Result: 在全球球面上对不同 Lamb 参数（Lamb parameter）值进行模拟，观察到旋转诱导的稳健纬向急流（latitudinal jets）形成，且纬向风（zonal wind）振幅随纬度增加而减小，这与浅水大气模型的结果一致；同时计算了动能谱（kinetic energy spectra）作为未来研究的参考基准。

Conclusion: 本文发展的 Casimir 保持数值方法能够有效模拟球面上大气环流的长期演化，准确捕捉旋转效应下的急流结构，为未来相关研究提供了可靠的数值工具和参考数据。

Abstract: In this work, we consider a Shallow-Water Quasi Geostrophic equation on the sphere, as a model for global large-scale atmospheric dynamics. This equation, previously studied by Verkley (2009) and Schubert et al. (2009), possesses a rich geometric structure, called Lie-Poisson, and admits an infinite number of conserved quantities, called Casimirs. In this paper, we develop a Casimir preserving numerical method for long-time simulations of this equation. The method develops in two steps: firstly, we construct an N-dimensional Lie-Poisson system that converges to the continuous one in the limit $N \to \infty$; secondly, we integrate in time the finite-dimensional system using an isospectral time integrator, developed by Modin and Viviani (2020). We demonstrate the efficacy of this computational method by simulating a flow on the entire sphere for different values of the Lamb parameter. We particularly focus on rotation-induced effects, such as the formation of jets. In agreement with shallow water models of the atmosphere, we observe the formation of robust latitudinal jets and a decrease in the zonal wind amplitude with latitude. Furthermore, spectra of the kinetic energy are computed as a point of reference for future studies.
