### [118] [Batchelor's formula and infrared renormalization for sedimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09995)
*Mitia Duerinckx,Antoine Gloria*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文在维度d>2且满足定量去相关假设的稳态悬浮体下，通过红外重整化方法严格构造了无穷大体平均沉降速度，并验证了Batchelor公式在稀薄极限下的两粒子项修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Stokes流中长期程流体相互作用的红外发散（infrared divergence）阻碍了Batchelor公式的严格推导，本文旨在克服这一困难。

Method: 采用红外重整化（infrared renormalization）处理流体力学相互作用，将无穷大可观测分解为奇异部分和正则剩余部分；在稀薄簇展开中通过类似于反射法（method of reflections）的有限图展开孤立主导发散子结构并实现抵消。

Result: 在d>2且满足定量去相关假设的稳态悬浮体中，构造了无穷大体平均沉降速度，证明其独立于容器形状地控制大容器中粒子的相对沉降速度；并在稀薄极限下计算至两粒子项，验证了Batchelor公式。

Conclusion: 确立了Batchelor公式的严格数学基础，展示了红外重整化方法在处理流体力学长程相互作用中的有效性。

Abstract: We study the sedimentation of stationary random suspensions of rigid particles in Stokes flow. Batchelor's formula predicts the first dilute correction to the infinite-volume mean settling speed due to hydrodynamic interactions between suspended particles. A rigorous derivation has long been obstructed by the long-range nature of the Stokes flow, which gives rise to infrared divergences in the large-volume limit. In dimension $d>2$, for stationary suspensions satisfying quantitative decorrelation assumptions, we construct the infinite-volume mean settling speed and show that it governs the relative settling speed of particles in large containers, independently of the container shape. We then establish a renormalized cluster expansion of this mean settling speed in the dilute regime and compute it up to the two-particle term, thereby justifying Batchelor's formula. The proof is based on the infrared renormalization of hydrodynamic interactions. Infinite-volume observables are decomposed into an explicit singular part, carrying the non-integrable large-scale contribution, and a regular remainder controlled by elliptic estimates. The singular part is renormalized through counterterms that encode the diverging mean backflow generated by the suspension. At the level of the dilute cluster expansion, the renormalization is implemented cluster by cluster and the singular-regular decomposition is achieved through a finitary diagrammatic expansion of hydrodynamic interactions, inspired by the method of reflections, which isolates the leading divergent substructures and exposes the key cancellations.

*Xiaojian Yang,Gaocheng Liu,Kun Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非平衡湍流模拟框架仍有局限，且WPTS方法此前缺乏完整的模型方程推导及其物理机制的清晰解释；此外，该方法尚未有效拓展至壁面有界流动。

Method: 从波-粒子分解（wave-particle decomposition）视角显式推导WPTS的完整模型方程，并对各项的物理机制进行解释；将WPTS与壁面模型（wall model）耦合，以缓解近壁面网格分辨率约束。

Result: 耦合方法在粗网格上实现了对平板转捩的精确预测；在充分发展湍流区域，计算的壁面摩擦系数（skin-friction coefficient）和平均速度剖面与直接数值模拟（DNS）参考数据吻合良好，且精度在相同网格下显著优于气体动理学格式（GKS）。

Conclusion: 多尺度WPTS方法在转捩流模拟中展现出显著的应用前景。

Abstract: Recently, the wave-particle turbulence simulation (WPTS) has been proposed as a novel framework for non-equilibrium turbulence modeling and simulation. In this work, for the first time the complete model equations of WPTS are explicitly derived from the perspective of wave-particle decomposition, and the physical mechanism of each term is clearly interpreted. To extend its applicability to wall-bounded flows, the WPTS coupled with wall model is developed, and the introduction of wall model substantially alleviates the near-wall grid-resolution constraint. In the bulk region, the wave component resolves the large-scale structures, whereas the particle component accounts for subgrid-scale modeling through the non-equilibrium transport mechanism. As a result, the coupled method enables accurate predictions of the flat-plate transition on coarse-grid. In particular, the computed skin-friction coefficient and mean velocity profiles in the fully turbulent region agree well with the reference data from direct numerical simulation, and the accuracy is markedly superior to that of the gas-kinetic scheme (GKS) under the identical grid. These findings underscore the considerable promise of the multi-scale WPTS method for transitional flow simulations.

Abstract: In this paper, we provide a systematic investigation of SO(2) theory to machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) and identify the limitations of conventional SO(2) Linear architectures relative to SO(3) Clebsch-Gordan Tensor Products (CGTP). Building on these insights, we propose direct Cartesian construction and recursive Clebsch-Gordan construction of Wigner D-matrices and introduce two novel interaction building blocks. First, we propose the Edge Complex Product Basis based on Generalized Asymmetric Contraction, a new formulation for many-body expansion that directly constructs higher-order interactions on edges through complex-valued equivariant multiplications. Second, we introduce Radial Rotary Complex Attention(RRA), which enhances extrapolation performance and surpasses existing attention vector formulations. We also introduce several improvements to the Atomic Cluster Expansion module. Building on these advances, we train our models on OMat24, sAlex, and MPTrj, and introduce TECE-OAM-RRA-1.0, which achieve state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance on the Matbench Discovery.

### [121] [The Neutron Electric Dipole Moment from Lattice QCD using a Background Electric Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10606)
*Thomas Blum,Fangcheng He,Taku Izubuchi,Luchang Jin,Hiroshi Ohki,Sergey Syritsyn*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文利用2+1味畴壁费米子系综，在固定晶格间距和不同π介子质量下，通过外部静态均匀背景电场诱导的能量偏移提取中子电偶极矩（nEDM）。基于Feynman-Hellmann定理，通过时间切片拓扑荷采样替代全局拓扑荷，显著提升统计精度；并通过非厄密广义本征值问题构建基态，消除激发态污染。最终外推到物理点得到d_n = -0.0050(4)^stat(8)^sys θ̄ e fm。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子电偶极矩（nEDM）是研究强CP破坏（strong CP violation）的关键观测量，其QCD θ项诱导的贡献对理解CP对称性破缺机制具有重要意义。但晶格QCD计算中nEDM的统计精度和激发态污染问题长期存在，亟需发展更精确的提取方法。

Method: 使用2+1味畴壁费米子（domain wall fermion）系综，固定晶格间距a≈0.11 fm，在π介子质量为340、420、576 MeV下计算。通过外部静态均匀背景电场中CP破坏QCD θ项引起的能量偏移提取nEDM。基于Feynman-Hellmann定理，采用单时间切片（single time-slice）上的拓扑荷（topological charge）q_top(t)采样，而非全局拓扑荷Q_top，以大幅提升统计精度。计算背景电场变形下核子中拓扑荷密度的前向矩阵元（forward matrix element）。为消除激发态污染，通过求解非厄密广义本征值问题（non-Hermitian generalized eigenvalue problem）构造变形核子的基态。

Result: 传统正宇称投影核子算符的结果受严重激发态污染影响；新方法下不同核子插值算符（无论协变或非协变）给出一致的nEDM值。经外推到物理点，得到d_n = -0.0050(4)^stat(8)^sys θ̄ e fm，系统误差包含欧几里得时间拟合的激发态效应变化以及施加电场强度的依赖性。

Conclusion: 提出的方法显著提高了nEDM的统计精度并有效控制了激发态污染，给出了当前最可靠的θ项贡献的nEDM晶格计算结果。离散化效应、有限体积效应和手征外推等传统系统误差将在后续工作中处理。

Abstract: We present the calculation of the neutron electric dipole moment (nEDM) $d_n$ using 2+1 flavor domain wall fermion ensembles with fixed lattice spacing $a\approx 0.11\,\text{fm}$ and pion masses of 340, 420, and 576 MeV. We show that the neutron electric dipole moment can be extracted from the energy shift induced by a static uniform external background electric field in the presence of the CP-violating QCD theta-term, $\barθQ_{top}$. Motivated by the Feynman-Hellmann theorem, we employ sampling of the topological charge $q_\text{top}(t)$ on a single time-slice rather than the global topological charge $Q_\text{top}=\int q_\text{top}(t) \, dt$, which dramatically improves the statistical precision of the $θ$-induced nEDM. Key to our method is to calculate the forward matrix element of the topological charge density in the nucleon deformed by a background electric field. We find that calculation with the traditional positive parity-projected nucleon operator is subject to large excited-state contamination. To remove the contamination, we construct the ground state of the deformed nucleon by solving a non-Hermitian generalized eigenvalue problem. With this approach, we find consistent values for the nEDM when using different nucleon interpolating operators, regardless of whether they are covariant or non-covariant under chiral transformations. Finally, after extrapolating to the physical point, we obtain $d_n=-0.0050(4)^\text{stat}(8)^\text{sys}\barθ$ $e$ fm, where the systematic uncertainty includes excited-state effects estimated as variation with the Euclidean-time fits and the dependence on the strength of the electric field applied to the neutron. Conventional systematic errors like discretization, finite-volume, and chiral extrapolation effects will be addressed in future work.

</details>


### [122] [Chiral and $U(1)_A$ symmetries in background magnetic fields from lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11625)
*Heng-Tong Ding,José Javier Hernández Hernández,Dan Zhang*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文利用格点量子色动力学（lattice QCD）研究了背景磁场下QCD的手征对称性（chiral symmetry）和单态U(1)_A对称性，首次在格点QCD中通过中性扇区磁化率劈裂（susceptibility splitting）定量刻画了磁催化（magnetic catalysis）和逆磁催化（inverse magnetic catalysis）现象在对称性破缺中的对应表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在纯磁场背景下，轻夸克电荷不等导致非单态味对称性被显式破缺，中性扇区的对称性结构尚未被充分澄清。本文旨在利用格点QCD系统地研究强磁场对手征对称性和单态U(1)_A对称性的影响，并区分中性非单态轴矢对称性和单态U(1)_A对称性各自的响应。

Method: 采用固定标度（fixed-scale）(2+1) 味HISQ（highly improved staggered quark）系综，轻夸克质量设为m_l = m_s^{phys}/10，对应零磁场下π介子质量约220 MeV。通过计算中性π介子（π^0）、σ介子、δ介子等磁化率（susceptibility）之差来提取手征伙伴劈裂（chiral-partner splitting）和U(1)_A伙伴劈裂（singlet U(1)_A partner splitting），并讨论中性π介子磁化率中 disconnected 贡献的连续统约束（continuum constraint）。

Result: 低温下中性手征伙伴劈裂随磁场强度eB增大而增大（磁催化效应）；在交叉区（crossover）附近足够大的eB下劈裂减小（逆磁催化效应）。单态U(1)_A伙伴劈裂在低温区也有类似的增强，在交叉区附近大场下受到抑制，但抑制出现在更大的eB且程度比手征通道更温和。

Conclusion: 本文首次在格点QCD中实现了对背景磁场下中性扇区手征伙伴和单态U(1)_A伙伴磁化率劈裂的系统研究，为磁催化和逆磁催化现象提供了磁化率劈裂层面的定量对应。

Abstract: We study chiral symmetry and singlet $U(1)_A$ symmetry in QCD in a background magnetic field using lattice QCD. We first clarify the neutral-sector symmetry structure in a pure magnetic background, where the unequal electric charges of the light quarks explicitly reduce the non-singlet flavor symmetry. We identify the neutral-pion--sigma susceptibility difference, $χ_{π^0}-χ_σ$, as the chiral-partner splitting associated with the surviving neutral non-singlet axial symmetry, and the neutral-pion--delta susceptibility difference, $χ_{π^0}-χ_{δ^0}$, as the singlet $U(1)_A$ partner splitting. We also discuss the disconnected contribution to the neutral-pion susceptibility and its continuum constraint. Numerical results are obtained on fixed-scale $(2+1)$-flavor HISQ ensembles with $m_l=m_s^{\rm phys}/10$, corresponding to a pion mass of about $220~{\rm MeV}$ at vanishing magnetic field. We find that the neutral chiral-partner splitting increases with the magnetic field strength $eB$ at low temperature and decreases at sufficiently large $eB$ near the crossover, providing susceptibility-splitting counterparts of magnetic catalysis and inverse magnetic catalysis, respectively. The singlet $U(1)_A$ partner splitting shows an analogous low-temperature enhancement and large-field suppression near the crossover, with the suppression setting in at larger $eB$ and remaining milder than in the chiral channel. These results provide a first lattice-QCD study of neutral-sector probes of chiral and singlet $U(1)_A$ partner susceptibility splittings in background magnetic fields.

</details>

### [123] [Anisotropic Dirac-Born-Infeld Inflation with Non-Vacuum Initial States: Primordial Perturbations, Non-Gaussianity, and Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11842)
*Narges Rashidi,Maryam Roushan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究非真空初始态下的各向异性狄拉克-玻恩-因费尔德（DBI）暴胀模型，推导了曲率扰动的功率谱、双谱及等边非高斯性参数，并结合多种观测数据（Planck 2018、BK18、BAO、DESI+CMB+DESY5）约束了各向异性参数 c 和初始态参数 N_{k,0} 的可行范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有各向异性DBI暴胀模型研究多假设标准真空（Bunch-Davies）初始态，未充分探索非真空初始态对该类模型可观测信号（如功率谱、非高斯性）的影响，也缺乏与最新观测数据的系统性对比。

Method: 基于ADM（Arnowitt-Deser-Misner）形式论将作用量展开至曲率扰动的二阶和三阶，推导标量与张量功率谱、双谱及等边非线性参数 f_{NL}^{\mathrm{equil}}；采用慢滚近似（slow-roll approximation）和Bogoliubov系数引入各向异性修正与非BD初始条件；考虑中间暴胀场景结合激发态占据数 N_k 的唯象模型进行数值分析。

Result: 将模型预言与Planck2018 TT/TE/EE+lowE+lensing+BK18+BAO和DESI+CMB+DESY5数据集比较，在参数空间中找到与当前标量谱指数、张量标量比及等边非高斯性观测约束相容的区域；各向异性参数 c 与初始态参数 N_{k,0} 存在允许范围。

Conclusion: 非真空初始态的各向异性DBI暴胀模型在适当的参数区间内与当前观测数据兼容，为理解早期宇宙各向异性起源和非标准初始条件提供了可行的理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate linear and nonlinear primordial perturbations in an anisotropic Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) inflationary model with a non-vacuum initial state. Using the Arnowitt-Deser- Misner (ADM) formalism, we expand the action up to second and third order in the curvature perturbation and derive the corresponding scalar and tensor power spectra, as well as the bispectrum and the equilateral non-linearity parameter \(f_{NL}^{\mathrm{equil}}\). The effects of anisotropic corrections and non-Bunch-Davies (non-BD) initial conditions are incorporated through the slow-roll sector and Bogoliubov coefficients. For the numerical analysis, we consider an intermediate expansion scenario together with a phenomenological ansatz for the excited-state occupation number \(N_k\). By comparing the model predictions with recent observational datasets, including Planck2018 TT, TE, EE + lowE + lensing + BK18 + BAO and DESI+CMB+DESY5 data, we identify observationally viable regions in the parameter space of the model. Our analysis indicates that the anisotropic DBI scenario with non-vacuum initial conditions can remain compatible with current constraints on the scalar spectral index, tensor-to-scalar ratio, and equilateral non-Gaussianity for suitable ranges of the anisotropy parameter \(c\) and the initial-state parameter \(N_{k,0}\).

</details>


### [124] [Breaking the Dark Sector Degeneracy with Nonparametric Expansion--Growth Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11813)
*Changyu You,Rong-Gen Cai,Tao Yang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动的非参数化膨胀-增长框架，同时重建暗能量状态方程（EoS）和暗物质-暗能量耦合，解决了背景膨胀层面的简并问题。通过高斯过程（Gaussian processes）重建暗能量和相互作用历史，结合多个观测数据集，发现数据与ΛCDM模型一致，未检测到显著的暗能量动力学或暗扇区相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗能量状态方程（equation of state, EoS）与可能的暗扇区相互作用在背景膨胀层面存在简并（degeneracy）：相同的膨胀历史既可解释为随时间变化的暗能量，也可解释为与暗物质（dark matter）的能量交换，或两者的混合。现有参数化方法无法有效区分这两种物理起源。

Method: 提出一种数据驱动、非参数化的膨胀-增长（expansion–growth）框架：允许相互作用物质密度自由演化，将耦合项纳入线性物质扰动方程（linear matter perturbation equation），并利用高斯过程（Gaussian processes）同时重建膨胀历史和增长历史。超参数通过贝叶斯方法边缘化（marginalized）。

Result: 在红移范围 $0\lesssim z\lesssim 2$ 内，重建的暗能量状态方程 $w_{\rm de}(z)$ 和相互作用历史均与ΛCDM极限一致。未发现具有统计显著性的非零相互作用或暗能量动力学证据。

Conclusion: 建立了一种针对耦合暗扇区的膨胀-增长一致性检验（expansion–growth consistency test），提供了一条模型无关（model-independent）的路径，用以区分真正的暗能量动力学与有效的暗扇区能量交换。

Abstract: The dark energy equation of state (EoS) and a possible dark-sector interaction are degenerate at the level of background expansion: the same expansion history may be interpreted as time-varying dark energy, energy exchange with dark matter, or a mixture of both. We introduce a data-driven, nonparametric expansion--growth framework that breaks this degeneracy by simultaneously reconstructing the dark energy EoS and the dark-sector coupling. Allowing the interacting matter density to evolve freely, we incorporate the coupling into the linear matter perturbation equation and reconstruct the expansion and growth histories using Gaussian processes, with hyperparameters marginalized in a Bayesian treatment. Applying this method to Pantheon+, cosmic chronometers, BAO measurements including DESI DR2, and redshift-space-distortion data, we infer both $w_{\rm de}(z)$ and the interaction history over $0\lesssim z\lesssim 2$, without assuming either a parametric EoS or a prescribed interaction form. We find no statistically significant evidence for either a nonzero interaction or dark energy dynamics: the reconstructed coupling and dark energy EoS remain consistent with the $Λ$CDM limit. Our results establish an expansion--growth consistency test for coupled dark-sector physics and provide a model-independent route to distinguish genuine dark energy dynamics from effective dark-sector energy exchange.

</details>


### [125] [Anisotropic separate universe : Long-wavelength perturbations and conserved quantities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11814)
*Daiki Saito,Atsushi Naruko*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在均匀-𝒩规范下，利用空间梯度展开方法，将各向同性FLRW宇宙中已知的“分离宇宙（separate-universe）”图像推广到各向异性背景，推导出超视界尺度的完整解，并建立了曲率扰动与各向异性膨胀之间的耦合关系，同时给出了各向异性版本的δN形式论以及曲率扰动与原初引力波之间的显式关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解各向异性背景（anisotropic background）下线性扰动的长波演化，并推广各向同性FLRW宇宙中成熟的分离宇宙图像及δN形式论（δN formalism）到旋转对称性破缺的情形。

Method: 采用均匀-𝒩规范（uniform-𝒩 gauge）中的空间梯度展开（spatial gradient expansion），推导超视界（superhorizon）解，并将其与均匀各向异性背景的无穷小变分建立对应关系；通过标量场、背景剪切（shear）和规范场倾斜（gauge-field tilt）三个守恒通道分析曲率扰动演化。

Result: 建立了各向异性背景下超视界方程的自洽系统，识别出推广各向同性宇宙中守恒Wronskian量的守恒量；发现曲率扰动的超视界模由三个独立的守恒通道（标量场、背景剪切、规范场倾斜）及一个来自各向异性几何的动力剪切贡献共同决定；推导出曲率扰动与原初引力波（primordial gravitational waves）之间的显式关系。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架为预测原初标量和张量扰动中的统计各向异性（statistical anisotropies）提供了实用基础，揭示了各向异性背景下曲率扰动演化的内在丰富性，并给出了从视界穿越（horizon-crossing）涨落直接计算最终曲率扰动的实用方案。

Abstract: We investigate the long-wavelength evolution of linear perturbations in a homogeneous and anisotropic background with a scalar field coupled to a vector field. Using the spatial gradient expansion in the uniform-$\mathcal{N}$ gauge in which the number of $e$-folds is unperturbed, we derive the complete set of superhorizon solutions and establish their correspondence with infinitesimal variations of the homogeneous anisotropic background. This extends the separate-universe picture, previously known for isotropic FLRW cosmology, to anisotropic spacetimes despite the mixing of scalar, vector, and tensor perturbations induced by broken rotational symmetry.
  We show that the long-wavelength equations form a self-consistent system and identify a conserved quantity that generalizes the conserved Wronskian of isotropic cosmology. Unlike the isotropic case, the superhorizon modes sourcing the curvature perturbation are governed by three independent conserved channels associated with the scalar field, the background shear, and the gauge-field tilt, together with an additional dynamical shear contribution originating from the anisotropic geometry. This reveals that the evolution of curvature perturbations around anisotropic background is intrinsically richer than in isotropic multi-field models.
  Our formulation provides a practical prescription for computing the final curvature perturbation directly from horizon-crossing fluctuations, thereby establishing the anisotropic generalization of the $δN$ formalism. We further derive an explicit relation between curvature perturbations and primordial gravitational waves, demonstrating how anisotropic expansion couples scalar and tensor sectors on superhorizon scales. Our framework provides a practical basis for predicting statistical anisotropies in primordial scalar and tensor perturbations.

</details>


### [126] [Reconstructing the kinematics of Laniakea using Type Ia Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11860)
*Francesco Sorrenti,Erick Pastén,Leonardo Giani*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个运动学框架，将光度距离（luminosity distance）的单极、偶极和四极与描述拉尼亚凯亚超星系团（Laniakea supercluster）动力学的椭球性本动速度场（ellipsoidal peculiar velocity field）联系起来。通过正确考虑CMB和拉尼亚凯亚参考系之间的变换，并选取超星系团体积内的Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae），证明光度距离多极可以编码本地速度场的膨胀与剪切，从而直接从超新星观测推断拉尼亚凯亚的椭球运动学。研究结果为拉尼亚凯亚动力学主导区域内的光度距离各向异性提供了物理动机明确的解释，并表明未来超新星观测能够独立重建本地宇宙中的大尺度结构（large-scale structures）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观测已发现光度距离存在各向异性，但这些各向异性与大尺度结构（如拉尼亚凯亚超星系团）之间的物理联系尚未被清晰建立。本文旨在提供一个运动学框架，将光度距离多极与拉尼亚凯亚本动速度场的椭球膨胀和剪切直接关联，从而为这些各向异性提供物理解释。

Method: 构建了一个运动学框架，将光度距离的多极展开（单极、偶极、四极）与描述拉尼亚凯亚超星系团的椭球性本动速度场相联系。通过正确完成CMB参考系与拉尼亚凯亚参考系之间的坐标变换，并选取拉尼亚凯亚体积内的Ia型超新星观测数据，推导出光度距离多极对本地速度场膨胀与剪切参数的编码关系。

Result: 结果表明，光度距离的多极（monopole, dipole, quadrupole）能够编码拉尼亚凯亚超星系团本地速度场的膨胀与剪切信息，使得该超星系团的椭球运动学可以直接从超新星观测中推断出来。该框架为拉尼亚凯亚动力学主导体积内的光度距离各向异性提供了物理解释。

Conclusion: 本文建立的框架表明，未来更丰富的超新星观测数据有望实现对本地宇宙大尺度结构的独立重建，从而将光度距离各向异性作为研究宇宙大尺度运动学的有效探针。

Abstract: We develop a kinematic framework that relates the monopole, dipole, and quadrupole of the luminosity distance to an ellipsoidal peculiar velocity field describing the dynamics of the Laniakea supercluster. By properly accounting for the transformations between the CMB and Laniakea reference frames and selecting Type Ia supernovae within the volume associated with the superstructure, we show that luminosity distance multipoles encode the expansion and shear of the local velocity field. This allows the ellipsoidal kinematics of Laniakea to be inferred directly from supernova observations.
  Our results provide a physically motivated interpretation of luminosity distance anisotropies within the volume dynamically dominated by Laniakea as signatures of its large-scale kinematics. The framework developed here suggests that future supernova observations can enable the independent reconstruction of large-scale structures in the local Universe

</details>

### [127] [An Autonomous Scientific Knowledge Generation Framework for AI-Driven Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09806)
*Dibakar Datta*

Main category: cs.DL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自主科学知识生成框架（Autonomous Scientific Knowledge Generation Framework），该框架能将科学出版物转化为统一且AI就绪的结构化知识库。作为概念验证，该框架被应用于电光材料领域，从约1000篇出版物中提取并整合出7条规范化科学记录，展示了从非结构化文献到AI可用知识库的完整转化流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据库加速了数据驱动的材料研究，但预测建模和逆向设计所需的大量知识仍以非结构化形式存在于科学文献中，这从根本上限制了人工智能（AI）在科学发现中的有效性。

Method: 该框架整合了本体引导的文献获取（ontology-guided literature acquisition）、混合科学知识抽取（hybrid scientific knowledge extraction）、语义对齐（semantic harmonization）、知识融合（knowledge fusion）以及验证（validation）等步骤，构成一个统一的工作流，逐步将科学出版物转化为结构化、语义一致且保留来源信息的知识。

Result: 在电光材料（electro-optic materials）的概念验证中，框架自主检索并验证了约1000篇出版物；其中8篇出版物经完整工作流处理后生成29条结构化科学记录，最终融合为7条规范化科学记录。

Conclusion: 该框架证明了从科学文献到AI就绪知识库的完整转化能力，保留了定量测量数据、操作条件、来源信息和科学上下文，为预测性AI、生成式AI及闭环AI驱动科学发现提供了可扩展、领域无关的基础。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is transforming scientific discovery, but its effectiveness is fundamentally limited by the availability of structured scientific knowledge. Although existing databases have accelerated data-driven materials research, much of the knowledge needed for predictive modeling and inverse design remains embedded in unstructured scientific literature. We present an Autonomous Scientific Knowledge Generation Framework that transforms scientific publications into a Unified AI-Ready Scientific Knowledge Base. The framework integrates ontology-guided literature acquisition, hybrid scientific knowledge extraction, semantic harmonization, knowledge fusion, and validation within a unified workflow. Rather than treating literature retrieval, information extraction, and database construction as separate tasks, the framework progressively converts scientific publications into structured, semantically consistent, and provenance-preserving knowledge suitable for AI-driven reasoning. As a proof of concept, the framework was applied to electro-optic materials. Autonomous literature acquisition retrieved and validated about 1,000 publications from multiple scholarly repositories. A representative subset of eight publications was processed through the complete workflow, generating 29 structured scientific records that were harmonized into 7 canonical scientific records. The results demonstrate the complete transformation from scientific literature to an AI-ready scientific knowledge base while preserving quantitative measurements, operating conditions, provenance, and scientific context. The proposed framework provides a scalable, domain-independent foundation for predictive AI, generative AI, and closed-loop AI-driven scientific discovery.

### [128] [On Orbifold Quantum Cohomology of Foldings of $ADE$ Resolutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11766)
*Jingxiang Ma*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文计算了Kleinian奇点极小分解的特定有限循环商（称为折叠）的$\mathbb{C}^\times$-等变轨形量子上同调（$\mathbb{C}^\times$-equivariant orbifold quantum cohomology）的非扭曲部分，基于Crepant Resolution Conjecture（对偶分解猜想）提出了完整等变轨形量子上同调的猜想并给出两项证据，同时将得到的Frobenius结构（Frobenius structure）与相应非单李根系（non-simply-laced root system）相关的已知Frobenius结构进行了等同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于Crepant Resolution Conjecture（对偶分解猜想），旨在将Kleinian奇点极小分解（minimal resolutions of Kleinian singularities）的特定有限循环商（即折叠，foldings）的$\mathbb{C}^\times$-等变轨形量子上同调（$\mathbb{C}^\times$-equivariant orbifold quantum cohomology）与已知的Frobenius结构（Frobenius structure）建立联系。

Method: 首先计算了折叠（foldings）非扭曲部分（untwisted part）的$\mathbb{C}^\times$-等变轨形量子上同调，接着基于Crepant Resolution Conjecture提出了完整等变轨形量子上同调的猜想，并提供了两项支持性证据。

Result: 得到了非扭曲部分的显式计算；提出了完整等变轨形量子上同调的猜想并给出两项支持证据；将所得Frobenius结构与对应于非单李根系（non-simply-laced root system）的已知Frobenius结构进行了等同。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了Kleinian奇点折叠的等变轨形量子上同调与非单李根系Frobenius结构之间的深层联系，为Crepant Resolution Conjecture在相关情形下提供了新的支持。

Abstract: We compute the untwisted part of the $\mathbb{C}^\times$-equivariant orbifold quantum cohomology of certain finite cyclic quotients of the minimal resolutions of Kleinian singularities, which we refer to as their foldings. We then formulate a conjecture for the full $\mathbb{C}^\times$-equivariant orbifold quantum cohomology, motivated by the Crepant Resolution Conjecture, and provide two pieces of supporting evidence. We also identify the resulting Frobenius structure with known Frobenius structures associated with the corresponding non-simply-laced root systems.

### [129] [Higher-order interactions for controlling time-delayed Kuramoto model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10759)
*Narumi Fujii,Martin Moriamé,Maxime Lucas,Hiroya Nakao,Timoteo Carletti*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 提出一种基于高阶无延迟近似的框架，用于控制含时间延迟的Kuramoto模型集体动力学；通过Ott–Antonsen假设和二阶平均法得到序参量的一维约化方程，数值模拟表明该近似比传统两两近似更准确，并实现了双稳态和中间同步态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间延迟（time delay）广泛存在于振子网络（oscillator networks）的相互作用中，但传统两两近似（pairwise approximation）无法准确描述延迟耦合下的集体动力学，制约了对同步行为的控制和预测。

Method: 基于高阶无延迟近似（delay-free, higher-order approximation）替代延迟相互作用；运用Ott–Antonsen假设（Ott–Antonsen ansatz）和二阶平均法（second-order averaging method）将得到的高阶Kuramoto模型约化为序参量（order parameter）的一维动力学方程。

Result: 数值模拟表明，该高阶近似对原延迟系统动力学的预测精度优于传统两两近似，并能够实现双稳态（bistability）和中间同步状态（intermediate synchronization states）。

Conclusion: 高阶解释（higher-order interpretations）时间延迟的方法能有效控制具有时滞相互作用的振子网络，为延迟耦合系统的同步调控提供了新途径。

Abstract: We propose a framework for controlling the collective dynamics of the time-delayed Kuramoto model based on a delay-free, higher-order approximation of the delayed interactions. By applying the Ott--Antonsen ansatz and the second-order averaging method to the resulting higher-order Kuramoto model, we obtain a one-dimensional reduced equation for the order parameter dynamics. Numerical simulations demonstrate that the higher-order approximation predicts the dynamics of the original delayed system more accurately than the conventional pairwise approximation and enables the realization of bistability and intermediate synchronization states. Our results demonstrate the effectiveness of higher-order interpretations of time delays for the control of oscillator networks with time-delayed interactions.

</details>

### [130] [Landau-Zener tunneling and quantum interference of Andreev states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09859)
*Mikhail S. Kalenkov,Andrei D. Zaikin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 基于微观理论推导了非平衡超导纳米结中安德烈夫态（Andreev states）的有效哈密顿量，通过求解类薛定谔方程得到波函数并计算电流，发现量子干涉可在约瑟夫森相位（Josephson phase）下产生明显的超流（supercurrent）相干振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非平衡条件下超导纳米结（superconducting nanojunction）中安德烈夫态（Andreev states）的量子动力学行为，并探索其对电流输运的影响。

Method: 基于微观理论（microscopic theory）推导出控制非平衡超导纳米结中安德烈夫态的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），并通过求解类薛定谔方程（Schrödinger-like equation）获得安德烈夫能级（Andreev levels）的“波函数”，进而评估在外加电压偏置（external voltage bias）下的结电流。

Result: 发现当势垒透射率（barrier transmission）略低于1时，安德烈夫态的量子干涉（quantum interference）可在约瑟夫森相位（Josephson phase）下产生显著的超流（supercurrent）相干振荡（coherent oscillations）。

Conclusion: 该新效应预期在具有扩散势垒（diffusive barriers）的结中也有进一步的应用意义。

Abstract: With the aid of a microscopic theory we derive an effective Hamiltonian that controls quantum dynamics of Andreev states in superconducting nanojunctions out of equilibrium. Resolving the corresponding Schrödinger-like equation we obtain the "wave functions" for Andreev levels and evaluate electric current across the junction in the presence of an external voltage bias. We demonstrate that quantum interference of Andreev states may yield pronounced coherent oscillations of the supercurrent as a function of the Josephson phase in junctions with barrier transmissions slightly below unity. Further implications of this novel effect are expected for junctions with diffusive barriers.

</details>


### [131] [Superconducting dome and field-enhanced superconductivity of PLD synthesized Nd1-xEuxNiO2 thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10332)
*Wenlong Yang,Qiang Zhao,Xingke Fu,Gaofei Ren,Zhongjing Wu,Zhen Chen,Jianping Sun,Boseng Wang,Jiacai Nie,Pengtao Yang,Jinguang Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了利用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition, PLD）结合CaH₂拓扑还原法成功合成无限层结构Nd₁₋ₓEuₓNiO₂薄膜。PLD制备的薄膜在掺杂范围0.2<x<0.5内呈现超导穹顶（superconducting dome），其中x=0.3样品的最优超导转变温度Tc约为31 K，显著高于其他真空外延技术生长的薄膜。磁输运测量在欠掺杂和过掺杂区域均发现了稳健的场增强及重入超导现象（field-enhanced and re-entrant superconductivity），而霍尔电阻的非线性行为可能源于磁性杂质散射。这些结果揭示了磁性Eu²⁺离子在产生无限层镍酸盐奇异物理性质中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同合成方法（特别是PLD）对无限层镍酸盐薄膜质量及超导性能的影响，并理解磁性稀土离子（Eu²⁺）在产生该体系奇异物理性质中的作用机制。

Method: 采用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition, PLD）技术制备Nd₁₋ₓEuₓNiO₂薄膜，随后通过CaH₂进行拓扑还原（topotactic reduction）以获得无限层结构；利用电阻测量和磁输运测量（magneto-transport measurements）表征薄膜的超导及输运性质。

Result: PLD制备的薄膜在0.2<x<0.5掺杂范围内呈现超导穹顶，其宽度优于分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）方法，与化学合成相当；x=0.3样品的超导转变温度Tc约31 K，为真空外延技术中的最高值；在欠掺杂和过掺杂区域均观察到场增强及重入超导现象；低温和接近超导起始温度时，霍尔电阻表现出非线性行为。

Conclusion: PLD是制备高质量、高Tc的Nd₁₋ₓEuₓNiO₂超导薄膜的理想方法；磁性Eu²⁺离子在无限层镍酸盐的奇异物理性质（如场增强和重入超导）中发挥着关键作用。

Abstract: We report on the synthesis of infinite-layer Nd1-xEuxNiO2 (0<x<0.7) thin films using pulsed laser deposition (PLD) followed by topotactic reduction with CaH2. Resistivity measurements on these films reveal a superconducting dome within the doping range 0.2<x<0.5, which is wider than that achieved by molecular beam epitaxy and comparable to that obtained by chemical synthesis. The x=0.3 PLD film exhibits the optimal superconducting transition temperature Tc~31 K, much higher than those grown by other vacuum epitaxial techniques. This result indicates that PLD is an ideal approach for fabricating high-quality, high-Tc Nd1-xEuxNiO2 superconducting films. Magneto-transport measurements reveal robust field-enhanced and re-entrant superconductivity in both underdoped and overdoped regimes. At low temperatures just above the onset Tc, the Hall resistance exhibits nonlinear behavior, which may originate from magnetic impurity scattering. These results highlight the crucial role of magnetic rare-earth Eu2+ ions in producing the exotic physical properties of the infinite-layer nickelates.

### [132] [Anomalous field evolution of the mixed-state linewidth in the second superconducting dome of LaFeAsO$_{1-x}M_x$ ($M={\rm F,H}$)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10348)
*Rustem Khasanov,Pierre Dalmas de Réotier,Samuele Sanna,Gianrico Lamura,Hubertus Luetkens,Matteo Moroni,Pietro Carretta,Rhea Kappenberger,Rowena Wachtel,Bernd Büchner,Sabine Wurmehl,Nikolai D. Zhigadlo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文利用μSR技术测量了LaFeAsO$_{1-x}M_x$（M=F, H）家族中两个超导穹顶（SC1与SC2）代表性样品的混合态内部场分布。研究发现SC2样品在3T附近出现反常的局域最大超导线宽，与增强的Pauli顺磁效应相关，揭示了两个超导穹顶的不同电子特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LaFeAsO$_{1-x}M_x$（$M={\rm F,H}$）家族中两个超导穹顶（SC1与SC2）的混合态内部场分布差异，从而揭示其不同的超导配对机制和电子特性。

Method: 采用横向场μ子自旋旋转/弛豫（transverse-field muon-spin rotation/relaxation, μSR）技术，测量LaFeAsO$_{0.89}$F$_{0.11}$（SC1）和LaFeAsO$_{0.75}$H$_{0.25}$（SC2）两种样品的内部场分布线宽。

Result: 两种样品在超导转变温度$T_{\rm c}$以下均出现内部场分布线宽增大，表明涡旋晶格（vortex lattice）形成；$T_{\rm c}$以上线宽呈各向异性Knight shift导致的场依赖。扣除正常态贡献后，SC1样品在4K时超导线宽$σ_{\rm sc}$随场增强单调下降，而SC2样品在3T附近出现明显的局域极大值，且该极大值对应的场强位置$H_{σ,\max}(T)$随升温向低场移动并趋近$T_{\rm c}$时消失。

Conclusion: SC2样品中观测到的反常场演化行为与增强的Pauli顺磁效应（Pauli-paramagnetic effects）贡献一致，突出了两个超导穹顶不同的电子特性本质。

Abstract: We report a transverse-field muon-spin rotation/relaxation ($μ$SR) study of the internal-field distribution in the mixed state of LaFeAsO$_{0.89}$F$_{0.11}$ and LaFeAsO$_{0.75}$H$_{0.25}$, representative of the first (SC1) and second (SC2) superconducting domes of the LaFeAsO$_{1-x}M_x$ ($M={\rm F,H}$) family, respectively. Below the superconducting transition temperature $T_{\rm c}$, the linewidth of the internal-field distribution increases in both samples, indicating the formation of a vortex lattice. Above $T_{\rm c}$, the linewidth remains field dependent and increases approximately linearly with field, consistent with broadening of the powder spectrum caused by an anisotropic Knight shift. After subtraction of this normal-state contribution, the superconducting linewidth $σ_{\rm sc}$ exhibits qualitatively different field dependences in the two samples. At 4K, the SC1 ($x_{\rm F}=0.11$) sample shows the expected monotonic decrease with increasing field, whereas the SC2 ($x_{\rm H}=0.25$) sample develops a pronounced local maximum near 3T. A contour representation of $σ_{\rm sc}(T,H)$ further reveals a ridge of local maxima whose field position, $H_{σ,\max}(T)$, shifts to lower fields upon warming and disappears near $T_{\rm c}$. The anomalous field evolution observed in the SC2 sample is consistent with an additional field-induced contribution associated with enhanced Pauli-paramagnetic effects, highlighting the distinct electronic character of the two superconducting domes.

</details>


### [133] [Effect of superconducting fluctuations on nonreciprocal dichroism and gyrotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10464)
*Alex Levchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过含时金兹堡-朗道理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory），研究了二维非中心对称超导体在临界温度以上由涨落诱导库珀对（fluctuation-induced Cooper pairs）产生的非互易空间色散电导率，计算了回旋电导率（gyrotropic conductivity）的阿斯马拉佐夫-拉金贡献（Aslamazov-Larkin contribution），并分析了其频率依赖、温度增强行为及与超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect）的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示非中心对称超导体中涨落效应如何产生非互易（nonreciprocal）且波矢奇函数（odd-in-wavevector）的光电响应，并探索其在临界温度附近的增强机制。

Method: 采用推广至包含粒子-空穴不对称性（particle-hole asymmetry）和三角超导体三次李夫希兹不变量（cubic Lifshitz invariant）的含时金兹堡-朗道理论，解析计算了回旋电导率的阿斯马拉佐夫-拉金贡献的闭合形式及其完整频率依赖关系。

Result: 耗散部分描述非互易方向二色性（nonreciprocal directional dichroism），在频率上呈奇函数且非单调，峰值出现在库珀对衰减率量级的频率处；其克拉默斯-克勒尼希对偶分量描述回旋双折射（gyrotropic birefringence），在静态极限下有限且随温度趋近T_c而强烈增强。两种效应均依赖于同时破缺反演对称性（inversion symmetry）和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）以及粒子-空穴不对称性。

Conclusion: 涨落诱导的临界增强主导平滑的正常态回旋效应，该机制与超导二极管效应及近T_c处巨磁手征各向异性（giant magnetochiral anisotropy）源于相同的非对称库珀对色散；研究结果为利用氮-空位中心量子噪声谱学（nitrogen-vacancy-center quantum noise spectroscopy）探测门控过渡金属硫族化合物（如MoS₂）中的超导动力学提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study the spatially dispersive conductivity of a two-dimensional noncentrosymmetric superconductor, demonstrating that it acquires a nonreciprocal, odd-in-wavevector component from fluctuation-induced Cooper pairs above the critical temperature $T_c$. Utilizing time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory generalized to include particle-hole asymmetry and the cubic Lifshitz invariant of trigonal superconductors, we compute the Aslamazov-Larkin contribution to the gyrotropic conductivity in closed form, including its complete frequency dependence. The dissipative part describes nonreciprocal directional dichroism: it is odd in frequency and displays a nonmonotonic dependence, peaking at frequencies comparable to the decay rate of fluctuating Cooper pairs. Its Kramers-Kronig dual component describes gyrotropic birefringence, which remains finite in the static limit and is strongly enhanced as the temperature approaches $T_c$. Both effects require simultaneously broken inversion and time-reversal symmetries, are dependent on particle-hole asymmetry in close analogy to the fluctuation Hall effect, and trace to the same asymmetric Cooper-pair dispersion responsible for the superconducting diode effect and the giant magnetochiral anisotropy observed near $T_c$. This critical enhancement dominates over the smooth normal-state gyrotropy, which we evaluate for the same band model as a baseline. Finally, we frame our analysis within the context of gated transition metal dichalcogenides like MoS$_2$, discussing the implications for probing superconducting dynamics through nitrogen-vacancy-center quantum noise spectroscopy.

</details>


### [134] [Soft point-contact Andreev reflection spectroscopy in a palm-type cubic anvil-pressure cell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10668)
*Qingxin Dong,Fengrui Shi,Yan Zhang,Tong Shi,Yi Liu,Shaoheng Ruan,Zhongjin Wu,Jianping Sun,Zhaoming Tian,Yoshiya Uwatoko,Guanghan Cao,Xin Lu,Bosen Wang,Jin-Guang Cheng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过将基底锚定策略与外部分线技术相结合，在掌式立方砧压力单元中实现了软点接触安德烈夫反射谱（PCARS），可在最高15 GPa的静水压下稳定形成多个点接触结。对超导元素Nb的基准测量显示出高可重复性，得到零温超导能隙及能隙比3.3。进一步将该技术应用于Kagome金属超导体CsCrSb5和双层镍酸盐超导体La2PrNi2O7，观测到显著的零偏压电导峰，并研究了其随温度、磁场和压力的演化，提供了支持非常规超导电性的谱学证据。该工作建立了一个连接宏观电输运与微观谱学探针的稳健实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高压超导研究多依赖宏观电输运测量，但缺乏在高压条件下直接获取微观谱学信息（如配对对称性）的有效实验手段。为突破这一技术瓶颈，需要开发一种能在高压环境中稳定实现点接触安德烈夫反射谱测量的实验方案。

Method: 采用基底锚定策略与外部分线技术，在掌式立方砧压力单元中构建软点接触安德烈夫反射谱（PCARS）装置；通过金属Nb进行基准测试验证系统可靠性；随后将技术应用于CsCrSb5和La2PrNi2O7等非常规超导体，测量其谱学特征及随温度、磁场和压力的演化。

Result: 成功在最高15 GPa静水压下实现多个点接触结的稳定形成；Nb基准测试获得零温超导能隙及能隙比3.3，验证了高可重复性；在CsCrSb5和La2PrNi2O7中观测到显著的零偏压电导峰，并获得了其随温度、磁场和压力演化的谱学数据。

Conclusion: 该技术为高压条件下研究非常规超导体的配对对称性提供了谱学证据支持的实验平台，填补了宏观电输运与微观谱学探针之间的技术鸿沟，为系统研究压力诱导非常规超导体的配对机制开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We have implemented soft point-contact Andreev reflection spectroscopy (PCARS) in a palm-type cubic anvil pressure cell by combining a substrate anchoring strategy with an external wire-splitting technique. This design enables the stable formation of multiple point contact junctions under hydrostatic pressures up to 15 GPa. Benchmark measurements on the elemental superconductor Nb demonstrate high reproducibility and yield a zero-temperature superconducting gap with a gap ratio of 3.3. We further apply this technique to the Kagome metal superconductor CsCr3Sb5 and the bilayer nickelate superconductor La2PrNi2O7. Pronounced zero-bias conductance peaks are observed, and their evolution with temperature, magnetic field and applied pressure is investigated, together with the superconducting gap magnitude and possible pairing symmetries. These measurements provide spectroscopic evidence consistent with unconventional superconductivity in these materials. Our work establishes a robust experimental platform that bridges macroscopic electrical transport and microscopic spectroscopic probes, opening a new avenue for investigating pairing symmetry in a wide range of pressure-induced unconventional superconductors.

</details>


### [135] [Evolution from an acoustic-plasmon-mediated superconductivity to an acoustic-phonon-mediated superconductivity in bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10835)
*Shuyang Wang,Sankar Das Sarma,Jay D. Sau*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本论文利用Eliashberg理论重新审视了由轻层（LL）和重层（HL）组成的双层体系中的声学等离激元（acoustic plasmon）超导机制，通过随机相位近似（RPA）建模了层间屏蔽相互作用，并系统研究了从声学等离激元介导超导到声子介导超导的演化过程，同时分析了非绝热效应对任意质量比的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受范德瓦尔斯异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）最新实验进展的启发，作者希望重新探讨双层体系中声学等离激元超导机制的理论基础，并澄清从等离激元超导到声子超导的连续过渡行为。

Method: 采用Eliashberg理论（Eliashberg theory）描述超导配对，通过随机相位近似（random phase approximation, RPA）计算双层体系中的屏蔽相互作用（screened interaction），并引入频率截断（frequency cut off）参数系统研究非绝热（nonadiabatic）效应对任意质量比的影响。

Result: 当重层质量从轻层电子质量的几个数量级范围内变化时，超导临界温度 $T_c$ 连续演化：较低重层质量对应双层声学等离激元机制；较重质量极限接近玻恩-奥本海默（Born-Oppenheimer）框架下的声学声子介导的强延迟配对，并满足米格达尔定理（Migdal's theorem）。论文给出了 $T_c$ 作为频率截断函数的定量关系。

Conclusion: 该研究系统揭示了双层体系中从声学等离激元超导到声子超导的连续过渡图像，并通过频率截断方法统一处理了任意质量比下的非绝热效应，为理解范德瓦尔斯异质结中的超导机制提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Motivated by recent developments in van der Waals heterostructures, we revisit the acoustic plasmon mechanism of superconductivity in bilayer systems composed of a light layer (LL) and heavy layer (HL) by employing Eliashberg theory. The exchange of virtual plasmons in the HL can lead to a retarded in time attractive interaction between electrons of LL that we model through the screened interaction in the bilayer system within the random phase approximation. We explore the evolution from acoustic plasmon mediated superconductivity to phonon mediated superconductivity by studying the evolution of $T_c$ as the HL mass is increased by a few orders of magnitude compared with the electronic mass in LL. The lower HL mass corresponds to the bilayer acoustic plasmon, while the latter regime is closer to the Born-Oppenheimer regime of acoustic phonon mediated strongly retarded pairing. The heavy HL mass limit is known to obey Migdal's theorem by virtue of the small ratio of the two individual layer masses. We study the nonadiabatic effects for the arbitrary mass ratio with no small parameter systematically by using a frequency cut off in the Eliashberg theory, providing $T_c$ as a function of this cut off.

</details>


### [136] [A minimal model for the Weyl nodes and Fermi arcs of PtBi$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10937)
*Tobias Cristófoli,Manuel Alonso Lemos,Jorge I. Facio,Pablo S. Cornaglia*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文基于密度泛函理论（DFT）计算和对称性约束，为三角PtBi₂发展了低能能带的最小描述模型，该模型捕捉了Weyl节点随自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的演化、节点湮灭及表面费米弧（Fermi arcs）的自旋-动量锁定，为理解该材料中的表面超导性提供了微观基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Weyl半金属（Weyl semimetals）在表面拥有拓扑保护的费米弧（Fermi arcs），三角PtBi₂中已观察到与费米弧相关的超导迹象，但此前的理论描述依赖于与材料微观电子结构无直接关联的有效模型，缺乏第一性原理指导的微观描述。

Method: 以密度泛函理论（DFT）计算为指导，在相关晶体对称性和时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetries）的完全约束下，建立用于描述低能能带的最小模型。

Result: 该模型捕捉了Weyl节点随自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的演化，包括节点湮灭过程；能够描述表面费米弧（Fermi arcs）的自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking），并再现了PtBi₂的轨道成分（orbital content）和能带拓扑（band topology）。

Conclusion: 所发展的模型为后续研究提供了微观起点，有助于进一步理解PtBi₂中的表面超导性（surface superconductivity）等物理现象。

Abstract: Weyl semimetals host topologically protected Fermi arcs on their surfaces, originating from the Chern number of the bulk Weyl nodes. In trigonal PtBi$_2$, superconducting signatures have been associated with the Fermi arcs. Theoretical descriptions of this surface superconductivity have so far relied on effective models that are not directly tied to the microscopic electronic structure of the material. In this work we develop a minimal description of the low-energy bands guided by density functional theory calculations and fully constrained by the relevant crystalline and time-reversal symmetries. The model captures the evolution of the Weyl nodes with spin-orbit coupling, including node annihilations, and is able to describe the spin-momentum locking of the surface Fermi arcs. It reproduces the orbital content and the band topology of PtBi$_2$ and provides a starting point for further studies.

</details>


### [137] [Ferroelectric--Superconducting Interaction in Epitaxial YBa2Cu3O7-δ/BaTiO3 Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11003)
*Louis Oppong-Antwi,David L. Cortie,Qi Zhang,Avi Bendavid,Nagarajan Valanoor,Wendy Purches,Golrokh Akhgar*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过实验证实了在BaTiO3/YBa2Cu3O7-δ异质结构中，铁电体邻近效应会显著降低超导层的临界温度，并强调了多技术表征手段对揭示铁电-超导耦合微妙特征的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微观理论预测铁电体邻近效应可强烈改变超导层的临界温度，但此前缺乏实验证据。因此，本研究旨在通过精确生长的铁电/超导异质结构实验验证这一耦合效应。

Method: 利用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition, PLD）在SrTiO3 (001)衬底上制备BaTiO3 (BTO)/YBa2Cu3O7-δ (YBCO)异质结构，精确控制生长条件和氧化学计量；采用压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy, PFM）确认铁电开关特性，中子反射测量（neutron reflectometry）评估埋藏界面粗糙度，并通过电阻与磁化测量表征超导转变温度。

Result: 单层YBCO的电阻超导转变温度约为86 K，磁化测量转变温度约为80–85 K；而相同条件下生长的YBCO/BTO/YBCO异质结构的电阻与磁化转变温度分别降至约75 K和约55 K，且整体磁化率（susceptibility）降低。

Conclusion: 研究证实了BTO/YBCO异质结构中存在铁电-超导耦合效应，该体系有望用于可调氧化物电子学（tunable oxide electronics）和可重构超导器件（reconfigurable superconducting devices）。

Abstract: Microscopic theories predict that the critical temperature of a superconducting layer can be strongly modified in proximity to a ferroelectric; however, experimental evidence is lacking. We report on BaTiO3 (BTO)/YBa2Cu3O7-δ (YBCO) heterostructures grown on SrTiO3 (001) substrates using pulsed laser deposition (PLD), with precise control of growth conditions and oxygen stoichiometry. Piezoresponse force microscopy confirms ferroelectric switching within both single-layer and heterostructured films. Neutron reflectometry measurements show low roughness parameters for the buried interfaces, which is critical for mediating the interfacial coupling between superconductivity and ferroelectric polarization. The superconducting transition temperature ($T_{\mathrm{C}}^{R}$) measured from the $R(T)$ curve of the single-layer YBCO was approximately 86 K, and a transition temperature ($T_{\mathrm{C}}^{M}$) of approximately 80-85 K was observed from the $M(T)$ curve. For the heterostructure film (YBCO/BTO/YBCO) grown under the same conditions, both resistivity and magnetization measurements indicate lower transition temperatures of approximately 75 K and approximately 55 K, respectively, as well as a lower overall susceptibility. These findings highlight the need to combine multiple techniques to characterize BTO/YBCO heterostructures and identify subtle features of the ferroelectric--superconducting coupling. This establishes BTO/YBCO heterostructures as promising systems for tunable oxide electronics and reconfigurable superconducting devices.

### [138] [Strain-Tuned Nodal Superconductivity in the Charge-Ordered Kagome Metal CsV$_3$Sb$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11115)
*Yusuke Takeuchi,Akito Kobayashi,Saki Uchida,Takumi Nagao,Seigo Ogawa,Rui Zhou,Shinji Kawasaki,Fei Song,Hao Ni,Yong Zhao,Guo-qing Zheng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过原位单轴压力下的核四极共振（NQR）实验，发现kagome金属CsV₃Sb₅中拉伸应变可独立于电荷密度波（CDW）提升超导转变温度，并观测到从有节点（nodal）到无节点（nodeless）能隙的双重超导转变，证实环境压力下存在简并的不同能隙对称性超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome金属CsV₃Sb₅中超导配对对称性（superconducting pairing symmetry）的本质及其与电荷密度波（CDW）有序的关系是尚未解决的核心问题，亟需实验揭示其内在机制。

Method: 使用¹²¹Sb核四极共振（NQR）技术，在原位单轴压力（in-situ uniaxial pressure）条件下研究CsV₃Sb₅中超导性的演化。

Result: 拉伸应变显著提升超导转变温度（T_c），而CDW保持不变，表明超导可独立于体电荷有序被调控。在ε = +0.90%拉伸应变下，核自旋-晶格弛豫率（nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate）揭示出一个双重转变（double transition）：上转变T_c1 = 3.6 K对应有节点能隙态（nodal gap state），下转变T_c2 = 3.0 K以无节点能隙（nodeless gap）为特征。

Conclusion: 这些结果证明kagome金属在环境压力下存在具有不同能隙对称性（gap symmetry）的简并超导态（degenerate superconducting states），这些简并态在应变下发生分裂；同时表明单轴压力可有效调控超导电性。

Abstract: The nature of the superconducting pairing symmetry in the kagome metal CsV$_3$Sb$_5$ and its relationship with the charge density wave (CDW) order are central unresolved issues. Here, we investigate the evolution of superconductivity in CsV$_3$Sb$_5$ under in-situ uniaxial pressure using $^{121}$Sb nuclear quadrupole resonance (NQR). We find that tensile strain significantly enhances the superconducting transition temperature, $T_{\rm c}$, while the CDW remains unchanged, demonstrating that superconductivity can be tuned independently of the bulk charge order. At a tensile strain of $\varepsilon$ = +0.90%, the nuclear spin-lattice relaxation rate reveals a remarkable double transition: an upper transition at $T_{\rm c1}$ = 3.6 K to a nodal gap state, and a lower one at $T_{\rm c2}$ = 3.0 K characterized by a nodeless gap. These results evidence degenerate superconducting states with different gap symmetry in the kagome metal at ambient pressure which split under strain. Our work demonstrates a high tunability of superconductivity by uniaxial pressure.

### [139] [Iron-Based Superconductors: A Decade of Materials, Magnetism, and Mechanisms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11355)
*Xingye Lu,Hechang Lei,Jun Zhao,Hideo Hosono,Pengcheng Dai*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了自2008年发现以来铁基超导体（iron-based superconductors, FeSCs）在过去十余年的主要进展，聚焦于实验技术、配对机制（pairing mechanisms）和新兴应用，并指出其配对态需在材料特定框架下讨论，同时FeSCs在高上临界场和中等各向异性等性能方面持续推动基础物理与技术应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁基超导体作为多带电子关联材料中研究高温超导电性的核心平台，其复杂的电子、磁性与超导基态之间的相互作用尚未被完全理解，亟需系统梳理近年来的实验进展与理论共识。

Method: 通过化学替代（chemical substitution）、压力和外延生长（epitaxial growth）等结构调控手段，精确控制电子、磁性和超导基态；利用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）表征自旋波与自旋激发；结合薄膜生长、插层化学和界面工程（interface engineering）等先进实验技术。

Result: 电子向列相（electronic nematic phase）和条纹型反铁磁序（stripe-type antiferromagnetic order）常共存或竞争，是理解相图的关键。高能自旋激发在掺杂超导体中保留了大量谱权重，而低能区存在与超导耦合的集体自旋激发——“共振模”（resonance）。该共振的动量结构为符号反转配对（sign-changing pairing）提供了强证据。配对态需在材料特定框架下讨论$s_{\pm}$、$s_{++}$、节点$s$波、$d$波及多分量态。

Conclusion: 铁基超导体凭借高上临界场（upper critical fields）、中等各向异性和不断提升的临界电流密度，持续推动超导领域的基础研究和技术应用。FeSe基体系的薄膜、插层和界面工程技术已实现增高的超导临界温度（$T_c$）和新颖器件结构。

Abstract: Since its discovery in 2008, iron-based superconductors (FeSCs) have become a central platform for exploring high-temperature superconductivity in multiband, electron-correlated materials. This review focuses on major developments over the past decade or so, emphasizing experimental advances, pairing mechanisms, and emerging applications. Structural tuning through chemical substitution, pressure, and epitaxial growth enables precise control of the electronic, magnetic, and superconducting ground states, thereby revealing their interplay. In particular, the electronic nematic phase and stripe-type antiferromagnetic order-often coexisting or competing-are central to understanding the phase diagrams. Spin waves in magnetically ordered parent compounds and spin excitations (fluctuations) in doped superconductors are extensively characterized by inelastic neutron scattering. While high-energy spin excitations in doped superconductors retain substantial spectral weight across a wide energy range reminiscent of spin waves in their undoped parents, the low-energy response reveals a collective spin excitation termed ``resonance'' coupled to superconductivity. The momentum structure of superconductivity-induced resonance provides strong evidence for sign-changing pairing in many FeSCs, while disorder effects, orbital-fluctuation scenarios, quasiparticle damping, and compound-dependent gap structures indicate that $s_{\pm}$, $s_{++}$, nodal $s$, $d$-wave, and multicomponent states must be discussed in a material-specific framework. Advances in thin-film growth, intercalation chemistry, and interface engineering-particularly in FeSe-based systems-have enabled enhanced $T_{c}$ and novel device geometries. With high upper critical fields, moderate anisotropy, and improving current densities, FeSCs continue to drive both fundamental insight and technological applications in superconductivity.

### [140] [Interference-Enhanced Large Electron-Phonon Coupling from Raman-active Breathing Modes in Moiré Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11425)
*Ning Mao,Shaozheng Wang,Cheng Xu,Xumin Chang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Claudia Felser,Shengwei Jiang,Yang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过结合填充依赖的拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）与机器学习第一性原理计算（machine-learning first-principles calculations），在包含数千至上万个原子的大尺度超胞（supercell）中逐模获取了扭转WSe₂和MoTe₂莫尔半导体（moiré semiconductors）中的电子-声子耦合（EPC）。研究发现，莫尔声子耦合遵循一种干涉选择定则（interference selection rule）：只有当声子位移模式与静态晶格重构图案（lattice-reconstruction pattern）匹配时耦合才强，否则会被相消干涉抑制。该定则揭示的大角度呼吸模式耦合峰值与超导出现的角度范围一致，表明声子对莫尔超导可能有显著甚至主导的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在扭转WSe₂和MoTe₂中观测到超导电性，引发了一个核心问题：配对是由电子关联（electronic correlations）、声子（phonons）还是两者共同驱动？回答此问题需要确定这些莫尔半导体中的电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling, EPC），但其在包含数千个原子的真实超胞中的计算超出了直接第一性原理方法（first-principles methods）的能力范围。

Method: 将填充依赖的拉曼光谱（filling-dependent Raman spectroscopy）与机器学习第一性原理计算（machine-learning first-principles calculations）相结合，实现了对包含数万个原子的大尺度超胞中电子-声子耦合的逐模分析。

Result: 拉曼光谱仅显示少数莫尔声子（moiré phonons）的频率随填充强烈移动；作者将其归因于一种干涉选择定则：仅当声子位移纹理（displacement texture）与静态晶格重构图案匹配时耦合才强，否则被相消干涉（destructive interference）抑制。该定则选择了拉曼中观测到的低频和高频呼吸模式，并使耦合在大扭转角（large twist angles）处达到峰值，该角度范围恰与超导出现的角度接近。

Conclusion: 晶格重构干涉（lattice-reconstruction interference）由此作为莫尔电子-声子耦合的一个组织性原理（organizing principle）出现，表明声子对大角度配对（large-angle pairing）有显著、甚至可能是主导的贡献。

Abstract: Superconductivity was recently observed in twisted WSe2 and MoTe2, raising a central question: is the pairing driven by electronic correlations, by phonons, or by both? Answering it requires determining the electron-phonon coupling (EPC) in these moiré semiconductors, whose calculation in realistic supercells of thousands of atoms lies beyond the reach of direct first-principles methods. Here we combine filling-dependent Raman spectroscopy with machine-learning first-principles calculations to obtain the EPC mode by mode in supercells of up to tens of thousands of atoms. Raman reveals only a few moiré phonons whose frequencies shift strongly with filling; we trace this to an interference selection rule: a phonon couples strongly only when its displacement texture matches the static lattice-reconstruction pattern, and is otherwise suppressed by destructive interference. The rule selects the low- and high-frequency breathing modes seen in Raman and makes the coupling peak at large twist angles, near those at which superconductivity appears. Lattice-reconstruction interference thus emerges as an organizing principle for moiré EPC, pointing to a substantial, potentially dominant, phonon contribution to large-angle pairing.

</details>


### [141] [Microscopic equivalence of the vortex-entry current and the depairing current in a superconducting thin-film strip](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11518)
*Takayuki Kubo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用脏极限 Usadel 理论的固定电流吉布斯泛函（fixed-current Gibbs functional），从微观角度将涡旋进入超导条带（superconducting strip）的临界电流重新表述为无涡旋载流态失去局部稳定性的问题，并证明边缘势垒消失电流（barrier-disappearance current）恰好等于解对电流（depairing current），该电流由均匀扰动决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pearl-London理论通常将涡旋进入超导条带的电流解释为边缘势垒（edge barrier）的消失，本文希望从微观理论出发重新审视该问题，以澄清临界电流的物理本质。

Method: 采用脏极限 Usadel 理论（dirty-limit Usadel theory）的固定电流吉布斯泛函，在零外加磁场、忽略自场效应、理想均匀薄膜条带的条件下，分析无涡旋载流态对空间均匀与非均匀扰动的稳定性。

Result: 边缘势垒消失电流由均匀扰动（spatially uniform perturbation）决定，且该电流恰好等于解对电流（depairing current）。

Conclusion: 涡旋进入超导条带的临界电流的微观判据是无涡旋态失去局部稳定性，而非简单的势垒消失；该电流与解对电流一致，且可在任意温度下由 Usadel 理论描述。

Abstract: The current at which vortices enter a superconducting strip is usually identified in Pearl--London theory with the disappearance of an edge barrier. This work reformulates the same question microscopically as the loss of local stability of the vortex-free current-carrying state, using the fixed-current Gibbs functional of dirty-limit Usadel theory, which is valid at arbitrary temperatures. For an ideal homogeneous thin-film strip at zero applied field, with self-field effects neglected, the stability of the vortex-free state is examined against both spatially uniform and nonuniform perturbations. The barrier-disappearance current is shown to be set by the uniform perturbation and to coincide exactly with the depairing current.

</details>


### [142] [Correlation-renormalized spin-fluctuation pairing and the stabilization of $s_{\pm}$ superconductivity in pressurized La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11786)
*Shuhong Tang,Liang-Jian Zou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过结合单站点双轨道动力学平均场理论（DMFT）与自能重整化随机相位近似（RPA），发现在加压La₃Ni₂O₇中，考虑强关联重整化后，超导配对对称性从裸RPA下的B₂g d_xy通道转变为A₁g s±通道，表明强关联效应对预测该材料的配对对称性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加压La₃Ni₂O₇的超导能隙对称性（superconducting gap symmetry）尚未确定，因为传统弱耦合计算常使系统接近相互竞争的s波和d波符号变化配对不稳定性（sign-changing s- and d-wave instabilities）。该研究旨在通过适当处理强关联效应来澄清这一问题。

Method: 采用Xia等人提出的四轨道Wannier哈密顿量（four-orbital Wannier Hamiltonian），将单站点双轨道动力学平均场理论（DMFT）与自能重整化随机相位近似（self-energy-renormalized RPA）相结合。核心步骤是用G_DMFT G_DMFT泡利气泡替换普通RPA中的裸粒子-空穴气泡G₀G₀，同时保留相同的残余Slater-Kanamori相互作用顶点。此外，利用含局部DMFT顶点的对偶Bethe-Salpeter方程（dual Bethe-Salpeter equation）独立计算静态自旋磁化率（static spin susceptibility）进行双粒子验证。

Result: 裸RPA基准中，主导配对本征值（leading pairing eigenvalue）属于B₂g d_xy通道；引入DMFT自能后，层级反转：A₁g符号变化s±态成为主导，B₁g d_x²-y²通道为次主导，原始B₂g不稳定性被强烈抑制。pocket-pair分解和轨道分辨磁化率表明，反转源于d_3z²-r²扇区的轨道选择性重整化（orbital-selective renormalization），该重整化过滤了裸RPA中稳定d_xy配对的γ-pocket散射过程，同时保留了有利于s±配对的分布式inter-pocket过程。静态自旋磁化率保留宽泛的有限动量磁响应（broad finite-momentum magnetic response），且在Γ点附近较弱，增强了关联稳定化s±态的自旋涨落背景（spin-fluctuation background）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，强关联效应（strong correlations）在La₃Ni₂O₇中并非次要修正，对关联重整化准粒子（correlation-renormalized quasiparticles）进行恰当处理是预测超导配对对称性的关键。

Abstract: The superconducting gap symmetry of pressurized La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ remains unsettled because conventional weak-coupling calculations often place the system close to competing sign-changing $s$- and $d$-wave instabilities. Using the four-orbital Wannier Hamiltonian of Xia et al., we combine single-site two-orbital dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) with a self-energy-renormalized random-phase approximation (RPA). The central step is to replace the bare particle-hole bubble $G_0G_0$ of ordinary RPA by a $G_{\rm DMFT}G_{\rm DMFT}$ bubble, while keeping the same residual Slater--Kanamori interaction vertices. In the bare RPA benchmark, the leading pairing eigenvalue belongs to the $B_{2g}$ $d_{xy}$ channel. Once the DMFT self-energy is included, the hierarchy is reversed: the $A_{1g}$ sign-changing $s_{\pm}$ state becomes dominant, the $B_{1g}$ $d_{x^2-y^2}$ channel is subleading, and the original $B_{2g}$ instability is strongly suppressed. Pocket-pair decomposition and orbital-resolved susceptibilities show that the reversal originates from orbital-selective renormalization of the $d_{3z^2-r^2}$ sector, which filters the $γ$-pocket scattering processes that stabilize $d_{xy}$ pairing in bare RPA while preserving distributed inter-pocket processes favorable to $s_{\pm}$ pairing. As an independent two-particle validation, we further compute the static spin susceptibility using the dual Bethe--Salpeter equation with the local DMFT vertex. The resulting susceptibility retains a broad finite-momentum magnetic response and is weak near $Γ$, strengthening the spin-fluctuation background for the correlation-stabilized $s_{\pm}$ state. Our results demonstrate that strong correlations are not a secondary correction in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$: an appropriate treatment of correlation-renormalized quasiparticles is essential for predicting the superconducting pairing symmetry.

</details>

### [143] [The muon Moonshot: Moon subsurface tomography with upward-going muons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10403)
*Zimo Hu,Leyun Gao,Zhengyun You,Qite Li,Qiang Li,Yuhong Yu,Liangwen Chen,Xueheng Zhang,Zhiyu Sun*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于月球风化层逃逸的向上缪子（upward-going muon）进行月球地下断层成像（lunar subsurface tomography）的“月球缪子登月计划”（muon Moonshot）概念。通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）分析缪子能谱、角分布与积分通量，证明该通量对探测器高度敏感，可在短至一分钟内检测到地下空洞，约十分钟内区分水信号，为未来月球任务提供新的非侵入式探地手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球缪子断层成像（muon tomography）已用于地质勘探与结构监测，但月球表面缺少大气层，现有技术难以探测浅层地下结构。本研究旨在利用月球风化层逃逸的向上缪子，为月球浅层地下空洞、水冰等资源探测提供一种非侵入式的新方法。

Method: 研究者提出向上缪子来源于月球风化层中逃逸的强子（hadron）在飞行中衰变这一物理机制，采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）计算缪子的能谱（energy spectrum）、角分布（angular distribution）与积分通量（integrated flux），并比较不同理论模型与探测器配置下的结果，分析平坦地形假设下探测器高度对通量的影响。

Result: 模拟结果表明，月球缪子通量对探测器高度敏感，在平坦地形假设下具有显著的响应差异。案例研究显示，地下空洞可在不到一分钟的观测时间内引起通量变化，而较弱的含水信号约在十分钟的数据采集后可被区分。

Conclusion: 该研究验证了向上缪子作为月球浅层地下结构非侵入式探针（non-invasive probe）的可行性，并讨论了在月球表面或近月轨道部署探测器用于未来月球任务的实际应用前景。

Abstract: We propose a novel muon Moonshot concept for lunar subsurface tomography based on upward-going muons originated from the lunar regolith. Unlike the Earth, the Moon lacks an atmosphere, leaving a dense regolith below and a near-vacuum environment above. Consequently, while most downward-going hadrons are absorbed before decaying, upward-going hadrons escaping the regolith can decay in flight, producing a significant source of lunar muons. These muons are detectable by instruments on the lunar surface or in near-lunar orbit. We perform Monte Carlo simulations to investigate their energy spectra, angular distributions, and integrated fluxes under various theoretical and detector configurations. The results indicate that the lunar muon flux is sensitive to detector altitude under a flat-terrain assumption, demonstrating its potential as a novel non-invasive probe of shallow subsurface voids. We also present case studies on detecting underground cavities and water resources, with cavity-induced flux variations observable in less than a minute and weaker water signals distinguishable after about ten minutes of data collection, and discuss potential implementations in future lunar missions.

</details>

*Deep Ray,Souvik Roy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于深度学习的计算算法，用于解决光声层析成像（photoacoustic tomography）中部分径向设置下的圆形Radon变换（circular Radon transform）反演问题。通过ResBlock U-Net替代传统的截断奇异值分解（truncated SVD）方法，有效消除了后者的严重伪影，在含噪完全视图和有限视图数据下均表现出优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光声层析成像中的部分径向圆形Radon变换反演问题缺乏有效求解算法。现有的唯一传统方法——基于截断奇异值分解（truncated singular value decomposition, TSVD）的算法——会引入严重伪影（artifacts），导致重建场无法使用。因此，需要克服这一计算瓶颈。

Method: 训练一个基于ResBlock的U-Net（ResBlock-based U-Net）模型，该网络直接对测量数据（measured data）进行操作，以恢复推断场（inferred field）。

Result: 在增强的Shepp-Logan体模（augmented Shepp-Logan phantoms）上进行的数值实验表明，在含噪完全视图（full view）和有限视图（limited view）数据两种场景下，所提出的算法均优于传统TSVD方法。

Conclusion: 深度学习（deep learning）方法能够有效解决传统算法因伪影而失效的光声层析成像反演问题，为部分径向圆形Radon变换的数值求解提供了更优的计算方案。

Abstract: We present a deep learning-based computational algorithm for inversion of circular Radon transforms in the partial radial setup, arising in photoacoustic tomography. We first demonstrate that the truncated singular value decomposition-based method, which is the only traditional algorithm available to solve this problem, leads to severe artifacts which renders the reconstructed field as unusable. With the objective of overcoming this computational bottleneck, we train a ResBlock based U-Net to recover the inferred field that directly operates on the measured data. Numerical results with augmented Shepp-Logan phantoms, in the presence of noisy full and limited view data, demonstrate the superiority of the proposed algorithm.

### [145] [Interpreting learning dynamics of autoencoders: Transient scaling and emerging concepts of the Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10285)
*Max Weinmann,Miriam Klopotek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究无监督自编码器（unsupervised autoencoder）在伊辛模型（Ising model）微观自旋构型上学习宏观理论相关变量的过程，揭示了由超参数控制的磁化主导与能量主导两种动力学机制，并通过递归动力学轨迹分析建立了学习过程的非平衡统计力学解释框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索无监督自编码器在未嵌入领域知识的情况下，能否从微观数据中自发学习到与物理理论相关的宏观变量，并理解其学习过程的动力学本质。

Method: 以伊辛模型的微观自旋构型为训练数据，训练无监督自编码器；在不同空间粗粒化（coarse-graining）尺度上量化表征学习质量；分析模型深度、宽度和学习率等超参数的影响；提出递归动力学轨迹（recursive-dynamic trajectories）分析方法，研究预测误差诱导的流场（flow fields）及其轨迹拓扑结构。

Result: 发现了两种由超参数控制的动力学机制：磁化主导（magnetization-dominated）与能量主导（energy-dominated）机制，两者在表征质量上存在权衡；磁化主导机制表现出动力学标度（dynamical scaling）和涨落；能量主导机制则将分辨率转向小尺度；中高速率训练的深层模型在学习到达这些机制前即停滞（arrested）；所有表征空间中存在共同的轨迹拓扑结构。

Conclusion: 学习过程可被理解为一种由训练数据和优化器引入的涨落驱动、远离平衡态的非平衡统计力学（non-equilibrium statistical mechanics）过程；该动力学视角为理解物理世界及其机器表征模型提供了统一的解释基础。

Abstract: We study how unsupervised autoencoders trained on microscopic spin configurations from the Ising model learn macroscopic, theory-relevant variables underlying the data-generating process. Without embedding domain knowledge, we mimic a typical discovery setting: We quantify learning across multiple spatial (coarse-graining) scales and reveal two distinct dynamical regimes controlled by main hyperparameters (model depth, width, and learning rate) -- a magnetization-dominated regime and an energy-dominated regime characterized by trade-offs in their representation quality. The first regime is a transitory state exhibiting dynamical scaling and fluctuations that follow an ordering-to-scale; the second gradually shifts resolution towards smaller scales relevant for the energy representation. Deep models trained at moderate and fast rates become arrested before reaching these regimes. With a novel analysis of recursive-dynamic trajectories, we demonstrate that prediction errors induce flow fields that produce a common trajectory topology across all representation spaces. A dynamical viewpoint of learning is established in which intrinsic properties expose the effects of forced changes in representation during training. We utilize the intuition that learning operates as a process driven far from equilibrium by fluctuations from the training data and optimizer to provide an interpretive basis grounded in both the physical world and the machine models that represent it.

</details>


### [146] [Learning from Noise: Effective-Rank Collapse and Out-of-Distribution Rejection in Restricted Boltzmann Machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10506)
*Oshada Rathnayake,Nikhil Shukla*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）在分布外（OOD）输入下分类脆弱的机理，发现该问题源于可见-可见相互作用矩阵 J=WW^T 的谱结构。通过引入辅助随机二值图像并赋予拒绝标签进行训练，可诱导有效秩坍缩（effective-rank collapse），使谱权重集中于少数主特征方向，从而提升 OOD 拒绝能力，同时保持分布内分类精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machine, RBM）作为能量基分类器，在分布外（out-of-distribution, OOD）输入下表现脆弱——训练分布外的样本可能被错误地吸收到某个已学习的类别盆地（class basin）中而非被拒绝。本文旨在从相互作用矩阵谱的角度分析该失效模式，并探索一种缓解策略。

Method: 通过可见-可见相互作用矩阵 J=WW^T 的谱（spectrum）来分析 RBM 的 OOD 失效模式，其中 W 为可见-隐藏权重矩阵。以 Marchenko-Pastur 随机矩阵参考为基准，对比常规训练与引入辅助随机二值图像（赋拒绝标签）后的谱演化。分析了有效秩（effective rank）的变化及其与经验数据协方差矩阵的关系。

Result: 常规训练会将谱权重分散到大量弱、与体（bulk）兼容的方向上，增加了 J 的有效秩。引入辅助随机图像并赋予拒绝标签后，训练诱导了有效秩坍缩（effective-rank collapse）：弱体模式（bulk-like modes）被耗散，谱权重集中于更少的主特征方向，J 的有效秩趋近于经验数据协方差矩阵的有效秩。

Conclusion: 采用随机辅助曝光（random auxiliary exposure）训练的 RBM 能在保持 MNIST 分类精度的同时有效拒绝结构化的 OOD 图像数据集。该方法能够重塑相互作用谱（interaction spectrum）和能量基分类器的自由能景观（free-energy landscape），为提升能量基模型的 OOD 鲁棒性提供了一种谱层面的理解与可行方案。

Abstract: Restricted Boltzmann machines (RBMs) represent data by shaping an energy landscape over visible and hidden configurations, but their discriminative use is fragile under out-of-distribution (OOD) inputs: samples outside the training distribution can be absorbed into one of the learned class basins rather than rejected. Here, we analyze this failure mode through the spectrum of the induced visible--visible interaction $J=WW^{T}$, where \(W\) is the visible--hidden weight matrix. Relative to a Marchenko--Pastur random-matrix reference, conventional training spreads spectral weight into many weak, bulk-compatible directions, increasing the effective rank of $J$. When auxiliary random binary images are assigned to a rejection label during training, the learned interaction undergoes effective-rank collapse: weak bulk-like modes are depleted, spectral weight concentrates into fewer dominant eigendirections, and the effective rank of $J$ approaches that of the empirical data covariance matrix. The resulting RBM rejects structured OOD image datasets while preserving MNIST classification accuracy, showing that random auxiliary exposure can reshape both the interaction spectrum and the free-energy landscape of an energy-based classifier.

</details>


### [147] [CatRetriever: Contrastive Representation Learning for Slab-to-Bulk Retrieval in Generative Catalyst Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11712)
*Jungho Oh,Woosung Kim,Dong Hyeon Mok,Jonggeol Na,Seoin Back*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出CatRetriever，一种基于对比表征学习（contrastive representation learning）的模型，用于解决催化剂逆设计（inverse design）中 slab 结构与对应体相（bulk）结构之间的缺失连接问题。该模型将 slab 和 bulk 晶体表征对齐到共享潜空间（shared latent space），能够以高准确率（R@1 > 91%，R@3 > 98%）从 slab 查询中检索出合理的候选体相结构，并进一步扩展为面向吸附能目标的体相发现流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有催化剂表面生成模型（surface generative models）通常仅在 slab 层面操作，不提供对应的母体体相（parent bulk）结构，导致难以评估依赖于体相的性质，如形成能（formation energy）、表面能（surface energy）、晶体学对称性（crystallographic symmetry）和可合成性（synthesizability）。本文旨在填补这一 slab 到 bulk 的连接缺失。

Method: 将 slab 到 bulk 的对应问题建模为检索任务（retrieval problem），提出 CatRetriever 模型，采用对比表征学习（contrastive representation learning）方法，将 slab 和 bulk 晶体结构的表征对齐到共享潜空间（shared latent space）。在此基础上，构建了面向吸附能（adsorption energy）目标的体相发现管线，结合 bulk 检索、生成式搜索空间扩展（generative search space expansion）和吸附能分布分析（adsorption energy distribution analysis）。

Result: CatRetriever 在分布内（in-distribution）和留出（holdout）评估集上均实现了 R@1 > 91% 和 R@3 > 98% 的检索准确率，表明其能够从 slab 查询中准确检索出合理的母体体相候选结构。

Conclusion: CatRetriever 提供了一种可扩展的途径（scalable route），将催化剂生成模型与物理上合理且吸附能兼容的体相催化剂发现相连接，从而支持更全面的催化剂逆设计。

Abstract: Inverse design is an emerging data-driven paradigm for efficiently navigating vast chemical spaces to discover new materials with targeted properties, and in the context of heterogeneous catalysis, surface generative models have recently advanced this goal by directly generating catalyst surface-adsorbate structures. However, these models typically operate at the slab level and do not provide the corresponding parent bulk structure, making it difficult to assess bulk-dependent properties such as formation energy, surface energy, crystallographic symmetry, and synthesizability. Here, we address this missing slab-to-bulk connection as a retrieval problem and introduce CatRetriever, a contrastive representation learning model that aligns slab and bulk crystal representations in a shared latent space. From a slab query, CatRetriever accurately retrieves plausible parent bulk candidates with R@1 > 91% and R@3 > 98% on both the in-distribution and holdout evaluation sets. We further extend the CatRetriever framework into an adsorption energy targeted bulk discovery pipeline that combines bulk retrieval, generative search space expansion, and adsorption energy distribution analysis. This workflow evaluates candidates by both structural compatibility with the query slab and their ability to access the target adsorption energy range across diverse surface environments. CatRetriever therefore provides a scalable route for connecting catalyst generative models with physically plausible and adsorption energy compatible bulk catalyst discovery.

</details>
