### [148] [Interwoven long-range order induced by random fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10337)
*Jeremiah Bender,Thomas Vojta*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型长程有序相——“implectic相”，该相由随机场（random-field）无序诱导产生，基于复合遗迹序参量（composite vestigial order parameter）的对称性破缺，并在随机场形成的空间交织畴结构（spatially interwoven domain structure）背景上自发出现。通过层状J1-J2伊辛模型（Ising magnet）的大规模蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证了该相的存在，并讨论了在电荷密度波与自旋密度波系统（包括阻挫磁体、铜氧化物超导体、铁基超导体和超冷原子）中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究中，杂质和缺陷通常被视作破坏长程有序的因素。本文旨在提出一种反直觉的机制——杂质与缺陷通过局部破坏序参量对称性，能诱导出新型的长程有序相（implectic相），从而拓展对无序系统相行为的理解。

Method: 通过大规模蒙特卡洛模拟，在层状J1-J2伊辛磁体中系统性地研究随机场无序（random-field disorder）对复合遗迹序参量的影响，验证implectic相的存在及其物理性质。

Result: 成功证明了在随机场无序作用下，系统可在空间交织的畴结构背景上发生自发对称性破缺，形成一种全新的长程有序相，即implectic相。

Conclusion: 该发现表明杂质和缺陷不仅可以破坏有序，还能通过复合序参量耦合机制创造出新型有序相。该机制具有广泛的适用性，为理解阻挫磁体、铜氧化物和铁基超导体以及超冷原子系统中的电荷密度波（charge density wave）和自旋密度波（spin density wave）有序提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We propose a distinct type of long-range ordered phase that can occur in classical and quantum many-particle systems. It is induced by impurities and defects that locally break a subset of the order-parameter symmetries, i.e., by random-field disorder that couples to a composite vestigial order parameter. The proposed ``implectic'' phase is characterized by spontaneous symmetry breaking on the background of the spatially interwoven domain structure created by the random fields. We explicitly demonstrate the existence of this phase in a layered $J_1-J_2$ Ising magnet by means of large-scale Monte Carlo simulations. We then discuss numerous potential applications in systems featuring charge and spin density wave order including frustrated magnets, cuprate and iron-based superconductors, and ultracold atoms.

</details>


### [149] [Spectral Signatures of Replica Symmetry Breaking in Optimization-Induced Random Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10513)
*Isaac Pérez Castillo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文研究了由吉布斯测度（Gibbs measures）诱导的优化矩阵系综，发现单一诱导矩阵的谱会抹去玻璃态结构，而两个独立热样本的矩阵差谱则能显式编码玻璃态吉布斯几何（glassy Gibbs geometry），并通过Parisi理论和蒙特卡洛模拟验证了该机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究由无序（quenched disorder）加权的吉布斯测度所诱导的矩阵系综的谱性质，特别是其是否能继承底层玻璃态吉布斯几何（glassy Gibbs geometry）的结构信息。

Method: 在稠密张量优化模型（dense tensor optimization model）中，分析单一诱导矩阵与两个独立热样本之差的矩阵谱；采用Parisi理论和蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟对简单相和玻璃态相进行验证。

Result: 单一诱导矩阵的主体谱（leading bulk）是普适的，会抹去玻璃态组织；而两个独立热样本的矩阵差谱则能显式地反映玻璃态吉布斯几何，其信息由样本间互重叠（mutual overlaps）的分布编码。

Conclusion: Parisi理论和蒙特卡洛模拟均证实了上述谱机制在简单相和玻璃态相中均成立，表明矩阵差谱可作为探测玻璃态几何结构的有力工具。

Abstract: We study optimization-induced matrix ensembles generated by Gibbs measures. The same quenched disorder that weights configurations also supplies the matrix entries observed on them. For glassy Gibbs measures this raises a natural question: does the induced spectrum inherit the underlying glassy Gibbs geometry? In a dense tensor optimization model we find a selective answer. A single induced matrix has a universal leading bulk that washes out the glassy organization. The difference of two matrices built from independent thermal samples in the same disorder does not: its spectrum gives an explicit image of the glassy Gibbs geometry, encoded by the distribution of mutual overlaps between samples. Parisi theory and Monte Carlo confirm this mechanism across simple and glassy phases.

</details>


### [150] [Learning as a Geometric Phase Transition: Renormalization Group Flow and Anisotropic Symmetry Breaking in Deep Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10770)
*G. Le Pera,C. Nordio*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文将特征学习（feature learning）表述为张量积提升度量（lifted tensor-product learning metric）的几何临界现象。核心对象不是标量交叠，而是目标-活跃几何（target-active geometry），其中性相是目标各向同性的，学习对应于该不动点的失稳和目标对齐无迹张量本征态的出现。论文推导了离散Dyson展开和连续Callan-Symanzik流，并通过异步梯度更新产生的同步度量应变识别了β函数的局域空间源，建立了深度重整化群（depth RG）流与随机训练动力学之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对特征学习的理论理解通常依赖于标量交叠（scalar overlap）等简化量，缺乏对深度学习训练过程中几何结构与临界现象的深层刻画。本文旨在建立特征学习作为一种几何临界现象的形式化框架，将训练动力学与重整化群（renormalization group）的语言联系起来。

Method: 论文引入张量积提升度量，其核心对象为\mathcal N_{0,L}，纠缠了前向拉回存活（forward pullback survival）与后向推前可见性（backward push-forward visibility）。推导了局域各向异性插入的离散Dyson展开及其连续Callan-Symanzik流。从微观运动学出发，将异步梯度更新产生的同步度量应变（metric strains）中的目标-活跃对称无迹分量识别为类曲率缺陷（curvature-like defects），进而构建深度威尔逊重整化群流。

Result: 学习对应于目标各向同性不动点（target-isotropic fixed point）的失稳，以及目标对齐无迹张量本征态（traceless target-aligned eigentensors）的出现。在无标度计数假设（scale-free counting hypothesis）下，目标-活跃提升几何的谱呈现重尾（heavy-tailed）分布，匹配的拉回-推前扇区（matched pullback--push-forward sector）内出现指数加成。深度RG流由缺陷的输运、平衡和粗粒化无关性（coarse-grained irrelevance）所主导。

Conclusion: 本文将特征学习重新诠释为深度威尔逊重整化群框架下的几何临界现象，将深度RG流与时间上的随机训练动力学以及学习通道在经验权重Gram矩阵上的运动学印记（kinematic imprint）相关联。

Abstract: We formulate feature learning as a geometric critical phenomenon of the lifted tensor-product learning metric. The central object is not a scalar overlap, but the target-active geometry of \[ \mathcal N_{0,L}=\frac1N\sum_{r=1}^{L}Σ_{r\to L}\otimes T_{0\to r-1}, \] which entangles forward pullback survival with backward push-forward visibility. The neutral phase is target-isotropic: after restriction to endpoint target-active states and trace normalization, the lifted metric is proportional to the identity. Learning corresponds to an instability of this target-isotropic fixed point and to the emergence of traceless target-aligned eigentensors. We derive discrete Dyson expansions for local anisotropic insertions and their continuous Callan--Symanzik flow. Crucially, before constructing the full temporal mean-field theory, we identify the local spatial source of the $β$-functions directly from microscopic kinematics: asynchronous gradient updates generate synchronous metric strains, whose target-active symmetric traceless components act as curvature-like defects. The Wilsonian depth RG flow is then governed by the transport, balance, and coarse-grained irrelevance of these defects. Heavy-tailed spectra arise, under a scale-free counting hypothesis, as the spectrum of the target-active lifted geometry, with exponent addition in the matched pullback--push-forward sector. Finally, we relate this depth RG picture to temporal stochastic training dynamics and to the kinematic imprint of the learned channel on empirical weight Gram matrices.

</details>


### [151] [Analytical mobility edge in nonreciprocal quasiperiodic lattices with next-nearest-neighbor hopping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10996)
*Wenmin Wang,Xiaosen Yang,Xianqi Tong*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究一维非厄米Aubry-André模型中非互易跳跃（nearest-neighbor和next-nearest-neighbor）导致的局域化转变与谱拓扑，推导出能量依赖迁移率边（mobility edge）的闭合表达式，并展示了谱绕数（winding number）如何标记混合相边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期晶格中的局域化转变与迁移率边是凝聚态物理的重要问题，而实际系统常存在非互易（nonreciprocal）跳跃与非厄米（non-Hermitian）效应，亟需一个能够统一描述能量依赖局域化、谱拓扑与非互易性的解析框架。

Method: 将费米面点匹配法（Fermi-surface point-matching method）推广至非互易跳跃情形，推导出迁移率边的闭合形式表达式；同时利用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）验证解析边界，并分析周期边界条件下的谱绕数随基能量的变化。

Result: 迁移率边在能量-势能平面上形成单条抛物线；nearest-neighbor非互易刚性移动局域化边界，next-nearest-neighbor非互易降低边界曲率从而展宽扩展态与局域态共存窗口。谱绕数在下带边降低标志着第一个局域态出现，在上带边降低标志着最后一个扩展态局域化，从而刻画混合相区间。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个连接能量依赖局域化、谱拓扑与非互易性的紧凑解析框架，成果可直接在光子、原子和电路平台中实验检验。

Abstract: We investigate localization transitions and spectral topology in a one-dimensional non-Hermitian generalization of the Aubry-André model in which both the nearest-neighbor and the next-nearest-neighbor hopping amplitudes are nonreciprocal. By extending the Fermi-surface point-matching method to nonreciprocal hopping, we derive a closed-form expression for the energy-dependent mobility edge in which the two nonreciprocity parameters are absorbed into exponentially renormalized effective hopping amplitudes. The mobility edge forms a single parabola in the energy--potential plane: nearest-neighbor nonreciprocity rigidly shifts the localization boundary toward stronger potentials, whereas next-nearest-neighbor nonreciprocity reduces the curvature of the boundary and thereby broadens the energy window in which extended and localized states coexist. Exact diagonalization confirms the analytical boundary for purely nearest-neighbor, purely next-nearest-neighbor, and combined nonreciprocity, and recovers the known Hermitian mobility edge in the reciprocal limit. We further analyze the spectral topology under periodic boundary conditions and show that the spectral winding numbers evaluated at base energies near the two band edges directly bracket the mixed phase: the winding number at the lower band edge drops when the mobility edge enters the spectrum and the first localized states appear, while the winding number at the upper band edge drops when the last extended states localize, delineating the full potential-strength window over which extended and localized states coexist. These results provide a compact analytical framework that connects energy-dependent localization, spectral topology, and nonreciprocity in quasiperiodic lattices, and they are directly testable in photonic, atomic, and electrical-circuit platforms.

</details>


### [152] [Emergent quantum chaos from correlations on a random graph](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11662)
*Mrinal Sarkar,Valerio Pagni,Tilman Enss,Nicolò Defenu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该工作证明，在一维无相互作用的单粒子哈密顿量中，仅靠稀疏的长程随机键就能产生量子混沌谱关联并驱动局域化相变。在σ较小时体系呈现高斯正交系综（Gaussian orthogonal ensemble, GOE）能级统计（量子混沌），σ较大时呈现泊松统计（局域化），相变发生在σ_c ≈ 0.80–0.85区间，远高于平均跃迁轮廓的可加性阈值（σ=0）。基于伯努利键的均值和方差构建的高斯场论将相变阈值预测为σ=1，暗示高阶累积量在红外（infrared）下是相关的。该结果指向一个不同于幂律随机带矩阵模型和标准安德森相变的普适类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在没有在位无序（on-site disorder）和相互作用的条件下，仅靠一维长程随机跳跃能否产生量子混沌谱关联和安德森局域化（Anderson localization）转变。

Method: 构建一维环模型，每对格点之间以概率p_{ij}=d_{ij}^{-(1+σ)}独立连接，键上为等幅跳跃（hopping）且无在位无序。通过精确对角化和能级统计（level statistics）分析谱关联，并对比高斯场论（仅保留伯努利键的均值和方差）的预测。

Result: 小σ时出现高斯正交系综（GOE）能级统计（量子混沌），大σ时出现泊松统计（局域化）；相变发生在σ_c ≈ 0.80–0.85区间，远高于平均跃迁轮廓的可加性阈值（σ=0）。高斯场论预测的相变阈值为σ=1，与精确结果不符。

Conclusion: 仅凭一维长程随机键即可驱动量子混沌-局域化转变，且该转变的临界行为不同于幂律随机带矩阵模型（power-law random banded matrix model）和标准安德森相变（standard Anderson transition），可能属于新的普适类（universality class）。

Abstract: This work demonstrates that sparse long-range random bonds on a one-dimensional lattice alone can generate quantum-chaotic spectral correlations and also drive a localization transition in a noninteracting single-particle Hamiltonian. The model is a one-dimensional ring in which each pair of sites is connected independently with a probability $p_{ij}= d_{ij}^{-(1+σ)}$. Each bond carries identical unit hopping and on-site disorder is absent. Despite the absence of on-site disorder and interaction, the model displays quantum chaotic spectra with Gaussian orthogonal ensemble (GOE) level statistics at small $σ$ and localized eigenstates with Poisson statistics at larger $σ$. The transition occurs in the range $ 0.80 \lesssim σ_c \lesssim 0.85$, far above the summability threshold of the mean hopping profile ($σ=0$). A Gaussian field theory retaining only the mean and variance of the Bernoulli bonds instead predicts a threshold at $σ=1$, suggesting that higher cumulants are infrared-relevant. Our findings hint towards a universality class that is distinct from both the power-law random banded matrix model and the standard Anderson transition.

</details>

Method: 采用综述（review）方法，整合现有研究，从三个空间尺度——单孔隙（single pore）、多孔隙介观尺度（mesoscale of many pores）和宏观景观（broader landscape）——分析细菌运动性（motility）、生长（growth）和感知（sensing）的物理学基础。

Result: 揭示了细菌与土壤环境之间动态反馈（dynamic feedback）如何在三个尺度上主导细菌的物理行为，包括运动、生长和环境感知。

Conclusion: 土壤细菌活动必须被理解为一种双向反馈过程，而非单向响应；多尺度视角对于揭示土壤微生物生态学的物理基础至关重要。

Abstract: Soil harbors much of Earth's bacterial life. The activity of these bacteria governs plant growth, carbon and nitrogen cycling, and the response of land to a changing climate. Understanding this activity is difficult, however: soil is structurally and chemically heterogeneous and optically opaque, and its bacteria not only respond to their surroundings but continually reshape them, a two-way feedback that most idealized experiments and theories overlook. Here we review how this dynamic feedback governs the physics of bacterial motility, growth, and sensing in soil across three scales -- the single pore, the mesoscale of many pores, and the broader landscape.

### [154] [Carrollian limit of NS-NS and Heterotic Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09847)
*Romina Ballesteros,Eric Lescano,Sergio Patiño-López*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过超相对论展开构建了NS-NS和杂化超引力的Carrollian极限，通过适当缩放膨胀子获得有限作用量，并将构造推广至包含非阿贝尔规范场和Green-Schwarz机制的杂化超引力，同时展示了α'修正下的有限性，最后讨论了与Carrollian弦论世界面形式体系的潜在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极端非相对论（ultra-relativistic）极限下构建弦论低能有效理论——NS-NS超引力与杂化（heterotic）超引力的Carrollian极限，以探索弦论在类光边界（null boundary）上的行为及其与Carrollian弦论（Carrollian string theory）的衔接。

Method: 采用超相对论展开（ultra-relativistic expansion）对场变量进行标度，通过适当缩放膨胀子（dilaton）消除NS-NS超引力拉格朗日量中的发散项，使w→∞时作用量有限；对于杂化超引力，将非阿贝尔规范场（non-Abelian gauge field）与Green-Schwarz（GS）机制纳入展开框架，并通过场重新定义（field redefinitions）使Carrollian 1-形式场的GS机制平凡化；同时从展开相对论运动方程和变分原理（variational principle）两条路径推导Carrollian运动方程。

Result: 成功得到了具有有限作用量的Carrollian NS-NS超引力以及包含与引力一致耦合的有限规范扇区的Carrollian杂化超引力；证明领头阶α'修正的$\hat{\rm Riem}^2$项在弦参数重标度$\alpha'\rightarrow \frac{\alpha'_c}{w^2}$下保持有限。

Conclusion: 所构造的Carrollian超引力为研究完整四导数有效作用量（four-derivative effective action）奠定了基础，并可能为建立Carrollian弦论的世界面形式体系（worldsheet formalism）提供桥梁。

Abstract: We construct the Carrollian limit of NS--NS and heterotic supergravity through an ultra-relativistic expansion of the fields. An appropriate scaling of the dilaton renders the measure finite and compensates the divergences arising from the NS-NS supergravity Lagrangian, giving a finite action as $w\rightarrow\infty$. We then extend the construction to heterotic supergravity (neglecting fermions) by incorporating the non-Abelian gauge field together with the Green--Schwarz (GS) mechanism. The resulting theory contains a finite gauge sector consistently coupled to gravity, and the GS mechanism for the Carrollian 1-form field can be trivialized imposing field redefinitions. Then, we investigate the Carrollian equations of motion by both expanding the relativistic equations and deriving them from a variational principle. We also show that the leading $α'$-corrected $\hat{\rm Riem}^2$ contribution remains finite under a rescaling of the string parameter $α'\rightarrow \frac{α'_c}{w^2}$, opening further research towards the full four-derivative effective action. Finally, we discuss the potential connection with the worldsheet formalism of the Carrollian string theory.

### [155] [Anomaly cancellation for two $U(1)$ factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09879)
*Ben Gripaios,Khoi Le Nguyen Nguyen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，4维规范理论中阿贝尔部分的局域反常消除条件，等价于在代数/算术几何中寻找有理数上三次超曲面的(K-1)维射影子空间问题，并利用该等价关系解决了一系列秩为2的实例。最简单的非平凡物理例子（U(1)²规范群与六个费米子）对应Segre三次原始三维流形中直线的Fano簇，这是一个具有15个不可约分支（平面）和6个不可约分支（分裂del Pezzo 5次曲面）的曲面，所有分支均为有理簇，使得反常消除条件的解集能够被参数化并描述其集体性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将4维规范理论中阿贝尔部分的局域反常取消条件，转化为一个纯代数/算术几何问题，从而利用几何工具系统性地求解反常消除条件。

Method: 建立局部反常消除条件与有理数上三次超曲面的(K-1)维射影子空间问题之间的等价关系；利用该几何重构方法分析秩为2的实例，特别是U(1)²规范群加六个费米子的情况，该情况对应于Segre三次原始三维流形中直线的Fano簇。

Result: 发现该Fano簇的曲面有15个不可约分支为平面（对应位于Segre三次原始中的15个平面，产生非手征费米子），以及6个不可约分支为分裂del Pezzo 5次曲面（产生手征费米子）。所有分支均为有理簇，因此反常消除条件的所有解均可被参数化，并可描述其拓扑结构和渐近分布。

Conclusion: 代数/算术几何中的线性子空间问题为系统地求解和分类4维规范理论中的反常消除条件提供了新的框架，并揭示了物理问题与几何结构（如Fano簇和del Pezzo曲面）之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We show that solving the abelian part of the local anomaly cancellation conditions for a 4-d gauge theory whose gauge Lie algebra has an abelian summand with rank $K \geq 1$ is equivalent to the problem in algebraic/arithmetic geometry of finding $(K-1)$-dimensional projective linear subspaces of a cubic hypersurface over the rational numbers, where the cubic is determined by the data of the semisimple summand and the representation thereof carried by the Weyl fermions. We then use this reformulation to solve a variety of examples with rank 2.
  The simplest non-trivial example from physics, namely gauge Lie group $U(1)^2$ and six fermions, nevertheless has a rich (and well-studied) geometry: it corresponds to the Fano variety of lines in the Segre cubic primal threefold. This is a surface with 15 irreducible components that are planes (which correspond to lines lying in the 15 planes in the Segre cubic primal and which give rise to non-chiral fermions) and 6 components that are split del Pezzo surfaces of degree 5 (which give rise to chiral fermions). These components are all rational varieties, enabling all solutions to the anomaly cancellation conditions to be parametrized and their collective properties (e.g. their topology and asymptotic distribution) to be described.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在二维修正Villain标量模型（modified Villain scalar model）中构造手征格点费米子算符，并计算其关联函数；该模型具有超局域作用量（ultra-local action）和超局域对称性，后者在玻色化下实现费米子手征对称性。

Result: 重建的格点狄拉克算符无加倍模式，但呈现非局域性（non-local），这一结果与Nielsen-Ninomiya定理一致；该非局域性在有限格点间距下不阻碍对模型的无反常对称性（non-anomalous symmetries）进行规范耦合，模型本身仍是超局域的。

Conclusion: 玻色子格点模型能够通过超局域结构实现手征费米子的格点正则化，且其非局域性不影响无反常对称性的规范耦合，为手征格点规范理论提供了可行的构造路径。

Abstract: Thanks to bosonization, bosonic lattice models can offer a lattice regularization of chiral fermions. We construct chiral lattice fermion operators in the 2D modified Villain scalar model and evaluate their correlation functions. This microscopic bosonic model has an ultra-local action and an ultra-local symmetry that realizes the fermionic chiral symmetry under bosonization. The reconstructed lattice Dirac operator has no doublers, but is consistent with the Nielsen-Ninomiya theorem because it turns out to be non-local. The non-locality of this derived quantity at finite lattice spacing does not pose any obstructions to gauging the non-anomalous symmetries of the model, which is itself ultra-local.

### [157] [Color-factor symmetry using perturbiner methods for tree-level amplitudes of Yang-Mills theory coupled to matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10006)

Abstract: Bern-Carrasco-Johansson relations are helicity-independent constraints among the partial amplitudes of tree-level processes containing gluons and possibly also matter fields. ### [158] [Superspace invariants and 3-point correlators in 3d $\mathcal{N}=3,4$ SCFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10133)
*Aditya Jain,Amin A. Nizami*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文利用辅助极化旋量形式（auxiliary polarization spinor formalism）和超空间技术（superspace techniques），构建了三维超共形场论（SCFTs）中 $\mathcal{N}=3$ 和 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超共形对称性下完整且最小的三点不变量结构列表，并利用这些不变量枚举了自旋三点关联函数的结构形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维超共形场论中 $\mathcal{N}=3$ 和 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超共形对称性具有非阿贝尔 $R$-对称性（non-abelian $R$-symmetry），由此产生由反对称不变张量构成的新型不变量结构。这些结构对于理解自旋三点关联函数的完整形式至关重要，但此前缺乏系统完备的构造。

Method: 采用辅助极化旋量形式结合超空间技术，系统构造满足超共形对称性约束的三点不变量结构。对于保守算子（conserved operators），进一步分析其关联函数中宇称奇偶结构的数目与形式。

Result: $\mathcal{N}=3$ 保守关联函数被固定为一个宇称偶（parity-even）结构和一个宇称奇（parity-odd）结构；$\mathcal{N}=4$ 保守关联函数则允许两个宇称偶结构和一个宇称奇结构，其中第二个宇称偶结构与镜对称性破缺（mirror symmetry breaking）相关联。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了 $\mathcal{N}=3$ 和 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超共形场论中自旋三点关联函数的最小完整结构分类，并揭示了 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 情形下宇称偶结构的额外自由度与镜对称性之间的关系。

Abstract: We use the auxiliary polarization spinor formalism together with superspace techniques to construct a complete and minimal list of 3-point invariant structures in three-dimensional superconformal field theories (SCFTs) with $\mathcal{N}=3$ and $\mathcal{N}=4$ superconformal symmetry. The existence of non-abelian $R$-symmetry for $\mathcal{N}=3,4$ gives rise to novel invariant structures built from the antisymmetric invariant tensor. These invariants are used to enumerate the structural form of spinning 3-point correlators of general as well as conserved spinning superfield operators in 3d SCFTs. For conserved operators, we find that the $\mathcal{N}=3$ correlators are fixed upto one parity-even and one parity-odd structure, while $\mathcal{N}=4$ conserved correlators admit two parity-even structures and one parity-odd structure, with the second parity-even structure associated with mirror symmetry breaking.

### [159] [D-branes in $AdS_2 \times H^2 \times H^2$ under the non-Abelian T-duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10448)

TL;DR: 本文通过应用非阿贝尔T-对偶性（non-Abelian T-duality，作为半阿贝尔对偶上的Poisson-Lie T-对偶），构造了AdS₂ × H² × H²背景的非阿贝尔对偶对。研究表明，对偶背景由B-场和含物理奇点的度规支撑；在小坐标区域，对偶度规与零场强及非平凡胀子场构成单圈beta-函数方程的解；在大坐标区域，原始AdS₂ × H² × H²解在对偶下保持不变。此外，基于规范变换推导了胶合矩阵（gluing matrix）的七种情况，揭示了D-膜之间的对称对偶作用链。

Motivation: 构造AdS₂ × H² × H²背景的非阿贝尔对偶对，并研究其几何性质、对偶保持行为及D-膜胶合矩阵的对称结构。

Method: 采用非阿贝尔T-对偶性（Poisson-Lie T-对偶），利用6维李群A₂ ⊗ A₂ ⊗ A₂的参数化构造原始σ-模型；通过规范变换描述胶合矩阵，分析对偶对下D-膜的边界条件。

Result: 对偶背景由B-场和含物理奇点的度规支持；小坐标区域中，对偶度规、零场强与非平凡胀子场满足单圈beta-函数方程；大坐标区域中AdS₂ × H² × H²解在对偶下保持；得到七类不同的胶合矩阵，展示了对偶作用的对称性。

Conclusion: 非阿贝尔T-对偶性成功应用于AdS₂ × H² × H²背景，产生了具有丰富结构的新对偶背景，并在D-膜间建立了对称的对偶链接链。

Abstract: We proceed to construct a non-Abelian dual pair for the $AdS_2 \times H^2 \times H^2$ background by applying the non-Abelian T-duality (here as Poisson-Lie T-duality on a semi-Abelian double). By using a certain parameterization of the $6$-dimensional Lie group ${A}_2 \otimes {A}_2 \otimes A_2$ we construct the original $σ$-model including the $AdS_2 \times H^2 \times H^2$ metric in the absence of $B$-field. It is shown that the dual background constructed by means of the Poisson-Lie T-duality is supported by a $B$-field and a metric whose contains a physical singularity. By studying the behavior of the dual spacetime at small $(r , y, u)$ coordinates, we show that the dual metric with a zero field strength and a non-trivial dilaton field make up a solution for the vanishing of the one-loop beta-function equations. Furthermore, at large $(r , y, u)$, it is shown that the $AdS_2 \times H^2 \times H^2$ solution is preserved under the non-Abelian T-duality. Finally, using the duality map obtained from the canonical transformation description of the Poisson-Lie T-duality for the gluing matrix which locally defines the properties of the D-brane, we find seven different cases of the gluing matrices for the $AdS_2 \times H^2 \times H^2$ $σ$-model and its dual pair. ### [160] [Krylov Complexity for Time-Dependent Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10454)
*Amin Faraji Astaneh,Parsa Kafashi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究时间依赖哈密顿量下态的Krylov扩展复杂度（Krylov spread complexity），针对周期性驱动系统在Floquet理论框架内利用Magnus展开（Magnus expansion）进行系统性近似，并将该框架扩展到非周期驱动情形，提出了全局与分段Magnus展开两种实用方法，用于分析广泛时间依赖量子系统中的复杂度增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间依赖哈密顿量（time-dependent Hamiltonians）驱动的量子态复杂度演化是一个基础而尚未充分探索的问题，现有工具在处理此类系统时存在局限性。

Method: 对于周期性驱动系统，在Floquet理论（Floquet theory）框架内利用Magnus展开对Floquet哈密顿量进行系统性近似；对于非周期驱动情形，在全局截断Magnus展开失效时，引入分段Magnus展开（piecewise Magnus expansion）作为替代方案。

Result: 证明了Magnus展开在Floquet哈密顿量无法闭合形式表达时提供了有效的近似方法；同时表明分段Magnus展开在全局展开失去收敛性或精度时仍可靠。

Abstract: We investigate Krylov spread complexity for states evolving under time-dependent Hamiltonians. For periodically driven systems, we formulate the problem within Floquet theory and show how the Magnus expansion provides a systematic approximation when the Floquet Hamiltonian is not available in closed form. We then extend this framework beyond periodic driving and demonstrate that, in addition to the globally truncated Magnus expansion, a piecewise Magnus expansion provides a reliable method when the global expansion loses convergence or accuracy. Our results provide practical tools for analyzing complexity growth in a broad class of time-dependent quantum systems.

### [161] [Quantum Horizon and Quantum Membrane Paradigm from Black Hole Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10561)
*Chong-Sun Chu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从黑洞的矩阵量子力学出发，发展了微观量子膜范式（quantum membrane paradigm）。通过模糊球（fuzzy sphere）拓扑诱导的Berry磁单极（Berry monopole）及最低朗道能级（LLL）态，构建了由微观LLL自由度组成的动态量子膜，并导出了包含量子、频率和螺旋度依赖修正的边界条件，推广了经典入射膜条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于黑洞的矩阵量子力学模型，其中量子黑洞由模糊球及半填充的费米海（half-filled Fermi sea）视界部分子（horizon partons）描述。分析模糊球拓扑诱导的Berry磁单极，证明部分子耦合到该单极形成最低朗道能级（LLL）态，其引导中心动力学产生欧姆电流、霍尔电流和极化电流。引入包含黑洞、环境和双基本链接区的双块矩阵构型，通过离对角链接模的凝聚将视界规范场与外部Maxwell场的边界值锁定。

Result: 部分子电流成为外部场的物理边界源。所构建的动态量子膜取代了经典膜范式的虚构膜，并由微观LLL自由度占据。导出的边界条件推广了经典入射膜条件，给出了显式的量子、频率依赖和螺旋度依赖的修正，为探测视界的微观量子结构提供了可能。

Abstract: We develop a microscopic quantum membrane paradigm from the matrix quantum mechanics of black holes [1]. It was proposed that a quantum black hole is described by a fuzzy sphere together with a half-filled Fermi sea of horizon partons. We show that the topology of the fuzzy sphere induces a Berry monopole, providing a microscopic origin for the monopole appearing in the tunneling description of the decay of quantum black hole. Because the partons couple to the fuzzy sphere as fundamental degrees of freedom, they are sensitive to this monopole and form Lowest-Landau-Level (LLL) states rather than ordinary propagating two-dimensional fermions. Their guiding-center dynamics generates Ohmic, Hall, and polarization currents on the horizon. To couple these currents to an external electromagnetic field, we introduce a two-block matrix configuration comprising black-hole, environmental, and bifundamental link sectors. Off-diagonal link modes become tachyonic near the fuzzy sphere and condense, dynamically locking the horizon gauge field to the boundary value of the external Maxwell field. The parton current thereby becomes a physical boundary source for the exterior field. Our construction replaces the fictitious membrane of the classical paradigm with a dynamical quantum membrane populated by microscopic LLL degrees of freedom. The resulting boundary condition generalizes the classical ingoing membrane condition and yields explicit quantum, frequency-dependent, and helicity-dependent corrections, offering a possible probe of the microscopic quantum structure of the horizon.

### [162] [Certified boundary-magic witness for state-dependent proto-area in a holographic code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10663)
*Luis Lozano*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了四量子比特乘积-EPR全息码（product-EPR holographic code）中七种不同形变对边界熵、恢复保真度及稳定子Rényi魔力的影响，发现仅物质控制的键运动形变产生边界熵的二次逻辑态依赖，并提出一个基于投影稳定子Rényi二次型的边界见证量（boundary witness），该量在六种对比形变（comparison deformations）下为零、在键运动形变下为全局凸正，但受资源划分的投影空间限制而普适性有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索全息纠错码（holographic error-correcting code）中形变效应与边界熵（boundary entropy）、逻辑态依赖（logical-state dependence）之间的关系，并寻找一种仅由形变本身决定、不依赖魔力（magic）的边界响应见证量。

Method: 采用一个四量子比特乘积-EPR全息码，比较局域（local）、二分（bipartite）、键稳定子（bond-stabilizing）和键移动（bond-moving）等七种哈密顿量形变。通过精确对角化获得边界熵的逻辑态依赖性；通过优化信道Choi态的相干信息（coherent information）选择状态无关的物理恢复（state-independent physical recovery），并利用半正定规划（semidefinite program）最大化纠缠保真度（entanglement fidelity）。将精确稳定子Rényi二次型（stabilizer-Rényi quadratic form）向配对Pauli切空间外投影，定义了一个前导阶边界见证量。

Result: 仅物质控制的键运动形变产生前导二次逻辑态依赖的边界熵；物理恢复在固定耦合下达到半正定规划最优值至数值精度，但恢复熵减法留下非零变分前面积响应（variational proto-area response）。总稳定子Rényi魔力在无边界响应的形变下仍非零，因此不能表征该效应。边界见证量的全局凸最小值在键运动形变下为正，在六种对比形变下为零；但在参考-物质-几何资源划分下，配对Pauli张成完整投影切空间，该见证量对所有厄米形变均为零。两边界扩展仍保留该退化性，但展现出分裂几何结构残余（split-geometry structural residual）和逻辑态依赖的切割切换（logical-state-dependent cut switch）。

Conclusion: 该研究构建了一个有限码边界见证量，但并非通用魔力定律（universal magic law）或连续引力动力学（continuum gravitational dynamics）的推导。

Abstract: We study a four-qubit product-EPR holographic code whose reconstructing region contains matter and one leg of a geometry bond. Seven deformations compare local, bipartite, bond-stabilizing, and bond-moving operators. Exact spectra show that only matter-controlled bond motion produces a leading quadratic logical-state dependence of the boundary entropy. We select one state-independent physical recovery by optimizing coherent information of the channel Choi state. A separate semidefinite program maximizes entanglement fidelity over all channels. At fixed coupling the physical recovery attains that optimum to numerical precision, while recovered-entropy subtraction leaves a nonzero variational proto-area response. Total stabilizer Renyi magic is also nonzero for deformations with no boundary response, so it does not characterize the effect. Projecting the exact stabilizer-Renyi quadratic form away from pairwise Pauli tangents defines a leading-order boundary witness. Its global convex minimum is positive for the bond-moving deformation and zero for the six comparisons. For the reference-matter-geometry resource partition, however, pairwise tangents span the full projective tangent space at the product-EPR base, so the witness vanishes for every Hermitian deformation. A two-bound extension retains this degeneracy but exhibits a split-geometry structural residual and a logical-state-dependent cut switch. These results establish a finite-code witness, not a universal magic law or continuum gravitational dynamics.

Abstract: The one-loop effective Lagrangian of quantum electrodynamics for dyons (dQED) with a $U(1) \times U(1)$ gauge symmetry is derived using the Schwinger proper-time method. We identify the analog of the Schwinger pair-production limit and compute the corresponding nonlinear equations of motion. The electromagnetic response of the model is analyzed by linearizing the equations of motion around a purely magnetic background. From the resulting plane-wave solutions, we obtain the effective permittivity and permeability tensors, along with the associated dispersion relations and refractive indices for parallel and perpendicular polarization modes. The refractive indices involve hybrid superpositions of both gauge sectors, as illustrated in the symmetric case $q_{(1)} = q_{(2)}$. ### [164] [Krylov Complexity from Loschmidt Amplitude](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10921)
*Debarghya Chakraborty*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过将Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）表达为Loschmidt振幅（Loschmidt amplitude）对扰动参数的导数，建立了两个量子动力学诊断量之间的解析联系，并基于此框架推导出Krylov复杂度的几何上界、时间导数表达式及基于扰动力度的分类方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Krylov复杂度是量子动力学（quantum dynamics）的重要诊断工具，与量子混沌（quantum chaos）和算符增长（operator growth）等度量存在明确关联。Loschmidt振幅的衰减受经典Lyapunov指数控制。建立两者之间的解析联系，有助于统一理解量子复杂度的动力学行为。

Method: 利用Krylov复杂度算符（Krylov complexity operator）的代数性质，将Krylov复杂度表达为Loschmidt振幅对角度变量φ的导数，其中φ参数化两哈密顿量之间的扰动。由此定义编码整个复杂度分布的谱传播子（spectral propagator），并研究时间与φ张成的二维量子几何（quantum geometry）。

Result: 证明了Krylov复杂度受其对应的二维几何体积（volume）的上界约束；将Krylov复杂度的时间导数表达为另一Loschmidt振幅；根据Lanczos系数（Lanczos coefficients）的增长性质，该振幅中的扰动项可被截断；提出了基于扰动强度对Krylov复杂度动力学进行分类的方案，并将其与谱传播子的φ导数相关联。

Conclusion: 建立了Krylov复杂度与Loschmidt振幅之间的一般性解析关系，导出了存活振幅（survival amplitude）时间依赖性与Krylov空间度量（Krylov space measures）之间的普适联系，为量子复杂度的分类和几何理解提供了统一框架。

Abstract: Krylov complexity is a powerful diagnostic of quantum dynamics, with clear connections to other measures of quantum chaos and operator growth. One such measure is the Loschmidt amplitude, defined as the overlap of initially identical states evolved under two slightly different Hamiltonians. Its decay in certain systems is controlled by the classical Lyapunov exponent. Using the algebraic properties of the Krylov complexity operator, we express Krylov complexity as the derivative of a Loschmidt amplitude whose perturbation is parameterized by an angular variable $φ$. This formulation allows us to define a spectral propagator that encodes the entire complexity distribution, which we characterize for specific types of systems. We study the two-dimensional quantum geometry spanned by time and $φ$ where the original and deformed trajectories reside, demonstrating that Krylov complexity is upper-bounded by its volume. We also express the time derivative of Krylov complexity in terms of a distinct Loschmidt amplitude. Depending on the growth of the Lanczos coefficients, the perturbation term in this amplitude can be truncated. We propose that the strength of this perturbation provides a classification scheme for Krylov complexity dynamics and relate it to the $φ$-derivative of the spectral propagator. Using this analytical framework, we derive general relations between the time-dependence of the survival amplitude and Krylov space measures.

### [165] [Revisiting wormhole-induced global symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10981)
*Kiyoharu Kawana*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文论证量子引力中虫洞（wormhole）效应不会必然破坏整体对称性（global symmetry），因为对α参数的系综平均（ensemble average）会由对称点主导，对称性破缺临界点的贡献被双重指数因子压制。标准U(1) Peccei–Quinn模型属于此类，传统轴子品质问题（axion quality problem）在虫洞诱导的有效理论中不会出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力理论中普遍认为整体对称性不能存在，其关键机制是引力瞬子（gravitational instantons）或欧几里得虫洞（Euclidean wormholes）通过α参数产生局域对称性破缺算符。本文质疑这一结论是否必然成立，即虫洞是否一定会显式破坏整体对称性。

Method: 通过对α参数进行系综平均（ensemble average）分析，研究对称破缺临界点与对称点对路径积分贡献的相对大小。利用瞬子作用量（instanton action）$S_{\rm ins}$ 刻画破缺贡献的压制程度。

Result: 系综平均由对称点 $\overrightarrowα=0$ 主导，对称性破缺临界点 $\overrightarrowα\neq 0$ 的贡献被双重指数因子 $\exp(-e^{2S_{\rm ins}})$ 强烈压制。标准U(1) Peccei–Quinn模型属于此类，虫洞诱导的有效理论中不会出现传统轴子品质问题。该分析对一般U(1) p-形式整体对称性（p-form global symmetry）均适用。

Conclusion: 虫洞效应对整体对称性的破坏并非必然，通过对α参数的系综平均，对称性可以被有效恢复。这一结果为量子引力中整体对称性的存在性提供了新的理解视角。

Abstract: It is widely believed that global symmetries cannot exist in a consistent theory of quantum gravity. A prominent mechanism underlying this expectation is provided by gravitational instantons or Euclidean wormholes, whose contributions to the Euclidean path integral generates local symmetry-breaking operators in the effective action with couplings parametrized by the $α$-parameters $\overrightarrowα=(α_1^{},α_2^{},\cdots)$. The appearance of these $α$-parameters is often taken as evidence that wormholes explicitly break global symmetries. In this paper, we argue that this conclusion is premature. The fate of the symmetry is determined by the ensemble average over these $α$-parameters. We show that, under broad situations, this average can be sharply dominated by the symmetric point $\overrightarrowα=0$, while contributions from other symmetry-breaking critical points $\overrightarrowα\neq 0$ are typically suppressed by a doubly exponential factor $\exp(-e^{2S_{\rm ins}})$, where $S_{\rm ins}$ is the instanton action. In particular, standard $\mathrm{U}(1)^{}$ Peccei--Quinn models fall into this class, implying that the conventional axion quality problem does not arise in the wormhole-induced effective theory. Our analysis is formulated for general $\mathrm{U}(1)^{}$ $p$-form global symmetries.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在建立纽结理论中经典构造（卫星与拼接）与三维拓扑量子场论（TQFT）中链环补空间态之间的系统联系，期望利用TQFT框架为这些构造提供算子化的描述，并揭示其与JSJ分解的内在关系。

Method: 将卫星和拼接构造转化为沿环面边界（torus boundaries）粘合流形的操作，TQFT为这些构建块赋予作用于对应环面希尔伯特空间（torus Hilbert space）的多线性算子（multilinear operators）；给出这些算子的显式构造，并利用它们构建链环补空间态；通过纠缠熵计算分析不同JSJ结构下的纠缠模式。

Result: 给出了卫星和拼接构造对应的TQFT多线性算子的显式公式，展示了如何用这些算子构建链环补空间态；通过Seifert纤维化链环补、Hopf链补及Whitehead加倍Hopf链补的纠缠熵计算，验证了不同JSJ分解结构导致不同的纠缠模式。

Conclusion: TQFT视角为卫星和拼接构造提供了一个统一的算子化框架，该框架与JSJ分解自然相容，能够将链环补空间态表达为JSJ片段对应的基本算子网络；不同的JSJ结构在纠缠熵上表现出可区分的模式，表明TQFT方法有望成为研究纽结补空间拓扑结构的有效工具。

Abstract: We consider the classical satellite and splice constructions of knot theory from the perspective of link-complement states in three-dimensional topological quantum field theory (TQFT). These states are prepared by a TQFT on a link-complement manifold, namely a manifold with multiple disjoint torus boundaries, obtained by removing a thickened link from a closed ambient three-manifold. In this setting, satellite and splice constructions are realized by gluing manifolds along torus boundaries, and the TQFT assigns to these building blocks multilinear operators acting on the corresponding torus Hilbert spaces. We give explicit prescriptions for these operators and show how they can be used to build link-complement states. This construction is closely related to the JSJ decomposition of link-complement manifolds. While splicing builds manifolds by gluing along tori, the JSJ decomposition cuts a manifold along essential tori into canonical pieces. From the TQFT point of view, this expresses a link-complement state as a network of elementary operators associated with the JSJ pieces. We illustrate this framework by studying the entanglement entropy of Seifert-fibered link complements, Hopf-chain complements, and complements of Whitehead-doubled Hopf chains, showing how their different JSJ structures lead to distinct entanglement patterns.

</details>


### [167] [Evading Cosmological Strong Coupling in Non-minimally Coupled Vector Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11125)

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入额外的导数相互作用，解决了Proca理论中非最小曲率耦合导致的标量自由度零传播速度（c_s²=0）问题，恢复了标量扰动的非退化二次动力学，并在参数空间的开区域中实现了正定标量动能矩阵与实正高频传播速度。研究还揭示了矢量凝聚趋于零时的非均匀极限行为，并确认了一个稳定的de Sitter不动点。

Method: 作者在Proca理论中引入一个额外的导数相互作用（derivative interaction），以提升标量自由度的零传播速度退化，恢复标量扰动（scalar perturbations）的非退化二次动力学。

Result: 在参数空间的开区域中，标量动能矩阵（scalar kinetic matrix）为正定，高频传播速度为实正，从而在二次层次上消除了与c_s²=0模式相关的强耦合特征。同时发现，当时间矢量凝聚（temporal vector condensate）趋于零时存在非均匀极限：在固定非零A₀下，形式上的极端紫外区域出现一个鬼场（ghost），而零凝聚分支的动力学结构不同。该鬼场出现的动量尺度随A₀→0推向越来越高能。此外，确认了一个稳定的de Sitter不动点（de Sitter fixed point），其A₀≠0，周围存在有限区域满足标量无鬼条件（no-ghost condition）和高频稳定性条件。

Conclusion: 所提出的导数相互作用可以有效消除Proca理论中由非最小曲率耦合引起的强耦合退化问题；但鬼场是否最终位于有效场论截断（EFT cutoff）之上，取决于EFT截断的独立确定。

Abstract: Recent analyses of Proca theories with non-minimal curvature couplings have uncovered an additional scalar degree of freedom with an identically vanishing propagation speed, $c_s^2=0$, signaling a scale-dependent strong-coupling problem. In this {\it Letter}, we show that an additional derivative interaction can lift this zero-speed degeneracy and restore a non-degenerate quadratic dynamics for the scalar perturbations. In an open region of parameter space, the scalar kinetic matrix is positive definite and the high-frequency propagation speeds are real and positive. At quadratic order, this removes the specific signature of strong coupling associated with the $c_s^2=0$ mode. We also uncover a non-uniform limit as the temporal vector condensate approaches zero: at fixed nonzero $A_0$, the formal extreme-ultraviolet regime develops a ghost, while the kinetic structure of the exactly vanishing-condensate branch is different. The momentum scale at which this ghost appears is pushed toward increasingly high values as $A_0\to0$. Whether the ghost scale ultimately lies above the EFT cutoff depends on an independent determination of the EFT cutoff. Finally, we identify a stable de Sitter fixed point with $A_0\neq0$, surrounded by a finite region in which the scalar no-ghost and high-frequency stability conditions remain satisfied.

### [168] [Conjugate Boundary Conditions, Kaluza-Klein Fermions, and an Extended Seesaw Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11150)

Abstract: In this paper, we discuss the conjugate boundary condition (CBC), which has recently been studied as a way of realizing a Majorana fermion within a compactified five-dimensional theory ($\mathcal M^4\otimes S^1/Z_2$). Although each nonzero Kaluza-Klein (KK) mode is also naively expected to be described by two Majorana fermions, we show by direct calculation that they can be combined into a Dirac spinor in the free theory or up to the level of the quadratic term in the Lagrangian. This difference comes from the fact that an accidental U(1) symmetry exists in the KK mode sector, though such a symmetry does not appear in the zero mode sector. We also point out that the compatibility between the CBC and the axial U(1) transformation plays a crucial role in the diagonalization of the KK mode.

We find that a nontrivial bulk interaction between a CBC fermion and a chiral-orbifold fermion is allowed. As an application, we construct an extended seesaw scenario by utilizing both boundary conditions and such nontrivial bulk interactions. The resulting seesaw scenario has a different property in contrast with the conventional extended seesaw scenario; namely, the above new non-trivial interactions cause lepton number violation (LNV), while the Majorana mass term in our model does not violate lepton number.

### [171] [Brouwer Degree of Thermodynamic Multicritical Points in Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11394)
*Bidyut Hazarika,Prabwal Phukon*

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于黑洞热容（heat capacity）的拓扑框架，通过构造二维热力学向量场，利用Brouwer度（Brouwer degree）刻画临界点的局域拓扑，并证明每个AdS黑洞系统具有全局守恒的拓扑荷（topological charge）。系统临界点数目变化时总拓扑荷保持不变，拓扑转变由携带相反Brouwer度的拓扑中性缺陷对（topologically neutral defect pairs）的产生或湮灭驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于黑洞热容构造一个二维热力学向量场（two-dimensional thermodynamic vector field），其孤立零点对应系统的临界点。利用Brouwer度表征每个临界点的局域拓扑，作为局域守恒的拓扑量。将该形式体系应用于多个AdS黑洞解进行验证。

Result: 每个AdS黑洞系统具有一个全局守恒的拓扑荷。当热力学参数变化导致临界点数目改变时，总拓扑荷保持不变。拓扑转变由携带相反Brouwer度的拓扑中性缺陷对的产生或湮灭主导。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一的拓扑框架，用于理解黑洞系统中热力学多重临界点的涌现、演化和分类。

Abstract: In this manuscript, we propose a novel topological framework based on the heat capacity of black holes to investigate the topology of thermodynamic multicritical points. We construct a two-dimensional thermodynamic vector field whose isolated zeros correspond to the critical points of the system. The local topology of each critical point is characterized by its Brouwer degree, which serves as a locally conserved topological quantity. Applying this formalism to several AdS black hole solutions, we demonstrate that each system possesses a globally conserved topological charge. Although the number of thermodynamic critical points changes as the thermodynamic parameters are varied, the total topological charge remains invariant throughout the evolution. We show that these topological transitions are governed by the creation or annihilation of topologically neutral defect pairs carrying opposite Brouwer degrees. Our results provide a unified topological framework for understanding the emergence, evolution, and classification of thermodynamic multicritical points in black hole systems.

Abstract: In this paper, we considered two-particle variants of the N-extended Euler-Calogero-Moser and Calogero models. Due the translation invariance, the center of mass can be decoupled (together with the corresponding fermions), leaving us with specific superconformal mechanics. Additional bosonic variables (spin variables) can easily be incorporated into the supercharges and the Hamiltonian. In the case of the Euler-Calogero-Moser model, the supersymmetry in the two-particle cases admits an unexpected extension from Osp(N|2) to SU(1,1|N) superconformal symmetry. The case of the Calogero model leads to purely Osp(N|2) superconformal mechanics. The way to get rid of the well-known problems along this path is to have a higher number of fermions present in the system.

### [174] [Bethe Ansatz without Nesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11617)
*Gleb Arutyunov,Hrachya Babujian,Minghao Gao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对有理 $\mathfrak{gl}_\ell$ 自旋链的矢量表示，发展了一种非嵌套 Bethe  ansatz 描述，通过量子谱曲线（quantum spectral curve）和分离变量（separation-of-variables）框架，推导出仅涉及动量承载 Bethe 根的封闭 Bethe 方程系统，并识别出由基本转移矩阵递归层级构成的谱结构，最终将全部谱数据压缩至第一个 Baxter 多项式 $Q_{1}(u)$ 中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的嵌套 Bethe ansatz（nested Bethe ansatz）在处理高秩 $\mathfrak{gl}_\ell$ 自旋链时引入了大量辅助 Bethe 根，导致描述复杂。本文旨在消除这些辅助根，建立一种更紧凑的非嵌套表述，以简化谱的表征并揭示量子谱曲线、转移矩阵融合关系（transfer-matrix fusion relations）与 $Q$-系统之间的内在联系。

Method: 从量子谱曲线和分离变量框架出发，推导了仅含动量承载 Bethe 根的封闭 Bethe 方程系统。具体对 $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ 和 $\mathfrak{gl}_4$ 自旋链显式构造，再推广至任意秩。通过基本转移矩阵的递归层级结构，由低阶转移矩阵的正则性条件（regularity conditions）生成层级关系，并最终由普遍秩-$\ell$ 方程 $\mathcal{R}_{\ell}=0$ 闭合。还研究了准经典 Gaudin 极限，以 $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ 为例展示了无极点形式的 Gaudin 方程如何自然定义标量三阶 $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ oper。

Result: 得到以下主要结果：(1) 非嵌套 Bethe 方程仅涉及动量承载根，消除了所有辅助 Bethe 根；(2) 本征态的完整谱数据仅由第一个 Baxter 多项式 $Q_{1}(u)$ 编码；(3) 所有基本转移矩阵的特征值均可表示为仅含动量承载根的显式表达式；(4) 在准经典极限下，$\mathfrak{gl}_3$ 自旋链的非嵌套 Bethe 方程退化为无极点形式的 Gaudin 方程，对应于标量三阶 $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ oper。

Conclusion: 本文建立的非嵌套 Bethe ansatz 框架为有理 $\mathfrak{gl}_\ell$ 自旋链的谱提供了一种紧凑的描述，揭示了量子谱曲线、转移矩阵融合关系与截断 $Q$-系统（truncated $Q$-system）之间的直接联系。该工作在理论上简化了高秩自旋链的可解性结构，并为后续 Gaudin 模型及经典极限下的几何对应提供了新视角。

Abstract: We develop a non-nested Bethe ansatz description of rational $\mathfrak{gl}_\ell$ spin chains in the vector representation. Starting from the quantum spectral curve and the separation-of-variables framework, we derive closed systems of Bethe equations involving only the momentum-carrying Bethe roots. The construction is worked out explicitly for the $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ and $\mathfrak{gl}_4$ spin chains and then generalized to arbitrary rank. A central result of this work is the identification of a recursive hierarchy associated with the fundamental transfer matrices. The hierarchy is generated by regularity conditions of the lower transfer matrices and closes through a universal rank-$\ell$ equation $\mathcal{R}_{\ell}=0$. This equation replaces the final level of the conventional nested Bethe ansatz and eliminates all auxiliary Bethe roots. Consequently, the complete spectral data of an eigenstate are encoded solely in the first Baxter polynomial $Q_{1}(u)$. We further obtain explicit expressions for the eigenvalues of all fundamental transfer matrices in terms of the momentum-carrying roots alone. The resulting formulation provides a compact characterization of the spectrum of rational $\mathfrak{gl}_\ell$ spin chains and reveals a direct connection between the quantum spectral curve, transfer-matrix fusion relations, and a truncated $Q$-system underlying the non-nested description. Finally, we investigate the quasi-classical (Gaudin) limit of the non-nested Bethe equations. For the $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ spin chain, we show that the leading non-trivial contribution gives rise to Gaudin equations whose pole-free form naturally defines a scalar third-order $\mathfrak{gl}_3$ oper.

</details>


### [175] [Holographic Timelike Entanglement and Subregion Complexity in Localized AdS3*S3*T4 Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11641)
*Jitendra Pal,Yu Shi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在渐近 AdS₃×S₃×T₄ 几何的局域化黑洞（black-pole解）中研究了类时纠缠熵（timelike entanglement entropy）和类时子区域复杂度（timelike subregion complexity），发现二者以不同方式探测几何结构：类时纠缠产生复数提升面积，而类时复杂度产生实有限重整化体积。在精确 black-pole 几何中，时间族呈现非单调行为，需固定边界区间选择，且当边界区间增大时，所选分支向内移动并敏感于局域化 cap-horizon 过渡区，展示了 BTZ 解和大 r 描述中不存在的局域化几何效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展类时洛伦兹型可观测量（timelike Lorentzian observables）在非全局对称黑洞背景下的应用，弥补 BTZ 解无法刻画局域化内部球面（internal sphere）效应的不足。

Method: 采用局域化类时方案（localized timelike prescription），在角标签 θ₀ 处构建分支轮廓（branch profile），随后沿物理内角 θ 提升；通过 spacelike 和 timelike 洛伦兹分支构造可观测量，并在精确 black-pole 几何中进行计算。

Result: 类时纠缠熵给出复数提升面积，类时复杂度给出实有限重整化体积；大 r 区域主导角依赖消失，恢复短区间行为；精确 black-pole 中时间族非单调，需固定边界区间选择；随边界区间增大，分支向内移动并敏感于 cap-horizon 过渡区域。

Conclusion: 类时洛伦兹可观测量能够探测 BTZ 解和大 r 描述中缺失的局域化几何效应，为研究局域化黑洞结构提供了新的诊断工具。

Abstract: We study timelike entanglement entropy and timelike subregion complexity in localized black holes with asymptotic AdS3*S3*T4 geometry, focusing on the black-pole solution. Unlike the BTZ solution, the black pole exhibits a nontrivial dependence on the internal sphere through the functions $K_y(r,θ)$ and $G(r,θ)$. Both observables are constructed from spacelike and timelike Lorentzian branches, but they probe the geometry in different ways: timelike entanglement yields a complex lifted area, while timelike complexity gives a real, finite renormalized volume. We employ a localized timelike prescription in which the branch profile is built at an angular label $θ_0$ and subsequently lifted over the physical internal angle $θ$. In the large-$r$ regime, the leading angular dependence drops out, recovering the expected short-interval behaviour. In the exact black-pole geometry, the temporal families become non-monotonic, making a fixed-boundary-interval selection essential. As the boundary interval increases, the selected branches move inward and become sensitive to the localized cap-horizon transition region. These results demonstrate that timelike Lorentzian observables probe localized-geometry effects that are absent in BTZ and in the leading large-$r$ description.

</details>


### [176] [Notes on the bootstrap of four-point conformal integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11645)
*Xuhang Jiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个自举工作流（bootstrap workflow），结合主奇点（leading singularities）、单值多重对数（single-valued multiple polylogarithms）和区域展开（expansion by regions）边界数据，用于计算位置空间中的四点共形积分（four-point conformal integrals），成功处理了包含所有非平面f-图扇区在内的三圈和四圈情形，并提供了适用于当前AI模型读取的软件包。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四点共形积分在共形场论（conformal field theory）和散射振幅计算中具有基础性地位，但现有方法在处理高阶（尤其是四圈及以上）非平面积分时面临计算困难，亟需一种系统且可拓展的计算框架。

Method: 采用自举工作流（bootstrap workflow），以主奇点（leading singularities）为起点，构造单值多重对数（single-valued multiple polylogarithms）形式的积分核函数（ansätze），并通过区域展开（expansion by regions）提供边界数据（boundary data）。对于三圈情形，15个不等价积分基（inequivalent integrand basis）中有14个可直接由HyperlogProcedures计算，最后一个由Gram恒等式（Gram identity）确定。对于四圈情形，通过将具有多个主奇点的积分分解为具有更简单切割结构（cut structure）的片段来降低复杂度。

Result: 三圈情形下所有不等价积分基均被成功计算。四圈情形下，一些目前其他方法难以或无法计算的积分通过该工作流得以求解。

Conclusion: 该方法不仅适用于三圈情形，也可拓展至四圈及可能更高圈阶；针对多主奇点积分的分解策略显著提升了自举方法的处理能力。此外，提供的包含技能文件（skill files）的软件包可直接被当前AI模型读取和使用，有利于自动化计算。

Abstract: We set up a bootstrap workflow to study four-point conformal integrals in position space, using leading singularities, single-valued multiple polylogarithmic ansätze and boundary data from expansion by regions. These four-point conformal integrals are general in the sense that they are generated by the four-point projections of all possible $f$-graphs, including all non-planar $f$-graph sectors. For three-loop cases, fourteen of the fifteen inequivalent integrand basis can be directly calculated by \texttt{HyperlogProcedures} and the last one is fixed by Gram identity. Then we concentrate on how far the bootstrap workflow can go for four-loop cases, though it works for three-loop cases as well. We show that integrals with several leading singularities can be made tractable by decomposing them into pieces with simpler cut structure. Some four-loop integrals which can not be calculated or very hard to be calculated by other methods for now are obtained in this way. We also provide a package with skill files which is suitable to be read and used by current AI models.

</details>


### [177] [Modular structures in the DSSYK partition function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11828)
*Matteo Beccaria,Eleonora Alfinito*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了双标度SYK模型（DSSYK）磁盘配分函数$Z(β)$的低温展开，证明其可由拟模Eisenstein级数$E_{2},E_{4},E_{6}$及其微分恒等式组织，并利用模$S$对偶性推导出半经典低温展开，分解为微扰塔（perturbative tower）和非微扰扇区（non-perturbative sector），后者由$\widetilde q=e^{-4π^{2}/λ}$控制。非微扰修正的闭式表达与双局域-Liouville（bilocal-Liouville）鞍点作用量的指数精确匹配，暗示了这些非微扰修正的体时空起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前人关于双标度SYK模型（double-scaled SYK model, DSSYK）的低温行为研究主要局限于严格$β\to\infty$的极限，缺乏对有限低温下微扰与非微扰结构的系统理解。本文旨在通过精确的Bessel函数表示，建立DSSYK磁盘配分函数$Z(β)$在低温区域（大$β$展开）的完整组织结构，并揭示其与拟模形式（quasi-modular form）及模对偶性（modular $S$-duality）的深层联系。

Method: 利用DSSYK磁盘配分函数$Z(β)$的精确Bessel函数表示，在大自变量（低温）下展开，将其组织为经典的拟模Eisenstein级数环$E_{2},E_{4},E_{6}$及其微分恒等式的形式。利用该环的模$S$对偶性（modular $S$-duality）导出小耦合$λ$下的半经典低温展开，分离出微扰塔（perturbative tower）和非微扰扇区（non-perturbative sector）。在每个$\widetilde q$阶数上确定$λ$二阶的非微扰修正闭式解，并证明整个结构源于一个将模导数（modular derivative）与温度导数耦合的精确微分方程。

Result: 低温展开可被Eisenstein级数环系统组织；半经典展开分裂为微扰部分和非微扰部分，非微扰扇区由$\widetilde q=e^{-4π^{2}/λ}$控制；在每个$\widetilde q$阶数上给出了$λ$二阶的非微扰修正闭式表达式，且该级数可重求和（resum）为紧凑的Eisenstein级数形式，将先前半经典结果推广到$β$有限区域；发现整个结构遵循一个耦合模导数与温度导数的单一精确微分方程；证明了$Z(β)$的非微扰扇区在所有$λ$阶数上精确支持与已知双局域-Liouville鞍点（bilocal-Liouville saddles）的on-shell作用量相同的指数。

Conclusion: DSSYK磁盘配分函数的低温结构完全由拟模形式决定，其非微扰修正具有明确的体时空解释，指向DSSYK Schwarzian极限中双局域-Liouville鞍点的bulk起源。

Abstract: We study the low-temperature expansion of the disk partition function $Z(β)$ of the double-scaled SYK model (DSSYK) at fixed coupling $λ=2p^{2}/N$, where $N$ is the number of Majorana fermions and $p$ is the number of fermions in each interaction term, both taken to infinity. We show that the exact Bessel-function representation of $Z(β)$, expanded at large argument (corresponding to low temperature), can be organized in terms of the classical ring of quasi-modular Eisenstein series $E_{2},E_{4},E_{6}$ and their differential identities. Exploiting the modular $S$-duality properties of this ring, we derive the semiclassical (small $λ$) low-temperature expansion of $Z(β)$, splitting it into a perturbative tower and a non-perturbative sector controlled by $\widetilde q=e^{-4π^{2}/λ}$. At each order in $\widetilde q$, we determine the non-perturbative correction in closed form up to second order in $λ$; the resulting series resums into a compact expression in the same Eisenstein series, extending previous semiclassical results beyond their strict $β\to\infty$ limit. We further show that this entire structure follows from a single, exact differential equation coupling a modular derivative to derivatives with respect to temperature. Finally, we prove that the non-perturbative sector of $Z(β)$ is exactly supported, to all orders in $λ$, on the same exponents as the on-shell actions of known bilocal-Liouville saddles of the DSSYK Schwarzian limit, pointing to a well-defined bulk origin for these non-perturbative corrections.

</details>


### [178] [Effective dynamics and quantum information in de Sitter wedge holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11848)
*Sabyasachi Maulik,Soumen Pari*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于楔形全息（wedge holography）思想，研究德西特（de Sitter, dS）楔形区域中的余二维全息对偶（codimension-two holography）。提出一个由两条端世界膜（end-of-the-world branes）和反德西特（Anti-de Sitter, AdS）体时空构成的构造，其与一个生活在d-1维球面上的非酉共形场论（CFT）对偶。通过配分函数和全息纠缠熵的计算支持该对偶，并验证了纠缠熵第一定律与岛规则（island prescription）在Page曲线中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将全息原理推广到德西特时空背景，研究德西特时空的量子引力性质；具体基于楔形全息框架探索余二维全息对偶的可行性。

Method: 构造一个d+1维反德西特体时空，由两条带有d维德西特几何的端世界膜所边界限制；通过配分函数计算、全息纠缠熵分析、质量谱分析以及纠缠熵第一定律的验证来检验该对偶关系；并采用岛规则研究简化模型中的Page曲线。

Result: 配分函数和全息纠缠熵的计算支持所提出的双重对偶关系；表明对偶共形场论是非酉的；在框架内验证了纠缠熵第一定律。

Conclusion: 所提出的德西特楔形全息构造确实实现了一种余二维全息对偶，其对偶场论生活在d-1维球面上且具有非酉性，该框架能够容纳纠缠熵第一定律和岛规则下的Page曲线分析。

Abstract: In this paper, we study codimension-two holography in a de Sitter (dS) wedge setup, based on the idea of wedge holography. We consider a $d+1$-dimensional Anti-de Sitter (AdS) bulk spacetime bounded by two end-of-the-world branes with $d$-dimensional de Sitter geometry. We propose that this configuration is holographically dual to a conformal field theory (CFT) living on a $d-1$-dimensional sphere. Our computations of the partition function and holographic entanglement entropy support this duality and indicate that the dual CFT is non-unitary. We also analyze the mass spectrum in dS wedge holography. We verify the first law of entanglement entropy within this framework. Finally, we make use of the island prescription to study the Page curve in a simplified model within our dS wedge holography framework.

### [179] [Extending the infrastructure of the BAM code towards resistive general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamics: tests and first applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11670)
*Matthew Beaudoin,Maximilano Ujevic,Ramon Jaeger,Anna Neuweiler,Henrique Gieg,Kenta Kiuchi,Tim Dietrich*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在数值相对论代码BAM中扩展实现了电阻性广义相对论磁流体动力学（resistive GRMHD）描述，并通过基准测试和孤立/双中子星系统模拟验证了该框架，发现平行磁场方向的电场分量可达总电场强度的10%，揭示了非理想效应对后并合残骸长期演化建模的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星内部极强的磁场与脉冲星、短伽马射线暴等天体现象密切相关。理想磁流体动力学（ideal magnetohydrodynamics）近似（假设无限电导率）虽能很好描述中子星内部，但无法捕捉欧姆耗散（Ohmic dissipation）和磁重联（magnetic reconnection）等非理想过程，因此需要发展包含有限电导率的电阻性广义相对论磁流体动力学框架。

Method: 在现有数值相对论代码BAM中引入电阻性广义相对论磁流体动力学（general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic, GRMHD）描述；通过一套狭义相对论磁流体动力学基准测试进行验证，并对孤立和双中子星系统进行稳定模拟。

Result: 在双中子星系统的模拟中，研究了有限电导率对磁场放大、质量抛射及非理想GRMHD效应的影响。特别地，在理想情况下为零的平行于磁场的电场分量在该模型中可达总电场强度的10%。

Conclusion: 非理想效应对后并合残骸的长期演化建模具有潜在重要性，尤其在低密度区域。尽管目前研究限于简化的分段多方状态方程（piecewise-polytropic equations of state），但新开发的电阻性GRMHD框架已展现其能力，为未来采用更真实微观物理的研究铺平了道路。

Abstract: Many astrophysical phenomena, including pulsars and short gamma-ray bursts, are associated with the extremely strong magnetic fields present in neutron stars and neutron star mergers. While the ideal magnetohydrodynamic approximation, which assumes infinite conductivity, provides an excellent description of the neutron-star interior, it cannot capture non-ideal processes such as Ohmic dissipation and magnetic reconnection. To overcome this limitation, we present an extension of the numerical-relativity code BAM incorporating a resistive general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic (GRMHD) description. We validate the new implementation through an extensive suite of special-relativistic magnetohydrodynamic benchmark tests and by performing stable simulations of isolated and binary neutron star systems. For the latter, we investigate the impact of finite conductivity on magnetic-field amplification, mass ejection, and non-ideal GRMHD effects. In particular, we find that the component of the electric field parallel to the magnetic field, which is zero in the ideal case, can reach up to 10% of the total electric field strength. This highlights the potential importance of non-ideal effects for accurately modeling the long-term evolution of post-merger remnants, particularly in low-density regions. Although the present study is restricted to simplified piecewise-polytropic equations of state, it demonstrates the capabilities of the new resistive GRMHD framework and paves the way for future investigations employing more realistic microphysics.

</details>


### [180] [Tidal deformation and strain accumulation of solid compact stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11780)
*Hongxiang Shen,Yong Gao,Hong-Bo Li,Ren-Xin Xu*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文基于奇异子星（strangeon-star）模型构建了固态致密星潮汐形变的建模框架，发现固态与流态奇异子星的潮汐形变度存在约40%的相对差异，且双星并合过程中内部应变积累可达~10⁴⁶ erg，引发大规模断裂并释放能量，后者可作为短伽马暴的前驱信号，结合引力波波形特征为固态致密星的存在提供多信使（multi-messenger）检验途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉泽星这类致密星的内部究竟是流体还是固态，目前尚缺乏有效检验，而两种状态所预测的潮汐响应（tidal response）截然不同。现有引力波观测（如GW170817）仅在流体内部假设下约束物态方程，亟需建立固态致密星潮汐形变的模型以填补这一空白。

Method: 基于奇异子星模型，引入剪切模量（shear modulus）μ = 10³⁴ erg cm⁻³，构建固态致密星潮汐形变的理论框架；通过比较固态与流态下的潮汐形变度（tidal deformability）及I–Love关系偏差，分析双星旋近过程中内部应变（internal strain）的积累与断裂行为。

Result: 固态与流态1.4 M☉奇异子星的潮汐形变度相对差异约为40%，对应约10%的I–Love关系偏离；内部应变峰值位于星体中心，当引力波频率达数百赫兹时发生大规模断裂，可释放~10⁴⁶ erg的弹性能量，足以驱动短伽马暴前驱（short γ-ray-burst precursor）。

Conclusion: 固态到流态的转变会改变潮汐响应，从而在引力波波形及相位中留下印记；结合前驱电磁辐射，这些引力波特征提供了检验脉泽星内部固态性质的多信使观测途径。

Abstract: The tidal deformability of compact stars encodes the equation of state of dense matter, and gravitational-wave observations such as GW170817 have begun to constrain it under the assumption of a fluid interior. Yet whether the interior of pulsar-like compact stars is fluid or solid remains largely untested, despite the distinct tidal responses the two states predict. In this work, based on the strangeon-star model, we develop a framework for modeling tidal deformation in solid compact stars. Adopting a shear modulus of $μ= 10^{34}\,\mathrm{erg}\,\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$, we find a relative difference of approximately $40\%$ in tidal deformability between solid and fluid strangeon stars of $1.4\,M_\odot$, corresponding to a $\sim 10\%$ deviation from the universal I--Love relation. We further model the accumulation of internal strain during binary inspiral and find that it peaks near the stellar center. When the gravitational-wave frequency reaches several hundred $\rm Hz$, large-scale fracturing occurs and can release up to $\sim 10^{46}\,\mathrm{erg}$ of elastic energy, sufficient to power short $γ$-ray-burst precursors. This solid-to-fluid transition alters the tidal response and imprints on the waveform and phase of the emitted gravitational radiation. Combined with the precursor electromagnetic emission, these gravitational-wave signatures offer a multi-messenger avenue to test the solid nature of pulsar-like compact stars.

</details>

# nucl-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [181] [Exploring the origin of D$^0$ meson elliptic flow in PbPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.02 TeV using event shape engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11017)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 基于CMS探测器在铅铅（PbPb）对撞中收集的5.02 TeV数据，利用事件形状工程（event-shape engineering）方法，研究了初始态几何对粲夸克强子——D⁰介子椭圆流（elliptic flow）的影响。结果表明D⁰介子的二阶傅里叶系数v₂与带电粒子的v₂强相关，说明初始态几何显著影响粲夸克强子的集体流行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究高能重离子碰撞中初始态几何对粲夸克强子（charm hadron）——具体为D⁰介子——椭圆流（elliptic flow）的影响程度，以理解重夸克在夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）中热化与集体运动机制。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在2018年采集的铅铅（PbPb）对撞数据（质心系能量5.02 TeV，积分亮度0.607 nb⁻¹），采用事件形状工程（event-shape engineering）技术，从前向区域横向能量分布中提取非对称参数q₂，并以其线性关联的带电粒子v₂作为初始态离心率（eccentricity）代理变量，进而分析近快度区域D⁰介子v₂与带电粒子v₂的相关性。

Result: D⁰介子的v₂值（横向动量2–30 GeV范围内）与带电粒子的v₂值在基于相似q₂区间选择时呈现强相关关系，表明初始态几何对粲夸克强子流的形成有显著影响。

Conclusion: 初始态几何显著影响粲夸克强子在重离子碰撞中的集体流发展；模型计算（涉及D⁰介子与带电粒子的热化与集体运动）与实验结果进行了比较，为进一步理解重夸克在QGP中的输运性质提供了约束。

Abstract: The influence of the initial-state geometry on the elliptic flow of prompt D$^0$ mesons in high-energy heavy ion collisions is explored. A lead-lead (PbPb) data sample at a center-of-mass energy per nucleon pair of 5.02 TeV and with an integrated luminosity of 0.607 nb$^{-1}$ was collected in 2018 with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC. Based on these data, an event-shape engineering technique is used to isolate collisions with similar geometrical properties. An asymmetry parameter, $q_2$, is first determined from the distribution of transverse energy in the forward region of the detector. This parameter is shown to be linearly correlated with the elliptic anisotropy of inclusive charged particles measured near mid-rapidity, as characterized by the second-order Fourier coefficients, $v_2$. Taking the charged particle $v_2$ coefficients as proxies for the initial-state eccentricity, the correlation of D$^0$ meson $v_2$ values near mid-rapidity with those of inclusive charged particles is then studied. For D$^0$ mesons with transverse momenta in the range of 2$-$30 GeV and for different degrees of collision overlap, the $v_2$ values are found strongly correlated with those for charged particles when selected based on similar $q_2$ intervals. This correlation suggests that the initial-state geometry substantially impacts the development of charm-hadron flow in heavy ion collisions. A model calculation that explores the thermalization and collective motion of D$^0$ mesons and charged particles is compared to the experimental results.

</details>


### [182] [Search for two-neutrino double electron capture in $^{36}$Ar with the DarkSide-50 detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11476)
*DarkSide-50 Collaboration,:,P. Agnes,I. F. M. Albuquerque,T. Alexander,A. K. Alton,M. Ave Pernas,H. O. Back,G. Batignani,W. M. Bonivento,B. Bottino,S. Bussino,M. Cadeddu,M. Cadoni,A. Caminata,N. Canci,M. Caravati,N. Cargioli,M. Carlini,S. Chashin,A. Chepurnov,S. Davini,S. De Cecco,D. Díaz Mairena,F. Dordei,G. Fiorillo,D. Franco,F. Gabriele,C. Galbiati,G. K. Giovanetti,M. Gromov,M. Gulino,B. R. Hackett,F. Hubaut,A. Ianni,V. Ippolito,F. Karpeshin,D. Korablev,G. Korga,M. Kuss,M. La Commara,M. Lai,M. Lissia,O. Lychagina,I. Machulin,S. M. Mari,J. Maricic,R. Milincic,M. Morrocchi,P. Musico,M. Pallavicini,L. Pandola,E. Pantic,E. Paoloni,K. Pelczar,V. Pesudo,A. Pocar,S. Pordes,P. Pralavorio,M. Razeti,A. L. Renshaw,M. Rescigno,D. Sablone,O. Samoylov,S. Sanfilippo,R. Santorelli,C. Savarese,A. Sheshukov,M. Skorokhvatov,O. Smirnov,A. Sotnikov,S. Stracka,Y. Suvorov,R. Tartaglia,G. Testera,A. Vishneva,B. Vogelaar,M. Wada,Y. Wang,S. Westerdale,M. M. Wojcik,C. Yang,G. Zuzel*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用DarkSide-50实验的低放射性地下液氩靶，首次对$^{36}$Ar的双中微子双电子俘获（two-neutrino double electron capture）过程（KK壳层和KL壳层）进行搜索，未发现显著信号，设定了半衰期下限 $T_{1/2} > 9.2 \times 10^{19}$ yr（90%置信水平），并对未来DarkSide-20k实验的灵敏度进行了评估，预期可提升约100倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中微子双电子俘获是一种罕见的核衰变过程，此前实验未曾探测到该过程。本文旨在首次搜索$^{36}$Ar中KK壳层和KL壳层的双中微子双电子俘获，以填补该衰变通道的实验空白。

Method: 利用DarkSide-50实验的低放射性地下液氩靶（underground argon, UAr），结合约12吨·天的曝光量，对$^{36}$Ar的双电子俘获衰变进行搜索。同时考虑UAr中$^{36}$Ar的同位素丰度（0.007%），并在统计显著无信号的情况下推导半衰期下限，还评价了未来DarkSide-20k实验的预期灵敏度。

Result: 未观察到统计显著的信号，在90%C.L.下设定$^{36}$Ar双电子俘获过程半衰期下限为 $T_{1/2} > 9.2 \times 10^{19}$ yr。未来DarkSide-20k实验运行10年的预期灵敏度约为当前结果的100倍。

Conclusion: 首次对$^{36}$Ar的双中微子双电子俘获进行了实验搜索，给出了目前最严格的半衰期下限，并指出未来DarkSide-20k实验将大幅提高该衰变通道的探测灵敏度。

Abstract: Two-neutrino double electron capture is a rare nuclear decay where two electrons are simultaneously captured from the atomic shells and two neutrinos are emitted. We report on the first search for two-neutrino double electron capture in the $\textit{KK}$- and $\textit{KL}$-shells of $^{36}$Ar using the low-radioactivity liquid argon target from underground sources in the DarkSide-50 experiment. No statistically significant excess was observed with approximately 12 ton-day exposure of underground argon (UAr) and, taking into account the $^{36}$Ar isotopic abundance in UAr (0.007%), we set a limit on the half-life of the two-electron capture process in $^{36}$Ar of $T_{1/2} > 9.2 \times 10^{19}$ yr at 90% C.L. The sensitivity of the DarkSide-20k experiment, which will become operational in the next few years, was also evaluated and is expected to increase by a factor $\sim$100 with 10 years of expected operation and assuming the same $^{36}$Ar abundance as in the DarkSide-50 underground argon target.

</details>

Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于LHCb探测器收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对$B^-\rightarrow \itΛ^+_c\overline{p}π^{-}$衰变进行了振幅分析（amplitude analysis），在$\itΛ^+_cπ^{-}$不变质量谱中观测到两个新的粲重子态$\itΣ_c(2900)^0$和$\itΣ_c(3200)^0$，并确定了三个高质量态的质心质量（mass）与宽度（width）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展粲重子谱学（charm baryon spectroscopy）的已知态清单，深入理解粲重子的内部结构与动力学（structure and dynamics）。

Method: 利用LHCb探测器在质心能量为7、8、13 TeV下收集的质子-质子对撞数据（总积分亮度$9\text{ fb}^{-1}$），对$B^-\rightarrow \itΛ^+_c\overline{p}π^{-}$衰变进行振幅分析；对高质量态采用Breit-Wigner线形（Breit-Wigner line shapes）进行质量与宽度的拟合。

Result: 在$\itΛ^+_cπ^{-}$不变质量谱中确认了已知的$\itΣ_c(2455)^0$、$\itΣ_c(2520)^0$、$\itΣ_c(2800)^0$重子，并发现了两个新态$\itΣ_c(2900)^0$和$\itΣ_c(3200)^0$；测定了三个高质量态的质量和宽度。

Conclusion: 该结果扩展了粲重子谱学的已知态清单，为理解粲重子的结构与动力学提供了关键实验依据。

Abstract: An amplitude analysis of the $B^-\rightarrow \itΛ^+_c\overline{p}π^{-}$ decay is performed using proton-proton collision data, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $9\text{ fb}^{-1}$, collected with the \mbox{LHCb} detector at center-of-mass energies of 7, 8, and 13$\text{ TeV}$. In the $\itΛ^+_cπ^{-}$ invariant-mass spectrum, the known $\itΣ_c(2455)^0$, $\itΣ_c(2520)^0$, $\itΣ_c(2800)^0$ baryons are observed, along with two new states: $\itΣ_c(2900)^0$ and $\itΣ_c(3200)^0$. The masses and widths of the three high-mass states, modeled with Breit--Wigner line shapes, are determined. This result expands the landscape of charm baryon spectroscopy and provides crucial data for understanding charm baryon structure and dynamics.

</details>

Varghese,I. Vasilyev,G. Vasseur,E. Villa,U. Virginet,T. Vladisavljevic,T. Wachala,H. T. Wallace,J. G. Walsh,D. Wark,M. O. Wascko,A. Weber,R. Wendell,M. J. Wilking,C. Wilkinson,C. Winterstein,C. Wret,J. Xia,Z. Xie,K. Yamamoto,T. Yamamoto,T. Yamazumi,C. Yanagisawa,Y. Yang,T. Yano,N. Yershov,U. Yevarouskaya,M. Yokoyama,Y. Yoshimoto,N. Yoshimura,A. Zalewska,J. Zalipska,G. Zarnecki,J. Zhang,X. Y. Zhao,H. Zheng,H. Zhong,M. Ziembicki,M. Zito*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了利用T2K ND280探测器测量缪子中微子（muon-neutrino）在氧核上的带电电流（charged-current）截面，以运动学不平衡量（kinematic imbalance, KI）为函数，末态无π介子且至少有一个质子。同时对碳和氧靶进行联合提取，揭示了核效应建模的新见解，并指出现有中微子事件生成器都无法完全描述实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子振荡实验（如T2K和Hyper-Kamiokande）使用多种靶核，其系统不确定性受核效应建模精度制约。现有模型对中微子-原子核相互作用的描述尚不完善，亟需高精度、多靶核联合测量的截面数据，以约束模型并降低振荡参数测量的系统误差。

Method: 利用T2K ND280探测器，测量无π介子、末态至少含一个质子的缪子中微子带电电流反应截面，以运动学不平衡量（KI）为观测量。截面同时对碳靶和氧靶进行双微分联合提取，直接比较两种靶核的相关性。

Result: 在测量的所有相空间区域，广泛使用的中微子事件生成器（neutrino event generators）均无法完全描述实验数据。碳和氧靶的联合测量提供了对两种靶核间关联的直接敏感性。

Conclusion: 现有核效应模型尚需改进，研究结果为当前及未来中微子振荡实验中中微子-原子核相互作用建模的优化指明了方向。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of muon-neutrino charged-current cross section as a function of kinematic imbalance (KI) observables on oxygen with no pions and at least one proton in the final state, using the T2K ND280 detector. The cross section is extracted simultaneously for carbon and oxygen targets and double-differentially as a function of several KI observables, providing new insight into the modeling of nuclear effects. This joint measurement offers direct sensitivity to the correlations between two targets, a key ingredient for reducing systematic uncertainties in neutrino oscillation experiments that employ multiple target nuclei, such as T2K and Hyper-Kamiokande. Comparisons with predictions from widely used neutrino event generators show that none of the models fully describe the data across all regions of measured phase space. These results highlight possible directions where improvements in neutrino-nucleus interaction modeling are needed for current and future neutrino oscillation experiments.

</details>

Shvarev,A. Shvartsman,V. Siccardi,N. Skrobova,K. Skwarczynski,D. Smyczek,M. Smy,J. T. Sobczyk,H. Sobel,F. J. P. Soler,A. J. Speers,R. Spina,A. Srivastava,P. Stowell,Y. Stroke,I. A. Suslov,A. Suzuki,M. Suzuki,S. Y. Suzuki,M. Tada,A. Takeda,Y. Takeuchi,K. Takeya,H. K. Tanaka,H. Tanigawa,A. Teklu,V. V. Tereshchenko,N. Thamm,C. Touramanis,N. Tran,T. Tsukamoto,M. Tzanov,M. Vagins,M. Varghese,I. Vasilyev,G. Vasseur,E. Villa,U. Virginet,T. Vladisavljevic,T. Wachala,H. T. Wallace,J. G. Walsh,D. Wark,M. O. Wascko,A. Weber,R. Wendell,M. J. Wilking,C. Wilkinson,C. Winterstein,C. Wret,J. Xia,Z. Xie,K. Yamamoto,T. Yamamoto,T. Yamazumi,C. Yanagisawa,Y. Yang,T. Yano,N. Yershov,U. Yevarouskaya,M. Yokoyama,Y. Yoshimoto,N. Yoshimura,A. Zalewska,J. Zalipska,G. Zarnecki,J. Zhang,X. Y. Zhao,H. Zheng,H. Zhong,M. Ziembicki,M. Zito*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本论文基于T2K实验的ND280探测器，首次实现了碳靶与氧靶上缪子中微子CC0πNp相互作用的联合测量，在δp_T-δα_T和p_N-cosθ_μ两个双微分运动学不平衡（KI）观测量空间中开展分析。结果表明现有中微子-原子核相互作用模型无法充分描述数据，KI观测量展现出强大的区分能力，凸显了改进中微子相互作用发生器中理论核模型（nuclear model）的必要性，以提高中微子振荡测量的精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前中微子振荡实验的精度受限于中微子-原子核相互作用的建模不确定性。现有模型对碳靶和氧靶上具体相互作用通道（如CC0πNp）的描述缺乏充分的实验检验，亟需高分辨率的观测量来区分不同模型的差异。

Method: 利用T2K实验的ND280探测器，对缪子中微子（muon neutrino）在碳和氧靶上产生的带电流无π子（CC0π）且包含质子喷注（Np）的相互作用进行联合测量。研究在δp_T-δα_T和p_N-cosθ_μ两个双微分运动学不平衡（kinematic imbalance, KI）观测量空间内分析数据，详细定义了信号区与控制区的事件选择、系统不确定性评估以及信号提取流程，并进行了验证研究。

Result: 分析结果表明，当前的中微子-原子核相互作用模型无法充分描述实验数据。KI观测量展现出很强的模型区分能力（discriminating power），能够有效揭示现有模型的不足。

Conclusion: 该测量凸显了在中微子相互作用发生器（neutrino interaction generator）中改进理论核模型（nuclear model）的迫切性，这是实现更高精度中微子振荡测量的关键前提。

Abstract: We present the first joint measurement of muon neutrino CC$0πNp$ interactions on carbon and oxygen targets, in two double-differential kinematic imbalance (KI) observable spaces, $δp_{T}$-$δα_{T}$ and $p_{N}$-$\cosθ_μ$. The measurement employs the ND280 detector of the T2K experiment and includes a detailed description of the event selection used to define signal and control regions, the evaluation of systematic uncertainties, and the signal extraction procedure, together with validation studies supporting a robust cross-section measurement. The results of this analysis indicate that current neutrino-nucleus interaction models do not adequately describe the data, and demonstrate the strong discriminating power of KI observables. This measurement highlights the need for improved theoretical nuclear modeling within neutrino interaction generators to achieve increased precision in neutrino oscillation measurements.

</details>


### [186] [Search for dark matter in a signature with a four-prong large-radius jet in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11016)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用CMS探测器在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，搜索与初态辐射喷注（initial-state radiation jet）共产生的非瞬发暗物质（nonprompt dark matter）对候选者。信号特征包含一个四叉大半径喷注（four-prong large-radius jet），由长寿命暗区粒子衰变产生；通过基于图神经网络（graph neural network）的喷注子结构标记器进行识别。未观测到超出标准模型预期的显著信号，在95%置信水平上对信号强度设定了上限。这是首次在洛伦兹增强拓扑（Lorentz-boosted topology）下针对非瞬发暗物质对进行的搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质（dark matter, DM）的存在已获天体物理和宇宙学观测广泛支持，但其粒子性质仍未知。标准模型中不存在合适的暗物质候选者，因此需要超出标准模型的新物理。该研究旨在通过LHC对撞实验，搜索长寿命暗区粒子衰变产生的非瞬发暗物质对，以检验基于矢量或轴矢量媒介子（vector/axial-vector mediator）的暗物质信号模型。

Method: 分析基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度138 fb⁻¹。信号模型包含一个重矢量或轴矢量媒介子，产生长寿命暗区粒子，进而衰变为一个稳定暗物质粒子和一个轻玻色子（light boson），后者衰变为夸克。候选信号要求存在一个四叉大半径喷注，由基于图神经网络（graph neural network）的喷注子结构标记器识别，以重建轻暗物质媒介子衰变为四个夸克的过程。标准模型背景通过专用控制区（control regions）从数据中估计，并在缺失横动量（missing transverse momentum）谱中寻找潜在信号。

Result: 未观测到超出标准模型预期的显著信号过剩。在95%置信水平上，对信号强度设定了上限，上限值表示为媒介子质量或相关耦合的函数。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在洛伦兹增强拓扑（Lorentz-boosted topology）下搜索非瞬发暗物质（nonprompt dark matter）对，其特征为大半径喷注和大缺失横动量。未发现新物理现象，设定了相应的排除上限，为后续暗物质搜索提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for a pair of nonprompt dark matter (DM) candidates produced in association with an initial-state radiation jet, in a signature containing a four-prong large-radius jet, is presented. The signal model contains a heavy vector or axial-vector mediator, which produces long-lived dark-sector particles that decay to a stable DM particle and a light boson, which decays to quarks. The analysis is based on data collected in the years 2016$-$2018 with the CMS detector at the LHC in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Signal candidates feature large-radius jets, which are identified using a jet substructure tagger based on a graph neural network. The large-radius jet aims to reconstruct the decay of light DM mediators into four quarks, which are produced in association with two stable DM particles. The standard model background contributions are estimated from data using dedicated control regions. The missing transverse momentum spectrum is probed for a potential signal over the expected background. No significant excess over the standard model expectation is observed. Upper limits at 95% confidence level are set on the signal strength as functions of either the mediator mass or the relevant coupling. This is the first search for a pair of nonprompt DM candidates in the Lorentz-boosted topology, characterized by a large-radius jet and large missing transverse momentum.

</details>


### [187] [Antineutron reconstruction in electromagnetic calorimeters with mixed-representation learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11139)
*Yangu Li,Hongtian Yu,Yuyang Huang,Zhi Cao,Yunxuan Song,Yunfan Liu,Yajun Mao,YangHeng Zheng,Xiao-Rui Lyu,Qixiang Ye*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于物理启发的表示方法——混合表示量热网络（MrCAL），用于从电磁量能器（ECAL）读出数据中重建长寿命中性强子（反中子）。该方法将互补的视觉与序列表示分支集成到统一的目标检测架构中，联合预测粒子身份、动量方向与动量大小。实验表明，反中子动量方向重建精度最高提升96%，并首次实现仅从ECAL读出直接测量动量大小，在1 GeV/c下动量分辨率约为17%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在GeV量级加速器实验中，用传统电磁量能器（ECAL）重建长寿命中性强子（如反中子）长期存在瓶颈，因为这些强子与原子核的相互作用超出了ECAL的原生响应范围。

Method: 基于高能反中子在ECAL中沉积能量的两种不同模式，提出混合表示量热网络（MrCAL, Mixed-representation Calorimetric Network），在统一的目标检测（object-detection）架构中集成互补的视觉表示分支与序列表示分支，联合预测粒子身份、动量方向与动量大小。

Result: 反中子动量方向重建精度最高提升96%；首次实现仅从ECAL读出直接测量动量大小，在1 GeV/c下动量分辨率约为17%；模型在多种物理过程与背景环境的泛化测试中保持稳健性能。

Conclusion: 该工作为大型实验设施的现有ECAL系统解锁了新的测量能力，通过创新的末态中性强子探测拓宽了其科学应用范围。

Abstract: A long-standing bottleneck in GeV-scale accelerator experiments lies in reconstructing long-lived neutral hadrons in conventional electromagnetic calorimeters (ECALs), where hadron--nucleus interactions fall outside the detector's native response regime. In this paper, we develop a physics-inspired representation approach for antineutron reconstruction using a large corpus of real collision data. Motivated by two distinct energy deposition patterns from the penetrating high energy antineutrons in ECALs, we propose a Mixed-representation Calorimetric Network (MrCAL) that integrates complementary visual and sequential representation branches within a unified object-detection architecture. This architecture jointly predicts particle identity, momentum direction, and momentum magnitude. Our approach improves the precision of antineutron momentum-direction reconstruction by up to 96% and, for the first time, enables direct measurement of momentum magnitude solely from ECAL readouts, achieving a momentum resolution of approximately 17% at 1 GeV/c. The model maintains robust performance through comprehensive generalization tests spanning a wide variety of physics processes and background environments. This work unlocks a novel measurement capability for legacy ECAL systems at large experimental facilities, broadening their scientific scope via innovative final-state neutral-hadron detection.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次以超过10σ的显著性观测到η_c → p\bar{p}η衰变过程，基于BESIII探测器收集的约27亿ψ(3686)事件样本。测量了两种干涉情景（相长/相消）下的联合分支比和η_c衰变分支比，并完整给出了统计、系统及外输入不确定度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: η_c → p\bar{p}η衰变此前尚未被实验观测到，对其进行测量有助于检验量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）在粲偶素（charmonium）衰变中的非微扰行为，并理解共振与非共振过程的干涉效应。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器采集的(2712.4 ± 14.3)×10^6个ψ(3686)事例，通过ψ(3686) → γ p\bar{p}η过程进行分析。考虑η_c共振衰变与非共振ψ(3686) → γ p\bar{p}η过程之间的干涉，分别在相长干涉（constructive interference）和相消干涉（destructive interference）两种假设下提取信号。

Result: 联合分支比ψ(3686)→γη_c, η_c→p\bar{p}η在相长干涉下为(3.2 ± 0.1 ± 0.9)×10^{-6}，相消干涉下为(8.7 ± 0.3 ± 2.1)×10^{-6}。η_c→p\bar{p}η的分支比在相长和相消干涉下分别为(0.90 ± 0.04 ± 0.21 ± 0.13)×10^{-3}和(2.42 ± 0.07 ± 0.48 ± 0.34)×10^{-3}。观测显著性超过10个标准差（standard deviation）。

Conclusion: 首次观测到η_c→p\bar{p}η衰变，显著性超过10σ。测量结果表明共振与非共振过程的干涉效应显著影响分支比的提取，需在两种干涉情景下分别给出结果。第三个不确定度来源于ψ(3686)→γη_c分支比的外输入误差。

Abstract: The decay $η_c\to p\bar{p}η$ is observed for the first time with a significance of exceeding $10σ$. It is found by analyzing $(2712.4 \pm 14.3)\times10^{6}$ $ψ(3686)$ events accumulated at the BESIII detector. The measured branching fraction of $η_c\to p\bar{p}η$ via $ψ(3686) \to γp \bar{p} η$ is significantly influenced by the interference between the resonant $η_c$ decay and the non-resonant process $ψ(3686) \to γp \bar{p} η$ and is measured in both constructive- and destructive-interference scenarios. The joint branching fraction of $ψ(3686)\to γη_c$, $η_c\to p\bar{p}η$ is measured to be $(3.2 \pm 0.1 \pm 0.9)\times10^{-6}$ or $(8.7 \pm 0.3 \pm 2.1)\times10^{-6}$ for constructive- or destructive-interference solutions, respectively, where the first uncertainties are statistical and the second systematic. The branching fraction of $η_c\to p\bar{p}η$ is determined to be $\mathcal{B}(η_c\to p\bar{p}η)=(0.90 \pm 0.04 \pm 0.21 \pm 0.13)\times10^{-3}$ or $(2.42 \pm 0.07 \pm 0.48 \pm 0.34)\times10^{-3}$ for the two solutions, respectively, where the third uncertainties are due to the uncertainty in the branching fraction of $ψ(3686)\to γη_c$.

### [189] [Study of the proccess $e^+e^-\to π^+π^-π^0π^0η$ in the c.m. energy range 1.6--2.0 GeV with the CMD-3 detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11556)
*R. R. Akhmetshin,A. N. Amirkhanov,A. V. Anisenkova,V. M. Aulchenkoa,N. S. Bashtovoy,E. V. Bedarev,D. E. Berkaev,A. E. Bondar,A. V. Bragin,V. S. Denisov,D. A. Epifanov,L. B. Epshteyn,A. L. Erofeev,G. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量e+e-湮灭到多π介子与η介子末态的反应截面，为低能强子物理、介子谱学及量子色动力学（QCD）唯象学提供实验数据。

Method: 基于CMD-3探测器在VEPP-2000对撞机上采集的积分亮度为372 pb^{-1}的数据样本，在质心能量（center-of-mass energy）范围1.6–2.0 GeV内选取信号事件，并利用不变质量分布分析反应动力学。
