Conclusion: 在1.6–2.0 GeV能区成功测量了$e^+e^- \to π^+π^-π^0π^0η$过程的截面，识别出以$\omega(782)\pi^0\eta$为主的反应动力学，并发现$\rho(770)^{\pm}$及可能的$a_0(980)$共振贡献。

Abstract: The cross section of the process $e^+e^- \to π^+π^-π^0π^0η$ has been measured using a data sample with the integrated luminosity of 372 pb$^{-1}$ collected with the CMD-3 detector at the VEPP-2000 $e^+e^-$ collider. 6300$\pm$145 signal events have been selected in the center-of-mass energy range 1.6--2.0 GeV. The total systematic uncertainty of the cross section is about 10\%. The production dynamics is dominated by the $ω(782)π^0η$ final state with a possible small contribution of the $a_0(980)$ resonance in the $π^0η$ combination. We also observe a presence of the $ρ(770)^{\pm}$ resonance signal in the $π^{\pm}π^0$ invariant mass distribution.

### [190] [Machine Learning-Based Reconstruction for Resistive Silicon Sensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11585)
*Alexander Aoki,Gaetano Barone,Leena Diehl,Gabriele Giacomini,Vagelis Gkougkousis,Hanshal Goyal,Rohan Kher,Daniel Li,Anna Macchiolo,Yevhenii Padnuik,Daria Senina,Samantha Sunnarborg,Jessica Tang,Alessandro Tricoli,Lixing Wang,Don C. Wong*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究探索了基于机器学习的重构与压缩方法，用于AC-LGAD电阻型硅传感器。通过利用关联垫片的全波形信息，引入LSTM循环神经网络和基于Transformer的拓扑无关架构，实现了约10微米位置分辨率，并支持任意垫片数量与几何形状，为未来电阻型硅传感器设计提供指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AC-LGAD传感器在实现高填充因子和良好空间分辨率的同时，信号共享机制导致读出复杂：电荷扩散至多个垫片，有用信号接近电子噪声阈值，矩阵求逆方法计算量大且对非对角线噪声敏感。因此需要开发更高效、鲁棒的重构与压缩方法。

Method: 采用基于全波形信息的机器学习方法：首先引入基于LSTM层的循环神经网络模型作为全波形重构的概念验证，并利用HLS工具测试FPGA部署可行性；随后研究波形光栅化（waveform rasterisation）与窗口选择（window-selection）方法以实现带宽缩减；最后扩展到拓扑无关的基于Transformer的架构，将垫片坐标作为输入的一部分。

Result: 基于LSTM的模型可作为全波形重构的概念验证，并已测试FPGA部署可行性；Transformer架构支持任意垫片数量和几何形状，可缓解边缘畸变，在500微米×500微米间距传感器上保持约10微米的位置分辨率。

Conclusion: 机器学习方法能有效利用关联垫片的全波形信息，正则化重构过程并提取超越二进制读出或幅度摘要的空间信息；所提出的拓扑无关架构可指导未来电阻型硅传感器的设计。

Abstract: Low-Gain Avalanche Diodes (LGADs) and AC-coupled Low-Gain Avalanche Diodes (AC-LGADs) are promising technologies for precision timing and four-dimensional tracking. In AC-LGADs, the AC pad is coupled to the resistive n$^{+}$ layer through a dielectric layer, while the gain layer remains unsegmented. This structure provides a 100\% fill factor and enables good spatial resolution with a relaxed readout pitch. The same signal-sharing mechanism that makes interpolation possible complicates the readout: charge spreads across multiple pads, the useful information can approach the electronic-noise threshold, and matrix-inversion approaches can become computationally challenging and sensitive to off-diagonal noise. In this work, we study machine-learning-based reconstruction and compression for resistive silicon sensors. We use full-waveform information from correlated pads to regularise the reconstruction and extract spatial information beyond what is available from binary readouts or reduced-amplitude summaries. We first introduce recurrent neural network models based on LSTM layers, which provide a proof-of-concept implementation for full-waveform reconstruction and have been tested for FPGA deployment using \hls. We also study routes towards bandwidth reduction with waveform rasterisation and window-selection methods, and extend the approach beyond the first model to topology-agnostic transformer-based architectures that use pad coordinates as part of the input. These models are designed to support arbitrary pad counts and geometries, mitigate edge distortions, preserve approximately $10~μ\mathrm{m}$ position resolution for $500~μ\mathrm{m}\times500~μ\mathrm{m}$ pitched sensors, and guide future resistive-silicon sensor designs

</details>


### [191] [Analytical Markov Chain for Spatiotemporal Flux Evolution of the Inner Filter Effect in Fluorescent Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11815)
*Xuhui Yang,Guofu Cao*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于时空解耦（spatiotemporal decoupling）的解析马尔可夫输运模型，通过拉普拉斯变换将多组分荧光介质中因二次内滤效应（IFE）导致的光谱畸变计算复杂度从指数级（O(N_λ^n)）降至线性级（O(N_λ + n)），从而在亚秒级时间内快速且准确地预测瞬态衰减时间谱和稳态波长谱畸变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多组分荧光介质中的发射与衰减时间谱对识别材料本征性质和优化探测器至关重要，但二次内滤效应（secondary inner filter effect, IFE）产生的波长演化会扭曲这些可观测谱。尽管蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo, MC）光线追踪能够模拟这种畸变，但其计算耗时长，阻碍了高维参数空间的优化。

Method: 提出一种基于时空解耦（spatiotemporal decoupling）的解析马尔可夫输运模型（analytical Markovian transport model）。利用拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）将连续域上的多层嵌套卷积积分转换为离散的马尔可夫转移矩阵，从而将计算复杂度从关于波长区间数 N_λ 和级联阶数 n 的指数级 O(N_λ^n) 降低至线性级 O(N_λ + n)。

Result: 得到的代数解能在亚秒级时间内将瞬态衰减时间谱评估为伽马波包（Gamma wave packets）的连续叠加，并预测由 IFE 驱动的稳态波长谱畸变。在正交和正面光谱仪配置下的验证显示，计算谱线形与 MC 模拟结果匹配。

Conclusion: 该模型可作为快速正演引擎用于加速参数空间筛选、提供探测器早期设计参考，以及作为受物理约束的输入用于事件顶点重建算法。

Abstract: Characterizing emission and decay time spectra in multi-component fluorescent media is essential for identifying intrinsic material properties and optimizing detectors. However, wavelength evolution from the secondary inner filter effect (IFE) distorts these observable spectra. While Monte Carlo (MC) ray-tracing can simulate this distortion, accumulating adequate tracking statistics requires long computation times, which hinders parameter optimization within high-dimensional spaces. This paper presents an analytical Markovian transport model based on spatiotemporal decoupling. A Laplace transform converts the multi-nested convolution integrals over continuous domains into a discrete Markov transition matrix, reducing the computational complexity from an exponential scale with respect to wavelength bins $N_λ$ and cascade order $n$, $\mathcal{O}(N_λ^n)$, to a linear scale, $\mathcal{O}(N_λ + n)$. The resulting algebraic solutions evaluate transient decay time spectra as a continuum superposition of Gamma wave packets and predict steady-state wavelength spectrum distortions driven by the IFE within a sub-second timescale. Validations across orthogonal and front-face spectrometer configurations show that the calculated spectra match MC simulations in lineshape. This model can serve as a fast forward engine to accelerate parameter space screening, provide early-stage detector design references, and act as a physics-constrained input for event vertex reconstruction algorithms.

</details>

### [192] [Computable Ergodic Optimisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11404)
*Léo Gayral,Mathieu Hoyrup*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明在零温遍历优化（zero-temperature ergodic optimisation）背景下，对于可计算势能（computable potential）并满足若干合理假设时，最大遍历平均值（maximum ergodic average）是可计算实数（computable real number），最大化测度集（set of maximising measures）是Π₁-可计算紧集（Π₁-computable compact set）；在符号动力学（symbolic dynamics）的有限型子转移（subshifts of finite type）及有限程相互作用（finite-range interactions）的更具体设定中，进一步给出了有限时间内同时计算最大遍历平均值与最大化测度集的显式算法，并配有可运行的代码库。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，物理系统与可计算性（computability）属性之间的联系成为活跃研究领域。本文受此前在正温吉布斯测度（positive temperature Gibbs measures）背景下工作的启发，旨在探索零温遍历优化框架下的可计算性问题。

Method: 在一般设定中，针对可计算势能与合理假设，利用可计算分析（computable analysis）方法证明最大值与最大化测度集的可计算性；在有限型子转移的符号动力学具体设定中，设计一个显式算法，结合有限程相互作用结构，在有限时间内输出结果，并配套提供代码仓库。

Result: 最大遍历平均值为可计算实数，最大化测度集为Π₁-可计算紧集；在有限型子转移与有限程相互作用的特例下，实现了可在有限时间内运行的显式算法。

Conclusion: 本文从可计算性视角拓宽了零温遍历优化理论的结果，并提供了实用的算法实现，有助于连接理论物理模型与计算复杂度理论。

Abstract: Links between physicals systems and computability properties have been an active field of investigation in recent years. Inspired by a previous work in the context of positive temperature Gibbs measures, we prove here that in the context of zero-temperature ergodic optimisation, for a computable potential and provided with several reasonable assumptions, the maximum ergodic average is a computable real number, and the set of maximising measures is a $Π_1$-computable compact set.
  Then, in the more specific context of symbolic dynamics, with finite-range interactions on subshifts of finite type, we provide an explicit algorithm to compute both the maximum ergodic average and the set of maximising measures in finite time, with a matching code repository.

</details>

### [193] [PHITSBench: an execution-scored benchmark for AI-assisted PHITS radiation-transport input generation using natural language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09789)
*Xianglin Ji,Svetlana V. Boriskina*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出PHITSBench——一个基于执行评分的蒙特卡罗粒子与重离子输运代码系统（PHITS）基准测试。该基准包含282个可评分任务，覆盖参数编辑、语法修复和从自然语言生成完整模拟三种工作流。评估发现，基础模型在没有领域知识时在编辑和修复任务上表现良好，但无法从头生成正确模拟；引入结构化知识目录后，从头生成成功率提升至57%，智能体执行进一步改善至66-73%，但剩余错误主要由物理可观测量的选择与配置错误主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型语言模型（LLM）在科学计算领域的评估多侧重于语法正确性，缺乏对物理可观测量的执行级验证。作者旨在构建一个可执行打分的基准测试，以系统评估AI在辐射输运建模中的实际能力。

Method: 构建PHITSBench基准，包含282个可输运评分任务，分为参数编辑（Edit）、语法修复（Repair）和从自然语言描述生成完整模拟（Reproduce）三类。每个任务采用复合指标分数（Composite Metric Score）进行评估，该分数综合执行成功率和生成结果与参考输运可观测量的一致性。使用五个基于GPT-5.4的配置进行评测，涵盖零样本提示、知识增强及智能体工作流。

Result: 无领域知识时，模型在编辑和修复任务上分别达到95%和70%成功率，但在从头生成（Reproduce track）任务上成功率为0%。引入结构化PHITS知识目录后，单次从头生成成功率升至57%；智能体执行进一步提升至66-73%，但计算成本增加。错误分析表明，剩余错误主要源于物理可观测量（observables）的选择与配置不当，而非语法生成问题。

Conclusion: 未来人工智能辅助辐射输运建模的进展，不仅依赖于基础模型自身的改进，同样取决于机器可读的知识库、领域训练数据集和执行级评估环境的建设。

Abstract: We introduce PHITSBench, an execution-scored benchmark for the Monte Carlo Particle and Heavy Ion Transport code System (PHITS). PHITSBench comprises 282 transport-scorable tasks spanning three common workflow categories: parameter editing (Edit), syntax repair (Repair ), and complete simulation generation from natural-language descriptions (Reproduce). Each task is evaluated using a Composite Metric Score that combines execution success with agreement between generated and reference transport observables. Using PHITSBench, we evaluate five GPT-5.4-based configurations ranging from zero-shot prompting to knowledge-augmented and agentic workflows. Without domain-specific knowledge, the model performs well on editing and repair tasks (95% and 70% success, respectively) but fails to generate correct simulations from scratch (0% success on the Reproduce track). A structured, machine-readable PHITS knowledge catalog, supplied alongside the user manual, raises single-shot Reproduce-task success to 57%. Agentic execution provides a further improvement to 66-73%, but at increased computational cost. Failure analysis shows that the remaining errors are dominated by incorrect selection and configuration of physical observables rather than syntax generation. These results suggest that future progress in AI-assisted radiation-transport modeling will depend as much on machine-readable knowledge bases, curated domain-training datasets, and execution-grounded evaluation environments as on advances in foundation models themselves.

</details>

### [194] [Low-Noise SiPM Light Readout and ASIC-Based Charge Readout of a Liquid Argon Time Projection Chamber for MeV Gamma-Ray Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11336)
*Satoshi Takashima,Hirokazu Odaka,Shota Arai,Kentaro Shirahama,Ryutaro Tatsumi,Hodaka Kawamura,Masashi Tanaka,Shintaro Arai,Tsuguo Aramaki,Aya Bamba,Lorenzo Fabris,Georgia Karagiorgi,Haruki Kuramoto,Jonathan LeyVa,John W. Mitchell,Aiko Miyamoto,Reshmi Mukherjee,Kaito Murakami,Azuki Nagao,Arathi Suraj,Sayana Takatsuka,Chihiro Watanabe,Shin Watanabe,Yutaro Yano,Kazushi Yawata,Hiroki Yoneda,Kohei Yorita,Jiancheng Zeng*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文研制了一款紧凑型液氩时间投影室（LArTPC）探测器NanoGRAMS，作为GRAMS项目的技术验证平台。实验表明，该探测器可成功探测60Co源的双击事件，重建的康普顿边与理论值一致，反投影成像能准确定位源位置，验证了其作为MeV伽马射线康普顿相机的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液氩时间投影室（LArTPC）有望在MeV伽马射线波段实现具有空前有效面积的康普顿相机（Compton camera），而NanoGRAMS作为伽马射线与反物质巡天（GRAMS）项目的技术验证平台，旨在验证该技术的可行性。

Method: NanoGRAMS有效体积为5.12×5.12×10 cm³，配备低噪声闪烁体与电荷读出系统：闪烁光由16个硅光电倍增管（SiPM）探测，经低温跨阻抗放大器（transimpedance amplifier）求和放大；电离电子通过3.2 mm间距像素读出，由VATA-SGD ASIC处理，基于FPGA的数据采集系统提供同步。探测器接受60Co源（1173和1332 keV）辐照，采用现象学复合模型（phenomenological recombination model）将收集电荷转换为沉积能量，并基于Geant4的蒙特卡洛模拟评估探测器响应。

Result: 成功探测到单击和双击事件；重建能谱中康普顿边（Compton edge）位于963和1118 keV，与预期值一致；对双击事件识别了相互作用序列，重建的反投影图像（back-projection image）与源位置吻合。

Conclusion: 上述结果验证了NanoGRAMS作为MeV伽马射线成像能谱学康普顿相机的可行性。

Abstract: We have developed a compact liquid argon time projection chamber (LArTPC), NanoGRAMS, as a technology demonstrator for the Gamma-Ray and AntiMatter Survey (GRAMS). LArTPCs have the potential to enable Compton cameras with unprecedented effective area in the MeV gamma-ray band. NanoGRAMS has an active volume of $5.12 \times 5.12 \times 10~\mathrm{cm^3}$ and is equipped with a low-noise scintillation and charge readout system. The scintillation light is detected by an array of 16 SiPMs ($6 \times 6~\mathrm{mm^2}$ each), whose signals are summed and amplified by a low-noise transimpedance amplifier operable at liquid argon temperature. Ionization electrons are read out with $3.2\,\mathrm{mm}$-pitch pixels and processed by VATA-SGD ASICs, with synchronization provided by an FPGA-based data acquisition system. We irradiated the detector with a $^{60}\mathrm{Co}$ source (1173 and $1332\,\mathrm{keV}$) and successfully detected both 1-hit and 2-hit events. The collected charge was converted to deposited energy using a phenomenological recombination model, and the detector response was evaluated with a Geant4-based Monte Carlo simulation. The reconstructed energy spectrum shows Compton edges at 963 and $1118\,keV$, consistent with the expected values. For 2-hit events, the sequence of interactions was identified, and the reconstructed back-projection image agrees with the source position. These results demonstrate the feasibility of NanoGRAMS as a Compton camera for MeV gamma-ray imaging spectroscopy.

</details>

### [195] [Searching for heavy charged relics in the Earth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09845)
*Reza Ebadi,Peter W. Graham,Surjeet Rajendran,Erwin H. Tanin,Samuel S. Y. Wong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过检测地球物质中捕获的重带电粒子来探索暗物质（dark matter）的新方法。通过离心或重力沉降浓缩目标材料（水或地质岩石）中的稀有粒子，再利用质谱（mass spectrometry）进行鉴定，该方法能够探测质量在1–10¹² TeV范围内、占局部暗物质密度极小比例（低至f_X~10⁻²⁰）的带电遗迹粒子（charged relics）。仅使用1升水和一台离心机（或约1立方米水无需离心）运行一个月的探路者实验，即可达到f_X~10⁻¹⁰，从而探索新的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重带电粒子作为暗物质候选体（dark matter candidate）难以通过传统直接探测方法发现，因为其与普通物质的相互作用截面极小且数量稀少，需要极大的曝光量（exposure）和高效的浓缩技术。

Method: 该方法利用重带电粒子撞击地球后在陆地物质中损失能量并被困住的特性，选用水或地质岩石等高曝光量的目标材料进行积累。随后通过离心（centrifugation）或重力沉降（gravitational settling）将稀有粒子从大量背景物质中浓缩，最后使用质谱（mass spectrometry）进行粒子鉴定。

Result: 该方法可探测质量范围1–10¹² TeV的带电遗迹粒子，其占局部暗物质密度的比例可低至f_X~10⁻²⁰（最低质量端）。一个使用1升水加一台离心机（或约1立方米水无需离心）、运行一个月的探路者实验即可达到f_X~10⁻¹⁰的灵敏度，探索现有的新参数空间。

Conclusion: 所提出的浓缩-质谱联合方案为探测超重带电暗物质候选体提供了一条可行的实验路径，且所需实验规模较小，可在短期内实现对新参数空间的探索。

Abstract: We propose a method for detecting an ambient density of heavy, electrically-charged particles. Such particles would impact the Earth, lose energy in terrestrial matter, and become trapped. We study the accumulation of these rare particles in multiple target materials that provide large exposure, such as water and geological rocks. We discuss strategies for concentrating the particles by centrifugation or gravitational settling, along with particle identification using mass spectrometry. This method enables the discovery of charged relics with masses $1-10^{12}\,{\rm TeV}$ comprising a tiny fraction of the local dark matter density, reaching down to $f_X\sim 10^{-20}$ at the lowest masses. A pathfinder experiment using only a liter of water and one centrifuge (or $\sim \text{m}^3$ and no centrifuge) operating for a month can already reach $f_X\sim 10^{-10}$ and probe new parameter space.

</details>


### [196] [Counting b-jets at the FCC-ee as a probe of top-quark flavor physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09856)
*Shaouly Bar-Shalom,Jose Wudka*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，FCC-ee在240 GeV运行能量下，通过计数末态b-喷注数目并利用b-宇称（b-Parity）这一近似守恒量子数，可将对味改变（flavor-changing）四费米子相互作用的新物理能标（new physics scale）探测灵敏度提升至约10 TeV，约为对撞机质心能量的40倍，比现有约束提高一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索未来正负电子对撞机FCC-ee对多TeV新物理（new physics）的灵敏度，特别是通过单顶夸克产生过程探测味改变（flavor-changing）的矢量（vector）、标量（scalar）和张量（tensor）接触相互作用（contact interactions）。

Method: 利用文献[1]提出的近似守恒的标准模型（Standard Model, SM）量子数"b-宇称"（b-Parity, $b_P$），将味改变$eetu_k$四费米子相互作用产生的$b_P$-奇（$b_P=-1$）信号与SM背景区分开。在质心能量$\sqrt{s}=240$ GeV的ZH运行阶段，通过计数末态b-喷注（b-jet）数目实现信号筛选。

Result: FCC-ee可探测产生矢量、标量和张量$eetu$和/或$eetc$相互作用的新重粒子所对应的新物理能标（new physics scale）$\Lambda \sim 10$ TeV，约为FCC-ee质心能量的40倍，比当前对这些四费米子算符的约束提高约一个数量级。

Conclusion: FCC-ee凭借高亮度（high luminosity）和优异的味标记（flavor-tagging）性能，是搜索b-宇称奇（$b_P$-odd）信号特征的理想平台。该探测能力高度依赖于高纯度的b-喷注标记（b-jet tagging）技术。

Abstract: We explore the sensitivity of a future FCC-ee to multi-TeV new physics (NP) that can generate vector, scalar and tensor flavor-changing (FC) $eetu_k$ contact interactions ($u_k=u,c$ for $k=1,2$), probed via single top-quark production, $e^+ e^- \to t \bar{u}_k, t \bar{u}_k γ$ (+ c.c.) and leading (following the top-quark decay) to two- and four-jet signals, $e^+ e^- \to 2j + X, 4j + X$, where $X$ denotes any non-jet final-state particles. Our analysis exploits an approximately conserved Standard Model (SM) quantum number introduced in [1] and termed "$b$-Parity" ($b_P$), which is applicable to scattering processes of the type $e^+ e^- \to n \cdot j_b + m \cdot j_\ell + X$, where $n$ and $m$ are the number of produced $b$-jets and light-jets ($u,d,c,s,$ and/or gluons) and $b_P=(-1)^n$. The FC $eetu_k$ four-fermion interactions can generate distinct $b_P$-odd ($b_P = -1$) signals in these multi-jet events, for which the only significant SM background stems from $b$-jet misidentification. We demonstrate that the FCC-ee, operating at a $\sqrt{s} = 240$ GeV (the $ZH$ run phase) with high luminosity and excellent flavor-tagging performance, is an ideal platform to search for these $b_P$-odd signatures. Indeed, by simply counting the number of final-state $b$-jets, the FCC-ee can probe NP scales of $Λ\sim 10$ TeV for the new heavy states that generate the vector, scalar and tensor $eetu$ and/or $eetc$ interactions. This reach, remarkably about 40 times the assumed FCC-ee center-of-mass energy, improves upon current bounds on some of these four-fermion operators by an order of magnitude and it critically relies on high-purity b-jet tagging.

</details>


### [197] [Benchmarking the Nearside Energy-Energy Correlators with Mellin Transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09860)
*Yuxun Guo,Feng Yuan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Mellin变换框架研究了小角度近端能量能量关联子（nearside EECs），将微扰QCD和禁闭后的标度行为统一描述，并仅用一个过渡尺度参数Λ，在NNLO精度和NNLL重求和水平上，成功描述了e⁺e⁻湮灭中的实验数据（包括ALEPH分析及跨能量早期测量）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有近端能量能量关联子（nearside energy-energy correlators）的理论描述在微扰（perturbative）与禁闭后（post-confinement）两个能区的衔接上缺乏统一框架，亟需一个能同时涵盖两种QCD标度行为的解析方案。

Method: 采用Mellin变换框架（Mellin-transform framework）将QCD在微扰和禁闭后两个能区的标度行为显式纳入；引入单一参数Λ刻画两个能区之间的过渡尺度（transition scale），结合next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) 精度与next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic (NNLL) 重求和（resummation）进行计算。

Result: 仅靠单一参数Λ，即可在NNLO+NNLL水平上精确描述e⁺e⁻湮灭中近端EECs的实验数据，涵盖ALEPH最新分析以及不同能量下的早期测量结果，拟合效果极佳。

Conclusion: 所提出的Mellin变换框架显著简化了近端EECs的理论描述，揭示了微扰与禁闭后标度行为之间过渡的单参数特征，为QCD关联函数的解析建模提供了新的有效途径。

Abstract: We investigate nearside energy-energy correlators (EECs) at small angles, explicitly incorporating the QCD scaling behavior in both the perturbative and post-confinement regimes through a Mellin-transform framework. As an illustration, we show that a single parameter, $Λ$, characterizing the transition scale between the two regimes, provides an excellent description of nearside EECs in $e^+e^-$ annihilation, including the recent ALEPH analysis as well as earlier measurements across different energies, with next-to-next-to-leading-order accuracy and next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic resummation.

</details>


### [198] [The Higgs boson through the lens of electroweak precision data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09861)
*Yannick Fischer,Johannes Haller,Andreas Hoecker,Roman Kogler,Finn Labe,Klaus Mönig,Dennis Schwarz,Jörg Stelzer*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于最新实验输入（特别是W玻色子质量的世界平均值）和前沿理论计算，更新了Gfitter全局电弱拟合分析，检验了标准模型（Standard Model）的量子结构。拟合确认了标准模型的内部自洽性，并通过κ框架结合ATLAS与CMS的信号强度测量，对希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）的总宽度及不可见/未检测衰变分支比给出了约束，同时提供了标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）中Wilson系数的边界以及FCC-ee上电弱拟合精度的展望。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过全局电弱拟合（global electroweak fit）检验标准模型（Standard Model）的量子自洽性，利用最新的实验测量（特别是更新的W玻色子质量）和更高阶的理论计算，对标准模型进行更严格的压力测试。

Method: 采用Gfitter分析框架，将最新的实验输入与前沿理论预言进行比对拟合；在希格斯扇区（Higgs sector）引入κ框架，将ATLAS与CMS的信号强度测量与电弱精确数据联合分析；并采用主导对数斜变解释（leading-logarithmic oblique interpretation）以及标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）方法对超出标准模型的效应进行参数化约束。

Result: 间接确定了W玻色子质量、希格斯玻色子质量、顶夸克质量以及有效轻子弱混合角（effective leptonic weak mixing angle）等精确可观测量，确认标准模型内部自洽性。对希格斯玻色子与矢量玻色子的耦合给出了电弱约束，从而将总宽度测定精度提升至约10%或更好，并给出了不可见和未检测衰变分支比的上限。此外还给出了SMEFT中Wilson系数的边界。

Conclusion: 当前标准模型（Standard Model）在全局电弱拟合中表现出高度内部自洽；希格斯玻色子宽度和衰变分支比的间接约束可媲美或优于直接搜索的灵敏度；未来FCC-ee实验有望显著提升全局电弱拟合的精度。

Abstract: The global electroweak fit tests the quantum structure of the Standard Model by confronting precision measurements with high-order theoretical predictions. This paper presents an updated Gfitter analysis using the latest experimental inputs, notably the new world average of the $W$-boson mass, and state-of-the-art theoretical calculations. The fit yields indirect determinations of precision observables, including the $W$ and Higgs-boson masses, the top-quark mass, and the effective leptonic weak mixing angle, confirming the remarkable internal consistency of the Standard Model. The analysis is further extended to the Higgs sector by combining ATLAS and CMS signal-strength measurements with electroweak precision data in the $κ$ framework. The resulting electroweak constraints on the Higgs couplings to vector bosons allow a determination of the total Higgs-boson width with a precision of about 10\% or better within a leading-logarithmic oblique interpretation, and provide bounds on invisible and undetected Higgs-boson branching fractions without using direct searches for invisible Higgs decays. The paper also presents bounds on Wilson coefficients in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory together with projections for the precision of the global electroweak fit achievable at the FCC-ee.

</details>


### [199] [Multipole structure of the $N \to Δ$ Transition Generalized Parton Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10901)
*June-Young Kim,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了 $N \to Δ$ 跃迁在广义部分子分布（GPDs）层面的多极结构，通过多极展开将四个跃迁 GPDs 分解为横向平面上的一个单极、两个偶极和一个四极分量，并在零倾斜极限下定义了冲击参数跃迁密度，从而在部分子层次上可视化该跃迁的横向多极结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对核子（nucleon）到 $\Delta$ 重子（baryon）跃迁的电磁和部分子结构进行更精细的刻画：传统研究主要关注跃迁形状因子（transition form factors），而广义部分子分布（GPDs）能提供更深层的 $x$ 依赖信息，因此有必要在 GPDs 框架下系统地解析该跃迁的多极结构。

Method: 利用三维自旋跃迁张量（spin-transition tensors）和横向动量转移对协变跃迁矩阵元（covariant transition matrix element）进行多极展开（multipole expansion），将四个 $N \to \Delta$ 跃迁 GPDs 分解为横向平面（transverse plane）上的单极（monopole）、两个偶极（dipole）和一个四极（quadrupole）分量，并与光前螺旋振幅（light-front helicity amplitudes）建立一一对应关系。

Result: 在零倾斜（zero-skewness）极限下，多极 GPDs 定义了冲击参数跃迁密度（impact-parameter transition densities），将横向跃迁电荷密度（transverse transition charge densities）推广到 $x$ 依赖层次。这些跃迁密度来源于两个不同强子态之间的非对角矩阵元（non-diagonal matrix elements），须与质子和 $\Delta$ 的对角密度加以区分。多极跃迁密度直观地展示了部分子 $N \to \Delta$ 跃迁在横向平面上的单极、偶极和四极结构。

Conclusion: 论文成功在 GPDs 层次揭示了 $N \to \Delta$ 跃迁的多极结构，将跃迁电荷密度推广至 $x$ 依赖的冲击参数空间，为理解该过程中部分子分布的非对角性质提供了系统框架。这一方法有助于深化对核子-$\Delta$ 跃迁内部动力学的认识。

Abstract: We establish the multipole structure of the $N \to Δ$ transition at the level of the generalized parton distributions (GPDs). We decompose the four transition GPDs into one monopole, two dipole, and one quadrupole components in the transverse plane by a multipole expansion of the covariant transition matrix element in terms of the three-dimensional spin-transition tensors and the transverse momentum transfer. These multipole components are in one-to-one correspondence with the light-front helicity amplitudes. In the zero-skewness limit, the multipole GPDs define impact-parameter transition densities, which generalize the transverse transition charge densities to the $x$-dependent level. These transition densities arise from non-diagonal matrix elements between two distinct hadronic states and must therefore be distinguished from the diagonal densities of the nucleon and the $Δ$. The multipole transition densities visualize the monopole, dipole, and quadrupole structures of the partonic $N \to Δ$ transition in the transverse plane.

</details>


### [200] [Determination of the Odderon amplitude in elastic cross-sections at high energies from scaling and analyticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11286)
*J. A. velazquez Corral,B. G. Giraud,R. Peschanski,C. Royon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文验证了LHC质子-质子（pp）弹性散射微分截面在dip-bump区域的标度律同样适用于Tevatron能量下的质子-反质子（p\bar p）散射，并通过引入负宇称振幅（Odderon）对dip/bump区域进行拟合，得到了与D0数据一致的无参数预测，最终提取并讨论了Odderon振幅的模与相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在验证LHC能量下质子-质子弹性散射微分截面在dip-bump区域的标度律（scaling amplitudes）是否同样适用于Tevatron最高能量下的质子-反质子散射，并进一步通过引入负宇称振幅（Odderon）来解释实验数据中的dip结构。

Method: 利用S矩阵（S-Matrix）形式体系固有的解析性（analiticity）推导出的“能量到相位”（energy to phase）关系，导出具有正宇称（positive signature）的标度振幅（即Pomeron）。通过拟合TOTEM合作组测量的质子-质子微分截面，并结合dip/bump区域的分析，确定负宇称振幅（negative signature amplitude，即Odderon）的贡献，从而对质子-反质子微分截面做出无参数预测。

Result: 正宇称标度振幅（Pomeron）对质子-质子散射数据的拟合在中等动量转移的dip区域与实验存在一定偏差。通过引入Odderon贡献得到的质子-反质子微分截面无参数预测与D0实验数据一致；进一步提取并讨论了Odderon振幅的模与相位。

Conclusion: 本文确认了质子-质子散射中的标度律可推广至质子-反质子散射，并表明Odderon振幅的引入是解释dip/bump区域实验数据的关键；对Odderon振幅模与相位的提取为进一步理解强相互作用的解析结构提供了依据。

Abstract: Scaling amplitudes describing $pp$ elastic scattering differential cross-sections in the dip-bump region of momentum transfer at the LHC have been recently derived~\cite{scaling}. We check that the same scaling is verified by the $p\bar p$ cross-section at the highest energy of the Tevatron. Applying the general "energy to phase" relation for a given signature, coming from the analiticity properties inherent to the S-Matrix formalism~\cite{chew}, we derive the scaling amplitude with positive signature (i.e. the Pomeron). Fitting the $pp$ differential cross-sections measured by the TOTEM collaboration leads to some tension with data in the experimental dip observed at moderate momentum transfer. Concentrating the study to the dip/bump region, we are able to determine a contribution of a negative signature amplitude (i.e. the Odderon) leading to a parameter free prediction for the $p\bar p$ differential cross-section which is in agreement with the D0 data. The extraction of the Odderon amplitude in both modulus and phase is then performed and discussed.

</details>


### [201] [Unitarization Schemes for High-Energy Elastic Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11504)
*E. G. S. Luna*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对比分析了eikonal与U-matrix幺正化方案在高能弹性散射中的应用，研究了仅由Pomeron交换主导的输入振幅，并重点评估了线性与非线性Pomeron轨迹对拟合参数稳定性和现象学描述的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更准确地描述高能弹性散射振幅的行为，需要比较不同幺正化方案（unitarization scheme）的适用性，并考察Pomeron轨迹（trajectory）形式假设对提取参数的影响。

Method: 采用eikonal幺正化方案与U-matrix幺正化方案两种框架，以仅由Pomeron交换驱动的渐近行为作为输入振幅，分别在线性（linear）与非线性（nonlinear）Pomeron轨迹假设下进行拟合并对比分析。

Result: 研究发现Pomeron轨迹的形式（线性 vs 非线性）显著影响拟合参数的数值及其稳定性，同时不同幺正化方案对数据现象学描述的适用性也存在差异。

Conclusion: Pomeron参数对轨迹假设敏感，线性与非线性轨迹在描述高能弹性散射数据时表现出不同效果；选择合适的幺正化方案与轨迹形式对获得稳定且可靠的拟合结果至关重要。

Abstract: We examine key features of the eikonal and $U$-matrix unitarization schemes and apply both frameworks to investigate the high-energy behavior of the elastic scattering amplitude, considering input amplitudes whose asymptotic behavior is driven exclusively by Pomeron exchange. Particular attention is devoted to assessing how the extracted Pomeron parameters depend on the assumed trajectory form. In this context, we compare linear and nonlinear Pomeron trajectories, evaluating their impact on the phenomenological description of the data and on the stability of the fitted parameters.

</details>


### [202] [An improved moment QCD sum rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11536)
*Jin-Peng Zhang,Xu-Liang Chen,Wei Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 针对QCD求和规则中Laplace求和规则(LSR)和矩求和规则(MSR)存在的参数选择主观性及基态质量结果不一致问题，提出改进矩求和规则(IMSR)框架，通过显式引入夸克-强子对偶性(quark-hadron duality)和对非物理参数的严格依赖条件，实现无需主观判据的唯一参数确定及基态质量与流耦合常数的同时提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QCD求和规则(LSR与MSR)虽为强子物理中重要非微扰工具，但存在显著缺陷：LSR依赖OPE收敛性(OPE convergence)与极点优势(pole dominance)等主观判据来约束参数空间；传统MSR无法提取插值流的耦合常数；且两种方法得到的基态质量经常不一致。这些不一致性和主观性长期困扰该领域，亟需改进。

Method: 提出改进矩求和规则(improved moment sum rule, IMSR)框架。显式引入夸克-强子对偶性(quark-hadron duality)，在OPE侧引入近似条件(approximation condition)作为参数的后验约束(a posteriori constraint)。对非物理参数(Q²₀, n)施加严格的依赖条件(rigorous dependence conditions)，以量化并控制其影响。

Result: IMSR框架能唯一确定对偶参数(duality parameter)的最优值及基态质量(ground-state mass)，无需任何特设(ad hoc)或主观判据，并允许同时提取流耦合常数(current coupling)。将其应用于赝标量(pseudoscalar) ud\bar{d}\bar{s} 四夸克系统(tetraquark system)，所得结果与先前LSR分析高度一致。

Conclusion: IMSR方法显著增强了QCD求和规则的稳健性(robustness)和可靠性(reliability)，有效消除了长期困扰传统表述的主观性。

Abstract: QCD sum rules are among the most important non-perturbative tools in hadron physics, with the Laplace sum rule (LSR) and moment sum rule (MSR) being the two most commonly used formulations. Despite their widespread application, both approaches have significant shortcomings: the LSR relies on subjective criteria -- namely OPE convergence and pole dominance -- to constrain the parameter space, while the conventional MSR cannot extract the coupling constant of the interpolating current. More critically, the ground-state masses obtained from these two methods are often inconsistent. In this work, we propose an improved moment sum rule (IMSR) framework that resolves these issues simultaneously. Our method explicitly incorporates quark-hadron duality, which introduces the approximation condition on the OPE side and provides a natural a posteriori constraint on the parameters. We impose rigorous dependence conditions on the unphysical parameters $(Q^2_0,n)$ to quantify and control their influence. As a result, our framework uniquely determines both the optimal value of the duality parameter and the ground-state mass, without invoking any ad hoc or subjective criteria. It also allows for the simultaneous extraction of the current coupling. Applying the IMSR to a pseudoscalar $ud\Bar{d}\Bar{s}$ tetraquark system, the results are in excellent agreement with our previous LSR analyses, validating the effectiveness of the proposed scheme. The IMSR method substantially enhances the robustness and reliability of QCD sum rules, effectively eliminating the subjectivity that has long plagued conventional formulations.

### [203] [Linearity, Nonlinearity and Universality of Regge Trajectories in Light Mesons: a Statistical Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11583)
*S. S. Afonin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对轻非奇异介子（light non-strange mesons）的质量参数化公式进行了统计与唯象比较分析，检验了两种线性Regge模型：一种具有不同的$L$和$n$斜率（Model 1），另一种采用统一斜率（Model 2）。基于两个实验数据集（27个基准态和85个扩展态）的定量模型选择表明，Model 2在整体上更优，且S波（$L=0$）态的特殊行为是造成模型间差异的主要原因。引入非线性$L$依赖修正后，S波态的质量亦可被成功描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻非奇异介子的质量可通过径向量子数$n$和轨道角动量$L$进行参数化。然而，对于不同Regge型公式（Regge-like formulas）之间的竞争性表现，缺乏系统的统计与唯象比较分析，尤其是关于斜率是否统一的模型选择问题尚未得到定量评估。

Method: 采用基于2024年粒子数据组（Particle Data Group, PDG）的27个基准态样本，以及一个包含85个态的扩展样本，对两种线性Regge模型进行拟合：Model 1为$M^2(L,n)\propto an+bL$（不同斜率），Model 2为$M^2(L,n)\propto a(n+L)$（统一斜率）。模型选择通过残差平方和（RSS）、调整后RSS、赤池信息准则（AIC）和贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）进行定量评估。

Result: 在27个基准态中，Model 2在统计上不被偏好，但这种差异主要由S波（$L=0$）态驱动。排除S波态后，两模型表现差异不再显著，信息准则选择Model 2为更简约的描述。引入物理动机驱动的非线性$L$依赖修正后，S波态的质量可被成功容纳。在85个扩展态数据集中，由于S波态的相对贡献显著减小，Model 2在统计上被优先选择，恢复了Regge谱中的库仑型简并性（Coulomb-like degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 统一斜率的线性Regge模型（Model 2）在描述轻非奇异介子质量谱时具有统计优势，S波态的特殊行为是导致模型间差异的关键因素。非线性$L$依赖修正可有效解释S波态质量，表明Regge谱中存在库仑型简并性。

Abstract: The masses of light non-strange mesons can be parameterized as a function of the radial quantum number $n$ and the orbital angular momentum $L$. We perform a comprehensive statistical and phenomenological comparative analysis of competing Regge-like formulas evaluated against two experimental datasets: a benchmark sample of 27 well-established states from the 2024 Particle Data Group (PDG) data, and an expanded sample of 85 states compiled within a recently proposed $(L,n)$-classification. Two linear Regge models for $M^2(L,n)$ are tested: one featuring distinct slopes for $L$ and $n$, $M^2(L,n)\propto an+bL$ (Model 1), and another assuming a universal slope, $M^2(L,n)\propto a(n+L)$ (Model 2). Model selection is conducted quantitatively using the Residual Sum of Squares (RSS), the adjusted RSS, the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC), and the Bayesian Information Criterion (BIC). Within the 27 benchmark states, Model 2 is statistically disfavored. We argue, however, that this discrepancy is driven by the specific behavior of $S$-wave ($L=0$) states. Upon their exclusion, the difference in performance between the two models becomes statistically insignificant, with information criteria selecting Model 2 as the more parsimonious description. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the masses of $S$-wave states can be successfully accommodated by a physically motivated, nonlinear $L$-dependent correction. A parallel analysis of the extended 85-state dataset, where the relative contribution of $S$-wave states is significantly smaller, reveals that Model 2 is statistically preferred, thereby restoring the Coulomb-like degeneracy in the Regge spectrum under consideration.

Method: 采用MiNLO方法，通过逆$k_T$-团簇算法识别额外喷注的最可能分支历史，动态确定重整化标度（renormalization scale）与因子化标度（factorization scale），并引入Sudakov形状因子（Sudakov form factors）处理大对数效应。该方法现已集成于Helac-NLO框架中。

Abstract: We compare standard fixed-order NLO QCD predictions for the full off-shell $pp \to e^+ν_e\, μ^-\barν_μ\, τ^+ν_τ\, b\bar{b} \, (j) + X$ processes in the multi-lepton decay channel with the results obtained using the MiNLO approach. The MiNLO method, now also implemented in the Helac-NLO framework, provides a dynamic determination of the renormalization and factorization scale settings by identifying the most likely branching histories of the additional jets through an inverse $k_T$-clustering algorithm. The inclusion of Sudakov form factors accounts for the large logarithms that arise in the presence of widely separated scales. We perform a dedicated comparison of the two approaches at both the integrated and differential (fiducial) cross-section levels for the LHC Run II energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV. Finally, we present the merging of the full off-shell predictions for $pp \to e^+ν_e\, μ^-\barν_μ\, τ^+ν_τ\, b\bar{b} \, + X$, $pp \to e^+ν_e\, μ^-\barν_μ\, τ^+ν_τ\, b\bar{b} \, j +X$ and $pp \to e^+ν_e\, μ^-\barν_μ\, τ^+ν_τ\, b\bar{b} \, jj$, with the aim of improving the description of the underlying $pp \to e^+ν_e\, μ^-\barν_μ\, τ^+ν_τ\, b\bar{b} + X$ process.

### [205] [ACT stands for Awkward Cosmology Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09808)
*Loris Del Grosso,Alfredo Urbano,Marcello Ziccolella*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文批判性地检验了两种调和Starobinsky暴胀（Starobinsky inflation）与ACT观测到标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）张力的策略：引入高曲率修正项（higher-curvature corrections）和修改再加热（reheating）动力学。结果表明，两种路径均面临理论困境，如精细调节（fine-tuning）问题、非标准再加热状态方程以及对紫外完备理论（UV-complete theories）的挑战，从而削弱了原始Starobinsky模型的极简性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ACT望远镜观测到的标量谱指数（scalar spectral index, n_s）与Starobinsky暴胀（Starobinsky inflation）的理论预言存在张力，亟需寻找调和二者矛盾的可行理论方案。

Method: 采用量纲分析（dimensional-analysis）论证，在引力作用量中引入高曲率修正项，形成包含一个耦合常数和两个质量标度的有效理论（effective theory）；同时，通过CMB模在再复合（recombination）前重新进入视界的条件，对再加热状态方程（equation of state, ω_reh）施加严格约束。

Result: 拟合ACT数据会将高曲率修正有效理论推向对紫外（UV）物理更敏感的参数区域，可能引入暴胀可观测量（inflationary observables）的精细调节问题；具体模型（无标度超引力no-scale supergravity与度规-仿射引力metric-affine gravity）等价于同一类f(R)理论。再加热方面，拟合ACT数据需要ω_reh > 1/3的奇异再加热相，与标准Starobinsky势中暴胀子（inflaton）振动的特征冲突。基于宇宙静滞（cosmological stasis）的再加热方案则需要具有负能量密度的态塔（tower of states）。

Conclusion: 调和Starobinsky暴胀与ACT数据所需的额外成分在紫外完备理论（UV-complete theories）的视角下难以自洽地动机化（motivate），从而严重削弱了原始Starobinsky模型的极简性（minimality）。

Abstract: Recent observations from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) point to a scalar spectral index in tension with the predictions of Starobinsky inflation. Two main strategies have been proposed to reconcile Starobinsky inflation with these data: (i) including higher-curvature operators in the gravitational action, and (ii) modifying the post-inflationary reheating dynamics. We critically re-examine both approaches. When higher-curvature corrections are included, dimensional-analysis arguments allow introducing a second mass scale suppressing higher-dimensional operators, resulting in a one-coupling, two-scale effective theory. We show that fitting the ACT data drives this class of effective theories toward a regime of stronger sensitivity to UV physics, potentially implying fine-tuning of the inflationary observables. We illustrate our general point with two concrete models, namely no-scale supergravity and metric-affine gravity, showing that they provide different realizations of the same underlying $f(R)$ theory. On the reheating side, requiring the CMB modes to re-enter the horizon before recombination leads to stringent constraints on the reheating equation of state, and fitting the ACT data favors an exotic reheating phase with $ω_{\rm reh} > 1/3$, incompatible with inflaton oscillations about the minimum of the standard Starobinsky potential. Finally, we explore the possibility that a phase of cosmological stasis, driven by a tower of decaying massive states, could play the role of the post-inflationary epoch. We find that accommodating ACT-preferred $n_s$ in this setup requires a tower of states with negative energy density. Taken together, our results suggest that reconciling Starobinsky inflation with the ACT data demands ingredients that are challenging to motivate from the perspective of UV-complete theories, undermining the minimality of the original Starobinsky model.

### [206] [Darkly Charged ALPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09852)
*Nicolás M. Arenaza,Enrique Fernández-Martínez,Belén Gavela,Elizabeth E. Jenkins,Aneesh V. Manohar,Pablo Quílez,Thomas Steingasser*

TL;DR: 本文提出了暗荷轴子（darkly charged ALPs）的有效场论框架，指出携带暗对称性守恒荷的轴子无法存在d=5有效相互作用，仅有两个d=6算符耦合到标准模型粒子，并探讨了其唯象学、暗物质候选性及紫外完备化示例。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于一般性对称性破缺模式（symmetry breaking pattern），构建暗荷轴子的有效拉格朗日量；利用有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）方法，识别低阶移位对称性（shift-symmetry）作用量算符，并分析更高阶算符与暗对称群类型。

Result: 若轴子携带暗守恒荷，则不存在d=5的ALP-标准模型有效相互作用；最低阶移位对称性有效拉格朗日量仅包含两个d=6算符。本文识别了更高阶EFT算符，并确定了哪些类型的暗对称群能产生暗荷轴子，同时提供了紫外完备化（ultraviolet completions）示例。

Conclusion: 暗荷轴子场景可作为暗物质候选，其模型无关的唯象学具有探测潜力。当前工作仅考虑无暗规范相互作用的情形，含暗规范相互作用的推广留待后续研究。

Abstract: The established $d=5$ ALP effective Lagrangian describes the interaction of scalars with approximate shift-symmetry which carry no Standard Model (SM) charges with SM fields. It implicitly assumes that ALPs are not charged under any symmetries of the dark sector. In this paper, we remove this assumption. For ALPs carrying conserved dark charges, no $d=5$ ALP effective interaction to SM particles is possible. We build the effective Lagrangian for these darkly charged ALPs stemming from a general breaking pattern, and we show that the lowest-order shift-symmetric effective Lagrangian contains just two $d=6$ operators coupling ALPs to SM particles. We explore the model-independent phenomenological implications of these interactions, as well as the question of whether the dark matter observed in the Universe may consist of darkly charged ALPs. We identify higher order operators of the effective field theory, and determine which types of dark symmetry groups can seed darkly charged ALPs. Illustrative examples of ultraviolet completions which result in darkly charged ALPs at low-energies are provided as well. The darkly-charged ALP scenario can be generalized by including dark gauge interactions. In this paper, we have considered only the case with no such interactions.

Abstract: Extra-dimensional QCD axion is well motivated by string compactifications and enjoys enhanced protection against quality-violating effects. We propose a dynamical suppression mechanism in warped five-dimensional models, where a radion-inflaton coupling sets the radion minimum at small inter-brane separation during inflation, temporarily enhancing the effective four-dimensional axion decay constant. After inflation, the radion minimum shifts to larger separation, restoring the standard QCD axion window. In a warped orbifold GUT with Goldberger-Wise stabilization, this mechanism can satisfy CMB isocurvature bounds while allowing substantially higher inflationary scales than in conventional pre-inflationary axion cosmology.

Motivation: 研究强磁场下QED中的费米子-光子顶点修正，探究洛伦兹对称性破缺如何影响顶点的结构以及相关的反常磁矩（anomalous magnetic moments）和能级跃迁行为。

Method: 在均匀恒定磁背景中，将费米子-光子顶点计算至单圈阶，分析树图阶和辐射修正后的张量分解，并基于此研究低朗道能级（Landau levels）之间的选择定则和跃迁振幅特性。

Result: 树图阶顶点因磁场破坏洛伦兹对称性而分裂为纵向和横向部分；辐射修正引入了包含横、纵及混合方向反常磁矩的丰富张量结构。跃迁振幅在初末态间差一个符号，且一般具有复数形式，对应衰减态的有限寿命。纯横向方向的反常磁矩在最低朗道能级间的跃迁被禁止；磁场充当了红外正则化（infrared regulator）机制。

Conclusion: 强磁场背景显著改变了QED中的费米子-光子顶点结构，诱导了对称性破缺与复杂的张量修正，并导致特殊的跃迁选择定则和红外行为。

Abstract: We compute the fermion-photon vertex in QED in the presence of a constant and uniform magnetic background up to one-loop order. We show that even at tree-level, the vertex is modified due to the loss of Lorentz invariance induced by the magnetic field, thus breaking into longitudinal and transverse pieces. Moreover, the radiative corrections induce the emergence of a rich tensor structure that includes the anomalous magnetic moments in the transverse, parallel, and mixed transverse/parallel directions. We concentrate on studying one of these anomalous magnetic moment components, the one in the purely transverse direction. We find the selection rules for transitions between a few low-lying Landau levels and show that the amplitudes for transitions from an initial to a final Landau level differ by a sign from the reverse process due to the loss of time reversal invariance induced by the presence of the field. Contrary to the vacuum case, the amplitudes are, in general, complex, and the phase factor can be interpreted in terms of a finite life-time of the decaying state. For the anomalous magnetic moment in the purely transverse direction, transitions between states occupying both the lowest Landau levels are forbidden. Moreover, for the computation of the allowed transitions, we find that it is not necessary to include a photon mass since the magnetic field acts as an infrared regulator.

</details>


### [209] [Do primordial quark pellets solve the dark matter puzzle?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10672)
*Domenec Espriu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出原始夸克团块（Primordial Quark Pellets, PQPs）——在约1 TeV温度下形成的超高密度夸克物质微型星——可作为基于标准模型（Standard Model）的暗物质候选体。形成概率为10^{-9}至10^{-4}每视界体积时即可复现当前暗物质密度，且质量低于10^{-7}太阳质量时可完全规避微引力透镜约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找一种基于标准模型、无需引入超出粒子物理标准模型新粒子且观测上可检验的暗物质（dark matter）解决方案。现有暗物质候选体（如弱相互作用大质量粒子）尚未被实验证实，因此有必要探索替代理论。

Method: 采用理论分析与数值计算相结合的方法：假设稀有重子数过密度由收缩的佩塞-奎恩畴壁（Peccei-Quinn domain walls）或类似超视界结构产生；使用含热夸克状态方程（hot quark equation of state）求解托尔曼-奥本海默-沃尔科夫方程（Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation），寻找稳定解。

Result: 发现稳定解的最大质量为10^{-2}太阳质量，半径约100米，但形成机制更倾向产生更小的天体。PQP形成后可冷却演化为微型中子星（mini neutron stars）或稳定奇异物质团块（strange matter nuggets），取决于量子色动力学（QCD）的基态性质。形成概率在10^{-9}至10^{-4}每视界体积范围内时足以复现当前暗物质密度，且不影响大爆炸核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis）或需要熵稀释。

Conclusion: PQP质量低于10^{-7}太阳质量时可完全规避微引力透镜约束，该质量范围可轻松容纳大部分暗物质。PQP因此构成一种保守的、基于标准模型且观测上可检验的暗物质难题解决方案。

Abstract: We show that primordial quark pellets (PQP), ultra dense quark matter mini-stars formed at around 1 TeV, naturally arise in a radiation dominated universe if rare baryon overdensities are produced by collapsing Peccei-Quinn domain walls or similar superhorizon structures. Solving the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equation with a hot quark equation of state, we find stable solutions with a maximum mass of $10^{-2}$ solar masses and radii of approximately 100 meters, although the formation mechanism favours much smaller objects. Once formed, PQPs cool and evolve intro mini neutron stars or stable strange matter nuggets, depending on the QCD ground state. Formation probabilities of $10^{-9}$ to $10^{-4}$ per horizon volume could suffice to reproduce the present dark matter density without altering Big Bang Nucleosynthesis or requiring entropy dilution. PQPs completely evade microlensing constraints if their mass is below $10^{-7}$ solar masses, a range that could easily accommodate most of the dark matter. PQPs thus potentially constitute a conservative, Standard-Model based, and observationally testable solution to the dark matter puzzle.

### [210] [Dynamical dark energy in the Bianchi Type-V Universe with DESI DR2 BAO, SNIa compilation and RSD measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09718)
*Shambel Sahlu,Álvaro de la Cruz-Dombriz,A. H. A. Alfedeel,Gonzalo J. Olmo,Amare Abebe*

Main category: physics.gen-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在Bianchi Type-V各向异性时空框架下，结合动力学暗能量（DDE）模型与1+3协变热力学方法，利用DESI DR2 BAO、Supernovae、CC、RSD等多重宇宙学数据集进行联合统计分析，发现各向异性与DDE的结合能够有效缓解H₀和S₈宇宙学张力，并通过模型选择指标检验了该扩展框架的可行性与可检验性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型在解释近期宇宙学观测，尤其是H₀和S₈参数之间的张力（cosmological tensions）方面面临挑战。本研究旨在探索各向异性时空与动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy, DDE）是否能为这些不一致提供可行的缓解机制。

Method: 采用Bianchi Type-V各向异性时空（anisotropic, spatially homogeneous Bianchi Type-V spacetime）框架，结合1+3协变热力学（1+3 covariant thermodynamics）方法。分别使用常数w和时变参数化状态方程（w₀, wₐ），通过准静态近似（quasi-static approximation）追踪背景膨胀历史与线性物质扰动。数据集包括DESI DR2 BAO、Union3和DESY5 Ia超新星样本、宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers, CC）以及红移空间畸变（Redshift-Space Distortion, RSD）测量。

Result: 空间各向异性与DDE的结合能有效容纳近期晚期宇宙学观测，并为缓解H₀和S₈张力提供可行机制。Akaike信息准则强烈支持扩展的Bianchi Type-V模型，但Bayesian准则因模型维度更高仍倾向于ΛCDM基线。研究给出了物质密度参数Ωₘ,₀、剪切参数Ωσ,₀以及暗能量演化参数的紧致约束。

Conclusion: 各向异性扩展（anisotropic extensions）在Bianchi Type-V框架下仍然是现代精密宇宙学中可行且可检验的理论方案。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of dynamical dark energy (DDE) models within an anisotropic, spatially homogeneous Bianchi Type-V spacetime framework using a $1+3$ covariant thermodynamics approach. By implementing both constant ($w$) and time-varying ($w_0, w_a$) parameterized equations of state, we evaluate the background expansion history and track linear matter perturbations via the quasi-static approximation. We confront these scenarios with the latest cosmological datasets, including the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) DR2 Baryon Acoustic Oscillations (BAO), the Union3 and Dark Energy Survey 5-year (DESY5) Type Ia Supernovae compilations, Cosmic Chronometers (CC), and Redshift-Space Distortion (RSD) measurements. Our joint statistical analyses reveal that the introduction of spatial anisotropy coupled with DDE efficiently accommodates recent late-time measurements and provides a viable mechanism to mitigate the persistent $H_0$ and $S_8$ cosmological tensions. Model selection metrics show that while Akaike criteria strongly support the extended Bianchi Type-V scenarios across most joint data combinations, Bayesian criteria continue to favor the simpler standard $Λ$CDM baseline due to its lower dimensionality. Finally, we establish tight constraints on the current matter density parameter $Ω_{m,0}$, the shear parameter $Ω_{σ,0}$, and the dark energy evolution parameters, confirming that anisotropic extensions remain viable and testable frameworks for modern precision cosmology.

### [211] [Varying Gravity from a Modified Fractional Model: Observational Constraints and Slow-Fast Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09722)
*Rami Ahmad El-Nabulsi,Genly Leon,Esteban González,Kevin Marroquín*

Main category: physics.gen-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个分数阶引力模型（fractional gravity model），其中哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）和引力常数（gravitational constant）因分数阶重整化群效应（fractional renormalization-group effects）而动态演化。模型包含与随时间变化的G耦合的标量场（scalar field），产生分数阶作用量宇宙学（fractional-action cosmology）特有的非局域修正（nonlocal corrections）。解析和数值解揭示了振荡、循环相位和快速变化模式，对原初核合成（Big Bang Nucleosynthesis, BBN）和早期宇宙演化有重要影响。贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）表明，μ=0的分数阶模型是唯一统计上可行的变体，哈勃参数h≃0.72保持稳定，但贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian Information Criterion, BIC）强烈支持ΛCDM模型。模型能再现晚期宇宙加速膨胀并模仿ΛCDM，同时引入独特的宇宙学特征（cosmographic signatures）。动力系统分析（dynamical systems analysis）揭示了稳定性结构和参数依赖性，表明分数阶非局域修正可能为解决H₀和S₈张力（tensions）提供新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索分数阶重整化群效应导致的引力常数和哈勃参数动态演化，以弥补标准宇宙学模型在解释早期宇宙演化、H₀张力和S₈张力等方面的不足，并寻求超越ΛCDM的新理论框架。

Method: 构建了一个标量场与随时间变化的引力常数G耦合的分数阶引力模型，通过解析和数值方法求解正则化系统；建立稳健的数值框架，将H(z)演化与哈勃参数、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations, BAO）、Ia型超新星（type Ia supernovae）、引力透镜（gravitational lensing）和黑洞阴影（black hole shadows）等观测数据进行比较，重构宇宙学量（cosmographic quantities）；采用贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）进行模型比较和参数推断。

Result: μ=0的分数阶模型是唯一统计可行的变体，其哈勃参数h≃0.72，分数阶参数α=1.20^{+0.25}_{-0.14}、ζ=0.43^{+0.39}_{-0.29}；动力学参数m=30.8^{+28.0}_{-20.9}、Γ=108.3±1.1，弛豫时间尺度τ_rel≃9 Gyr，确认系统处于过阻尼区（overdamped regime）；μ=0模型的χ²_min略低于ΛCDM，但BIC强烈偏好ΛCDM。

Conclusion: 该分数阶引力模型能再现晚期宇宙加速膨胀并模仿ΛCDM，同时具有独特的宇宙学特征；动力系统分析表明分数阶非局域修正可能为解决H₀和S₈张力提供新路径，但当前模型在参数简洁性上仍不及ΛCDM。

Abstract: We investigate a fractional gravity model in which both the Hubble parameter and the gravitational constant evolve dynamically due to fractional renormalization-group effects. The model incorporates a scalar field coupled to a time-varying $G$, generating nonlocal corrections characteristic of fractional--action cosmology. Analytical and numerical solutions reveal oscillatory regimes, cyclic phases, and rapid variations with implications for BBN and early-universe evolution. A robust numerical framework is developed to integrate the regularized system and compare the resulting $H(z)$ evolution with observational data from the Hubble parameter, baryon acoustic oscillations, type Ia supernovae, gravitational lensing, and black hole shadows, thereby enabling a consistent reconstruction of cosmographic quantities. A Bayesian analysis shows that the Fractional model with $μ=0$ is the only statistically viable variant. The inferred Hubble parameter is stable across models ($h\simeq 0.72$), while the fractional parameters are significantly better constrained in the $μ=0$ case ($α=1.20^{+0.25}_{-0.14}$, $ζ=0.43^{+0.39}_{-0.29}$). The dynamical sector yields $m=30.8^{+28.0}_{-20.9}$ and $Γ=108.3\pm1.1$, leading to a positive discriminant and a well-determined relaxation timescale $τ_{\rm rel}\simeq 9$ Gyr, confirming an overdamped regime. Although the $μ=0$ model attains a slightly lower $χ^2_{\min}$ than $Λ$CDM, the BIC strongly favors $Λ$CDM due to its smaller parameter space. Overall, the model reproduces late-time acceleration and mimics $Λ$CDM while introducing distinctive cosmographic signatures. The dynamical systems analysis clarifies the stability structure and parameter dependence, indicating that fractional nonlocal corrections may offer new pathways toward addressing the $H_0$ and $S_8$ tensions.

### [212] [Quantum Thermodynamics of Electron Transport along Chains of Redox Centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09728)
*Fabrizio Cleri,Ralf Blossey,Stefano Giordano*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）描述的开系统量子力学模型扩展至生物体内基于铁硫簇（iron-sulfur clusters）或血红素基团（heme groups）的氧化还原中心长链，用于描述细胞呼吸过程中的分子内电子输运，并对电子电流、平均转移时间、传输效率以及电子与蛋白质浴之间的热熵传递进行了系统表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，生物系统中的分子内电子输运被半经典的马库斯（Marcus）和霍普菲尔德（Hopfield）速率理论结合经典泡利型主方程（Pauli-type master equations）描述为扩散跳跃过程。然而，非平凡量子力学效应可能在特定生物分子过程的输运动力学中发挥功能性作用的可能性日益受到关注，因此需要发展更精确的量子力学模型。

Method: 通过林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）对开系统动力学（open system dynamics）进行量子力学建模，并将其扩展至基于铁硫簇或血红素基团的长链氧化还原中心这一关键生物组分，从而在广泛的物理参数范围内探索电子输运特性。

Result: 该方法揭示了多结构域蛋白质结构中电子输运的关键特征，并明确表征了电子电流（electron currents）、平均转移时间（average transfer times）以及输运过程的相对效率（relative efficiency）。特别关注了电子与蛋白质浴之间的热量（heat）和熵（entropy）传递，后者被视为模型物理现实主义（physical realism）的基准。

Conclusion: 该量子力学模型能够有效描述生物氧化还原中心长链中的电子输运，并通过对热熵传递的定量分析验证了模型的物理真实性。

Abstract: Intramolecular electron transport in biological systems is typically described as a diffusive hopping process, according to the semi-classical rate theories of Marcus and Hopfield combined with classical Pauli-type master equations. However, the possibility that non-trivial quantum mechanical effects could play a functional role in the transport dynamics in certain biomolecular processes has attracted increasing attention. Here, we extend the quantum mechanical model of open system dynamics by the Lindblad equation to a key biological component, the long chains of redox centers based on iron-sulfur clusters or heme groups that are widespread in many biological organisms, where they realize the cellular respiration. This approach allows to explore a wide range of physical parameters, showing key features of electron transport in these multi-domain protein structures. We pay particular attention to heat and entropy transfer between the electrons and the protein bath, which constitutes a benchmark of physical realism for the models. Electron currents, average transfer times and relative efficiency of the transport process are also explicitly characterized.

</details>


### [213] [Correlation-consistent Gaussian basis sets for copper solids from material-constrained atomic optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11711)
*Jincheng Yu,Xiaoyu Zhang,Min-Ye Zhang,Yu Cao,Qiming Sun,Hong-Zhou Ye*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种材料约束原子优化（MCAO）框架，用于生成适用于周期性固体的相关一致高斯基组（correlation-consistent Gaussian basis sets），并以Cu为例构建了Dunning风格的MCAO-cc-pVXZ基组，解决了扩散原子优化基函数在固体中引起的线性依赖问题，实现了对固体Cu及相关体系的可靠完整基组外推（CBS extrapolation）计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相关一致高斯基组（correlation-consistent Gaussian basis sets）在分子量子化学中至关重要，但其直接用于周期性固体时，扩散的原子优化原始基组（diffuse atomically optimized primitives）会引发严重的线性依赖（linear dependence）问题。这一问题在金属及含金属体系中尤为突出，而这类体系恰需可靠的完整基组外推（complete-basis-set, CBS extrapolation）用于相关波函数基准计算。

Method: 引入材料约束原子优化（material-constrained atomic optimization, MCAO）框架，在保持高斯基组的原子特性（atomic character）和相关一致性（correlation-consistent character）的同时，对代表性固体中的重叠矩阵条件数（overlap-matrix condition number）施加惩罚项。作为概念验证，为Cu生成了全电子（all-electron）、标量相对论全电子（scalar-relativistic all-electron）、有效核势（effective core potential, ECP）以及赝势（pseudopotential）处理的Dunning风格MCAO-cc-pVXZ基组（X = D, T, Q）。

Result: 生成的基组在Cu固体及表面计算中保持数值稳定性（numerically stable），同时能够复现分子Cu二聚体的能量学以及体相Cu的平面波参考性质。基于CBS外推的随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）计算进一步实现了对体相Cu及CO在Cu(111)表面吸附中赝势误差、相对论效应误差和基组误差的可控评估。

Conclusion: MCAO方法为周期体系提供了标量相对论全电子高斯基组基准，有助于解决CO吸附疑难（CO adsorption puzzle），表明该框架可推广至其他元素体系，用于弥合分子与固体量子化学之间在基组处理上的差距。

Abstract: Correlation-consistent Gaussian basis sets are central to systematic molecular quantum chemistry, but their direct use in periodic solids is often limited by severe linear dependence from diffuse atomically optimized primitives. This problem is particularly acute for metallic and metal-containing systems, where reliable complete-basis-set (CBS) extrapolation is needed for correlated-wavefunction benchmarks. We introduce material-constrained atomic optimization (MCAO), a basis-set optimization framework that preserves the atomic and correlation-consistent character of Gaussian basis sets while penalizing large overlap-matrix condition numbers in representative solids. As a proof of concept, we generate Dunning-style MCAO-cc-pVXZ basis sets (X = D, T, Q) for Cu with all-electron, scalar-relativistic all-electron, effective core potential (ECP), and pseudopotential treatments. The resulting basis sets remain numerically stable for Cu solids and surfaces while reproducing molecular Cu dimer energetics and plane-wave reference properties of bulk Cu. CBS-extrapolated random-phase approximation calculations further enable a controlled assessment of pseudopotential, relativistic, and basis-set errors in bulk Cu and CO adsorption on Cu(111), providing scalar-relativistic all-electron Gaussian-basis benchmarks for the CO adsorption puzzle.

</details>


### [214] [Unconventional Spin Valve Based on Normal Metal/Chiral Molecule/Altermagnet Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11788)
*Tian-Yi Zhang,Peng-Yi Liu,Yu-Fei Sun,Ai-Min Guo,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出将手性分子（chiral molecules）与交变磁体（altermagnets）结合构建高效可调的自旋阀，利用非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）和Landauer-Büttiker公式，理论证明了通过重定向交变磁体的奈尔矢量（Néel vector）可有效调控自旋阀的电导，且磁阻（magnetoresistance）随分子长度和交变磁各向异性增大；手性分子和分子自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的缺失会导致磁阻消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性分子因能产生高度自旋极化电流而受到广泛关注，这一现象即手性诱导自旋选择性效应（chiral-induced spin selectivity effect），在自旋电子学（spintronics）领域具有巨大潜力。本文旨在将手性分子与交变磁体结合，以构建高效且可调的自旋阀（spin valve）。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数方法（nonequilibrium Green's function method）和Landauer-Büttiker公式，计算了正常金属/手性分子/交变磁体（normal metal/chiral molecule/altermagnet）自旋阀的电导（conductance）和磁阻（magnetoresistance）。

Result: 理论结果表明，通过重定向交变磁体的奈尔矢量（Néel vector）可有效调控自旋阀的电导；磁阻随分子长度（molecular length）和交变磁各向异性（altermagnetic anisotropy）的增加而增大；对于非手性分子（achiral molecules）或在分子自旋-轨道耦合（molecular spin-orbit coupling）缺失的情况下，磁阻消失。

Conclusion: 该工作为开发高效、可控且无杂散场（stray-field-free）的自旋电子器件（spintronic devices）奠定了基础。

Abstract: Chiral molecules have attracted broad interdisciplinary interest for their ability to produce highly spin-polarized current. This phenomenon, known as the chiral-induced spin selectivity effect, holds great potential in the field of spintronics. Here, we propose to combine chiral molecules with altermagnets to construct highly efficient and tunable spin valves. Using the nonequilibrium Green's function method and the Landauer-Büttiker formula, we obtain the conductance and the magnetoresistance of a normal metal/chiral molecule/altermagnet spin valve. Our theoretical results reveal that the conductance of the spin valve can be effectively tuned by reorienting the Néel vector of the altermagnet, and the magnetoresistance of the spin valve increases with molecular length and altermagnetic anisotropy. Moreover, the magnetoresistance vanishes for achiral molecules or in the absence of molecular spin-orbit coupling. Our work paves the way for developing efficient, controllable, and stray-field-free spintronic devices.

### [215] [Compact stars in a large-tension braneworld: mildly negative Weyl coupling consistent with NICER and gravitational-wave data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09836)
*Samuel Isidoro dos Santos Júnior,Rafael Camargo Rodrigues de Lima,Pedro Henrique Ribeiro da Silva Moraes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究利用多信使天文观测（multi-messenger observations）进行贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference），在Sahni–Shtanov现象的膜世界模型（braneworld model）框架下约束致密星（compact stars）的参数空间。基于改进的Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff方程和SLy物态方程，通过仿射不变集成马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）分析GW170817和NICER观测数据，发现大膜张力（large-brane-tension）区域与轻微负的Weyl耦合（Weyl coupling）与当前观测一致，无需对广义相对论做大幅偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多信使天体物理观测为检验广义相对论之外的引力理论提供了新契机，膜世界模型作为高维引力理论的低能有效理论，其对致密星结构的预言尚缺乏系统的多信使约束。本研究旨在利用GW170817和NICER观测数据，对Sahni–Shtanov膜世界模型中致密星的参数空间进行贝叶斯推断，以检验该模型的可行性。

Method: 采用包含局域二次膜修正（local quadratic brane corrections）和非局域Weyl扇区（nonlocal Weyl sector）现象学闭包（phenomenological closure）的改进Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff方程描述星体结构，参数包括膜张力λ、Weyl耦合α_𝒰和Weyl物态方程参数w_𝒰。使用SLy物态方程，结合GW170817的质量-半径后验（mass–radius posteriors）和NICER对PSR J0740+6620及PSR J1231–1411的观测，进行仿射不变集成MCMC分析。

Result: 后验给出的膜张力为log₁₀(λ/km⁻²)=3.98⁺¹.⁵²₋₁.₄₄（68%置信区间），表明处于大膜张力区域；Weyl耦合约束为α_𝒰=−0.15⁺⁰.³⁰₋₀.₀₈（68%），而w_𝒰约束较弱，95%置信区间为[−1.25, 1.02]。最大质量M_max=2.30⁺⁰.¹⁴₋₀.₀₈ M⊙，1.4倍太阳质量对应半径R₁.₄=13.31⁺⁰.⁵⁴₋₀.₅₇ km（68%），均超过相同SLy物态方程下广义相对论的预言。

Conclusion: 大膜张力背景下轻微负的Weyl耦合与当前NICER和引力波观测约束一致，无需对广义相对论做出大幅偏离。95%后验区间虽延伸至GW190814次质量范围（secondary-mass range），但中位数和最佳拟合值仍低于该范围，表明该模型在现有观测精度下是可行的引力理论备选方案。

Abstract: We use Bayesian inference on multi-messenger observations to constrain the parameter space of compact stars in a phenomenological braneworld model inspired by the effective Sahni--Shtanov scenario. Stellar structure is described by modified Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equations including local quadratic brane corrections and a phenomenological closure for the nonlocal Weyl sector, parametrized by the brane tension $λ$, the Weyl coupling $α_{\mathcal{U}}$, and the Weyl equation-of-state parameter $w_{\mathcal{U}}$. Using the SLy equation of state, we perform an affine-invariant ensemble Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis combining mass--radius posteriors from GW170817 (LIGO/Virgo) and NICER observations of PSR~J0740$+$6620 and PSR~J1231$-$1411. The posterior yields $\log_{10}(λ/\mathrm{km}^{-2})=3.98^{+1.52}{-1.44}$ (68%), indicating a large-brane-tension regime where local high-energy corrections are subdominant. The Weyl coupling is constrained to $α{\mathcal{U}}=-0.15^{+0.30}{-0.08}$ (68%), while $w{\mathcal{U}}$ remains weakly constrained, with a 95% credible interval of $[-1.25,,1.02]$. The inferred stellar properties are $M_{\max}=2.30^{+0.14}{-0.08},M\odot$ and $R_{1.4}=13.31^{+0.54}_{-0.57},\mathrm{km}$ (68%), exceeding the corresponding General Relativity predictions for the SLy equation of state. The 95% posterior interval extends into the GW190814 secondary-mass range, although the median and best-fit values remain below it. These results show that a large-tension braneworld with a mildly negative Weyl coupling is consistent with current NICER and gravitational-wave constraints without requiring large deviations from General Relativity.

</details>


### [216] [Black-bounce spacetime and galactic rotation curves: from singularity resolution to observable gravitational effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09840)
*Farook Rahaman Aritra Sanyal Saibal Ray*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了黑跳（black-bounce）时空度规，它能消除施瓦西度规的中心奇点。作者通过黑洞视界结构、太阳系精密检验以及首次应用于星系动力学（拟合NGC 7331旋转曲线）三个观测窗口，给出了反弹参数a的第一个星系运动学观测约束（a=1.035±0.119 kpc），证实该度规在核心正则化的同时与大半径冷暗物质晕一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）存在中心奇点（singularity），需要引入正则化（regularized）修改以构建无奇点（singularity-free）替代模型。黑跳时空度规提供了一个可控的自由参数a，但其在天体物理尺度上的观测约束仍十分缺乏，尤其尚未在星系动力学（galactic dynamics）层面得到检验。

Method: 本文通过三个互补的观测窗口展开分析：(1) 黑洞视界结构分析，区分正则黑洞（a<2M）与可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole, a>2M）；(2) 太阳系精密检验，计算水星近日点进动、引力透镜（gravitational lensing）和雷达信号夏皮罗时延（Shapiro time delay）；(3) 首次将黑跳度规应用于星系动力学，导出圆速度场（circular velocity field）并拟合NGC 7331的观测旋转曲线，采用四组分质量分解：黑跳中心势、Freeman指数盘、Hernquist核球和Navarro–Frenk–White（NFW）暗物质晕。

Result: 太阳系检验显示反弹参数a引入了小但可测量的广义相对论修正。星系动力学拟合给出a=1.035±0.119 kpc，这是首次从星系运动学获得的反弹参数观测约束（observational constraint）。

Conclusion: 黑跳度规能在内区正则化星系核心，同时在大半径上与标准NFW暗物质晕完全一致，为经典黑洞的无奇点替代方案提供了一个强有力的检验平台（testbed）。

Abstract: The black-bounce spacetime provides a regularized modification of the Schwarzschild metric by introducing a free parameter $a$ that eliminates the central singularity while preserving the exterior geometry of a classical black hole. This work investigates the physical implications of this metric across three complementary observational windows. First, we examine the horizon structure and the transition between a regular black hole ($a < 2M$) and a traversable wormhole ($a > 2M$), offering a viable singularity-free alternative to classical black hole solutions. Second, we perform Solar System precision tests perihelion precession of Mercury, gravitational lensing, and the Shapiro time delay of radar signals demonstrating that the bounce parameter $a$ introduces small but measurable corrections relative to general relativity. Third, and for the first time, we apply the black-bounce metric to galactic dynamics by deriving the circular velocity field and fitting it to the observed rotation curve of NGC~7331. A four-component mass decomposition black-bounce central potential, Freeman exponential disc, Hernquist bulge, and a Navarro--Frenk--White dark matter halo yields $a = 1.035 \pm 0.119$~kpc , providing the first observational constraint on the bounce parameter from galaxy kinematics. Our results confirm that the black-bounce metric regularises the inner galactic core while remaining fully consistent with a standard dark matter halo at large radii, establishing this spacetime as a compelling testbed for singularity-free alternatives to classical black holes.

</details>


### [217] [Perturbative aspects of analogue FLRW spacetime Jellium models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09843)
*Matheus E. Pereira,Hermano Velten,Francisco B. Lustosa,Alexandre G. M. Schmidt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在均匀、各向同性且膨胀的Jellium模型（FLRW类比）中研究电声学微扰模，给出了线性解析解与完整数值演化，并通过引入尺度依赖的粒子数涨落功率谱，建立了理论与实验之间的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过类比宇宙学膨胀的Jellium模型，研究电声学微扰模式在均匀、各向同性膨胀背景（即Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker, FLRW类比）中的动力学行为，从而模拟牛顿宇宙学膨胀中的密度微扰。

Method: 采用Jellium模型（homogeneous, isotropic and expanding Jellium models）作为FLRW膨胀类比的平台；同时运用线性微扰的解析求解与全数值模拟两种手段；引入尺度依赖的粒子数涨落功率谱（scale dependent particle number fluctuation power spectrum）来刻画微扰的时间演化。

Result: 获得了特定类比宇宙学膨胀中线性微扰的新的解析解；通过全数值评估表征了电声学模在从线性到非线性区间的完整动力学演化；详细展示了粒子数涨落功率谱对模型物理参数的依赖性。

Conclusion: 所引入的尺度依赖粒子数涨落功率谱可作为连接理论与实验的有效工具；无论是压力支撑演化还是非绝热贡献驱动的模式，均可通过该功率谱系统地表征其时间演化行为。

Abstract: We study electro-acoustic perturbative modes in homogeneous, isotropic and expanding -- dubbed as Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) -- Jellium models, thereby mimicking density perturbations in analogous Newtonian cosmological expansions. We present both novel analytic solutions for linear perturbations in specific analogue cosmological expansions and full numerical evaluations that characterize the temporal evolution of the electro-acoustic modes capturing their full dynamical behavior across the linear and the nonlinear regimes. For both the case of pressure supported evolution or modes sourced by nonadiabatic contributions, we also characterize the temporal evolution of such perturbations by introducing their scale dependent particle number fluctuation power spectrum which can act as a tool to connect theory and experiments. The dependence of the latter on the physical parameters of the model is demonstrated in detail.

</details>


### [218] [GRACE: An Open-Source Framework for GPU-Accelerated Numerical Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09854)
*Carlo Musolino,Christian Ecker,Konrad Topolski,Marie Cassing,Keneth Miler,Harry Ho-Yin Ng,Khalil Pierre,Elias R. Most,Luciano Rezzolla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的 GPU 加速数值相对论框架 GRACE，基于开源库（Kokkos 和 p4est）构建，能在异构高性能计算平台上高效运行，实现了对理想 GRMHD 与爱因斯坦方程的耦合求解，并通过一套标准测试以及双中子星并合等应用进行了验证，同时在多种 GPU/CPU 架构上给出了吞吐率和可扩展性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在异构高性能计算（heterogeneous high-performance computing）平台上高效运行数值相对论（numerical-relativity）模拟，开发一种从头构建、基于开源库、具有性能可移植性（performance portability）的新框架。

Method: 使用 Kokkos 实现跨 CPU 和 GPU 架构的性能可移植性，采用 p4est 进行自适应网格加密（adaptive mesh refinement）；在固定或自适应细化网格上，采用约束输运（constrained transport）维持无散度磁场，将理想 GRMHD 方程与 Z4c 形式下的爱因斯坦方程组（Einstein equations）自洽耦合求解。

Result: 通过从磁化激波管到双黑洞并合等一系列标准测试验证了实现；在双中子星并合应用中，螺旋动力学与 FIL 代码吻合良好；报告了单设备吞吐率以及在多种 GPU/CPU 架构上的强可扩展性（strong scaling）和弱可扩展性（weak scaling）结果。

Conclusion: GRACE 是一个公开可用的、高效的 GPU 加速数值相对论框架，并附带基本后处理与数据分析环境 GRACEpy。

Abstract: We present GRACE, a new GPU-accelerated numerical-relativity framework designed to run efficiently on heterogeneous high-performance computing platforms. Developed from scratch and built exclusively on open-source libraries, GRACE employs Kokkos for performance portability across CPU and GPU architectures and p4est for adaptive mesh refinement. The code evolves the equations of ideal GRMHD -- with divergence-free magnetic fields maintained by constrained transport -- self-consistently coupled to the Einstein equations in the Z4c formulation, on fixed or adaptively refined grids. We validate the implementation against a suite of standard tests, ranging from magnetized shock tubes and the magnetic rotor in flat spacetime, through (magnetized) Bondi accretion onto a Schwarzschild black hole and the ringdown of a perturbed spinning puncture, to neutron-star oscillation spectra in fixed and dynamical spacetimes and the merger of binary black holes. As more demanding applications, we evolve two binary neutron-star mergers -- an equal-mass, unmagnetized system with an ideal-gas equation of state and an unequal-mass, magnetized system with a finite-temperature tabulated equation of state -- finding the inspiral dynamics to agree well with the FIL code. We also report single-device throughput together with strong- and weak-scaling results on multiple GPU and CPU architectures. GRACE is publicly released together with GRACEpy, a basic post-processing and data-analysis environment.

</details>


### [219] [Hawking Radiation in $f(\mathcal{R})$ Gravity: Survival of lighter black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09863)
*Mriganka Dutta,Panchajanya Dey,Banibrata Mukhopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究在 $f(\mathcal{R})$ 修正引力（modified gravity, MGR）框架下分析霍金辐射，发现原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）蒸发速度慢于广义相对论（general relativity, GR）预测。质量约为 $5 \times 10^{13}$ g 或更低的非旋转黑洞可存活至今，质量阈值比 GR 低约十倍，从而放宽了 PBHs 作为暗物质候选体的约束条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论在描述引力现象上极为成功，但现代宇宙学与天体物理学中的若干未解问题（如暴胀、暗能量）表明可能需要扩展或修正该框架。修正引力（modified gravity, MGR）理论（包括标量-张量模型和高维方法）试图在满足已有实验检验的同时填补这些空缺。

Method: 本研究在 $f(\mathcal{R})$ 引力理论（$\mathcal{R}$ 为标量曲率）框架下，分析霍金辐射的行为，并聚焦于其对原初黑洞作为暗物质候选体的影响。通过比较 MGR 与 GR 预言的黑洞蒸发时间，推导出新的质量阈值与约束条件。

Result: 非旋转黑洞在 MGR 中蒸发速度慢于 GR 预言。质量约为 $5 \times 10^{13}$ g 或更低的 PBHs 可存活至当前时期，该质量阈值比 GR 至少低约十倍，具体取决于 MGR 参数。

Conclusion: MGR 中 PBHs 蒸发时间线的延迟，放宽了 PBHs 作为暗物质候选体的可行性约束条件，从而重塑了暗物质问题的可能解决路径。该结果为进一步研究替代引力理论及其宇宙学后果提供了动机。

Abstract: Einstein's theory of general relativity (GR) has been remarkably successful in describing gravitational phenomena. However, several open questions in modern cosmology and astrophysics (e.g. inflation, dark energy) suggest the need for extensions or modifications to this framework. Modified gravity (MGR) theories, including scalar-tensor models and higher-dimensional approaches, attempt to address these gaps while maintaining consistency with established experimental tests. This work investigates Hawking radiation within an $f(\mathcal{R})$ gravity theory, with $\mathcal{R}$ being scalar curvature, focusing on its implications for primordial black holes (PBHs) as potential dark matter (DM) candidates. Our analysis reveals that PBHs evaporate slowly in MGR compared to GR predictions. Specifically, we find that non-rotating black holes with masses $\sim 5 \times 10^{13}$ g or lower would have survived by the present epoch, depending on the MGR parameter-a mass threshold approximately at least ten times smaller than in GR. This retarded evaporation timeline imposes relaxed new constraints on the viability of PBHs as DM constituents, thereby reshaping the landscape of possible solutions to the DM problem. This motivates further investigation into alternative gravitational theories and their cosmological consequences.

</details>


### [220] [Exceptional lines in the Kerr-Newman black hole spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09878)
*João Paulo Cavalcante,Maurício Richartz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究近极端克尔-纽曼黑洞（Kerr-Newman black holes）在标量场扰动下的准正则模（quasinormal mode）谱，发现了一组例外线（exceptional lines）和例外点（exceptional points），分析了由此产生的几何相位（geometric phases），并揭示了这些简并与零阻尼模（zero-damping modes）分支之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解近极端黑洞（near-extremal black holes）在标量场扰动下的准正则模谱结构，特别是模式简并（degeneracy）与例外点（exceptional points）的出现机制及其物理含义。

Method: 聚焦于$(\ell,m) = (1,1)$准正则模（quasinormal mode）谱，在近极端区域（near-extremal regime）识别例外线序列（sequence of exceptional lines）和对应的例外点（exceptional points）；通过参数空间中闭合回路的谱传输（transporting the spectrum around closed loops）分析几何相位（geometric phases），并推导极端极限下零阻尼模（zero-damping modes）频率的解析表达式。

Result: 发现一组例外线（exceptional lines），其上泛音频率（overtone frequencies）发生简并；对应地，无质量场（massless fields）情况下存在一组例外点（exceptional points）；这些简并与谱分支为零阻尼模（zero-damping modes）和阻尼模（damped modes）密切相关。

Conclusion: 准正则模谱的例外点简并（degeneracy at exceptional points）与近极端黑洞零阻尼模与阻尼模的谱分支（branching of the spectrum）存在内在关联，且极端极限下零阻尼模频率可由解析表达式精确描述。

Abstract: We investigate massive scalar perturbations of Kerr-Newman black holes, focusing on the $(\ell,m) = (1,1)$ quasinormal mode spectrum in the near-extremal regime. We identify a sequence of exceptional lines, at which overtone frequencies become degenerate, together with a corresponding sequence of exceptional points for massless fields. We analyze the geometric phases associated with these exceptional points by transporting the spectrum around closed loops in parameter space and examining the resulting permutation of quasinormal mode frequencies. We further show that these degeneracies are closely related to the branching of the spectrum into zero-damping and damped modes, and derive an analytic expression for the frequencies of the zero-damping modes in the extremal limit.

</details>


### [221] [Entropy and Non-Collapse in Lorentzian Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09940)
*Rohit Dhormare*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了洛伦兹型Raychaudhuri方程与Ricci流的Perelman非坍缩定理之间的几何对应关系，由此推导出洛伦兹版本的非坍缩定理，引入了一个协变熵泛函来描述因果体积演化，并提出了测地线熵容量（geodesic entropy capacity）——一种曲率有界的信息存储上限，从而在几何框架下统一了引力、热力学与信息理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立广义相对论中的测地线聚焦（geodesic focusing）与几何分析中Ricci流（Ricci flow）的单调性及熵泛函之间的深层联系，并借此将引力、热力学与信息理论统一在一个几何框架下。

Method: 通过将Raychaudhuri方程解释为Ricci流的洛伦兹类比，建立几何对应关系；利用该对应关系推导洛伦兹非坍缩定理（Lorentzian non-collapsing theorem），并引入协变熵泛函（covariant entropy functional）。

Result: 推导出洛伦兹版本的非坍缩定理，引入了协变熵泛函，并提出了测地线熵容量这一概念，即曲率所限制的时空区域可存储信息的容量上限。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一的几何框架，将引力、热力学和信息理论联系起来，为从几何角度理解时空的信息承载能力提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In this paper, we establish a geometric correspondence between the Lorentzian Raychaudhuri equation and Perelman's non-collapsing theorem for the Ricci flow. By interpreting the Raychaudhuri equation as a Lorentzian analogue of Ricci flow, we connect geodesic focusing in general relativity to the monotonicity and entropy functionals of geometric analysis. Using this correspondence, we derive a Lorentzian non-collapsing theorem and introduce a covariant entropy functional governing causal volume evolution. Finally, we propose the concept of geodesic entropy capacity, a curvature-bounded limit on the information that can be stored in spacetime regions, providing a unified geometric framework linking gravitation, thermodynamics, and information.

</details>


### [222] [Scalar and vector bosons in a Bonnor-Melvin-$Λ$ spacetime: an exact Duffin-Kemmer-Petiau analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09997)
*Francisco A. Cruz Neto,Luis B. Castro*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Bonnor–Melvin–Λ时空背景下，利用Duffin–Kemmer–Petiau (DKP)形式论对标量玻色子与矢量玻色子进行了精确求解，推导出闭合形式的径向本征函数，并揭示了该背景下所有物理扇区均呈现纯离散径向谱的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前对Bonnor–Melvin–Λ时空中玻色子的研究多基于锥形近似（conical approximation），缺乏精确的全局解。本文旨在通过DKP形式论，在不依赖锥形近似的前提下，对标量与矢量玻色子进行统一的精确处理，并澄清背景时空的全局几何结构对粒子约束和谱性质的影响。

Method: 采用DKP形式论，利用梅泽（Umezawa）投影算子分离物理的自旋-0与自旋-1扇区；在完整弯曲时空中推导精确的二阶运动方程；将径向动力学表述为奇异Sturm–Liouville问题，并通过Friedrichs自伴延拓（Friedrichs self-adjoint extension）固定物理径向定义域。

Result: 标量扇区的径向方程约化为具有三角Pöschl–Teller有效势的类薛定谔方程；矢量扇区中，纵模受相同有效势支配，横极化模则由广义三角Pöschl–Teller势描述。所有物理扇区的径向谱均呈纯离散谱，且本征函数以闭合形式给出。

Conclusion: 本文为Bonnor–Melvin–Λ时空中的标量与矢量玻色子提供了统一的精确解析处理，补充了基于锥形近似的前期分析，并阐明了背景时空的全局几何结构在形成约束和谱性质中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study scalar and vector bosons in the Bonnor--Melvin--$Λ$ spacetime within the Duffin--Kemmer--Petiau (DKP) formalism. By employing Umezawa's projection operators, we separate the physical spin-0 and spin-1 sectors and derive the corresponding exact second-order equations in the full curved spacetime, without relying on the conical approximation. For the scalar sector, the radial equation reduces to a Schrödinger-like equation with a trigonometric Pöschl--Teller effective potential. In the vector sector, the longitudinal mode is governed by the same effective potential, whereas the transverse polarizations are described by generalized trigonometric Pöschl--Teller potentials. Because the me\-tric function vanishes at a discrete set of radial points, the radial dynamics is naturally formulated as a singular Sturm--Liouville problem on a fundamental interval, with the physical radial domain fixed by the Friedrichs self-adjoint extension of the corresponding singular radial operators. As a result, all physical sectors exhibit purely discrete radial spectra, and their eigenfunctions are obtained in closed form. These results provide a unified exact treatment of scalar and vector bosons in the Bonnor--Melvin--$Λ$ spacetime, complement previous analyses based on the conical approximation, and clarify the role of the global geometric structure of the background in shaping confinement and spectral properties.

</details>

*Davide Batic,Denys Dutykh,Fabio Scardigli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索渐近安全引力（Asymptotically Safe Gravity, ASG）框架下Bonanno-Reuter规则黑洞的动力学特征，检验其无奇点几何的独特可观测信号。

Method: 基于重整化群改进的Schwarzschild度规（具有(Anti)deSitter非奇异核心），设定正值的跑动参数α使牛顿耦合在高能域趋于零；采用谱方法（Spectral Method, SM）计算标量、电磁和引力三种扰动下的拟正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）。

Result: 谱方法识别出Bonanno-Reuter黑洞的基模、大量泛音以及纯虚过阻尼模；与高阶WKB方法相比，谱方法精度更高，并且首次在该黑洞模型中解析了此前完全被遗漏的过阻尼模式。

Conclusion: 高精度谱方法对于探测量子引力启发黑洞模型的精细动力学信号至关重要，能够揭示常规近似方法（如高阶WKB）无法捕捉的关键特征。

Abstract: In this work, we explore the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of the Bonanno-Reuter black hole, one of the first regular black hole metric suggested by the Asymptotically Safe Gravity (ASG) program. The running parameter $α$ is set to a positive value, the related running Newton coupling vanishes at high energies, fully achieving an ultraviolet fixed point and eliminating non-physical UV divergences. This yields a singularity-free geometry. Hence, we focus on the resulting renormalisation-group-improved Schwarzschild metric, which naturally produces an (Anti)deSitter non-singular core. On the basis of this background, we compute the QNM spectrum for scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations by employing the Spectral Method (SM). This method, recognised for its enhanced precision compared to high-order WKB methods, allows the identification of fundamental modes, extensive collections of overtones, and purely imaginary overdamped modes that were entirely missed in previous analyses. These characteristics, resolved here for the first time in the Bonanno-Reuter black hole, underscore the crucial importance of high-precision spectral methods in investigating delicate signatures of black hole models inspired by quantum gravity.

### [224] [Magnetising de Sitter and Anti-de Sitter spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10213)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究在球对称条件下对德西特（de Sitter）和反德西特（Anti-de Sitter）时空进行磁化。弱场情形下，通过求解麦克斯韦方程在固定dS/AdS背景中得到磁场；强场情形下，考虑爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦引力与引力流体源，磁场引力反作用导致dS/AdS时空变形，生成dS/AdS型梅尔文磁宇宙（Melvin magnetic universe）类比解。该解通过哈里森变换（Harrison-like transformation）结合流体能量和压强的相应变换得到，并分析了解的部分物理与几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在具有宇宙学常数的弯曲时空（dS/AdS）中引入强磁场的可能性，并研究磁场对时空几何的反作用效应，填补磁化时空在非渐近平直背景下的研究空白。

Method: 弱场情形下直接求解麦克斯韦方程；强场情形下采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）理论耦合引力流体源，通过哈里森变换（Harrison transformation）构造含磁场的dS/AdS时空解，并相应变换流体的能量与压强。

Result: 强磁场通过引力反作用（gravitational backreaction）使dS/AdS时空变形，得到dS/AdS型梅尔文磁宇宙（Melvin magnetic universe）类比解；弱场下获得固定背景中的磁场解。

Conclusion: 成功构建了球对称dS/AdS时空中的磁化解，强磁场情形下的解具有类似梅尔文磁宇宙的结构，并展现出因磁场反作用导致的几何变形。

Abstract: We attempt to magnetise the de Sitter (dS) and Anti-de Sitter (AdS) spacetimes in spherical symmetry. First, the weak field case is considered where Maxwell's equation is solved to find magnetic fields in fixed dS/AdS backgrounds. For strong magnetic fields we consider Einstein-Maxwell gravity with a gravitating fluid source. With gravitational backreaction of the magnetic field taken into account, the strong fields deform the dS/AdS spacetime, resulting in a dS/AdS-type analogue of the Melvin magnetic universe. This solution is obtained via a Harrison-like transformation, along with appropriate transformations of the fluid energy and pressures. Some of its physical and geometrical properties of the solution are studied.
