### [225] [Probing the Strong Equivalence Principle through the External Field Effect. How Do Two Masses Fall?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10247)
*Ankit Kumar,Kelvin Tang Tee Tniam,Peng Chengxiaohe,Ng Li Yang,P. Arumugam,Tom Złośnik,Yen-Kheng Lim,Tomasz Paterek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了修正引力（特别是MOND）中的外场效应（External Field Effect），通过分析两种不同构型（对称轴平行或垂直于外重力场）的双球质量系统，推导了内部动力学解，发现了垂直于构型轴的横向力分量，并评估了区分这两种构型所需的实验灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于尚未确认暗物质粒子（dark matter particle）的存在，修正引力（modified gravity）作为一种替代解释持续受到关注。其中MOND理论预言的外场效应（External Field Effect）违反了强等效原理（strong equivalence principle, SEP），为实验检验修正引力提供了可行途径。

Method: 研究了两个球形质量组成的系统，其对称轴分别平行或正交于局域引力场（local gravitational field）。在强均匀外场（strong uniform external field）和径向外场（radial external field）两种条件下推导了描述系统内部动力学的解。

Result: 在径向外场中，若非相对论引力场（non-relativistic gravitational field）允许存在非零旋度（non-vanishing curl），则垂直构型中两质量的相互吸引力并不严格沿对称轴方向，而是产生一个小的横向分量（transverse component）。检测简单MOND插值函数（simple MOND interpolating function）的预言需要约0.1 fm的空间灵敏度，亚毫米质量演化约30分钟。

Conclusion: 区分两种构型所需的空间和时间灵敏度可通过悬浮微粒（levitated particles）或空间实验环境实现；较低分辨率的实验也可作为独立检验SEP的手段，并对修正引力理论施加约束。

Abstract: Despite compelling evidence, the absence of a confirmed dark matter particle has sustained interest in modified gravity as an alternative explanation for the observed phenomenology. One prominent example is Modified Newtonian Dynamics (MOND), which predicts that the internal dynamics of a system depends on the external gravitational field in which it is embedded. This so-called External Field Effect violates the strong equivalence principle (SEP) and is absent in canonical mechanics, making it a promising avenue for experimental tests of modified gravity. Motivated by this, we investigate the dynamics of two spherical masses arranged such that their symmetry axis is either parallel or orthogonal to the local gravitational field. We derive solutions describing the internal dynamics of such systems in both strong uniform and radial external fields. In particular, for a radial external field, if the non-relativistic gravitational field is free to have non-vanishing curl, we find that the mutual attraction of the masses in the perpendicular configuration is not strictly aligned with their symmetry axis. It acquires a small transverse component, even when the external gravitational field is everywhere balanced by non-gravitational forces. Using these solutions, we determine the spatial and temporal sensitivities required to distinguish the two configurations and systematically assess experimentally relevant effects, including air drag, object size, and surface interactions. As an example, detecting the prediction of the simple MOND interpolating function requires a spatial sensitivity of order 0.1 fm for sub-millimeter masses evolving over approximately 30 minutes. Such times may be achievable with levitated particles or in space-based environments. Experiments operating at lower resolutions are also interesting as independent tests of SEP and place constraints on modified-gravity theories.

### [226] [Circular orbits and particle collisions close to charged black holes surrounded by scalar clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10325)
*Maria Chivers,Betti Hartmann,Katherine Horton,Yves Brihaye*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析带电和带磁荷（dyonic）的标量毛发黑洞时空，求解大质量（不）带电检验粒子的运动方程，确定圆形轨道的存在条件与稳定性，并计算粒子碰撞的质心系能量（center-of-mass energy）。

Result: 标量毛发存在时，最多可存在四个圆形轨道（两个稳定、两个非稳定），以及角动量为零的静态轨道；带电粒子碰撞可产生无限大的质心系能量（infinite center-of-mass energy），与RN情况类似，但导致发散所需的电荷值依赖于视界上的标量场值。

Conclusion: 标量毛发的存在显著改变了黑洞周围粒子的圆形轨道结构，且对电荷发散条件产生非平凡依赖，拓展了对黑洞时空粒子动力学的理解。

Abstract: We study the motion of massive (un)charged test particles in space-times of electric and dyonic black holes which carry scalar hair. We determine the stable and unstable circular orbits and discuss the collision of massive test particles. In particular, we aim at demonstrating how the presence of the scalar hair of the black hole changes the circular orbits and particle collisions, respectively, as compared to the Reissner-Nordström (RN) space-time. We find that in the presence of scalar hair, up to four circular orbits (two unstable and two stable) as well as static orbits with $L=0$ can exist. Particle collisions can generate infinite center-of-mass energy when at least one of the particles is charged, very similar to the RN case. We find, however, that the value of the charge at which this divergence happens depends on the value of the scalar field on the horizon.

### [227] [Geodesics and shadows of the spindle-deformed Kerr black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10533)
*Hong-Da Lyu,Mingzhi Wang,Shoulong Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在一类精确的Ricci平坦旋转黑洞解（描述Kerr度规的纺锤形变）中研究了测地线运动与黑洞阴影，发现零测地线在${\cal O}(B^2)$阶可分离，并利用微扰分离方程解析了光子区域与阴影，数值结果验证了微扰处理的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在四维广义相对论（general relativity）中构造了一类新的精确Ricci平坦旋转黑洞解，其附加参数$B$刻画了Kerr几何的纺锤形变（spindle deformation）。为理解该形变对测地线运动与黑洞阴影（black-hole shadow）的影响，本文研究了该时空中的测地线动力学与阴影结构。

Method: 采用Hamilton-Jacobi方程分析类时与类零测地线（null geodesics）的可分离性；在${\cal O}(B^2)$阶利用微扰分离方程解析确定光子区域（photon region）、赤道光子轨道及黑洞阴影，并与精确时空中的直接射线追踪（ray tracing）数值结果进行对比。

Result: 类时和类零测地线的Hamilton-Jacobi方程均不完全可分离，但零测地线在${\cal O}(B^2)$主导阶变为可分离；类时测地线中纺锤形变移动了最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO），并可产生最外稳定圆轨道；微扰解析结果与数值射线追踪吻合，量化了与Kerr度规的偏差。

Conclusion: 微扰方法能够有效描述纺锤形变黑洞的零测地线行为与阴影特征，数值结果验证了该处理的准确性，并定量刻画了与标准Kerr黑洞的偏离。

Abstract: Recently, a new exact Ricci-flat rotating black-hole solution was constructed in four-dimensional general relativity, in which an additional parameter $B$ characterizes a spindle deformation of the Kerr geometry. We study geodesic motion and black-hole shadows in this spacetime. The Hamilton-Jacobi equation is not exactly separable for either timelike or null geodesics. Remarkably, however, at the leading nontrivial order, ${\cal O}(B^2)$, null but not timelike geodesics become separable. In the timelike sector, the spindle deformation shifts the innermost stable circular orbit and can give rise to an outermost stable circular orbit. In the null sector, exploiting the perturbatively separated equations, we analytically determine the photon region, equatorial photon orbits, and black-hole shadow, and compare the resulting predictions with direct ray tracing in the exact spacetime. The numerical results validate the perturbative treatment and quantify the deviations from Kerr.

### [228] [A winding number analysis of Schwarzschild black hole stability in light of Planck-scale modified kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10600)
*Mohsen Khodadi,Nosratolla Jafari,Shahin Mamedov*

TL;DR: 本文通过热力学拓扑（thermodynamic topology）方法分析普朗克尺度修正的运动学对史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）稳定性的影响。基于修正色散关系（MDR）导出的立方熵修正，研究发现仅存在一个不稳定分支（$w=-1, W=-1$），而另一个看似稳定（$w=+1$）的解因负质量/温度被排除。因此该类MDR无法产生稳定的史瓦西黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用一种熟知的唯象修正色散关系（phenomenological MDR），其主导修正项为 $\eta E^3/E_P$，并由此导出立方熵修正。基于熵-几何对应（entropy-geometry correspondence），施加物理约束条件（$S'(r_h) > 0, T > 0$）后，对史瓦西黑洞进行热力学拓扑分析。

Result: 对于修正参数的正负两种符号，均只存在一个不稳定分支（$w=-1, W=-1$）。另一个给出稳定信号（$w=+1$）的根因负质量/温度而被排除，且位于微扰论（perturbative regime）适用范围之外。

Conclusion: 该类型的修正色散关系不能产生稳定的史瓦西黑洞。但具有不同主导阶修正的MDR可能表现不同，因此寻找普朗克尺度稳定化的可能性仍是一个开放问题。

Abstract: Determining whether Planck-scale effects can stabilize black holes addresses fundamental questions about black hole evaporation and quantum gravity consistency. Here, we analyze the thermodynamic topology of Schwarzschild black holes under Planck-scale modified kinematics, using a cubic entropy correction derived from a well-known phenomenological MDR with leading correction \(ηE^3/E_P\). Enforcing physical constraints (\(S'(r_h) > 0\), \(T > 0\)) via the entropy-geometry correspondence, we find a single unstable branch with \(w = -1\) and \(W = -1\) for both signs of the correction parameter. A second root suggesting stability (\(w = +1\)) is excluded due to negative mass/temperature and lies outside the perturbative regime. Thus, this class of MDRs does not yield stable Schwarzschild black holes. However, MDRs with different leading-order corrections may behave otherwise, leaving the search for Planck-scale stabilization an open endeavor.

Method: 论文采用的核心方法是复化（complexify）JNW解中的参数，即执行Wick转动（Wick rotation），将实参数延拓为复参数，从而将原本含奇点的度量（metric）转变为正则度量。

Result: 通过参数复化后得到的正则度量出人意料地描述了一个双渐近平直（twice asymptotically flat）的正则可穿越虫洞，即由鬼标量场（ghost EMS）驱动的Ellis III类虫洞（Ellis class III wormhole）。

Conclusion: JNW解属于一个描述不同引力理论（gravity theories）的行动量层级（hierarchy of actions）。一旦JNW获得正则化版本，该层级中对应的其他引力理论也会自动获得相应的正则化解。

Abstract: We propose a novel way to achieve the regularization of the JNW globally naked singularity sourced by the canonical Einstein minimally coupled scalar field (EMS). The key idea is to complexify (Wick rotate) the JNW parameters, which yields a regular metric that surprisingly represents a twice asymptotically flat regular traversable wormhole, famously known as the Ellis class III wormhole sourced by the ghost EMS. We begin by arguing that the JNW solution belongs to a hierarchy of actions describing different gravity theories, which indicates that a regularized version of JNW automatically adds corresponding regular versions to the hierarchy of gravity theories.

### [230] [Scalarization of Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg black hole with multiple horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10614)
*Hong Guo,Yun Soo Myung*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-欧拉-海森堡-标量理论中，通过引入标量场与麦克斯韦项的二次耦合，研究了具有多重视界的爱因斯坦-欧拉-海森堡黑洞的标量化现象。发现磁荷EEH黑洞存在四类视界族，低、冷、高视界均可出现标量化分支，并通过稳定性分析确定了物理上可行的标量化黑洞参数窗口。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在EEH-标量理论中引入标量场与麦克斯韦项的二次耦合；固定质量M=1和欧拉-海森堡参数μ=0.03，分析磁荷q对不同视界族标量化的触发；构造标量化黑洞的三个基本分支，并基于质量正定性条件确定标量荷的上界；采用时域稳定性分析（time-domain stability analysis）评估解的稳定性。

Result: 磁荷EEH黑洞存在低、冷、负、热四类视界族，三重视界出现在磁荷q∈[0.95,1.0065]的窄带范围内。低、冷、高视界均可触发标量化并产生无限分支。质量正定性条件给出了低视界和冷视界标量化黑洞的主标量荷上界，从而限定了霍金温度与熵的允许区域。时域稳定性分析表明，不稳定性仅出现在小标量荷区域。

Conclusion: 在低视界和冷视界解的主标量荷中间窗口内，以及热视界解的主标量荷下界以上，存在稳定且物理上可行的标量化黑洞。

Abstract: Scalarizations of the Einstein-Euler-Heisenberg (EEH) black hole (EEHBH) with multiple horizons are investigated in the EEH-scalar theory by introducing a quadratic scalar coupling to the Maxwell term. For mass $M=1$ and Euler-Heisenberg parameter $μ=0.03$, the magnetically charged EEHBH admits four horizon families (low, cold, negative, and hot), with triple horizons appearing in the narrow band of magnetic charge $q\in[0.95,1.0065]$. The onset scalarization around the low, cold, and high horizons is then analyzed for the magnetic charge $q=0.5,\,1,\,2$, implying infinite branches of scalarized black holes for each case. We construct the three fundamental branches of scalarized black holes. From the positivity condition of their mass, we find the upper bounds on primary scalar charges $q_{s}$ for scalarized low and cold horizons. These bounds determine the allowable regions for the Hawking temperature and entropy. Furthermore, we perform a time-domain stability analysis and find that the instabilities arise only at small scalar charge regime. Therefore, stable and physically viable scalarized black holes exist in an intermediate window of the primary scalar charge for low and cold horizon solutions and a lower bound for hot horizon solution.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索光子与Weyl张量非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）在黑洞引力背景下的可观测效应，尤其是真空双折射（vacuum birefringence）如何影响偏振相关的光传播。

Method: 采用Riccati–Hankel匹配方案（Riccati–Hankel matching scheme）提取两种偏振态的散射矩阵；使用波光学与几何光学（geometric optics）联合计算灰体因子、吸收截面、微分散射截面等可观测物理量；利用三个独立射线追踪器交叉验证几何光学链。

Result: 耦合参数α使光子球（photon sphere）分裂，两种偏振态的临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）不同，产生双阴影（double shadow），当α/M²=0.75时阴影边缘分离度达阴影半径的62%。后向信号（backward signal）受宇称保护，在α=0时严格为零。

Conclusion: 后向信号是偏振敏感效应最干净的诊断手段，可用于检验光与Weyl张量的非最小耦合是否存在。

Abstract: A photon coupled non-minimally to the Weyl tensor propagates differently in its two linear polarization states: the vacuum around a black hole becomes a birefringent medium. On a Schwarzschild background the coupling $α$ splits the photon sphere and the critical impact parameter of the two polarizations, producing a double shadow and a polarization-dependent photon ring; the two shadow edges separate by $62\%$ of the shadow radius at $α/M^2=0.75$. We compute a unified set of wave-optical and geometric-optical observables for both polarizations across a range of $α$: greybody factors, absorption cross sections, differential cross sections and their glories, a backward birefringence signal, shadows, photon rings, and null trajectories. The two-polarization scattering matrices are extracted with a Riccati--Hankel matching scheme that keeps the phase-sensitive observables reliable, and the geometric-optics chain is cross-validated with three independent ray tracers. The cleanest diagnostic is the backward signal: it is protected by parity and vanishes identically at $α=0$.

### [232] [Corrections to inflationary models induced by non-minimal coupling between scalar field and curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10679)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量场与曲率的非最小耦合普遍存在于引力理论中，但对其在暴胀阶段产生的修正缺乏系统、模型无关的分析框架。本文旨在通过一种特定参数化，统一描述非最小耦合对暴胀模型特性（如势能形式、扰动参数）以及再加热阶段动力学的修正效应。

Method: 采用标量场与曲率非最小耦合的特定参数化方案；在暴胀阶段分析该参数化导致的标量场势能形变及宇宙学扰动参数的偏差；引入一种基于张标比 r 对标量扰动谱指数 n_s 依赖关系进行级数展开的模型无关分类方法。

Result: 该参数化使得再加热阶段动力学完全等价于爱因斯坦引力中最小耦合的情形；基于 r-n_s 级数展开的分类方法能将多种已知暴胀模型作为特例纳入统一框架。

Conclusion: 所提出的参数化及其模型无关分析方法为研究非最小耦合对暴胀模型造成的修正提供了统一的数学框架，并能涵盖已有暴胀模型作为特殊情况。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider possible corrections to the characteristics of inflationary models based on a specific parametrization of the non-minimal coupling between the scalar field and curvature. At the inflationary stage, these corrections lead to a deformation of the scalar field potential and a corresponding deviation in the determination of the cosmological perturbation parameters. At the same time, it is shown that the proposed parametrization yields a description of the reheating stage dynamics completely analogous to the case of Einstein gravity with minimal coupling between the scalar field and curvature. For a model-independent analysis of inflationary corrections induced by a non-minimal coupling, a classification of inflationary scenarios based on the expansion in series of the dependence of the tensor-to-scalar ratio on the spectral index of scalar perturbations is considered. It is also shown that this approach allows for the inclusion of well-known inflationary models as special cases.

### [233] [Regular black holes with Minkowskian cores: causal structure and observational degeneracy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10713)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 尽管新构造的黑洞内部几何（interior geometry）与奇异黑洞有本质差异，但其光学信号（optical signatures）与具有相同渐近参数的施瓦西和克尔时空高度接近，几乎不可区分。

Conclusion: 黑洞内部结构的巨大差异可能导致几乎无法区分的光学外观，这突显出利用当前阴影和成像观测探测致密天体（compact objects）内部结构所面临的严峻挑战。

Abstract: We construct a new family of asymptotically flat static and rotating regular black holes characterized by a Minkowskian core and a finite two-horizon structure. The solutions are obtained within the framework of gravitational decoupling and provide an analytically tractable realization of non-singular black hole geometries with a regular interior and well-defined asymptotic properties. We investigate the optical appearance of the rotating spacetime through shadow observables and ray-traced images of geometrically thin, optically thin accretion disks. Despite the substantial differences between the interior geometry of these solutions and that of singular black holes, their optical signatures are found to remain remarkably close to those of Schwarzschild and Kerr spacetimes with the same asymptotic parameters. Our results show that markedly different black hole interiors may lead to nearly indistinguishable optical appearances, highlighting the challenges of probing the internal structure of compact objects using current shadow and imaging observations.

### [234] [Nonlinear electrodynamics and stability of spherically symmetric space-times in scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10718)
*Kirill A. Bronnikov,Rustam Ibadov,Feruza Y. Shaymanova,Najibullokhon M. Shukurullokhon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories, STT）中静态球对称解的线性径向扰动，该理论源自由非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics, NED）驱动，属于Bergmann-Wagoner-Nordtvedt类。得到了有效势$V_{\rm eff}$的一般表达式，并证明若NED具有正确的Maxwell弱场极限，则在零电荷极限下NED的影响完全消失，且对于等电-磁荷情形，STT-Maxwell解的稳定性结果可直接推广至STT-NED解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用线性径向（monopole）扰动分析，针对Bergmann-Wagoner-Nordtvedt类标量-张量理论，推导了有效势$V_{\rm eff}$的一般表达式；考虑了标量场的任意自相互作用势以及可能在某些时空区域呈现幽灵（phantom）行为的标量场（即所谓的陷印幽灵，trapped ghosts）。

Result: 若NED具有正确的Maxwell弱场极限，则零电荷极限下$V_{\rm eff}$中不包含任何NED的痕迹，扰动动力学与真空STT解相同。对于等电-磁荷（$F=0$）情形，STT-Maxwell解的稳定性结果可直接推广至STT-NED解，无需修改。

Conclusion: 在特定条件下（Maxwell弱场极限、零电荷极限、等电-磁荷），非线性电动力学对标量-张量理论中静态球对称解的扰动稳定性不产生额外影响，表明此前基于Maxwell线性电磁场得到的稳定性结论具有更广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We study linear perturbations of static, spherically symmetric solutions of scalar-tensor theories (STT) of gravity from the Bergmann-Wagoner-Nordtvedt class, sourced by nonlinear electrodynamics (NED). We obtain a general expression for the effective potential $V_{\rm eff}$ governing the perturbation dynamics for theories with arbitrary scalar-electromagnetic interaction of the form $L(ψ, F)$, where $ψ$ is a scalar field and $F = F_{μν} F^{μν}$ the electromagnetic invariant. This consideration includes, in particular, arbitrary scalar self-interaction potentials and scalar fields that can be phantom in some regions of space-time (the so-called trapped ghosts). Only radial (monopole) perturbations are considered here as the most likely ones to cause an instability. It is shown, in particular, that if NED has a correct Maxwell weak field limit, the zero charge limit of $V_{\rm eff}$ does not contain any trace of NED, and the perturbation dynamics is the same as for vacuum STT solutions. The previously obtained stability results for STT-Maxwell solutions are shown to be extended without change to STT-NED solutions with equal electric and magnetic charges, implying $F =0$.

### [235] [Scalar-induced gravitational waves from a box-shaped curvature power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10730)
*Zu-Cheng Chen,Lang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文计算了由平坦原初曲率功率谱（在有限对数带内平坦、其余为零）在辐射主导时期二阶微扰产生的引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）随机背景，给出了窄带和宽带两种情况的解析结果，并提供了边缘函数的封闭形式替代公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次引力波（second-order GWs）是研究早期宇宙原初曲率涨落的重要探针，但以往对有限带宽且边界尖锐的谱形缺乏完整的解析处理。作者希望填补这一空白，为参数扫描提供高效可用的分析公式。

Method: 在辐射主导时期（radiation era），将原初曲率功率谱设定为有限波段 [k₋, k₊] 内 ln k 平坦、其余为零的对数盒（logarithmic box）形式。利用其尖锐边界简化源卷积的几何结构，将对动量三角形的重叠区域积分化为紧致的解析积分，并在窄带和宽带两种极限下分别计算。

Result: 窄带情形下，谱形等于单色（monochromatic）结果乘以几何重叠因子 Φ_box(κ,Δ)，该因子将红外斜率从 k³ ln²k 变为 k² ln²k，转折点位于 k_b=2k_* sinhΔ。宽带情形下，可分离出下边缘、尺度不变平台和上边缘三部分，分别给出红外 k³ ln²k 上升、尺度不变平台和硬端点 k=2k₊ 处的四次方截止行为，并统一为两个 Δ 无关的边缘函数的乘积表达式。

Conclusion: 本文提供了二阶引力波谱从窄带到宽带连续过渡的完整解析描述，并给出了无需数值积分的封闭形式替代公式（integral-free closed-form surrogate），可直接用于参数空间扫描（parameter scans）。

Abstract: We compute the stochastic background of gravitational waves (GWs) produced at second order in cosmological perturbation theory by a primordial curvature power spectrum that is flat in $\ln k$ over a finite band $[k_-,k_+]=[k_*e^{-Δ},k_*e^{+Δ}]$ and vanishes elsewhere. This logarithmic box interpolates between a monochromatic spectrum as $Δ\to0$ and a locally scale-invariant plateau as $Δ\to\infty$, and its sharp boundaries make the geometry of the source convolution unusually transparent. Working in the radiation era, we reduce the convolution to a compact integral over the overlap between the momentum triangle and the box, and evaluate it analytically in two regimes. For a narrow box we show that, to leading order in the width, the spectrum equals the Dirac-spectrum result multiplied by a purely geometric overlap factor $Φ_{\rm box}(κ,Δ)$; this factor turns the infrared slope from $k^{3}\ln^{2}k$ into $k^{2}\ln^{2}k$ at a break $k_b=2k_*\sinhΔ$. For a broad box we separate the lower edge, the scale-invariant interior, and the upper edge, derive the leading behaviour in each (an infrared $k^{3}\ln^{2}k$ rise, a scale-invariant plateau, and a quartic cut-off at the hard endpoint $k=2k_+$), and combine them into a single uniform formula cast as a product of two universal, $Δ$-independent edge functions. We also provide an integral-free closed-form surrogate for these edge functions for use in parameter scans.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在总共27个探测器对-事件测量中，有26个测量的事件峰值与对应的噪声系综在统计上不可区分，所有涉及独立Virgo探测器的对均符合此结果；唯一的例外是GW190412的H1×L1对。

Conclusion: 互相关统计量（cross-correlation statistic）不能作为独立稳健的引力波事件判别标准；LIGO-Virgo对中持续存在的可比相关结构表明，应变数据（strain data）中可能包含一个连续的关联物理成分，随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background）是一个合理的候选解释。

Abstract: We revisit the inter-detector cross-correlation criterion used in gravitational-wave validation by extending the analysis of Creswell et al.~\cite{Creswell2017} to nine LIGO--Virgo candidate events from the O2 and O3 observing runs. For each event, we analyze all three detector pairs (H1$\times$L1, H1$\times$V1, L1$\times$V1) and compare the normalized cross-correlation function $C(τ)$ in the event window with an empirical ensemble of $N=200$ surrounding off-source windows, using a band-pass-only pipeline. In 26 of 27 pair-measurements, the event peak is statistically indistinguishable from the corresponding noise ensemble, including all pairs involving the independent Virgo detector. The only exception is GW190412 in the H1$\times$L1 pair. We conclude that the cross-correlation statistic does not provide a robust standalone separation between event and noise. We interpret the persistence of comparable correlation structure in the LIGO--Virgo pairs as evidence that the strain data may contain a continuous correlated physical component, for which a stochastic gravitational-wave background is a plausible candidate.

### [238] [Post-Newtonian N-Body Dynamics in Extended Theories of Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10889)
*Antonio Tedesco*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了标量-张量-四阶引力（STFOG）中相对论性N体系统的完整第一后牛顿（1PN）拉格朗日量及运动方程，并以三个Yukawa函数统一描述了标量、引力磁和三体扇区，在广义相对论极限下恢复了爱因斯坦-英费尔德-霍夫曼（Einstein-Infeld-Hoffmann）方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为标量-张量-四阶引力（Scalar-Tensor-Fourth-Order Gravity, STFOG）及其特例非交换谱几何（Non-Commutative Spectral Geometry, NCSG）提供完整的1PN近似描述，建立适用于太阳系、双脉冲星和银河系中心恒星轨道等系统的统一相对论性天体力学框架。

Method: 在Φ∼Ψ（γ∼1）条件下，采用标准后牛顿（Standard Post-Newtonian）规范求解线性化四阶场方程；直接从点粒子作用量（point-particle action）出发构建变分拉格朗日量（variational Lagrangian）。

Result: 动力学由三个Yukawa函数ζ、𝒲和Ξ主导，分别对应标量、引力磁（gravitomagnetic）和三体扇区，依赖于附加传播模式的有效质量（m_R, m_Y, m_φ）；证明非线性度规分量^{(4)}g_{00}在1PN阶不起作用，并以闭式（closed form）获得了轨道运动方程。

Conclusion: 该形式主义为包含太阳系、双脉冲星PSR J0737-3039、银河系中心恒星轨道及三体系统在内的相对论性天体力学提供了统一框架，并在广义相对论极限下恢复了爱因斯坦-英费尔德-霍夫曼方程。

Abstract: We derive the complete first post-Newtonian (1PN) Lagrangian and corresponding equations of motion for the relativistic $N$-body system in Scalar-Tensor-Fourth-Order Gravity (STFOG), including the Non-Commutative Spectral Geometry (NCSG) sector as a special case. In the regime $Φ\sim Ψ$ ($γ\sim 1$), the linearized fourth-order field equations are solved in the Standard Post-Newtonian gauge, and the variational Lagrangian is built directly from the point-particle action. The resulting dynamics is governed by three Yukawa functions $ζ$, $\mathcal{W}$ and $Ξ$, which encode the scalar, gravitomagnetic and three-body sectors and depend on the effective masses $(m_R,m_Y,m_φ)$ of the additional propagating modes. In this context, we show that the nonlinear metric component ${}^{(4)}\!g_{00}$ plays no role at 1PN level. The 1PN orbital motion of the above extended theories is thus obtained in closed form, and the Einstein--Infeld--Hoffmann equations are recovered in the corresponding general-relativistic limit. The formalism provides a common framework for the relativistic celestial mechanics of the Solar System, binary pulsars such as PSR J0737-3039, Galactic-center stellar orbits and triple systems.

</details>

*Suman Kumar Panja,Yu Shi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究κ-闵可夫斯基时空（κ-deformed space-time）中最小长度尺度对Reissner-Nordström反德西特（RN AdS）黑洞热力学的修正，发现非对易性（non-commutativity）会轻微降低范德瓦尔斯（Van der Waals）类相变的临界比，并扩大焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀（Joule-Thomson expansion）中的冷却区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子引力在最小长度尺度上的可能观测信号，通过研究κ-变形时空中的非对易性对黑洞热力学性质的修正。

Method: 通过相空间对易关系（phase-space commutation relations）构造修正度规，进而推导出变形的霍金温度（Hawking temperature）、熵（entropy）和焓（enthalpy）。

Result: 非对易参数使得小-大黑洞相变的临界比轻微降低；焦耳-汤姆逊膨胀中冷却区域在温度-压力平面上扩大；共存区域（coexistence region）和反转曲线（inversion curves）被系统性形变。

Conclusion: 尽管整体热力学与范德瓦尔斯流体的类比关系仍然保持，但最小长度尺度系统地修正了共存区域和反转曲线，这可能为量子引力提供可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic modifications of the Reissner-Nordstroem anti-de Sitter (RN AdS) black hole induced by a minimal length scale,which naturally emerges in $κ$-deformed space-time. By constructing the modified metric via phase-space commutation relations,we derive the deformed Hawking temperature, entropy, and enthalpy. We analyze the thermal stability through the heat capacity and study the P-V criticality, revealing that the black hole undergoes a small-to-large phase transition analogous to the Van der Waals system, albeit with a critical ratio slightly lowered by non-commutativity. Furthermore, we examine the Joule-Thomson expansion and find that the non-commutative (NC) parameter expands the cooling region in the temperature-pressure plane. Our results demonstrate that while the overall thermodynamic analogy with the Van der Waals fluid persists, the minimal length scale systematically deform the coexistence region and inversion curves, offering potential observational signatures for quantum gravity.

Conclusion: 自由数据形式论为短脉冲型柯西数据的直接构造提供了有效途径，所得渐近平坦延拓结果显著提升了该领域已知结论的普适性。

Abstract: We make use of the free data formalism developed in \cite{CK25,CK26} to provide a direct construction of short-pulse type Cauchy data. ### [243] [Turbulence, Norm Inflation, and the Rendall Instability for the Einstein-Euler System with Positive Cosmological Constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11375)
*Elliot Marshall*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值方法首次在多于一维空间维度下研究了含正宇宙学常数和线性状态方程的Einstein-Euler方程扰动解中的Rendall不稳定性（Rendall instability），发现该不稳定性会引发向前的湍流级联（forward turbulent cascade）和流体能量密度的H^s范数膨胀（norm inflation），并证实该不稳定性可驱动晚期宇宙中的结构形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期数值与解析工作已揭示在扰动时空中流体密度梯度会在趋向未来类时无穷远（future timelike infinity）时形成陡峭梯度并爆发，即Rendall不稳定性；但该现象此前仅在1维空间中被研究，尚不清楚其在高维中的表现及物理后果。

Method: 对Einstein-Euler方程组的空间齐次且正交的精确解引入U(1)-对称扰动（U(1)-symmetric perturbations），在正宇宙学常数和线性状态方程p=Kρ（K∈(1/3,1)）条件下进行数值模拟，分析扰动随时间的演化行为。

Result: 数值结果强有力地表明，Rendall不稳定性会引发向前的湍流级联，并导致流体能量密度的H^s范数膨胀；这是在含有正宇宙学常数的场方程组解中首次观察到的小数据湍流（small data turbulence）现象。

Conclusion: Rendall不稳定性是多维现象，其引发的湍流效应能够驱动晚期宇宙中的结构形成，这对理解宇宙晚期动力学具有重要启示。

Abstract: We numerically study perturbations of spatially homogeneous and orthogonal solutions to the Einstein-Euler equations with positive cosmological constant and linear equation of state $p=Kρ$ for $K \in (\frac{1}{3},1)$. Recent numerical and analytic work has demonstrated that the fluid density gradient in these perturbed spacetimes can form steep gradients and blow up as future timelike infinity is approached, a phenomenon now known as the `Rendall instability'. In this article, we study the onset of this instability outside of one spatial dimension for the first time. Our results provide compelling evidence that the Rendall instability causes a forward turbulent cascade and $H^{s}$ norm inflation in the energy density of the fluid from arbitrarily small $U(1)$-symmetric perturbations. This is, to the best of our knowledge, the first example of small data turbulence for solutions of the field equations with a positive cosmological constant. Moreover, we find that this instability can drive structure formation in the late universe.

Abstract: We consider simple one dimensional models of acoustic black holes formed by Bose-Einstein condensates where the flow is stepwise homogeneous. These models can be thought of as acoustic black holes with a thick horizon. Particular attention will be devoted to the number of created particles and to the density-density correlation functions, these latter being at present time the experimental tool to identify Hawking like radiation in acoustic black holes.

We formulate the background evolution equations along with the corresponding slow-roll stability conditions, leading to analytic results for the scalar spectral index $n_s$ and the tensor-to-scalar ratio $R$. By applying these results to power-law potentials with $n=2$ and $n=4$, the model parameter space is constrained using the \emph{Planck} 2018 data. The findings indicate that the interaction between NMDC-induced gravitational friction and thermal dissipation effectively modulates $n_s$ and significantly expands the viable parameter space. In the $(n_s,R)$ plane, the predictions for $N=50$ fall within the 95\% confidence-level region, while those for $N=60$ extend into the 68\% confidence-level region and approach the observationally preferred central values. For the representative parameter choices examined, the tensor-to-scalar ratio is notably suppressed, generally within the range $10^{-8}\lesssim R\lesssim10^{-5}$. Moreover, the combined damping mechanism relaxes the slow-roll condition related to $η$ and limits the inflaton field excursion, thus addressing the $η$ problem without incurring super-Planckian field variations. These results indicate that warm DBI inflation with NMDC offers a theoretically coherent and observationally viable inflationary model, showcasing the complementary effects of thermal dissipation and enhanced gravitational friction in the context of modified gravity.

Method: 提出 Hadamard 重整化（Hadamard renormalization）的新表述，无需标准模式求和（mode-sum）构造即可获得 3+1 维弯曲时空中标量量子场的显式应力-能量张量；并构造了 Unruh 态（Unruh-like states）以捕获霍金辐射通量与视界处的负能量流。

Abstract: We solve the semiclassical Einstein equations for an evaporating Schwarzschild black hole in closed form, obtaining its backreacted geometry in 3+1 dimensions. This is achieved by a reformulation of the Hadamard renormalization prescription, which admits explicit stress-energy tensors for scalar quantum fields in 3+1-dimensional curved spacetimes without the standard mode-sum construction. The Unruh-like states we construct reproduce the Hawking flux at future null infinity and the associated ingoing negative-energy flux at the horizon, yielding the first analytical quasi-stationary solution describing black-hole evaporation in four-dimensional semiclassical gravity. The resulting geometry exhibits a timelike apparent horizon, providing a new analytical setting to study the causal structure of black-hole evaporation and its connection with the information-loss issue. Our results open a new route to semiclassical backreaction in four dimensions, extending the level of analytical control previously available only in two-dimensional effective models.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，有质量引力理论（massive gravity theories）的变体被广泛讨论以修正早期版本理论的缺陷，同时天文观测对引力子质量（graviton mass）的限制日益受到关注。

Method: 通过分析LIGO首次探测到的双黑洞引力波信号的波形轮廓（waveform profile），以及利用GRAVITY和Keck观测组对银河系中心附近明亮恒星轨道的追踪数据，获得引力子质量的约束。

Result: 从LIGO引力波信号和银河系中心恒星轨道观测中均得到了引力子质量的限制条件；此外，还简要讨论了其他天文学方法对引力子质量的约束途径。

Conclusion: 有质量引力理论及其变体是引力理论的重要替代方案，多种天文观测手段正协同对引力子质量施加越来越严格的约束。

Abstract: Along with a whole range of alternative theories of gravity, variants of the massive theory of gravity, i.e. the theory of gravity, in which the graviton has mass, have been actively discussed in recent years. Theorists have proposed versions of massive gravity theories that address the shortcomings of early versions of such theories. Astrophysicists and experimental physicists have been discussing limitations on the graviton mass from various astronomical observations. In particular, in the first LIGO paper, where the discovery of gravitational waves from binary black holes was reported, a limit on the mass of the graviton was obtained from the analysis of the profile of the gravitational wave signal. In the paper graviton mass constraints were obtained by analyzing the trajectory of a bright star in the vicinity of the center of our Galaxy, using observations from the GRAVITY and Keck groups. Briefly other astronomical ways to limit a graviton mass were discussed.

</details>


### [248] [Is there ghost and tachyon free bounce in UV complete gravity theory?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11765)
*Hao Hu,Alexey S. Koshelev,Abhishek Naskar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在解析无穷导数引力（analytic infinite derivative gravity）框架下证明，在不引入负宇宙学常数（negative cosmological constant）的情况下，无法构建无鬼魅（ghost）或快子（tachyon）不稳定性（instability）的反弹宇宙（bouncing Universe）解；已有的反弹解中，高阶导数形式因子（form factor）的解析性与解参数共同导致鬼魅辐射（ghost radiation）的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨在解析无穷导数引力理论中，是否可能在不出现鬼魅或快子不稳定性的前提下实现一个反弹宇宙解。

Method: 采用$(1+3)$形式（formalism）对闵可夫斯基（Minkowski）和德西特（de Sitter）时空进行自由度（degrees of freedom）的详细分析；并检验已知反弹解的性质。

Result: 在非常一般的条件下，若没有负宇宙学常数，无法构造无不稳定性的反弹解；已知反弹解中，高阶导数形式因子的解析性与解参数共同引入了鬼魅辐射。

Conclusion: 在该模型下，标量模式对宇宙微波背景（Cosmic Microwave Background, CMB）观测无影响；张量模式谱（tensor modes spectrum）被计算并讨论了其对应的物理含义。

Abstract: Analytic infinite derivative gravity theories provide a renormalizable and ghost-free description of gravity around covariantly constant backgrounds. These theories can have non-singular bouncing Universe solutions. In this paper we aim to address a question whether it is possible to realize a bouncing solution without the presence of a ghost or a tachyon instability in this framework. We perform a detailed analysis of degrees of freedom in $(1+3)$ formalism around Minkowski and de Sitter space-times. As a result it becomes clear that on a very general basis one cannot construct an instability free bounce without a negative cosmological constant. An analysis of known bouncing solutions in this model shows that an analyticity of higher derivative form factors in combination with solutions parameters result in the presence of a ghost radiation. Being motivated by the idea of resolving the cosmological singularity problem we proceed by analyzing scalar and tensor modes anyway. Scalar modes appear to not influence Cosmic Microwave Background observations at all, while tensor modes spectrum is computed and the corresponding implications are discussed.

</details>


### [249] [Universal Bounds on Black Hole Observables Imposed by Energy Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11840)
*Rahul Kumar Walia,Boris Georgiev,Chi-kwan Chan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了经典能量条件（classical energy conditions）与可观测黑洞性质之间的普适联系。通过在光子球（photon sphere）处局部施加能量条件，推导出了适用于广义相对论（General Relativity）中所有静态球对称黑洞的阴影大小、Lyapunov指数、Lyapunov时间和光子环时延的解析可检验上界。这些界限可直接用于现有及未来的视界尺度观测，为强场引力提供了独立于具体解或物质模型的互补检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对黑洞阴影和光子环等可观测性质的约束通常依赖于具体的黑洞解或物质模型，缺乏一种独立于模型、直接从能量条件出发的普适性检验框架。作者希望将经典能量条件——这个原本用于约束物质场时空曲率关系的理论概念——转化为可直接用于观测检验强场引力（strong-field gravity）的探针。

Method: 方法的核心是在光子球附近局域地施加经典能量条件（如零能量条件（null energy condition）和强能量条件（strong energy condition）），然后从广义相对论的场方程以及光子球处的几何条件出发，推导出黑洞阴影大小、Lyapunov指数、Lyapunov时间和光子环时延的解析上界。这些界限可同时用时空度规函数或应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）的局域分量两种等价形式表达。

Result: 得到了适用于广义相对论中所有静态球对称黑洞的阴影大小、Lyapunov指数、Lyapunov时间和光子环时延的解析且可检验的界限。这些界限与具体的黑洞解或物质模型无关，可直接应用于当前和未来的视界尺度观测（如事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope））。任何对这些界限的观测违背都指示要么是物质场违反了经典能量条件，要么是广义相对论在强场区域失效。

Conclusion: 经典能量条件可以被用作强场引力的观测探针。所得界限为检验强场引力提供了互补的观测手段，使能够同时对背景时空和被允许的物质来源施加约束。

Abstract: We establish a universal connection between the classical energy conditions and directly observable black hole properties. By imposing the energy conditions locally at the photon sphere, we derive analytic and testable bounds on the shadow size, Lyapunov exponent, Lyapunov time, and photon-ring time delay that apply to all static, spherically symmetric black holes in General Relativity. Expressed equivalently in terms of either the spacetime metric functions or the local components of the stress-energy tensor, these bounds provide complementary tests of strong-field gravity that are independent of any specific black hole solution or matter model. They are directly applicable to current and forthcoming horizon-scale observations, constrain both admissible black hole spacetimes and their underlying matter sources, and establish the classical energy conditions as observational probes of strong-field gravity. Any observational violation of these bounds would signal either a violation of the classical energy conditions by the matter fields or a breakdown of General Relativity in the strong-field regime.

</details>


### [250] [Corrected thermodynamics and radiation predictions of modified black bounce compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11851)
*Shokhzod Jumaniyozov,Javlon Rayimbaev,Yassine Sekhmani,Satimbay Palvanov,Olmos Tursunboyev,Dilshod Karshiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对修正引力中经 Simpson-Visser 正则化得到的 Schwarzschild 黑洞（称为 SV-MOG 时空）进行了热力学性质和辐射特征的系统分析。该时空在黑孔（regular black hole）、单向虫洞（one-way wormhole）与可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）之间光滑插值。研究推导了霍金温度（Hawking temperature）和热容（heat capacity），发现热容符号变化标识了二级相变；熵的量子引力修正通过对数项引入，在小视界半径区间显著偏离 Bekenstein-Hawking 面积律。在辐射方面，计算了几何薄吸积盘（geometrically thin accretion disk）的电磁通量、有效盘温度和谱光度，结果表明修正参数增大事件视界并增强辐射，而黑反弹参数（black bounce parameter）则抑制视界并使谱轮廓软化，提供了可观测的区分特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞模型（如 Schwarzschild）在经典广义相对论框架下存在奇点问题；Simpson-Visser 正则化提供了一种消除奇点的途径，但将其推广至修正引力（MOG）后的完整热力学和辐射特征尚待系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索 SV-MOG 致密天体在不同参数区间（黑孔/虫洞分支）的热力学相变与吸积盘辐射特征，并寻找区分其与标准 Schwarzschild 黑洞的可观测信号。

Method: 采用 Simpson-Visser 正则化方案应用于修正引力（MOG）中的 Schwarzschild 度规，构造 SV-MOG 时空；其时间流逝函数（lapse function）同时包含 MOG 耦合参数（MOG coupling parameter）和黑反弹参数（black bounce parameter）。在此基础上，分别针对黑洞分支和虫洞分支推导霍金温度和热容，识别二级相变；通过引入含系数的对数项纳入熵的量子引力修正。对于辐射部分，计算围绕黑洞和虫洞构型的几何薄吸积盘的电磁通量、有效盘温度和谱光度。

Result: 热容符号变化标志着二级相变（second-order phase transition）的发生；熵的量子引力修正导致在小视界半径处显著偏离 Bekenstein-Hawking 面积律。增大 MOG 修正参数会扩大事件视界并增强辐射发射；增大黑反弹参数则会抑制视界并使吸积盘辐射谱轮廓（spectral profile）软化。

Conclusion: SV-MOG 致密天体的热力学和辐射特征（尤其是视界尺度与谱轮廓对两个参数的依赖关系）提供了可观测的区分信号，有望将其与标准 Schwarzschild 黑洞以及仅含黑反弹参数的纯 SV（Simpson-Visser）致密天体区分开来。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamic properties and radiation characteristics of a regular compact object obtained by applying the Simpson-Visser regularisation to the Schwarzschild black hole in modified gravity. The resulting SV-MOG spacetime, whose lapse function involves both the MOG coupling parameter and the black bounce parameter, smoothly interpolates between a regular black hole, a one-way wormhole, and a traversable wormhole depending on the parameter. We derive the Hawking temperature and heat capacity for both the black hole and wormhole branches, identifying second-order phase transitions signaled by sign changes in the heat capacity. Quantum gravitational corrections to the entropy are incorporated via logarithmic terms parameterized by coefficients, and we show that deviations from the Bekenstein-Hawking area law become significant at small horizon radii. For the radiation sector, we compute the electromagnetic flux, effective disk temperature, and spectral luminosity of geometrically thin accretion disks surrounding both black hole and wormhole configurations. Our results demonstrate that increasing the modified parameter enlarges the event horizon and enhances the emission, while increasing the black bounce parameter suppresses the horizon and softens the spectral profile, providing observational signatures that may distinguish SV-MOG compact objects from their Schwarzschild and pure SV counterparts.

</details>


### [251] [Higher-derivative gravitational effective field theories are generically weakly hyperbolic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11879)
*Farid Thaalba,Fernando Abalos,Miguel Bezares*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文分析了度规高阶导数有效引力理论（metric higher-derivative effective theories of gravity）的初值问题（initial-value problem），证明任何特征速度（characteristic velocities）与度规导数无关的理论本质上都是弱双曲型（weakly hyperbolic），且这一障碍是物理固有的，无法通过规范选取或约束添加消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于：高阶导数引力理论在有效场论（effective field theory）框架中广泛出现，但其初值问题的适定性（well-posedness）长期存在疑问；已有工作观察到强双曲性（strong hyperbolicity）在此类理论中失效，但其根本原因尚不明确。

Method: 直接从特征方程（characteristic equation）中识别出自旋-2（spin-2）物理部分，而不引入降阶表述（order-reduced formulation），从而大幅简化计算；在此基础上分析特征速度与度规导数无关的度规高阶导数理论的双曲性（hyperbolicity）结构。

Result: 任何运动方程中超过二阶导数的度规理论（metric theory），在其自旋-2物理扇区中都包含一个弱双曲型分块（weakly hyperbolic block）；由于该障碍是物理扇区固有的，故无法通过任何规范选取或约束添加加以消除。

Conclusion: 该结果为该广泛理论类别中强双曲性失效提供了一个结构性的解释（structural explanation），表明此类理论在初值问题上的根本局限源于其内在结构，而非人为的规范或表述选择。

Abstract: We analyse the initial-value problem of metric higher-derivative effective theories of gravity. We show that any such theory whose characteristic velocities are independent of derivatives of the metric is intrinsically weakly hyperbolic, independently of the gauge fixing. To show this, we identify the spin-$2$ physical sector directly from the characteristic equation; this can be done without introducing an order-reduced formulation, which greatly simplifies the computation. In this sector, every metric theory with more than two derivatives in the equations of motion contains a weakly hyperbolic block. Since this obstruction is physical, no choice of gauge or constraint addition can remove it, providing a structural explanation for the failure of strong hyperbolicity in this broad class of theories.

</details>

### [252] [A d-Electron Route to Heavy-Fermion-Like Superconductivity via Geometrical Frustration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09924)
*Chaoguo Wang,Hyeonhu Bae,Jiaqi Tian,Qing-Ping Ding,Yongbin Lee,Yuji Furukawa,Shannon Gould,Brianna R. Billingsley,Si Athena Chen,Matthias Frontzek,Tai Kong,Binghai Yan,Sheng Ran,Xin Gui*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报道了Mo4PtGa17——一种具有几何阻挫呼吸烧绿石（breathing-pyrochlore）Mo晶格的非中心对称巡游d电子超导体，通过热力学、输运和核磁共振测量发现其呈现类重费米子（heavy-fermion-like）超导行为和增强的铁磁自旋涨落，理论计算表明Mo-4d态衍生的近平带、范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）和克莱默节线（Kramers nodal lines）是产生该现象的根源，揭示了通过几何阻挫实现d电子材料中类重费米子超导的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知的重费米子超导体多与具有近藤晶格（Kondo lattice）的f电子材料相关，而d电子的类重费米子体系则常与轨道选择局域矩、Hund金属物理或电荷密度波机制有关。本文旨在探索几何阻挫是否能为d电子材料提供一条通往类重费米子超导的新路径。

Method: 本研究通过热力学测量、输运测量和核磁共振（NMR）实验表征Mo4PtGa17的物性，并结合理论计算分析其电子结构，包括能带、范霍夫奇点和克莱默节线等特征。

Result: 实验发现Mo4PtGa17表现出类重费米子行为的超导电性和增强的铁磁自旋涨落，且处于铁磁不稳定性附近。理论计算表明，费米能级附近存在源于Mo-4d态的近乎平坦能带、范霍夫奇点和克莱默节线，这些特征对在位电子关联（on-site electronic correlations）具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 几何阻挫晶格使Mo4PtGa17产生了增强态密度、自旋磁化率和准粒子质量（quasiparticle mass）的电子结构，从而实现了d电子材料中经由几何阻挫的类重费米子超导新路径，并为研究从关联自旋涨落态中涌现的超导电性提供了平台。

Abstract: Heavy-fermion superconductors are mostly associated with f-electron materials with Kondo lattices, while known d-electron heavy-fermion-like systems are often linked to orbital-selective local moments, Hund-metal physics, or a charge-density-wave mechanism. Here we report Mo4PtGa17, a noncentrosymmetric itinerant d-electron superconductor with a geometrically frustrated breathing-pyrochlore Mo lattice. Thermodynamic, transport and NMR measurements reveal heavy-fermion-like behavior superconductivity and enhanced ferromagnetic spin fluctuations near a ferromagnetic instability. Theoretical calculations identify nearly flat bands, van Hove singularities and Kramers nodal lines near the Fermi energy, derived intrinsically from Mo-4d states and are robust against on-site electronic correlations. These results suggest that the geometrically frustrated lattice in Mo4PtGa17 generates an intriguing electronic structure that enhances the density of states, spin susceptibility and quasiparticle mass. Mo4PtGa17 therefore identifies a unique route to heavy-fermion-like superconductivity in d-electron materials through geometrical frustration. It also allows further investigations into superconductivity emerging from a correlated and spin-fluctuating state.

</details>


### [253] [Anyons and Inherently Complex F-symbols](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10181)
*Matthew Buican,Peter Huston,Jiannis K. Pachos*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明了并非所有任意子模型的F-符号（F-symbols）都能被实数化；通过展示两个缺少电荷共轭对称性（charge-conjugation symmetry）的辫子融合范畴（braided fusion categories）——Rep(ℤ₇⋊ℤ₃)和Rep(ℤ₅⋊ℤ₄）——的F-符号本质上是复数，揭示了这类“固有复数”F-符号的存在，并与同行工作中关于实F-符号与电荷共轭对称性之间关联的论点相呼应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对任意子（anyon）模型的描述主要依赖模数据（modular data）等辫子不变量，但这些量通常取复数值；而常见的任意子模型（如阿贝尔任意子、斐波那契任意子和伊辛任意子）的F-符号均可实化。因此，需要探究F-符号实化的普遍性，以更完整地理解任意子模型的算术性质。

Method: 通过研究缺少电荷共轭对称性的辫子融合范畴，具体分析最小秩的具有“固有复数”F-符号的范畴：Rep(ℤ₇⋊ℤ₃)和Rep(ℤ₅⋊ℤ₄)，并由此推导相应中心范畴Z(Rep(ℤ₇⋊ℤ₃))和Z(Rep(ℤ₅⋊ℤ₄))的任意子模型也具有固有复数F-符号。

Result: 发现了两个具体范畴——Rep(ℤ₇⋊ℤ₃)和Rep(ℤ₅⋊ℤ₄)——其F-符号无法被实数化，即属于“固有复数”类型；对应的中心范畴Z(Rep(ℤ₇⋊ℤ₃))和Z(Rep(ℤ₅⋊ℤ₄))的任意子模型同样具有固有复数F-符号。这些结果与同行工作证明的陈述（辫子融合范畴中实F-符号的存在与合适的电荷共轭对称性的存在相联系）的逆命题一致。

Conclusion: F-符号的实化并非普遍性质，缺少电荷共轭对称性会导致F-符号本质上为复数；该发现将具体例证与超越模数据（modular data）的任意子分类最新进展联系起来，表明完全描述任意子模型需要同时考虑融合结合性数据（fusion associativity data）的算术性质。

Abstract: Anyons in $2+1$ dimensions are not only characterized by exotic braiding statistics but also by intricate fusion properties. Two anyons may fuse into multiple topological charge sectors, and associativity of fusing three anyons to produce a fixed charge sector is governed by $F$-symbols. While braiding invariants, such as the modular data, are typically complex valued, a complete description of general anyon models requires understanding the arithmetic properties of its fusion associativity data as well. The $F$-symbols for many of the most common $2+1$d topological orders, including all Abelian anyon models as well as Fibonacci and Ising anyons, can be made real valued. We show this phenomenon is not universal by exhibiting braided fusion categories whose $F$-symbols cannot be made real. We call such $F$-symbols \lq\lq inherently complex." The examples we study lack a charge-conjugation symmetry and our results are therefore consistent with the converse of a statement proved in a companion work linking real $F$-symbols in braided fusion categories with the existence of a suitable charge-conjugation symmetry. We analyse the smallest-rank braided fusion categories we know of with inherently complex $F$-symbols: ${\rm Rep}(\mathbb{Z}_7\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_3)$ and ${\rm Rep}(\mathbb{Z}_5\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_4)$. Consequently, the corresponding $\mathcal Z({\rm Rep}(\mathbb{Z}_7\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_3))$ and $\mathcal Z({\rm Rep}(\mathbb{Z}_5\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_4))$ anyon models also have inherently complex $F$-symbols. Our presentation connects these examples with recent results on classifying anyons beyond modular data.

</details>


### [254] [Pinwheel-shaped bound triplet pairs in the magnetization plateaus of SrCu$_2$(BO$_3$)$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10877)
*Igor Vinograd,Philippe Corboz,Steffen Krämer,Yanan Li,Frédéric Mila,Hiroshi Kageyama,Masashi Takigawa,Mladen Horvatić*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过63,65Cu核磁共振（NMR）实验，证实了SrCu2(BO3)2中低磁化平台（1/8和2/15）由自旋-2束缚态（spin-2 bound states）的维格纳晶体（Wigner crystals）稳定，而非传统的三线态晶体或半经典上下构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SrCu2(BO3)2中观测到的1/8、2/15、1/6、1/4、1/3、2/5和1/2饱和磁化平台序列长期无法解释，基于张量网络（tensor networks）的数值模拟提示低磁化平台可能由自旋-2束缚态的维格纳晶体稳定，而非标准构型，这一假说亟需实验验证。

Method: 作者利用63,65Cu核磁共振（NMR）谱学技术，在高达41.9 T的磁场下测量了1/8和2/15平台区域的谱线，并基于1/3平台推导出的约束条件，将实验谱线与自旋-2束缚态和三线态晶体（crystal of triplets）的理论预测进行对比。

Result: 在1/8和2/15平台中，NMR谱与自旋-2束缚态的预言吻合，而与三线态晶体的预测不相容。

Conclusion: 束缚态维格纳晶体的形成可作为磁化平台理论中一种新的基本范式（fundamental paradigm），从而解释了长期悬而未决的SrCu2(BO3)2低场磁化平台序列。

Abstract: The sequence of magnetization plateaus at 1/8, 2/15, 1/6, 1/4, 1/3, 2/5, and 1/2 of the saturation observed in SrCu$_2$(BO$_3$)$_2$ remained a puzzle until tensor-networks-based numerical simulations suggested that the low-magnetization plateaus are stabilized as Wigner crystals of spin-2 bound states, and not as one of the standard configurations (semiclassical up-down, or crystals of triplets). We report on $^{63,65}$Cu nuclear magnetic resonance spectra up to 41.9 T: Based on constraints deduced from the 1/3 plateau, we show that the spectra in the 1/8 and 2/15 plateaus indeed agree with the prediction for the spin-2 bound states, while being incompatible with a crystal of triplets. This adds the formation of Wigner crystals of bound states as an alternative fundamental paradigm in the theory of magnetization plateaus.

</details>


### [255] [Generalized Keldysh formalism for nonequilibrium correlation functions and its application to fluctuation dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11055)
*Ken Inayoshi,Hiroshi Shinaoka,Yuta Murakami*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在广义Keldysh形式论中引入等时线依赖的虚拟探针场，提出了一种高效计算非平衡两粒子关联函数的方法。该方法采用基于量子张量列的线性积分方程和矩阵自由Krylov求解器，避免了显式构造四时顶点核，结合非平衡动力学平均场理论，揭示了顶点修正对非平衡对称破缺态中序参量涨落动力学的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间分辨光谱学的进展使得获取关联量子材料（correlated quantum materials）中的集体动力学成为可能，但计算相应的非平衡两粒子关联函数（nonequilibrium two-particle correlation functions）仍然是主要挑战。

Method: 在广义Keldysh形式论（generalized Keldysh formalism）中引入等时线依赖的虚拟探针场（contour-dependent virtual probe field），提出了一种包含顶点修正（vertex corrections）的计算方法。引入线性积分方程（linear integral equation）以避免显式构造四时顶点核（four-time vertex kernel），并基于量子张量列（quantics tensor trains）开发了矩阵自由Krylov求解器（matrix-free Krylov solver）。

Result: 结合非平衡动力学平均场理论（nonequilibrium dynamical mean-field theory），发现非平衡对称破缺态（nonequilibrium symmetry-broken state）中序参量的涨落动力学（fluctuation dynamics）显著依赖于是否包含顶点修正；涨落及其衰减时间在非热临界点（nonthermal critical point）附近增大。

Conclusion: 该方法为评估非平衡关联函数提供了一条实用路径，而这类函数正逐渐成为表征远离平衡态的关键观测量（key observables）。

Abstract: Recent advances in time-resolved spectroscopies provide increasing access to collective dynamics in correlated quantum materials. However, computing the corresponding nonequilibrium two-particle correlation functions remains a major challenge. Here, by introducing a contour-dependent virtual probe field within the generalized Keldysh formalism, we propose an approach that computes such correlation functions with the vertex corrections essential for describing collective dynamics. In particular, we introduce a linear integral equation that computes the correlation functions without explicitly constructing the four-time vertex kernel, and develop its matrix-free Krylov solver based on quantics tensor trains. Combining our method with nonequilibrium dynamical mean-field theory, we show that the fluctuation dynamics of the order parameter in a nonequilibrium symmetry-broken state depends significantly on whether vertex corrections are included, and that the fluctuation and its decay time grow near the nonthermal critical point. Our approach thus provides a practical route for evaluating nonequilibrium correlation functions, which are emerging as key observables for characterizing states far from equilibrium.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）为理解相变提供了现代视角，但直接获取共形代数并从微观层面揭示涌现的共形对称性（尤其在更高维度中）仍面临重大挑战。受近期通过模糊二球面揭示CFT特征进展的启发，本文旨在将该方法推广到更高维度，以暴露(3+1)维量子临界点处的共形性（conformality）。

Method: 本文通过朗道能级投影（Landau level projection）在模糊三球面（fuzzy three-sphere）上实现一个(3+1)维量子模型（等价于经典四维系统），并研究属于伊辛（Ising）和杨-李（Yang-Lee）普适类（universality classes）的量子相变。在临界点处计算能谱，以验证态-算符对应这一共形不变性（conformal invariance）的标志性特征。

Result: 在临界点处的能谱计算中，显式验证了态-算符对应关系，这是共形不变性的一个核心标志。

Conclusion: 结合先前进展，该工作为在高维相变中对涌现共形性进行微观研究建立了一条新途径。

Abstract: Conformal field theory (CFT) offers a modern viewpoint for understanding phase transitions. However, directly accessing the conformal algebra and microscopically uncovering the emergent conformal symmetry, especially in higher dimensions, remains a significant challenge. Motivated by recent advances in revealing CFT features via the fuzzy two-sphere, here we generalize this approach to higher dimensions and aim to expose the conformality at the (3+1)-D quantum critical point. We demonstrate this framework by investigating quantum phase transitions belonging to the Ising and Yang-Lee universality classes in a (3+1)-D quantum model (equivalent to a classical four-dimensional system), realized via Landau level projection on the fuzzy three-sphere. By computing the energy spectra at criticality, we explicitly verify the state-operator correspondence, a hallmark of conformal invariance. Together with prior advances, this work establishes a new pathway for the microscopic study of emergent conformality in higher-dimensional phase transitions.

### [257] [Fractionalized metals from doped anyons: Application to tMoTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11484)
*T. Senthil*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期扭曲 MoTe₂ 实验的启发，研究掺杂 σ_{xy}=2e²/3h 态后获得的金属态，旨在解释实验中观测到的高电阻率金属态的性质。

Method: 对于三种电荷为 1/3、统计角为 π/3 的任意子（anyon）构成的稀薄气体，构建了两种 U(3) 对称的 Z₃ 正交金属态；通过配对电荷 1/3 的费米子得到通常的电荷 2e 超导体。

Result: 两种 Z₃ 正交金属态由无能隙费米子变换为 SU(3) 三重态或单重态来区分；这些态即使分数量化准粒子处于良好金属区，也能自然产生大的电阻率；配对后得到的超导体可平滑连接到 BCS 态，但源于内禀分数量化的正常态。

Conclusion: 轻掺杂 2/3 态中的正常金属态可能具有分数量化电荷载流子，并讨论了相应的实验可观测信号。

Abstract: A fluid of mobile anyons may arise naturally when a Fractional Quantum Anomalous Hall (FQAH) state is doped. Motivated by recent experiments on twisted $MoTe_2$, we study metallic phases obtained by doping the $σ_{xy} = 2e^2/3h$ state. We propose that the high-resistivity metal observed adjacent to this FQAH state is a $Z_3$ Orthogonal Metal: a non-Fermi liquid with sharp charge $1/3$ fermionic quasiparticles coupled to a discrete $Z_3$ gauge field but with no sharp electronic quasiparticle. For a dilute gas of three species of charge-$1/3$ anyons with $π/3$ statistics, we construct two $U(3)$ symmetric $Z_3$ Orthogonal Metals, distinguished by whether the gapless fermions transform as $SU(3)$ triplets or singlets. We show that these states naturally yield large electrical resistivities even when the fractionalized quasiparticles are in a good metallic regime. Pairing of the charge-$1/3$ fermions produces an ordinary charge-$2e$ superconductor, smoothly connected to a BCS state but obtained through an intrinsically fractionalized normal state. We discuss experimental signatures of the idea that the normal metallic state in the lightly doped $2/3$ state may have fractionalized charge carriers.

### [258] [Stripe-Ordered Altermagnetism Emerging from Correlation-Driven Spin-Density-Wave Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11532)
*Zenghui Fan,Jingyao Meng,Tianxing Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过Hartree-Fock平均场和无偏行列式量子蒙特卡洛方法，揭示了铁基超导相关Hubbard模型中由(π,0)自旋密度波（SDW）不稳定性驱动的新型d_xy波条纹有序交变磁（SOAM）绝缘相，并通过精确有限尺寸标度证实该相在有限温度下稳定存在，将交变磁性的研究从传统反铁磁范式拓展至SDW不稳定性领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）传统上仅在共线反铁磁（collinear antiferromagnet）框架中被识别，其在自旋密度波（spin-density wave, SDW）等其他自旋不稳定性（spin instability）中的潜在实现仍是一个根本性的开放问题。本文旨在探索这一方向。

Method: 结合Hartree-Fock平均场（Hartree-Fock mean-field）方法和无偏行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo, DQMC）方法，研究一个与铁基超导（iron pnictides）相关的最小Hubbard模型（minimal Hubbard model）。

Result: 揭示了一个由关联诱导的(π,0) SDW不稳定性驱动的新型d_xy波条纹有序交变磁（stripe-ordered altermagnetic, SOAM）绝缘相。在该相中引入单轴交错电势（uniaxial staggered electric potential）可打破原有的联合时间反演与空间平移对称性（T_d T），保留联合时间反演与镜面对称性（M T），从而解锁显著的非相对论自旋分裂（nonrelativistic spin splitting）。DQMC模拟的精确有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）证实该SOAM相在有限温度下稳定存在。

Conclusion: 本研究将交变磁性的研究前沿从传统反铁磁范式拓展至SDW不稳定性领域，推进了对强关联电子系统（strongly correlated electron systems）中交变磁性的基本理解。

Abstract: Altermagnetism is conventionally identified within the paradigm of collinear antiferromagnets. Its potential realization within other spin instabilities, such as a spin-density wave (SDW), remains a fundamentally compelling open question. Here, we combine Hartree-Fock mean-field and unbiased determinant quantum Monte Carlo methods to investigate a minimal Hubbard model relevant to iron pnictides. We reveal a novel $d_{xy}$-wave stripe-ordered altermagnetic (SOAM) insulating phase driven fundamentally by the correlation-induced $(π,0)$ SDW instability. Within this phase, an introduced uniaxial staggered electric potential alters the underlying symmetry: it breaks the original combined time-reversal and spatial translation symmetry ($T_{d}\mathcal{T}$) and retains a combined time-reversal and mirror invariance ($M\mathcal{T}$), thereby unlocking the pronounced nonrelativistic spin splitting. Crucially, the exact finite-size scaling from our determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations confirms that this correlation-driven SOAM phase stably survives at accessible finite temperatures. Our study pushes the frontier of altermagnetism beyond the conventional antiferromagnetic paradigm into the realm of SDW instability, advancing the fundamental understanding of altermagnetism in strongly correlated electron systems.

### [259] [Electronic tuning of the soft-phonon transport anomaly in Ta$_2$Ni(S$_x$Se$_{1-x}$)$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11679)
*Yuan-Shan Zhang,Masahiko Isobe,Hidenori Takagi,Dennis Huang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过硫（S）替代硒（Se）调控Ta₂NiSe₅体系的能带重叠/能隙，发现软声子输运异常与电子不稳定性（如激子和杂化能隙涨落）密切相关，从而揭示了该体系中电子-空穴-晶格强相互作用的物理图景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ta₂NiSe₅在T_c=326 K处发生相变，伴随电子能隙打开和晶格畸变。热输运中观测到垂直于链方向传播的声子受到巨大各向异性散射，该现象与横声学声子软化（softening of a transverse acoustic phonon）有关，但其微观起源和物理意义尚不明确，需要进一步澄清。

Method: 利用硫（S）替代硒（Se）对Ta₂NiSe₅进行化学掺杂，调控正常态的能带重叠/能隙（band overlap/gap），系统研究软声子输运异常随S替代比例x的变化行为。

Result: 当S替代比例x较高、体系趋近于能带绝缘体（band insulator）且电子跃迁信号被抑制时，软声子输运异常也随之消失。在S端（x接近1），单一的晶格不稳定性（lattice instability）导致弱的结构相变，T_c降至约130 K；在Se端（x接近0），额外的电子不稳定性将T_c提升至326 K，并放大了相变的实验信号。

Conclusion: 建立了Ta₂Ni(S_xSe₁₋ₓ)₅体系的物理图像：电子、空穴与晶格之间的强相互作用表现为软声子输运异常，并伴随电子涨落（包括激子涨落和杂化能隙涨落）。该结果揭示了该体系中晶格自由度与电子自由度之间的深层耦合机制。

Abstract: Ta$_2$NiSe$_5$ continues to be investigated for its phase transition at $T_\textrm{c}$ = 326 K, where it develops both an electronic gap and a distortion of its Ta/Ni chains. One intriguing feature at $T_\textrm{c}$ seen in thermal transport is the giant anisotropic scattering of phonons moving perpendicular to the chains, which is apparently associated with the softening of a transverse acoustic phonon, but whose microscopic origin and significance demand clarification. By tuning the normal-state band overlap/gap with S substitution, we uncover a close connection between this soft-phonon transport anomaly and underlying electronic instabilities: When Ta$_2$Ni(S$_x$Se$_{1-x}$)$_5$ approaches a band insulator at high $x$, and signatures of the electronic transition are suppressed, the soft-phonon transport anomaly concomitantly vanishes. Our results establish the following picture for the Ta$_2$Ni(S$_x$Se$_{1-x}$)$_5$ family: Near the S end, a sole lattice instability gives rise to a weak structural transition with $T_\textrm{c}$ approaching 130 K. Near the Se end, additional electronic instabilities boost $T_\textrm{c}$ up to 326 K and amplify experimental signatures of the transition. The strong interaction between electrons, holes, and the lattice is manifested as a soft-phonon transport anomaly accompanied by electronic fluctuations, which include excitonic and hybridization-gap fluctuations.

### [260] [Statistics on Yau's conjecture: Variance asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09946)
*Michele Stecconi,Anna Paola Todino*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了紧流形上拉普拉斯特征函数节点体积的概率版本（Yau猜想），通过黎曼随机波的高频方差渐近分析，建立了节点体积波动的定量界（定理A），显著改进了已有结果，并证明了Berry相消现象在混沌流形上的发生。证明依赖于Kac-Rice公式、Wiener-Itô混沌分解以及点态Weyl定律的误差分析（定理B、C）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Yau猜想涉及紧流形上拉普拉斯特征函数节点体积的确定性下界，本文希望研究其概率对应物（probabilistic counterpart），即在高频极限下，随机波（Riemannian random waves）的节点体积（nodal volume）的波动行为。具体目标是为节点体积的方差建立定量界，并探索Berry相消现象（Berry's cancellation phenomenon）的条件。

Method: 采用局部与全局分析相结合的方法：使用Kac-Rice公式（Kac-Rice formula）处理节点体积的期望与方差；利用Stecconi和Todino（2025）新发展的Wiener-Itô混沌分解（Wiener-Itô chaos decomposition）将节点体积波动分解为不同阶的混沌分量；并结合对任意谱窗（spectral window）下点态Weyl定律（pointwise Weyl law）误差的精细分析（定理B）。在此基础上，提出一个通用机制（定理C），在满足相关衰减假设的广泛几何条件下确保方差衰减。

Result: 建立了节点体积波动的定量界（定理A），覆盖不同谱窗区间，包括单色情形（谱大小为1）。在无共轭对（conjugate pairs）的流形（特别是负曲率流形）上，该界比Canzani和Hanin（2020）的结果改进超过2次幂。作为推论，证明了Berry相消现象在此类混沌流形上的单色黎曼随机波中发生。

Conclusion: 本文在概率框架下推进了Yau猜想的研究，显著改进了现有方差界，揭示了负曲率流形上节点体积的抑制行为（Berry相消）。所发展的通用方差衰减机制（定理C）具有广泛的几何适用性，为后续研究提供了重要工具。

Abstract: We investigate the probabilistic counterpart of Yau's conjecture on the nodal volume of Laplace eigenfunctions on compact manifolds, by studying the high-frequency variance asymptotics of Riemannian random waves. We establish (Theorem A) a quantitative bound for the fluctuations of their nodal volumes, depending on different regimes of spectral windows, including the monochromatic one: with spectral size 1. Notably, our bounds improve, by more than a power 2, the existing results in the literature, cf. Canzani and Hanin (2020), in the case of manifolds without conjugate pairs, in particular negatively curved ones. As a corollary, we prove that Berry's cancellation phenomenon occurs for monochromatic Riemannian Random Waves on such chaotic manifolds. Our proofs rely on a local and global analysis combining the Kac-Rice formula, the new Wiener-Itô chaos decompositions of Stecconi and Todino (2025), and a sharp analysis of the error in the pointwise Weyl law associated to arbitrary spectral window (Theorem B). We introduce a general machinery (Theorem C), which ensures variance decay under broad geometric conditions, subject to correlation decay assumptions.

### [261] [Dynamical mean-field limit and replica-symmetric free energy for the orthogonally-invariant SK model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10102)
*Zhou Fan,Theodor Misiakiewicz,Leda Wang,Garrett G. Wen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类由对称矩阵 $X\in\mathbb{R}^{n\times n}$ 相互作用的扩散过程，当 $X$ 的特征向量在正交群上为 Haar 均匀分布时，推导了样本路径经验律的动态平均场极限（dynamical mean-field limit），推广了经典的 Sompolinsky–Zippelius 刻画。极限为带有相关高斯噪声和记忆的广义 Langevin 方程，其相关核与响应核通过自由累积量（free cumulants）与原始动力学相关联。针对过阻尼 Langevin 扩散，在快速混合假设下分析了平均场极限，证明了相关核与响应核具有时间平移不变性并满足涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）。该广义 Langevin 方程可通过一个辅助多元 OU 过程获得马尔可夫近似，并收敛到副本对称（replica-symmetric）的预测。自由能在显式高温条件下收敛到副本对称极限，对于 Ising 模型条件为 $\|X\|_{\mathrm{op}}<1/2$。基于近期动力学普适性结果，当 $X$ 满足一组确定性离域条件时，同一自由能刻画对无随机无序的确定性模型同样成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究由对称矩阵 $X$ 耦合的高维扩散过程，旨在建立其动态平均场极限理论，并将经典的 Sompolinsky–Zippelius 刻画从高斯正交系综（GOE）推广到更广泛的特征向量 Haar 均匀分布情形，从而理解非高斯随机矩阵以及确定性矩阵下此类系统的集体动力学行为。

Method: 从特征向量在正交群上 Haar 均匀分布的对称矩阵 $X$ 出发，推导样本路径经验律的动力学平均场极限，得到广义 Langevin 方程；对过阻尼 Langevin 扩散在快速混合假设下分析相关/响应核的时间平移不变性和涨落-耗散关系；通过辅助多元 OU 过程实现马尔可夫近似，并利用无穷小生成元刻画路径历史过程的提升半群；最后应用近期动力学普适性结果将结论推广到确定性离域矩阵情形。

Result: 得到了一个带有相关高斯噪声和记忆的广义 Langevin 方程作为平均场极限，其相关核与响应核通过 $X$ 特征值分布的 free cumulants 与原始动力学耦合。过阻尼情形下相关核与响应核具有时间平移不变近似并满足涨落-耗散关系，广义 Langevin 方程可被一个耦合多元 OU 过程的马尔可夫近似所逼近，经验坐标律收敛到副本对称预测。自由能在显式高温条件（Ising 模型为 $\|X\|_{\mathrm{op}}<1/2$）下收敛到副本对称极限，且该刻画对满足确定性离域条件的非随机模型同样成立。

Conclusion: 本文建立了特征向量均匀分布对称矩阵耦合扩散过程的动态平均场理论，给出了自由能的副本对称极限及其显式高温条件，并通过动力学普适性将结果推广到确定性离域矩阵模型，表明该平均场行为具有一定普适性。

Abstract: We study a class of diffusion processes on $\mathbb{R}^n$ interacting through a symmetric matrix $X\in\mathbb{R}^{n\times n}$. When eigenvectors of $X$ are Haar-uniform on the orthogonal group, we derive a dynamical mean-field limit for the empirical law of sample paths, extending the classical Sompolinsky--Zippelius characterization for $X\sim\mathrm{GOE}$. The limit takes the form of a generalized Langevin equation with correlated Gaussian noise and memory, whose correlation and response kernels relate to those of the original dynamics through convolution equations involving the free cumulants of the eigenvalue distribution of $X$.
  For the overdamped Langevin diffusion associated with $μ(\boldsymbolθ)\propto \exp\!\big(\frac12\boldsymbolθ^{\top}X\boldsymbolθ\big)\prod_{i=1}^nν(\mathrm{d}θ_i)$, we analyze the mean-field limit under a rapid-mixing assumption. The correlation and response kernels admit time-translation-invariant approximants satisfying a fluctuation-dissipation relation. The generalized Langevin equation admits a Markovian approximation coupled to an auxiliary multivariate OU process and converges to a replica-symmetric prediction for the empirical coordinate law under $μ$. This auxiliary correlation structure is characterized through the infinitesimal generator of a Markov semigroup for the lifted path-history process.
  Consequently, the free energy converges to a replica-symmetric limit under an explicit high-temperature condition, which for an Ising model is $\|X\|_{\mathrm{op}}<1/2$. By recent dynamical universality results, the same free-energy characterization holds for deterministic models without random disorder when $X$ satisfies a set of deterministic delocalization conditions.

</details>


### [262] [The four-dimensional Anderson model: a case study for critical SPDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10105)
*Yu Deng,Hao Shen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维环面上带有空间白噪声的弱耦合椭圆Anderson模型，证明了其随机Schrödinger算子的Green函数在适当中心化和缩放后收敛到一个具有显式协方差的高斯随机场，并为此发展了一套基于新版本Hepp树和多尺度分析的截断重正规化参数化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型是需要在任意高阶进行重整化（renormalization）的临界随机偏微分方程（critical SPDE）的基本例子，其扰动展开包含阶乘数量级的配对和快速增长的重整化项，传统方法难以处理。

Method: 构造截断重正规化参数解（truncated renormalized parametrix）并证明其余项的高阶界；基于新版本Hepp树（Hepp trees）进行多尺度分析（multiscale analysis），结合对置换求和（summations over permutations）的新估计，利用尺度求和中的对数损失与原始配对结构中的阶乘增益之间的精确平衡。

Result: 在耦合常数取为λ|log ε|^{-1/2}且λ>0足够小的条件下，证明了适当中心化和缩放后的Green函数收敛到一个中心高斯随机场，并给出了显式的协方差结构。

Conclusion: 本文方法为建立弱耦合临界随机偏微分方程的一般理论迈出了第一步。

Abstract: We study the weakly coupled elliptic Anderson model with spatial white noise on the four-dimensional torus, which provides a basic example of a critical SPDE requiring renormalization at arbitrarily high orders. With coupling $λ|\log\varepsilon|^{-\frac12}$ where $λ>0$ is sufficiently small, we prove that the Green's function of the corresponding random Schrödinger operator, suitably centered and rescaled, converges to a centered Gaussian random field with explicit covariance.
  The main difficulty is that, for such critical models, one must expand up to order $|\log\varepsilon|$, while the perturbative expansion contains factorially many pairings and a growing number of renormalization terms. To overcome this, we construct a truncated renormalized parametrix and prove sharp high-order bounds for its remainder. A central ingredient is a multiscale analysis based on a new version of Hepp trees, combined with new estimates for summations over permutations. These estimates reveal a precise balance between logarithmic losses from scale summation and factorial gains from the structure of primitive pairings. The methods developed here are intended as a first step toward a general theory for critical SPDEs with weak couplings.

</details>


### [263] [From the Airy line ensemble to the Gaussian free field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10725)
*Evgeni Dimitrov,Alex Fu,Zhengye Zhou*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究 Airy 线集（Airy line ensemble）关联高度函数的全局涨落，通过行列式结构和最速下降法证明：在适当标度下，中心化高度函数依联合矩收敛到高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）的一个显式拉回（pullback）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索 Airy 线集高度函数的大尺度全局涨落行为，揭示其与高斯自由场之间的精确关联。

Method: 利用 Airy 点过程的行列式结构（determinantal structure），对扩展 Airy 核（extended Airy kernel）实施最速下降分析（steepest-descent analysis）。

Result: 经过合适的重标度（rescaling）后，中心化的高度函数收敛到高斯自由场的显式拉回；该收敛在紧支撑连续测试函数（compactly supported continuous test functions）的线性统计量的联合矩（joint moments）意义下成立。

Conclusion: Airy 线集高度函数的大尺度全局涨落可由高斯自由场精确刻画，建立了可积概率与高斯自由场之间的桥梁。

Abstract: We study the global fluctuations of the height function associated with the Airy line ensemble. Using its determinantal structure and a steepest-descent analysis of the extended Airy kernel, we prove that, after a suitable rescaling, the centered height function converges to an explicit pullback of the Gaussian free field. The convergence holds in the sense of joint moments of linear statistics against compactly supported continuous test functions.

</details>


### [264] [Phase transition for weakly interacting focusing Gibbs measures with harmonic potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11608)
*Damiano Greco,Yuzhao Wang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究聚焦非线性薛定谔方程（focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation）在调和势（harmonic potential）与临界非线性（critical nonlinearity）下、耦合常数趋于零时的吉布斯测度（Gibbs measure）问题。在一维及高维（径向对称假设）情形下，确定了频率截断测度收敛到基态高斯测度（base Gaussian measure）的临界阈值，并在超临界区域证明了非收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该问题最初由 Brydges-Slade（1996）针对环面 $\mathbb{T}^2$ 上的 $\Phi^4_2$ 模型提出，本文将其推广到欧氏空间上的聚焦非线性薛定谔方程，以探索临界标度下吉布斯测度的存在性与收敛性。

Method: 采用频率截断（frequency truncation）方法构造近似测度，通过设定临界阈值区分亚临界与超临界区域，并在一维及高维（径向假设）情形下分别分析截断测度的收敛行为。

Result: 在一维和高维（径向对称）情形下，亚临界区域中频率截断测度收敛到基态高斯测度（可能带有重整化 $L^2$ 截断）；超临界区域中，即使考虑子序列，频率截断测度也不收敛。

Conclusion: 明确了聚焦非线性薛定谔方程在调和势与临界非线性下吉布斯测度收敛性的临界阈值，揭示了亚临界与超临界区域截然不同的收敛行为，为理解该类系统的统计力学性质提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the Gibbs measures on Euclidean spaces associated to the focusing nonlinear Schrödinger equation with harmonic potential and critical non linearity whose coupling constant tends to 0, a question initially posed by Brydges-Slade (1996) for the $Φ^4_2$-model on $\mathbb{T}^2$. In dimension one and in the higher dimensional cases (with radial assumption), we establish a critical threshold below which the frequency-truncated measures converge to the base Gaussian measure (possibly with a renormalized $L^2$ cut-off) while, in the supercritical regime, we prove non-convergence of the frequency-truncated measures, even up to a subsequence.

</details>

### [265] [Axion Generation in a Three-Dimensional Optical Trap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11589)
*Chunyu Zhang,Xinran Fang,Lichen Peng,Xuri Yao,Xiaoying Tang*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文设计并构建了一种基于激光的光学纺锤阱（optical spindle trap, OST），在自由空间中实现了类似“光穿墙实验”（LSW）中的光子-轴子-光子转换过程。通过监测光子数亏损并将超低光功率下的信号与单光子计数器和CCD成像互证，缺失的光子被归因于自旋耦合的轴子-光子相互作用转化为不可探测的轴子（axion），从而提供了一个桌面级自由空间轴子源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子（axion）是可能同时解释量子色动力学中的强CP问题（strong CP problem）与暗物质（dark matter）本质的理论粒子，但至今尚未在任何自由空间实验中被直接探测到。本研究旨在通过构建一种新型光学势阱，在自由空间中实现并验证光子-轴子转换过程，为轴子的实验研究提供可行方案。

Method: 本文设计并构建了一套基于激光的系统，生成了一个具有零中心区域的三维封闭俘获势场（trapping potential field），因其纺锤状几何结构被称为光学纺锤阱（optical spindle trap, OST）。沿传播轴方向，光子数分布从左端到右端先减少后恢复至基线值，该行为类似于光穿墙实验（light shining through wall, LSW）中的光子-轴子-光子转换过程。光子数使用工作于远低于饱和阈值下的单光子计数器（single-photon counter, SPC）监测，并在极低光功率下通过电荷耦合器件（charge-coupled device, CCD）成像进行交叉验证，以排除探测器伪影。

Result: 在光学纺锤阱中观测到了光子数先减少后恢复的现象，并且通过SPC和CCD两种独立探测手段排除了探测器伪影的干扰。在能量守恒约束下，缺失的光子被归因于通过自旋耦合的轴子-光子相互作用（spin-coupled axion photon interactions）转化为无法被SPC和CCD探测到的轴子。

Conclusion: 该毫米级光学纺锤阱提供了一种由桌面激光器产生的可行自由空间轴子源，可用于研究强CP问题以及轴子类暗物质候选粒子。这一工作为在实验室环境中直接产生和研究轴子开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The axion is a theoretical particle that could resolve multiple fundamental problems, most notably the strong Charge-conjugation-parity-symmetry (CP) problem in quantum chromodynamics and the nature of dark matter.To date, however, the axion has never been detected in any free-space experiment. In this work, we designed and constructed a laser-based system that generates a three-dimensional, closed trapping potential field with a null central region. Owing to its spindle-like geometry, we term this configuration an optical spindle trap (OST). Along the propagation axis, the photon population evolves in a distinct manner from the left to the right terminus of the trap: it first diminishes and then recovers to its baseline value.This behavior is analogous to the photon axion photon conversion process sought in light shining through wall experiments(LSW)1-3, in which a measured photon deficit would constitute evidence for axion conversion. The photon population was monitored with a single-photon counter (SPC) operated well below its saturation threshold, and the observed behavior was corroborated by charge-coupled device (CCD) imaging at extremely low optical powers, thereby excluding detector artefacts as the origin of the photon deficit.Under the constraint of energy conservation, the missing photons are attributed to conversion into axions that remain undetectable by both the SPC and the CCD. The underlying conversion mechanism is ascribed to spin-coupled axion photon interactions. This tens-of-millimeter-scale optical spindle trap thus provides a viable free-space axion source, generated by a table-top laser, for the study of the strong CP problem and axion-like dark matter candidates.

</details>


### [266] [Fourth-order Optoelectronic Response from Cascaded Circular Photogalvanic and Nonlinear Hall Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10012)
*Bhupendra Sharma,Sobhit Singh*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一种由圆光生伏打效应（CPGE）与贝里曲率偶极子（BCD）耦合产生的四阶非线性光电响应机制；以单层Td-WTe₂为原型，该机制在中红外光激发下产生级联光电压，其强度正比于光场四次方（E₀⁴），并通过调控光几何结构（如入射角）可实现超过两个数量级的信号增强，为探测量子几何与实现拓扑光电探测器及倍频器提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非线性光学跃迁与拓扑能带结构之间的耦合关系，以实现对光电流的有效控制，并寻找超越传统二阶非线性效应的新型量子光电响应。

Method: 基于单层Td-WTe₂作为原型材料，通过理论计算完整映射注入电流张量，分析圆光生伏打效应（CPGE）与贝里曲率偶极子（BCD）的级联耦合过程，并引入振幅调制锁相探测方案以分离线性Drude背景的干扰。

Result: 级联光电压正比于光场四次方（E₀⁴）；正常入射驱动面内共振分量Im(η_{yxy})，而45°斜入射激活主导的面外分量Im(η_{yyz})，信号增强两个数量级以上（约10² μV）；振幅调制结合锁相探测可有效隔离频率倍频的级联响应。

Conclusion: 该机制将中红外光转换为栅压可调的横向电信号，为探测量子几何（quantum geometry）、构建拓扑光电探测器（topological photodetectors）和频率倍频器（frequency doublers）提供了可行途径。

Abstract: The interplay between nonlinear optical transitions and topological band structure offers a route to control photocurrents. We reveal a fourth-order optoelectronic response that emerges due to an interlink between the circular photogalvanic effect (CPGE) and the Berry curvature dipole (BCD) in noncentrosymmetric 2D materials. Using monolayer $\Td$-WTe$_2$ as a prototype, we predict that circularly polarized mid-infrared light produces a steady dc injection current that induces an internal electric field, which in turn drives a transverse nonlinear Hall response through BCD. The resulting cascaded photovoltage scales as the fourth power of the optical field $E_0^4$. By mapping the full injection current tensor, we show that this cascaded voltage is strongly tunable by the optical geometry: normal incidence drives an in-plane resonance $\mathrm{Im}(η_{yxy})$, whereas oblique illumination ($θ= 45^{\circ}$) recruits a dominant out-of-plane component $\mathrm{Im}(η_{yyz})$ and amplifies the signal by more than two orders of magnitude (${\sim}10^2~μ$V). While the massive linear Drude background typically screens nonlinear responses in semimetals, we argue that the amplitude modulation of the optical pump allows lock-in detection to cleanly isolate the frequency-doubled cascaded response. The proposed mechanism converts mid-infrared light into a gate-tunable transverse signal, providing a route for probing quantum geometry and realizing topological photodetectors and frequency doublers.

### [267] [Three-dimensional excitonic dipole anisotropy enables ultrabroadband polarization photodetection in CrCl3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10752)
*Satyam Sahu,Jaganandha Panda,Martin Jindra,Mukesh Kumar Thakur,Farjana J. Sonia,Shankar Khanal,Kornelius Nielsch,Jana Vejpravova,Matěj Velický,Martin Kalbáč,Otakar Frank,Golam Haider*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文证明层状绝缘体 CrCl₃ 的本征介电各向异性可实现 300–1700 nm 超宽带偏振分辨光电探测；光响应由长寿命配体场激子主导（微秒级寿命、光电导增益 >4.5×10⁴），通过波长、偏振和角度分辨测量揭示不同激子跃迁具有不同光学偶极取向，导致面内偏振轴的激发能量依赖旋转；倾斜光照激活面外光偶极，竞争性跃迁驱动偏振各向异性的波长依赖旋转与反转，最终实现 -90% 至 +75% 的高度可调偏振度，建立了层状磁性范德华绝缘体中的三维矢量光-物质相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同时检测光谱与偏振特性的光探测在集成成像和光子技术中非常理想，但通常需要复杂多组件架构；本文旨在探索利用本征介电各向异性实现超宽带偏振分辨光电探测的简化途径。

Method: 利用层状绝缘体 CrCl₃ 的本征介电各向异性；结合波长分辨（wavelength-resolved）、偏振分辨（polarization-resolved）和角度分辨（angle-resolved）光电子测量来系统表征光响应特性。

Result: 在 300–1700 nm 超宽波段实现偏振分辨光探测；观察到光电导增益超过 4.5×10⁴；发现不同激子跃迁具有不同光学偶极取向，导致面内偏振轴的旋转和偏振各向异性在波长依赖下的反转；倾斜光照激活面外光偶极；实现了从 -90% 到 +75% 的高度可调偏振度。

Conclusion: 介电各向异性和激子偶极工程（excitonic dipole engineering）可作为紧凑型超宽带偏振敏感光探测器和多功能范德华光子系统的强大设计原理；该工作建立了层状磁性范德华绝缘体中的三维矢量光-物质相互作用。

Abstract: Simultaneous detection of the spectral and polarization properties of light is highly desirable for integrated imaging and photonic technologies but typically requires complex multi-component architectures. Here, we demonstrate that the intrinsic dielectric anisotropy of layered insulating CrCl3 enables ultrabroadband polarization-resolved photodetection spanning wavelengths from 300 to 1700 nm. The photoresponse is governed by long-lived ligand-field excitons, whose microsecond-scale lifetime produces a photoconductive gain exceeding 4.5 x 10^4. By combining wavelength-, polarization-, and angle-resolved optoelectronic measurements, we reveal that distinct ligand-field and higher-energy excitonic transitions possess different optical dipole orientations, leading to excitation-energy-dependent rotation of the in-plane polarization axis. Furthermore, oblique illumination activates out-of-plane optical dipoles, while competing excitonic transitions with distinct dipole orientations drive wavelength-dependent rotation and reversal of the polarization anisotropy. Together, these effects produce a highly tunable degree of polarization ranging from -90% to +75%, establishing intrinsic three-dimensional vectorial light-matter interactions in a layered magnetic van der Waals insulator. These findings establish dielectric anisotropy and excitonic dipole engineering as powerful design principles for compact ultrabroadband polarization-sensitive photodetectors and multifunctional van der Waals photonic systems.

### [268] [NaBiF$_4$: Er$^{3+}$, Yb$^{3+}$ upconversion particle as a multi-functional bio-marker](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11522)
*Atanu Ghosh,Krishna Kumari Swain,Agniva Das,Mrutyunjaya Rath,Snigdhadev Chakraborty,Bipeen Kumar,Yamini Selvam,Siddharth Dhomkar,Basudev Roy*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报告了铋掺杂上转换粒子（bismuth-doped UCPs）相比常规钇掺杂UCPs在量子产率和红光发射上分别提升3倍和4倍，并利用975 nm和1064 nm双红外波长选择性调控光致发光（PL），实现了亚衍射厚度、光学捕获和表面功能化，为高信噪比亚衍射成像提供了新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有镧系掺杂上转换粒子（UCPs）虽在生物成像中具有优异的光稳定性、低毒性和近红外激发优势，但在高噪声生物介质中实现高对比度和亚衍射成像仍面临挑战，且需避免使用高功率激光器。

Method: 研究制备了铋掺杂UCPs，采用975 nm和1064 nm双红外波长协议选择性调控光致发光（PL），并通过简化的受激发射耗尽（stimulated emission depletion, STED）三能级模型描述PL调控动力学。

Result: 铋掺杂UCPs的整体量子产率较常规钇掺杂UCPs提升3倍，其中红光发射提升4倍；通过调节975 nm激光功率可系统性地淬灭或增强PL，且粒子具有亚衍射厚度和光学捕获能力。

Conclusion: 铋掺杂UCPs在提高信噪比和实现亚衍射成像方面表现出优异潜力，可用于先进生物标志物操作。

Abstract: Lanthanide-doped upconversion particles (UCPs) have revolutionized optical bioimaging platforms because of their excellent photostability, non-toxicity, and utilization of near-infrared excitation, which facilitates deep tissue penetration with negligible autofluorescence. However, it remains a challenge to achieve high-contrast and sub-diffraction imaging in noisy biological media, without using a high-power laser. Here, we report various protocols applied to bismuth-doped UCPs address some of these challenges. Compared to the photoluminescence (PL) emission of the regular Yttrium doped UCPs, we observe a three-fold increment in the quantum yield of the overall emission of bismuth-UCPs, and a four-fold increment, specifically, in red emission. Leveraging this advantage, we devise a protocol employing two infrared wavelengths, 975 nm and 1064 nm, to selectively control the PL emission. Interestingly, our results reveal two distinct regimes in which PL can be systematically quenched or enhanced, by adjusting the 975 nm laser power. We model the overall dynamics as a simplified stimulated emission depletion process involving three energy levels. In addition, the particle has a thickness under sub-diffraction, shows optical trapping ability, and potential of surface functionalization to enable specific conjugation with diverse biospecimens. These studies establish bismuth doped UCPs as an excellent candidate in accomplishing advanced biomarker operating with enhanced signal-to-noise ratio and sub-diffraction imaging capabilities.

</details>
