### [269] [Spacetime from Entanglement: The Emergence of Metric, Gravity, or Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09823)
*Rasmus Jaksland*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了AdS/CFT对偶中“时空从纠缠涌现”这一表述实际上包含三种不同的涌现主张（度量、引力动力学和拓扑连通性），并检验它们是否满足涌现的两个必要条件——决定性（determination）和新颖性（novelty），结论是三种主张均不满足决定性条件，且仅有引力动力学满足新颖性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AdS/CFT对偶中常见“时空从纠缠涌现”的说法，但这类笼统表述可能掩盖了不同涌现主张之间的本质差异。本文旨在厘清这些主张各自指向的时空方面，并检验它们是否满足涌现的哲学必要条件。

Method: 论文将“时空从纠缠涌现”这一笼统主张拆解为三个不同的涌现主张，分别对应度量（metric）、引力动力学（gravitational dynamics）和拓扑连通性（topological connectivity）。随后采用哲学分析框架，检验每个主张是否满足涌现的两个必要条件：决定性（即涌现基础是否充分决定涌现物）和新颖性（即涌现物相对于涌现基础是否具有新颖性）。

Result: 三种涌现主张均不满足决定性条件，因为仅靠纠缠（entanglement）不足以构成完备的涌现基础。对于体度规（bulk metric），涌现基础还需包含边界上的诱导度规（induced metric）；对于拓扑连通性，涌现基础本身似乎已包含连通性概念。因此，度规和拓扑连通性的涌现主张也存疑。仅引力动力学在完备的涌现基础之上表现出新颖性。

Conclusion: 尽管三种涌现主张指向相似方向，但它们关注的是不同的时空方面，不能简单归为支持同一结论的证据。纠缠是涌现的重要成分，但并非充分条件；只有引力动力学在完备涌现基础上满足新颖性条件，而度规和拓扑连通性的涌现主张在哲学意义上是有问题的。

Abstract: In AdS/CFT, one often finds claims along the lines that ``spacetime emerges from entanglement." This paper argues that behind these general statements hide three distinct emergence claims about, respectively, metric, gravitational dynamics, and topological connectivity. Thus, despite being advertised with the same terminology, these results are not about the same spatiotemporal aspects. They can therefore not just be grouped as evidence for one unanimous conclusion, though they do point in similar directions. The paper also investigates whether the three emergence claims satisfy two of the necessary conditions for emergence: Determination and novelty. The paper argues that none of the emergence claims satisfies the determination condition: More than entanglement is needed to furnish the emergence basis. Besides entanglement, the emergence basis for the bulk metric must include the induced metric on the boundary. Thus, this claim might not satisfy the novelty condition for emergence that the emergent should be novel as compared to the emergence basis. Likewise, the emergence basis for topological connectivity seems to include connectivity whereby this emergence claim is also questionable. The paper concludes that only gravitational dynamics is novel compared to the fully furnished emergence basis.

</details>


### [270] [Cosmology: 100 years after A. A. Friedmann](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11791)
*A. F. Zakharov*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本论文回顾了弗里德曼（A. A. Friedmann）在1920年代提出的首个物理宇宙学模型（cosmological models），并指出尽管其工作发表后很快闻名，但在1930至1960年代的苏联，动态宇宙模型的研究实际上被禁止，原因是苏联哲学界和宣传界将其曲解为与圣经创世论相似的宗教观点，导致弗里德曼的工作在苏联长期被遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示弗里德曼的早期宇宙学贡献在苏联因意识形态原因被压制和遗忘的历史事实，旨在还原科学史上的这一非学术干预事件。

Method: 基于历史文献与史料分析，梳理弗里德曼宇宙学模型提出后的学术影响及在苏联被禁止的历史过程。

Result: 研究发现，弗里德曼的动态宇宙模型在1930至1960年代的苏联遭遇意识形态打压，苏联哲学家和宣传者将其错误地归因于莱梅特（Lemaître）应罗马教皇要求而提出，并类比为圣经式的神创论。

Conclusion: 弗里德曼的工作在苏联从1930年代至1960年代长期处于被遗忘状态，体现了政治与意识形态对科学传播的严重干扰。

Abstract: A. A. Friedmann (04.06.1888 -- 16.09.1925) proposed the first physical cosmological models in 1920s. Despite the fact that Friedmann's works were very famous soon after their publication, the study of dynamic models of the Universe in the USSR was actually banned in the 30s - 50s of the last century, and Soviet philosophers and propagandists wrote that models of the evolving Universe were invented by Lemaitre on the demand of the Roman Pope, because according to Soviet philosophers such the birth of the universe is very similar to the divine creation of the world described in the Bible. Thus, in the USSR, Friedman's works were in oblivion in since 1930s until 1960s.

</details>

### [271] [Structure-preserving variational neural fields: Uncertainty-quantified reduced-order modeling of nonlinear conservation laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10965)
*Aviral Prakash,Marc L. Klasky*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种变分潜在神经场框架（variational latent neural field framework），通过集成高斯过程启发代理（Gaussian process-inspired surrogates）实现预测不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）与守恒律精确保持（exact conservation-law preservation），并给出了无约束、物理信息约束和守恒结构保持三种变体。数值实验表明该方法在提供准确预测和不确定性估计的同时，对稀疏和含噪训练数据具有良好的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的降阶模型（reduced-order models，如潜在动力学模型）在加速非线性守恒律参数化物理系统模拟方面已取得进展，但大多数框架存在两个关键局限：无法提供模型预测的不确定性估计（uncertainty estimates），也不能保证遵守底层守恒律（conservation laws）。尽管这两个问题在已有工作中被分别讨论，但尚缺乏一个能够同时提供不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）和精确守恒律保持的统一框架。

Method: 开发了一个变分潜在神经场框架（variational latent neural field framework），该框架集成高斯过程启发代理以估计预测置信度。框架包含三种变体：IRS-UQ（无约束）、PI-IRS-UQ（物理信息约束）和 ECLEIRS-UQ（守恒结构保持）。精确的守恒结构保持通过将解动力学嵌入守恒律流形（conservation-law manifold）实现，具体通过解-通量场的时空散度自由表示（space-time divergence-free representation）。

Result: 通过三个数值实验（1-D平流方程、2-D欧拉方程、2-D浅水方程的参量化设置）验证了框架的适用性。该方法在提供准确预测和不确定性估计的同时，对稀疏和含噪训练数据具有鲁棒性。三种方法比较表明，守恒结构保持潜在表示（conservation-structure preserving latent representations）在训练数据退化时能提升鲁棒性，同时保持具有竞争力的预测精度和不确定性量化能力。

Conclusion: 该变分潜在神经场框架成功统一了不确定性量化与守恒律精确保持两大目标，填补了此前缺乏统一框架的研究空白；其中守恒结构保持变体在训练数据退化场景下表现最优。

Abstract: Reduced-order models, such as latent dynamics models, are becoming mainstream for accelerating simulations for parameterized physical systems governed by nonlinear conservation laws. However, most existing latent dynamics frameworks suffer from two important limitations: they do not provide uncertainty estimates for model predictions, and they do not guarantee adherence to the underlying conservation laws. While these challenges have been addressed separately in prior work, a unified framework that simultaneously provides uncertainty quantification and exact conservation-law preservation remains largely unexplored. In this work, we develop a variational latent neural field framework that integrates Gaussian process-inspired surrogates, enabling estimation of predictive confidence for both in-distribution and out-of-distribution parameter regimes. Three variants of the framework are considered: IRS-UQ, PI-IRS-UQ, and ECLEIRS-UQ, corresponding to unconstrained, physics-informed, and conservation-structure-preserving formulations, respectively. Exact conservation-structure preservation is achieved by embedding the solution dynamics within a conservation-law manifold through a space-time divergence-free representation of the solution-flux field. We demonstrate the applicability of the framework through three numerical experiments: 1) 1-D advection, 2) 2-D Euler and 3) 2-D shallow water equations in parameterized settings. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the proposed approach provides accurate predictions together with uncertainty estimates, while remaining robust to sparse and noisy training data. Comparisons between the proposed three approaches show that conservation-structure preserving latent representations improve robustness to degraded training data while maintaining competitive predictive accuracy and uncertainty quantification capability.

</details>


### [272] [Uncertainty-Aware Structure-Property Mapping of Spinodoid Metamaterials via Heteroscedastic Gaussian Process Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11209)
*Minwoo Park,Junseo Park,Mingyu Lee,Hugon Lee,Hanbin Cho,Ikjin Lee,Seunghwa Ryu*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种不确定性感知的结构-性能映射框架，将spinodoid超材料（spinodoid metamaterials）的锥角描述符（cone-angle descriptors）重新解释为与输入相关性能分布（input-dependent property distributions）相关联的随机描述符（stochastic descriptors），并通过异方差高斯过程回归（heteroscedastic Gaussian process regression, GPR）从稀疏数据中推断预测不确定性，进而证明该框架是进行可靠性感知逆向设计（reliability-aware inverse design）的必要工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spinodoid超材料的结构-性能关系通常被视为从锥角描述符到单一有效刚度值的确定性映射，但这忽略了基于高斯随机场（Gaussian random field, GRF）的拓扑生成中固有的随机性——相同的锥角描述符可能产生不同的形态实现（morphology realization）和性能散布（property scatter）。因此需要建立不确定性感知的映射框架。

Method: 采用异方差高斯过程回归（heteroscedastic GPR）框架，从每个设计点仅有一个实现（one-realization-per-point）的稀疏数据中推断输入相关的预测不确定性，无需在每个设计点处获取经验方差标签。将锥角描述符重新解释为与输入相关的性能分布相关联的随机描述符。

Result: 刚度散布在不同张量分量（tensor components）上存在差异，取决于各分量的力学活跃方向（mechanically active directions）。产生相同平均刚度的参数集可携带不同的偶然不确定性（aleatoric uncertainty）。确定性最优解在考虑形态诱导变异性后极易违反约束；同方差（homoscedastic）的基于可靠性的设计优化（RBDO）无法达到给定可靠性目标，而异方差（heteroscedastic）RBDO配方能够满足该目标。

Conclusion: 不确定性感知的代理建模（uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling）是实现spinodoid超材料可靠性感知逆向设计（reliability-aware inverse design）的必要基础。将该框架扩展至非线性响应（nonlinear responses）是未来工作方向。

Abstract: Spinodoid metamaterials offer a broad, tunable design space for anisotropic mechanical properties, yet their structure-property relationships are commonly treated as representative mappings from cone-angle descriptors to single effective stiffness values. This deterministic view overlooks the stochastic nature of Gaussian random field (GRF)-based topology generation, where identical cone-angle descriptors can produce different morphology realizations and property scatter. Here, we present an uncertainty-aware structure-property mapping framework that reinterprets cone-angle descriptors as stochastic descriptors associated with input-dependent property distributions. Using heteroscedastic Gaussian process regression (GPR), the framework infers input-dependent predictive uncertainty from sparse one-realization-per-point data without requiring empirical variance labels at every design point. The results show that stiffness scatter differs across tensor components according to each component's mechanically active directions, and that parameter sets yielding identical mean stiffness can carry different aleatoric uncertainty. Applying this uncertainty to reliability-based design optimization (RBDO), we show that a deterministic optimum is highly susceptible to constraint violation once morphology-induced variability is considered, and that a homoscedastic RBDO formulation fails to meet the prescribed reliability target - only the heteroscedastic formulation satisfies the reliability target under the heteroscedastic uncertainty evaluation. This establishes uncertainty-aware surrogate modeling as essential for reliability-aware inverse design of spinodoid metamaterials; extending the framework to nonlinear responses remains for future work.

</details>

### [273] [The Lorentzian geometry of relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10148)
*Lorenzo Gavassino*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文发现具有纯粹弛豫型激发谱的相对论性理论（如动理学理论和瞬态流体力学）在色散平面 $\{iω,ik\}$ 上天然具有类似于闵可夫斯基平面 $\{t,x\}$ 的洛伦兹几何结构，从而将因果性、稳定性等物理约束转化为几何问题，并导出了一系列普适约束和物理推论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性物质中的因果关系、稳定性与色散关系之间存在深刻关联，但长期以来缺乏统一的几何化视角。本文旨在揭示弛豫型相对论理论中色散平面内在的洛伦兹几何结构，将复杂物理问题转化为直观的几何问题。

Method: 通过识别色散平面 $\{iω,ik\}$ 与闵可夫斯基时空平面 $\{t,x\}$ 之间的结构类比，定义类时未来方向、类时过去方向和类空间方向，分别对应弛豫型（relaxation-like）、不稳定型（unstable-like）和消逝型（evanescent-like）模式。在此基础上，利用因果性要求将色散关系约束为类空轨迹，并借助几何方法进行分析。

Result: 推导了色散关系的普适约束、时间膨胀（time dilation）的偏离、谱层级（spectral hierarchies）的观测者依赖性、流体力学在 boosted 参考系中的有效区域、相对论性介质中最大允许的扩散率和黏度，以及动理学理论中非流体力学分支割线（non-hydrodynamic branch cuts）的存在性。

Conclusion: 该几何观点将相对论性物质物理中的若干长期问题归结为基本几何问题，并可图形化求解，为理解和约束相对论性体系的因果性与稳定性提供了简洁统一的框架。

Abstract: We show that relativistic theories with purely relaxational excitation spectra, such as kinetic theory and transient hydrodynamics, naturally endow the dispersion plane $\{iω,ik\}$ with a Lorentzian geometric structure analogous to that of the Minkowski plane $\{t,x\}$. In this picture, timelike future-directed, timelike past-directed, and spacelike directions correspond respectively to relaxation-like, unstable-like, and evanescent-like modes. Under mild structural assumptions on the underlying theory, causality constrains dispersion relations to follow spacelike trajectories on the plane. This geometric viewpoint recasts longstanding problems in relativistic matter physics as elementary geometric ones that can often be solved graphically. As applications, we derive universal constraints on dispersion relations, deviations from time dilation, the observer dependence of spectral hierarchies, the regime of validity of hydrodynamics in boosted frame, the maximal allowed diffusivity and viscosity of relativistic media, and the presence of non-hydrodynamic branch cuts in kinetic theory.

</details>

### [274] [Data-efficient continuous conditional denoising diffusion model for microstructure generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10429)
*Tarakram Ramgopal,Gowtham Nimmal Haribabu,Hussein Farahani,Cornelis Bos,Siddhant Kumar*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 提出了一种连续条件去噪扩散模型（continuous conditional denoising diffusion model），结合邻近损失训练策略（vicinal-loss training strategy），在紧凑数据集上实现基于连续工艺参数的微观结构高效生成，解决了传统模型数据需求量大和计算瓶颈问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统计算模型（如元胞自动机（cellular automata）和相场法（phase-field methods））模拟微观结构演化时面临计算瓶颈，限制了高通量按需工艺优化的应用。生成式机器学习方法（如去噪扩散模型（denoising diffusion models））虽能作为过程-结构映射的替代模型，但训练时需要大量数据，尤其是在工艺条件为连续变量而非离散类别变量时，数据效率问题尤为突出。

Method: 提出连续条件去噪扩散模型，在紧凑工艺-微观结构配对数据集上训练，通过先向微观结构图像添加噪声、再训练神经网络逐步去噪的方式学习结构统计模式。针对连续工艺条件导致的数据低效问题，提出邻近损失训练策略（vicinal-loss training strategy），将数据稀疏区域的工艺条件与数据集中邻近条件关联。结合无分类器引导（classifier-free guidance）和去噪扩散隐式采样（denoising diffusion implicit sampling），实现数据高效的连续条件微观结构生成。

Result: 模型成功生成以锰成分为条件（conditioned on manganese composition）的低碳钢代表性微观结构，准确匹配了相和晶粒形态、晶粒尺寸分布、相分数及界面面积分布等关键物理特征。

Conclusion: 相比经典去噪扩散模型，该方法实现了数据高效的连续条件微观结构生成，为材料及其微观结构的高效工艺设计和优化开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Traditional computational models, such as cellular automata and phase-field methods, are effective for simulating microstructural evolution but often face computational bottlenecks, limiting their application in high-throughput and on-demand process optimization. Generative machine learning approaches, such as denoising diffusion models, have emerged as powerful tools for surrogate modeling of process-structure maps, specifically producing representative microstructures conditioned on process parameters. However, they often require large amounts of data for training, particularly when process conditions are continuous rather than discrete categorical variables. To address this, we present a continuous conditional denoising diffusion model for generating microstructures conditioned on processing parameters. Trained on a compact dataset of process-microstructure pairs, this framework first adds noise to microstructure images and then trains a neural network to progressively remove the noise, learning the underlying statistical patterns of the microstructure. To address data inefficiencies associated with continuously valued process conditions, we propose a vicinal-loss training strategy that associates process conditions in data-sparse regions with nearby conditions in the dataset. Combined with classifier-free guidance and denoising diffusion implicit sampling, this approach enables data-efficient continuous conditional generation of microstructures compared to classical denoising diffusion models. The model successfully generates representative microstructures for low-carbon steel conditioned on manganese composition, matching key physical features such as phase and grain morphology, grain size distribution, phase fraction, and interfacial area distribution. More generally, this approach opens avenues for efficient process design and optimization of materials and their microstructures.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [275] [Resolvent algebras and limit states of interacting canonical ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10283)
*Detlev Buchholz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在预解代数（resolvent algebra）框架下，研究了受谐波力约束的大量相互作用玻色子的正则系综（canonical ensemble）在给定温度下的极限态。结果表明，无论相互作用类型如何，极限态都满足KMS条件或为基态；吸引作用下系综塌缩，部分可观测量消失；排斥作用下可能出现无限多粒子处于同一态的凝聚体（proper condensates）。通过推导谐波约束强度与粒子数的关系，将极限态的无约束平稳性条件与玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensates）研究中常用的条件统一起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究大量相互作用玻色子在谐波约束下的正则系综极限态，旨在理解吸引与排斥相互作用下系综的不同行为，以及谐波约束趋于零（热力学极限）时动态变化对极限态结构的影响。

Method: 采用预解代数（resolvent algebra）框架分析系综极限；通过哈密顿量与代数元素的交换子（commutator）定义导子（derivation）处理动态变化；对相互作用进行正则化（regularization）以确保映射保持在代数内；从极限态在无约束空间均匀极限动态下平稳（stationary/invariant）的条件推导约束强度与粒子数的关系。

Result: 无论相互作用类型，极限态均满足KMS条件或为基态；吸引系综塌缩导致部分可观测量在极限表示中消失；排斥系综若出现无限多粒子在同一态的凝聚体（proper condensates），也会发生类似消失；通过简单的模型说明了所得结构与解释；推导出的谐波约束强度与粒子数的关系涵盖了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚研究中常用的条件。

Conclusion: 预解代数框架为研究相互作用玻色子系综的极限态提供了一种统一且严谨的数学工具，能够系统地处理吸引和排斥相互作用下的系综塌缩与冷凝现象，并将热力学极限条件与凝聚体研究中的经验条件建立联系。

Abstract: The limit states of canonical ensembles of a large number of interacting bosons at a given temperature, which are confined by harmonic forces, are studied in the framework of the resolvent algebra. It is shown that the limits satisfy the KMS condition or are ground states, regardless of the type of interaction. In case of attractive forces, where the ensembles collapse, observables that become meaningless in the limit disappear from the limit representations. For repulsive forces, this can also happen if condensates with an infinite number of particles in the same state (proper condensates) appear in the limit. The resulting structures and their interpretation are illustrated by a simple model. The study of vanishing harmonic forces (thermodynamic limit) involves changes of the dynamics. It is conveniently based on derivations acting on the algebra. They are given by the commutator of the Hamiltonians with the elements of the algebra. To ensure that the images remain in the algebra, the interaction must be regularized. This is accomplished in a manner that has only a minor impact on the dynamics and may be of broader interest. With this input a relation between the strength of the confining harmonic forces and the number of particles in the ensembles is derived from the condition that the limit states are to be stationary (invariant) under the adjoint action of the unconfined, spatially homogeneous limit dynamics. This relation encompasses the conditions that are frequently used in studies of Bose-Einstein condensates.

</details>


### [276] [Semiclassical asymptotics of multiphotonic scattering probabilities with partial indistinguishability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10632)
*Alonso Botero,Hubert de Guise,Orlando Melo-Vargas*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 提出一个用于计算无损多端口干涉仪中多光子散射概率的框架，利用单粒子态张量幂的环面展开，建立从相对相位环面到概率单纯形的映射，揭示大光子数极限下概率的渐近行为，并推导出部分不可区分光子情形的新渐近公式，同时将经典映射的焦散（caustics）和空洞（voids）等特征直接关联到光子聚束模式的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多光子干涉是量子光学与量子信息处理的核心过程，但现有理论在处理任意光子数和任意不可区分度下的散射概率时缺乏统一且高效的渐近分析工具。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立一个能够同时涵盖全同与部分不可区分光子情形、并在大光子数极限下给出清晰渐近行为的通用框架。

Method: 利用多光子态在单粒子态张量幂（tensor powers of single-particle states）中的环面展开（toroidal expansion），定义了一个从相对相位环面（torus of relative phases）到概率单纯形（probability simplex）的映射；通过该映射分析散射概率在大光子数极限下的渐近行为。

Result: 证明了多光子散射概率集中在该映射定义的“经典允许区域”（classically allowed region）内，且多光子分布中的缓变部分重现了该映射诱导的经典测度（classical measure）。建立了部分不可区分光子一般情形下多光子概率的新渐近公式，并为全同光子情形下已知的多光子跃迁振幅提供了单粒子图像解释。此外，框架将经典映射的焦散和空洞等几何特征直接转化为光子聚束概率增大或指数压低的区域预测。

Conclusion: 该框架统一处理了任意光子数和不可区分度下的多光子散射问题，给出了可检验的新物理预测，尤其在大光子数极限下光子聚束模式的几何解释方面，为量子干涉与经典光学现象之间的深层联系提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: We propose a framework for computing multiphotonic scattering probabilities in a lossless multiport interferometer for arbitrary photon numbers and degrees of indistinguishability. By exploiting a toroidal expansion of multiphotonic states in tensor powers of single-particle states, the framework defines a map from a torus of relative phases to the probability simplex that governs the asymptotic behavior of scattering probabilities in the large-photon limit. Specifically, the probabilities concentrate on the "classically allowed region" defined by the map, and the slowly-varying part of the multiphotonic distribution reproduces a classical measure induced by the map. As a result, we are able to establish a new asymptotic formula for the multiphotonic probabilities in a general scenario of partially indistinguishable photons, while also providing a single-particle picture to explain the asymptotics of known multiphotonic transition amplitudes in the fully indistinguishable case. More broadly, our framework yields new, directly testable consequences in relation to asymptotic photon bunching patterns: it translates features of the classical map -- such as caustics and voids -- into direct predictions about regions of large or exponentially suppressed photon-distribution probability.

### [277] [Spectral gap of Lee-Yang Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10765)
*Chaithanya Rayudu,Jun Takahashi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 李-杨定理及其量子推广表明，一大类哈密顿量的配分函数（partition function）在复数磁场平面上的零点仅位于虚轴。本文旨在利用这一零点自由性（zero-freeness）来证明基态谱隙的存在性，并探索其计算上的可处理性。

Method: 利用Asano和Suzuki-Fisher给出的配分函数零点自由性，证明任意Z算符乘积的虚时关联（imaginary-time correlations）呈指数衰减，从而推导出基态谱隙的下界。

Result: 对于任意图上的李-杨哈密顿量（Lee-Yang Hamiltonian），在任意均匀Z场强度h下，基态谱隙至少为h/4，该下界与系统大小和耦合强度无关。

Conclusion: 该结果直接给出了一个多项式时间量子算法，用于计算任意李-杨哈密顿量的基态能量。

Abstract: The Lee-Yang theorem and its quantum extensions state that, for a broad class of Hamiltonians on any graph, the partition function's zeros in the complex magnetic field plane lie only on the imaginary axis. For these Hamiltonians, we prove that under a uniform Z-field of any strength h, the ground state has a spectral gap of at least h/4, independent of the system size and of the coupling strengths. The proof uses the zero-freeness of the partition function as given by Asano and Suzuki-Fisher to show exponential decay of the imaginary-time correlations for any product of Z-operators. Our result gives a polynomial-time quantum algorithm for computing the ground state energy of any Lee-Yang Hamiltonian.

### [278] [Moment-based PPT criteria for random bipartite states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11369)
*Cécilia Lancien,Kieran McShane*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用组合学中的置换技巧估计部分转置随机态矩的平均值，利用测度集中（concentration of measure）论证限定大局部维度 $d$ 下偏离平均值的概率，并结合正交多项式（orthogonal polynomials）下的Hankel行列式评估理论。

Result: 对于层次化矩基PPT准则的每个固定层级 $m \in \mathbb N$，找到了一个阈值环境维度 $s = \lambda_m d^2$，在该值处随机态的行为从违反判据切换到满足判据，且该切换以趋于1的概率发生。

Conclusion: 论文为基于矩的PPT松弛准则在典型高维二分系统中的检测能力提供了严格的渐近刻画，证实了存在一个明确的维度依赖阈值，决定了该类判据能否被随机混合态满足。

Abstract: Moment-based relaxations of the positive partial transpose (PPT) criterion have been recently introduced, as a hierarchy of entanglement criteria involving only experimentally accessible quantities of a given bipartite state. The goal of this work is to study their typical detection performance on high-dimensional bipartite systems. Concretely, we investigate whether random bipartite mixed states on $\mathbb C^d\otimes\mathbb C^d$, obtained as the marginal over an environment $\mathbb C^s$ of a uniformly distributed pure state, generically satisfy or violate them. For each fixed level $m\in\mathbb N$ in this hierarchy of moment-based PPT criteria, we are able to identify a threshold environment dimension $s=λ_md^2$ at which the behavior of the associated random state switches from violating to satisfying it, with probability going to $1$ as $d$ grows. The proof combines combinatorics of permutations techniques to estimate the average value of moments of partially transposed random states and concentration of measure arguments to bound the probability of deviating from such average, when the underlying local dimension $d$ is large. We additionally need tools from the theory of Hankel determinant evaluation via orthogonal polynomials.

### [279] [$p$-Form Gauge Dynamics and Digital Quantum Simulation -- Flux and Cosmological Constant Neutralization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10950)
*Soo-Jong Rey*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在任意维任意定向胞复形（cell complex）上为 ${\mathbb Z}_k$ $p$-形式规范场（$p$-form gauge field）建立了哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）框架，定义了规范四元数（gauge qudit）与带电边界四元数（charged boundary qudit），并将规范编码与量子纠错（quantum error correction）相联系。在 $p=2, k=2$ 的特例下，精确求解一形式高斯定律（Gauss law），将物理希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）参数化为面元电通量变量，约化后得到伊辛型（Ising-type）面模型。通过管-帽淬火（tube-cap quench）数值模拟发现帽区失去20%-37%的占据通量面积，管区几乎钉扎，并在 $(m/\varepsilon_E)_c\simeq1.89$ 处定位动力学交叉。非约化的面-链编码提供局域高斯定律检验与数字实现，约化哈密顿量提供精确基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于胞复形（cell complex）的边界映射 $\partial_p$ 与 $\partial_{p+1}$ 构造规范四元数、高斯定律生成元和磁检验（magnetic checks），定义局域带裙威尔逊算符（dressed Wilson operator），并在 $p=2,k=2$ 时通过精确求解一形式高斯定律将系统约化为伊辛型面模型，进一步采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）在 $4\times4$、$6\times4$ 和 $5\times5$ 环面（torus）上执行管-帽淬火数值模拟。

Result: 管-帽淬火中帽区失去20%-37%的占据通量面积，管区几乎不变；有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）发现张量-密度比（tension-to-density ratio）的动力学交叉点约为 $(m/\varepsilon_E)_c\simeq1.89$。非约化的面-链编码实现局域高斯定律检验与数字实现，约化哈密顿量提供精确基准。

Conclusion: 本文建立的哈密顿量框架将顶形式放电与宇宙学常数中和计算置于一般的高形式哈密顿量及编码框架之中，为规范量子模拟与量子纠错提供了统一的数学基础。

Abstract: I develop a Hamiltonian framework for ${\mathbb Z}_k$ $p$-form gauge fields on arbitrary oriented cell complexes in arbitrary dimensions. Gauge qudits are defined by $p$-cells, charged boundary qudits by $(p-1)$-cells, Gauss-law generators by boundary map $\partial_p$, and magnetic checks by $\partial_{p+1}$. The same cellular structure produces local dressed Wilson operators, and at $k=2$ a Calderbank-Shor-Steane check complex relevant to quantum error correction. I then specialize to $p=2, k=2$, where the magnetic 3-cell term is absent and the one-form Gauss-law can be solved exactly. The physical Hilbert space is parameterized by plaquette electric-flux variables, while the link configuration is reconstructed as the dynamical boundary of the evolving flux domains. The reduced Hamiltonian is an Ising-type plaquette model, where its local transverse-field term is the physical image of the boundary-dressed Wilson operator $σ_p^z\prod_{\ell\in\partial p}τ_\ell^z$. A tube-cap quench compares two initial flux fillings with the same initial boundary loops. Exact diagonalization on $4\times4$, $6\times4$, and $5\times5$ tori finds that the cap loses $20$-$37\%$ of its occupied-flux area, while the tube remains nearly pinned. A finite-size scaling locates a dynamical crossover of tension-to-density ratio near $(m/\varepsilon_E)_c\simeq1.89$. The unreduced plaquette-plus-link encoding provides local Gauss-law checks and a direct digital implementation, while the reduced plaquette-only Hamiltonian supplies the exact benchmark. The result places the specific top-form discharge and the cosmological constant neutralization calculation inside a general higher-form Hamiltonian and coding framework.

Abstract: We demonstrate how the interference effects for a quantum particle in the double-slit experiment can be described by classical probabilities. We investigate a classical field theory for a complex scalar field with probabilistic initial conditions. A central element are conserved charges leading to the concept of particles. These are statistical observables which describe properties of the probability distribution for field configurations. The conserved charges define subsystems for particle excitations of a vacuum state. We encode the probabilistic information for the one-particle subsystem in a complex wave function. The Liouville equation for the classical probability distribution implies that the time evolution of this wave function obeys the Schrödinger equation for a quantum particle in a potential. The potential arises from a space-dependence of the mass term in the otherwise relativistic classical field theory. It can be chosen arbitrarily, realizing the typical quantum effects of interference, tunneling or discrete energy spectra.

### [281] [Near-Optimal Mode Scaling for Finite-Dimensional Boson Sampling via Lie-Algebraic Leakage Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11708)
*Chon-Fai Kam,En-Jui Kuo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对基于确定性物质平台的玻色采样（boson sampling）中因局域希尔伯特空间截断导致的泄漏问题，建立了紧李群不可约表示上的统一框架，并通过戴森级数分析和非交换集中不等式，将多粒子聚束泄漏的谱范数上界收紧至$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{n})$，从而使所需模式数从$m=\Omega(n^4)$降至准最优的$m=\tilde{\Omega}(n^{1+2/(d-1)})$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在确定性物质平台上实现玻色采样时，玻色子模式须编码在有限维局域希尔伯特空间中，这引入了线性光学中不存在的泄漏通道——多粒子聚束（bunching）超出局部截断$d$。该泄漏会破坏采样计算的经典困难性，因此需要严格量化其影响并确定所需空间资源。

Method: 将非相互作用采样统一到紧李群（compact Lie group）的不可约表示框架下，其中跃迁振幅为单粒子跃迁矩阵子矩阵的immanant。通过戴森级数（Dyson series）将关联的多体泄漏算符分解为独立随机矩阵，再利用非交换集中不等式（non-commutative concentration inequalities），在高斯跃迁矩阵模型中证明谱范数集中在$\tilde{O}(\sqrt{n})$量级；随后通过子矩阵比较将结果推广至物理Haar系综。

Result: 谱范数的Haar系综数值结果与闭式$\sqrt{d(n-d+1)}$吻合至亚百分比精度，证实了理论界的紧性。所需模式数从$m=\Omega(n^4)$降至$m=\tilde{\Omega}(n^{1+2/(d-1)})$；对自旋-1表示（$d=3$），开销降至$m=\tilde{\Omega}(n^2)$，达到无碰撞阈值。

Conclusion: 该结果不依赖于粒子统计性质，适用于所有有限维李对称架构，量化了维持采样计算经典困难性所需的空间资源。

Abstract: Boson sampling demonstrates quantum advantage through the interference of indistinguishable particles, with output probabilities governed by matrix permanents. Realizing it on deterministic, matter-based platforms requires encoding the bosonic modes in finite-dimensional local Hilbert spaces, which introduces a leakage channel absent in linear optics: multi-particle bunching beyond the local truncation $d$. We develop a unified framework for non-interacting sampling on the irreducible representations of compact Lie groups, in which the transition amplitude is the immanant of a submatrix of the single-particle transition matrix, recovering the permanent in the bosonic case. Within this framework we bound the bunching leakage through a Dyson-series analysis: decomposing the correlated many-body leakage operator into independent random matrices and applying non-commutative concentration inequalities, we prove, in a Gaussian model of the transition matrix, that its spectral norm concentrates at $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{n})$ rather than the $O(n)$ worst-case of prior spin-based emulations; the passage to the physical Haar ensemble is reduced to a single submatrix-comparison input, verified at leading order. Exact numerics across local dimensions $d=2$--$5$ indicate that the bound is tight, the Haar-ensemble norm matching the closed form $\sqrt{d(n-d+1)}$ to sub-percent accuracy. This tightens the required mode number from $m=Ω(n^4)$ to the near-optimal $m=\tildeΩ(n^{1+2/(d-1)})$; for a spin-1 representation ($d=3$) the overhead falls to $m=\tildeΩ(n^2)$, matching the collision-free threshold. The result is independent of particle statistics and applies across finite-dimensional Lie-symmetric architectures, quantifying the spatial resources needed to preserve sampling hardness.

### [282] [Operational Concealment of Measurement Incompatibility by Quantum Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11762)
*Mohd Asad Siddiqui,Zizhu Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“操作隐藏（operational concealment）”概念，指测量不相容性（measurement incompatibility）在算子层面保持不变，但在量子信道（quantum channel）输出受限观测下变得不可访问。通过伴随-核（adjoint-kernel）框架对信道进行分类，定义隐藏鲁棒性（concealment robustness）并给出半定规划（SDP）表述，证明其与标准不相容鲁棒性（incompatibility robustness）在单射信道中一致，在非单射信道中更小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有测量不相容性理论主要关注算子层面的固有结构，但忽略了在信道输出受限条件下，不相容性可能变得“操作上不可访问”这一现象。为系统刻画这一现象，需要建立统一的理论框架和定量度量方法。

Method: 1) 建立伴随-核（adjoint-kernel）框架，将可观测量（observables）按伴随信道的核（kernel of the adjoint channel）划分为操作等价类（operational equivalence classes）；2) 通过核等价（kernel equivalence）和单调性（monotonicity）对信道进行结构分类；3) 定义隐藏鲁棒性（concealment robustness）度量，给出显式半定规划（SDP）表述；4) 建立近似隐藏（approximate concealment）框架，并对无偏二元量子POVM（unbiased binary qubit POVMs）在秩2单比特幺正信道（rank-2 unital qubit channels）下给出几何刻画。

Result: 1) 隐藏鲁棒性在单射信道（injective channels）下与标准不相容鲁棒性（incompatibility robustness）一致；2) 在非单射信道下严格更小，并通过显式解析族（explicit analytical families）加以验证。

Conclusion: 该工作为操作不可访问的测量不相容性提供了系统刻画和定量处理方法，对受限访问量子信息（restricted-access quantum information）和半设备无关认证（semi-device-independent certification）具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Measurement incompatibility can remain intact at the operator level yet become operationally inaccessible when observations are restricted to the output of a quantum channel; we refer to this phenomenon as operational concealment. We develop a systematic adjoint-kernel framework for operational concealment in which observables are organized into operational equivalence classes determined by the kernel of the adjoint channel. This framework yields a structural classification of channels via kernel equivalence and monotonicity, together with a concealment robustness measure admitting explicit SDP formulations. It also yields an approximate concealment framework and a geometric characterization of concealment for unbiased binary qubit POVMs under rank-2 unital qubit channels. We show that concealment robustness coincides with standard incompatibility robustness for injective channels but can be strictly smaller for non-injective channels, as demonstrated by explicit analytical families. These results provide a systematic characterization and quantitative treatment of operationally inaccessible measurement incompatibility, with implications for restricted-access quantum information and semi-device-independent certification.

</details>


### [283] [Optimal tomography of bosonic and fermionic Gaussian states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11847)

Motivation: 玻色子和费米子高斯量子态在量子光学、多体物理、量子化学、量子计算及量子信息论等领域具有核心作用，但其样本复杂度此前尚未被完全确定。

Result: 玻色子与费米子高斯量子态可在副本数随模式数二次标度（quadratically）下被学习，该结果对纯态和混态均成立，且不依赖于系统的任何能量上界。

Abstract: The sample complexity is the minimum number of copies required to learn an accurate classical description of a quantum state. Bosonic and fermionic Gaussian quantum states are families of quantum states that play a key role in quantum science and technology, from quantum optics and many-body physics to quantum chemistry, quantum computing, and quantum information theory. Despite their importance, their sample complexity had not been fully determined. We settle this open problem and show that both bosonic and fermionic Gaussian states can be learned using a number of copies that scales quadratically in the number of modes, regardless of whether the state is pure or mixed, and independently of any energy bound on the state. ### [284] [Paraparticles intrinsically exhibit Hardy-space breakdown](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11867)
*Kejun Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了非酉交换统计（paraparticle）的本质特征——非酉性——会破坏开放量子系统记忆核（memory kernel）的Hardy空间解析性，导致Kramers–Kronig关系在闭系统谱复化之前就失效，而费米子和玻色子由于交换是酉的，始终免疫这种破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非交换统计（即奇异物态）的记忆核（memory kernel）是否满足Kramers–Kronig（KK）关系，以及其解析结构（analytic structure）如何区别于普通粒子统计。

Method: 利用Hardy空间解析性（Hardy-space analyticity）条件（Laplace变换在上半平面解析）检验记忆核；通过R矩阵非酉性（non-unitarity of the R-matrix）导出度量η与物理Born内积的差异（相对Frobenius范数差异为0.51），并借助Schur引理（Schur's lemma）证明该度量是“影子度量”（shadow metric）；考察耦合到热库时耦合算符处于对称代数之外的情形。

Result: 非酉交换统计导致记忆核在耦合强度g_c ≈ 0.1时出现上半平面极点（upper-half-plane poles），破坏了标准色散关系（Kramers–Kronig relations），且这一破坏发生在闭系统谱复化之前。费米子与玻色子始终免疫；该破坏是内在的，可凭记忆核解析结构区分非酉与非平凡交换统计。

Conclusion: 非酉交换统计内在破坏Kramers–Kronig关系，产生了可在记忆核解析结构中观测的特征信号；这一发现提供了在开放系统层面区分奇异物态与普通粒子统计的新判据。

Abstract: The memory kernel of an open quantum system obeys Kramers--Kronig (KK) relations if and only if its Laplace transform is analytic in the upper half-plane -- a property known as Hardy-space analyticity. Here we show that non-unitary exchange statistics, the defining property of paraparticles, intrinsically breaks Hardy-space analyticity. The metric $η$ that guarantees a real closed-system spectrum for these particles necessarily differs from the physical Born inner product ($\|η- I\|_F / \|I\|_F = 0.51$) -- a mathematical consequence of the R-matrix's non-unitarity, not a parameter choice. This metric is a "shadow metric": Schur's lemma forces it to commute with every bilinear observable, making the distortion physically invisible in the closed system. But when the paraparticle is coupled to a bath, any coupling operator that lies outside the symmetry algebra -- that is, any interaction that sees the internal flavour structure -- exposes the distortion. The memory kernel then develops upper-half-plane poles at coupling $g_c \approx 0.1$, breaking standard dispersion relations before the closed-system spectrum complexifies. Fermions and bosons, whose exchange is unitary ($η= I$ as an analytic fact of the canonical anticommutation algebra), are immune at any coupling, because there is no distortion to expose. The violation is intrinsic: it distinguishes non-unitary exchange statistics from ordinary particle statistics at the level of the memory kernel's analytic structure.

</details>

Method: 本文引入一个数据高效的监督学习框架，利用从子系统提取的约化密度矩阵构造量子核，该量子核可在实验上高效估计。框架在小尺寸子系统（1-4个格点）上训练，用于分类一维格点模型（广义cluster-Ising自旋1/2链和各项异性Haldane自旋1链）的量子相图。

Conclusion: 结果表明，局域约化密度矩阵保留了全局拓扑相的关键特征（vital signatures），为实际表征量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）丰富相图提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: Characterizing quantum topological phases requires measuring non-local string order parameters, demanding access to the full system, which is often experimentally unfeasible. In this work, we introduce a data-efficient supervised learning framework that circumvents this limitation by recognizing quantum phases from small subsystems. Our protocol utilizes a quantum kernel constructed from the reduced density matrices of these subsystems, which can be efficiently estimated experimentally. We benchmark our framework with the classification of the phase diagrams of two spin models on one-dimensional lattices, namely the generalized cluster-Ising spin-1/2 chain and the anisotropic Haldane spin-1 chain. Remarkably, our approach achieves high accuracy in phase classification when operations are limited to as few as one to four sites, and it also generalizes to longer chains even when trained on moderate system sizes. These findings demonstrate that local reduced density matrices preserve vital signatures of global topological phases, offering a practical route to characterize rich phase diagrams of quantum many-body systems.

### [286] [Driven Quantum Stars as Controlled Primitives for Real-Time Spin Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10899)
*Michael Chertkov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将量子比特自旋模型约化为自旋-LL经典扇区与残余量子修正，提出一种基于物理的诊断方法，用于甄别实时自旋动力学中的量子优势边界。控制参数为图配位数（graph coordination），在自旋星模型上构建1/d展开层级，证明相干态返回振幅的叶消除定理，并验证L0与G1近似的收敛阶与数值斜率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子优势（quantum advantage）的评估应基于最强的经典替代模型，而非仅比较微观系统的量子比特性质。需要一种物理驱动的诊断方法，以明确区分可被经典自旋-朗道-利夫希茨（spin-Landau--Lifshitz, LL）动力学替代的行为与真正的量子离散扇区干涉。

Method: 将量子比特自旋模型约化为一个 spin-LL 经典扇区，并将残余量子扇区组织为受控修正。控制参数为图配位数（graph coordination），研究由 d 个叶节点（leaf）和 O(1/d) 枢纽-叶耦合（hub-leaf coupling）构成的自旋星（spin star）模型。对相干态（coherent-state）返回振幅（return amplitude）证明精确的叶消除（leaf elimination），并导出连续时间下的 1/d 层级展开：L0 为驱动单自旋弱平均场理论，G1 为高斯非局域时间影响修正。

Result: 在有界有限时间窗口内（避开边界振幅零点），层级展开给出\log\mathcal A-\log\mathcal A_{\rm L0}=O(1/d)与\log\mathcal A-\log\mathcal A_{\rm L0}-Δ_{\rm G1}=O(1/d^2)的收敛阶；全驱动各向异性系综的数值测试给出斜率分别为 -1.05 和 -2.03。静态、非均匀、对齐及全驱动自旋星构成验证阶梯，并与时间矩阵乘积影响函数基线（temporal matrix-product influence-matrix baseline）比较，划定了互补适用区间。

Conclusion: 该层级展开不同于特罗特网格（Trotter grid）上的秩压缩方法，由物理参数（配位数）排序、在连续时间下构建，且每个截断层级本身即为一种物理理论。LL扇区对应于高配位数极限，为量子优势的边界提供系统性的诊断框架。

Abstract: Quantum advantage in real-time spin dynamics should be assessed against the strongest relevant classical substitutes, not merely against the qubit nature of the microscopic system. We develop a physics-based diagnostic for this boundary by reducing a qubit spin model to a spin-Landau--Lifshitz (LL) classical sector and organizing the residual quantum sector as controlled corrections. The control parameter is graph coordination: we study a spin star with \(d\) leaves and \(O(1/d)\) hub--leaf couplings. In its homogeneous form the star benchmarks the transition from LL-substitutable dynamics to genuinely quantum, discrete-sector interference; in its fully driven form, with time-dependent fields and bilinear couplings, it is the basic message-passing primitive for tree and loopy spin structures. For coherent-state return amplitudes we prove exact leaf elimination and derive a continuous-time \(1/d\) hierarchy. L0 is a driven one-spin weak-mean-field theory, while G1 is a Gaussian nonlocal-in-time influence correction coupling leaf two-time kernels to the hub weak two-point function. On bounded finite-time windows away from zeros of the boundary amplitudes, the hierarchy gives \(\log\mathcal A-\log\mathcal A_{\rm L0}=O(1/d)\) and \(\log\mathcal A-\log\mathcal A_{\rm L0}-Δ_{\rm G1}=O(1/d^2)\); numerical tests on fully driven anisotropic ensembles give slopes \(-1.05\) and \(-2.03\). Static, inhomogeneous, aligned, and fully driven stars provide validation rungs, and comparison with a temporal matrix-product influence-matrix baseline delineates complementary regimes. Unlike rank compression on a Trotter grid, the hierarchy is ordered by a physical parameter, formulated in continuous time, and each truncation level is itself a physical theory, with the LL sector as the high-coordination limit.

Here it is argued that a distinct temporal renormalization-group eigenvalue is needed for quantum criticality in open systems weakly coupled to their finite-temperature environment. This new physics enables the formulation of a general scaling theory that can accurately account for the critical properties including the specific Kibble-Zurek scaling in such open quantum systems. Remarkably, the critical exponents of time-related quantities are altered nonperturbatively regardless of how weak the coupling is, except for an Ohmic bath. Beyond serving as a benchmark for quantum hardware, this geometry-resolved approach provides a route toward quantum simulations of fractional Chern insulators and strongly correlated topological phases in realistic two-dimensional materials.

By tuning the system parameters, we show that the direction of the NHSE under open boundary conditions can be reversed and can even become energy dependent. Our results establish staggered nonreciprocal inter-leg hopping as an effective mechanism for engineering both the non-Hermitian skin effect and topological phases in ladder systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于门操作的数字量子模拟为研究强关联系统的多体物理提供了新范式，但电子-声子模型中玻色子自由度（bosonic degrees of freedom）需要昂贵的有限维编码，对仅使用量子比特的模拟器构成挑战。为此，本文旨在探索一种替代方案，以避免代价高昂的玻色子编码，实现更高效的强关联电子-声子系统量子模拟。

Method: 本文采用数字-类比电路量子电动力学（digital-analog circuit QED）架构：费米子编码在transmon量子比特中，玻色子由微波谐振器直接表示。核心构建块是一个量子比特-谐振器拉比门（qubit-resonator Rabi gate），通过一系列共振Jaynes-Cummings门与单量子比特旋转层交替实现。以此拉比门为基本酉操作，构造了Hubbard-Holstein模型和Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型的量子电路。

Result: 文章展示了如何通过电路模拟探测上述模型中的非经典声子物理（nonclassical phonon physics）和量子混沌（quantum chaos）信号，并开发了适用于近期超导量子硬件的测量协议和变分协议。

Conclusion: 所提出的数字-类比电路QED架构为强关联电子-声子系统的量子模拟提供了一条可行的替代路径，能够在近期超导量子硬件上实现非经典声子物理和量子混沌现象的探测与验证。

Abstract: Gate-based digital quantum simulations offer an exciting new paradigm for studying the many-body physics of strongly correlated systems. In this context, electron-phonon models are challenging for qubit-only quantum simulators, as bosonic degrees of freedom require costly finite-dimensional encodings. Here, we elaborate on an alternative approach based on a digital-analog circuit QED architecture, where fermions are encoded in transmon qubits while bosons are represented directly by microwave resonators. The central building block of this framework is a qubit-resonator Rabi gate that emulates strong electron-phonon coupling and can be implemented through a sequence of resonant Jaynes-Cummings gates interleaved with layers of single-qubit rotations. Using this Rabi gate as the fundamental unitary operation, we construct quantum circuits for the Hubbard-Holstein and Yukawa-Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev models, which describe, respectively, strongly correlated electrons coupled to phonons and phonon-mediated interactions among Majorana fermions. We further demonstrate how nonclassical phonon physics and signatures of quantum chaos in these models can be probed through circuit simulations, and develop measurement and variational protocols tailored to near-term superconducting quantum hardware.

</details>


### [291] [Quantum probe advantage in learning many-body systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11829)
*Wenzheng Dong,Andrew G. Green,Vlatko Vedral,Jinzhao Sun*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，通过对量子探针（quantum probe）进行相干控制并在末端测量，能够构建比传统响应理论（response theory）更广的操作性学习框架。该框架通过量子电路描述统一了光谱学、探针显微术和基于探针的量子技术，使得从探针读出中学习多体性质成为可能，且所需探针资源取决于目标关联复杂度而非系统规模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统（quantum many-body system）中哪些性质在操作性上可访问，是光谱学、热力学和量子信息科学的核心问题。传统响应理论仅在系统范式中给出答案，而本文旨在证明可控量子探针能提供超出响应理论的操作性学习框架。

Method: 本文通过量子电路描述统一了光谱学、探针显微术和基于探针的量子技术，建立了共同的操作性框架。在此框架下，发展了仅从探针读出中学习多体性质的量子协议（quantum protocols），并利用纠缠探针（entangled probes）访问如冯·诺伊曼熵（von Neumann entropy）等多体性质。

Result: 量子探针的约化动力学（reduced dynamics）普遍编码了目标的反换位符（anti-commutator）和混合阶关联子（mixed-order correlators），因此探针测量可提供响应函数或单个探针一般无法访问的涨落、非平衡结构和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）。纠缠探针可访问冯·诺伊曼熵等性质，且所需探针资源与目标关联复杂度而非多体系统规模成比例。

Conclusion: 量子探针不仅是更灵敏的传感器，更提供了一种不同于层析成像（tomography）或量子模拟（quantum simulation）的学习多体性质的新途径。

Abstract: Which properties of a quantum many-body system are operationally accessible is a central question underlying spectroscopy, thermodynamics, and quantum information science. Conventional response theory answers this question within a system-only paradigm: one perturbs and measures the matter itself, obtaining susceptibility built from causally ordered nested commutators. Here we show that coherently controlled quantum probes, when measured at the end, define a strictly larger operational learning framework beyond that accessible from response theory. We establish this through a quantum-circuit description that unifies spectroscopy, probe microscopy, and probe-based quantum technologies within a common operational framework, from which we develop quantum protocols for learning many-body properties from probe readout only. This advantage arises because the reduced dynamics of quantum probes generically encode anti-commutator and mixed-order correlators of the target; therefore, measurements on the probe provide access to fluctuations, non-equilibrium structure, and entanglement entropy that are in general not accessible through response functions or a single probe alone. Moreover, we demonstrate that entangled probes can access many-body properties such as von Neumann entropy. We prove that the required probe resources scale with the complexity of the target correlations rather than with the size of the many-body system. Quantum probes are therefore not merely more sensitive sensors but provide a new way to learn many-body properties distinct from those of tomography or quantum simulation.

</details>


### [292] [Optimal operating temperature for industry-compatible silicon spin quantum computing: colder is not necessarily better](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11846)
*Paul Steinacker,Amanda E. Seedhouse,Nard Dumoulin Stuyck,Tuomo Tanttu,MengKe Feng,Santiago Serrano,Ensar Vahapoglu,Samuel K. Bartee,Philip Y. Mai,Alexis Shaw,Andreas Nickl,Sebastian Pauka,Brendan Harlech-Jones,Juan P. Dehollain,Fay E. Hudson,Kok Wai Chan,Thomas A. Ohki,David Reilly,Christopher C. Escott,Chih Hwan Yang,Wee Han Lim,Arne Laucht,Andre Saraiva,Andrew S. Dzurak,Jared H. Cole*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过门层析成像（gate set tomography）测量工业与学术环境制备的硅自旋量子比特在不同温度下的性能，结合低温冷却需求与量子纠错开销，构建了硅量子计算机的通用功耗模型，发现存在一个有限的最优工作温度，且当前器件在约1K附近存在交叉温度（crossover temperature），超过该温度后门保真度（gate fidelity）急剧下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅自旋量子比特（silicon spin qubits）因与半导体制造工艺兼容而成为大规模量子计算的主要候选方案。然而，规模化至可容错处理器将产生远超毫开尔文温度下可用冷却功率的热负载。提高工作温度可降低冷却要求，但会减少门保真度（gate fidelity），增加量子纠错（quantum error correction）开销。因此，确定使总功耗最小化的工作温度是实现商用可行量子计算机的关键挑战。

Method: 利用门层析成像（gate set tomography）对工业与学术环境中制造的双量子比特硅芯片在不同温度下进行基准测试。基于测量得到的相干时间（coherence time）、门保真度和态制备与测量（state-preparation-and-measurement, SPAM）不保真度数据，构建了一个结合低温冷却需求与量子纠错开销的通用功耗模型（general power model）。

Result: 升高温度显著缩短了相干时间，并增加了门和SPAM不保真度。模型表明存在一个有限的最优工作温度，且该温度受当前器件中约1K附近的交叉温度（crossover temperature）强烈影响，超过该温度后门保真度迅速退化。

Conclusion: 这些结果将器件层面的保真度限制与系统层面的功耗需求联系起来，为大规模硅量子计算机的设计提供了指导原则。

Abstract: Silicon spin qubits are a leading candidate for large-scale quantum computing owing to their compatibility with semiconductor manufacturing. However, scaling to useful fault-tolerant processors will likely generate thermal loads that exceed the cooling power available at millikelvin temperatures. Raising the operating temperature eases cooling requirements but reduces gate fidelity, increasing the overhead of quantum error correction. Identifying the operating temperature that minimizes total power consumption is therefore a key challenge for commercially viable quantum computers. Here, we use gate set tomography to benchmark two-qubit silicon chips fabricated in both industrial and academic environments over a range of temperatures. Elevated temperatures substantially shorten coherence times and increase gate and state-preparation-and-measurement infidelities. Based on these measurements, we develop a general power model for silicon quantum computers that combines cryogenic cooling requirements with error-correction overheads. We show that a finite optimal operating temperature exists and is strongly influenced by a crossover temperature near 1 K in current devices, above which gate fidelity degrades rapidly. These results connect device-level fidelity limitations to system-level power requirements, providing design guidelines for large-scale silicon quantum computers.

</details>

### [293] [Quality control and quality assurance evaluation of ALFE2, a large-dynamic-range front-end ASIC de-veloped for the ATLAS Liquid Argon Calorimeter high-luminosity LHC upgrade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10458)
*E. Buschmann,G. Carini,G. Chatzianastasiou,H. Chen,Y. Chen,M. Dabrowski,G. Deptuch,L. Duflot,M. Feo,J. Kierstead,T. Liu,H. Ma,D. Matakias,N. Morange,M. Oliveira,S. Rescia,E. Rossi,S. Tang,M. Tamari,H. Xu*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了专为ATLAS液氩量能器（LAr Calorimeter）HL-LHC升级设计的前端专用集成电路ALFE2。该芯片包含四个前置放大器/成形器通道（preamplifier/shaper channel），每个通道提供两种不同增益输出以覆盖16位动态范围。为此开发了自动化机器人质检系统，截至2025年9月已评估超过10%的8万颗芯片，建立了分级标准（grading criteria），评估良率超过85%。辐照测试显示总电离剂量（TID）下无显著性能退化，单粒子效应（SEE）测试外推得出HL-LHC运行期间整个ATLAS LAr量能器的单粒子翻转（SEU）率低于每天4.6次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计了一款包含四通道前置放大器/成形器、每通道提供双增益输出的专用ASIC（ALFE2）。开发了一套自动化机器人检测系统用于芯片的质量控制测试。对超过10%的8万颗芯片进行了评估以建立分级标准；并对芯片进行了总电离剂量（TID）辐照测试和单粒子效应（SEE）测试，以评估其抗辐照性能。

Result: 建立了分级标准（grading criteria），基于该标准的评估良率（yield）超过85%，该标准已应用于正在进行的全面生产质量控制（full-production QC）。总电离剂量（TID）测试中未观察到显著性能退化。基于单粒子效应（SEE）测试结果，外推得出HL-LHC运行期间ATLAS LAr量能器整体的单粒子翻转（SEU）率低于每天4.6次。

Conclusion: ALFE2芯片在性能、良率及抗辐照能力方面均满足ATLAS液氩量能器HL-LHC升级的要求。自动化机器人检测系统和分级标准的建立，为大规模生产质量管控提供了有效手段。

Abstract: ALFE2 is a front-end ASIC developed for the ATLAS Liquid Argon (LAr) Calorimeter upgrade during the High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider (HL-LHC) phase. ALFE2 comprises four preamplifier/shaper channels, each providing two distinct gain outputs to cover a 16-bit dynamic range. A robotic system has been developed for the automatic quality control test of ALFE2, and over 10% of the 80,000 chips have been evaluated by September 2025. The evaluation has allowed us to establish grading criteria. Using these criteria, a yield of over 85% was achieved in the evaluation tests, and these criteria are now being applied to the ongoing full-production QC. Irradiation tests were also performed for the quality assurance of ALFE2. No significant performance degradation was observed during the total-ionizing-dose (TID) test. Based on the single-event effect (SEE) test results, an error rate of fewer than 4.6 single-event upsets (SEUs) per day is extrapolated for the entire ATLAS LAr Calorimeter during HL-LHC operation.

### [294] [Self-organized quasicrystals and their excitations in dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates via optical feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10141)
*Liang-Jun He,Fabian Maucher,Yong-Chang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过在偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate）中结合固有偶极-偶极相互作用与光子介导相互作用，实现了多尺度竞争，从而在实验可行参数下产生了具有十二重旋转对称性的十二边形准晶（dodecagonal quasicrystals），并提出了动力学制备方案及集体激发谱的数值计算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准晶（quasicrystal）源于具有不可公度特征长度（incommensurate characteristic length scales）的竞争相互作用，但如何在可控实验体系中实现此类多尺度相互作用仍是挑战。本研究旨在通过偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的内在偶极相互作用与光学反馈诱导的光子介导相互作用的协同，构造所需的竞争条件。

Method: 引入偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate），利用固有偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions）与耦合至激发态能级（excited-state manifold）及光学反馈（optical feedback）产生的光子介导相互作用的协同效应；通过Bogoliubov激发谱（Bogoliubov excitation spectrum）分析系统的不稳定性，并发展集体激发谱的数值计算框架。

Result: 在Bogoliubov激发谱中出现两个显著的旋子不稳定性（roton instabilities），导致基态相图（ground-state phase diagram）中出现了具有十二重旋转对称性（twelvefold rotational symmetry）的十二边形准晶（dodecagonal quasicrystals），且对应的参数处于实验现实范围内。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中可通过多尺度相互作用实现准晶序，提出了动力学制备协议，并建立了计算准晶集体激发谱的通用数值方法，为准晶的超冷原子实验实现提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Quasicrystals emerge from competing interactions with incommensurate characteristic length scales that inhibit translational periodicity. Here, we show that such multiscale interactions can be realized in a dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate through the interplay between intrinsic dipole-dipole interactions and photon-mediated interactions generated by coupling to an excited-state manifold together with a suitably engineered optical feedback. This interplay gives rise to two pronounced roton instabilities in the Bogoliubov excitation spectrum, leading to a rich ground-state phase diagram including dodecagonal quasicrystals with twelvefold rotational symmetry for experimentally realistic parameters. We further propose a protocol to access these quasicrystals dynamically and develop a general numerical framework for calculating their collective excitation spectra.

</details>


### [295] [Edge-state interferometry as a probe of local flux in isolated quantum Hall systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.10868)
*Botao Wang,Nathan Goldman,André Eckardt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出在无外储库的孤立量子模拟平台（如超冷原子）中，通过静态边缘流直接提取量子点接触（QPC）处手征边缘态的散射特性，并利用其对Aharonov-Bohm型相位的敏感性，设计平衡态与非平衡态协议来探测局域磁通及任意子统计相位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现与固态系统中量子点接触（quantum point contact）类似的输运设置对于孤立量子模拟平台（如超冷原子）具有重要意义，但通常需要耦合到外部储库（reservoir），这在实验上极具挑战性。本文旨在寻找无需外储库即可从孤立晶格系统中提取QPC散射特性的方法。

Method: 利用手征边缘态（chiral edge states）在QPC处的散射对Aharonov-Bohm型相位（Aharonov-Bohm-type phases）的敏感性，从孤立无储库晶格系统的稳态边缘流（stationary edge currents）中直接提取散射信息。提出两种协议：平衡态协议通过基态边缘流探测局域磁通；动力学方案基于突然移除势偏置后的淬火后演化（post-quench evolution），对有限温度和粒子数涨落具有鲁棒性。

Result: 展示了无需外部储库即可从孤立晶格系统的稳态边缘流中提取QPC散射特性。平衡态协议可利用散射对Aharonov-Bohm型相位的敏感性探测局域磁通；动力学方案在有限温度与粒子数涨落下仍保持稳健。由于任意子激发（anyonic excitations）本身关联局域量子化磁通，该方法可推广至量子工程平台中任意子统计相位的探测。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种在孤立量子模拟平台中实现类似QPC输运测量的新途径，并有望扩展到对任意子统计相位（anyonic statistical phases）的探测，为量子工程化系统中的拓扑物态研究提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Quantum point contacts (QPCs) are essential tools for transport experiments in solid-state systems, enabling the detection of fractional charges and anyonic braiding statistics. Realizing analogous transport setups in isolated quantum-simulation platforms, such as ultracold atoms, remains challenging, since it typically requires coupling to external reservoirs. Here we show that the scattering properties of chiral edge states at a QPC can instead be extracted directly from the stationary edge currents of an isolated, reservoir-free lattice system. Exploiting the sensitivity of this scattering to Aharonov-Bohm-type phases, we propose an equilibrium protocol to detect local magnetic fluxes from ground-state edge currents. We further introduce a dynamical scheme, robust against finite temperature and particle-number fluctuations, based on the post-quench evolution following a sudden potential-bias removal. Since anyonic excitations are themselves associated with a local, quantized magnetic flux, our approach should extend to probing anyonic statistical phases in quantum-engineered platforms.

</details>


### [296] [Ab initio path integral Monte Carlo study of the 2D uniform electron liquid at finite temperatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.11406)
*Tobias Dornheim,Fotios Kalkavouras,Paul Hamann,Zhandos A. Moldabekov,Jan Vorberger,Panagiotis Tolias*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 通过从头算路径积分蒙特卡洛（PIMC）模拟，系统研究了二维均匀电子气（2DEG）在宽泛密度和温度参数范围内的结构、线性密度响应和谱性质，发现了强耦合区域动态结构因子中的旋子（roton）特征，并对新的介电理论实现进行了基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维均匀电子气（2DEG）是凝聚态物理中的重要模型系统，但现有理论在宽参数范围内的准确性缺乏系统的从头算（ab initio）基准测试。需要高精度的量子蒙特卡洛模拟数据来评估和指导理论发展。

Method: 采用从头算路径积分蒙特卡洛（ab initio path integral Monte Carlo, PIMC）方法，在密度参数 $r_s=0.1,\dots,50$ 和约化温度 $\Theta=0.5,\dots,16$ 的宽泛范围内模拟二维均匀电子气（2DEG），并分析其结构、线性密度响应和谱性质。

Result: 在强耦合（strong coupling）和中等波数区域，动态结构因子（dynamic structure factor）中发现了明确的旋子（roton-type）特征。此外，对 Kalkavouras 等人提出的新型介电理论（dielectric theory）实现进行了基准测试，评估了其在液态相图内结构和谱性质方面的表现。

Conclusion: 所提供的PIMC模拟结果可用于对现有理论和近似方法进行基准测试（benchmark），并为新方法的开发提供指导。

Abstract: We present extensive \emph{ab initio} path integral Monte Carlo (PIMC) simulations of the two-dimensional uniform electron gas (2DEG), covering a broad range of density parameters $r_s=0.1,\dots,50$ and temperatures $Θ=k_\textnormal{B}T/E_\textnormal{Fermi}=0.5,\dots,16$. This allows us to analyze various structural, linear density response and spectral properties. We find clear evidence of a \emph{roton-type} feature in the dynamic structure factor at strong coupling and intermediate wavenumbers. We also benchmark novel dielectric theory implementations for the 2DEG~[Kalkavouras \emph{et al.}~arXiv:2601.14989] for structural and spectral properties across the liquid phase diagram. The PIMC results can be used to benchmark existing theories and approximations, and guide the development of new methodologies.

</details>
